# Tabrat n ddheb

Beddeɣ zdat n tgennarit i fehmeɣ d lbusṭa. Nniɣ-d: ‚Ad kecmeɣ ɣer lbusṭa-agi ad steqsiɣ ma sÆiɣ tabrat.‛

Kecmeɣ amzun di tewwurt, la leḥḥuɣ daxel n umarur, simmal tedduɣ ɣer zdat simmal yettzad fell-i ṭṭiq. Ssiwḍeɣ armi d anida qrib ad mlilen fell-i yigufa. Mi waleɣ akken mačči d abrid yessufuɣen, Æerḍeɣ ad d-uɣaleɣ ɣer deffir. Maca ufiɣ ulamek i d-zziɣ ula s tmuɣli-w ɣer deffir. Mi ḥṣiɣ tenneqḍaÆ-iyi tuzzya ɣer deffir, fkiɣ timisit i ṭṭiq-nni, la tedduɣ s tidist. Mi Æyiɣ di tidist-nni, rfiɣ uɣaleɣ la tedduɣ qbala xas la d-yettzad fell-i lḥerṣ. Issiweḍ-iyi ṭṭiq-
nni la tedduɣ ɣer zdat la ttaǧǧeɣ aksum-iw ɣer deffir; ṭṭṭfeɣ iman-iw s ssber xas akken ur umineɣ ara s leslak-iw. Mi Æeddeɣ di tewwurt yessufuɣen si tgennarit-nni, ffɣeɣ ɣer yiwen n ubraḥ yewseÆ, rnu yegdes. Abraḥ-nni ur yettwalḥaq ara s tmuɣli!

Zdat tewwurt-nni seg i ffɣeɣ, yella yiwen n urgaz d ameÆdur, ssneɣ-t d amjahed aqdim, isem-is Ḥmed –u Muḥ u LaÆmara. Fehmeɣ-t d axeddam n lbusṭa-nni. Mi leḥqeɣ ɣer-s, nniɣ-as: ‚Ula ass-agi ur sÆiɣ ara tabrat a Dda Ḥmed?‛. Iwehha-yi-d s ufus-is am win ara yenhun wayeḍ akken ur iḥemmeq ara, sliɣ yenna-yi-d: ‚A Meẓyan a Meẓyan, rrbeḥ deg ufus n Rebbi. LaÆmara n WaÆrab yeÆya deg-s. Abrid-agi ad ak-aruɣ tabrat n ddheb, ad ak-tt-id-rren bihfih, ad ak-id-nadiɣ lxedma.‛

Ukiɣ-d si targit !

1979

Yeɣrreq lbabur yes-i Lliɣ di terba n yilmeẓyen nerkeb akamyun, neqqim d sin yiduren. YeqleÆ yes-neɣ ukamyun-nni si temdint yettusemman Rrɣaya, neqsed ɣer temdint n Lezzayer.

Anehha
r-nni d wid yeddan tama-s ur ten-neḥṣi ara d anwa-ten maca aqerru-nni n ukamyun ur yesÆi ara ula d aceqqiq i t-1id-yestewÆan ɣer-neɣ.

Nekk   iṣaḥ-iyi-d umkan  deg udur  n  tama   tayeffust.

Akamyun-nni   simmal   irennu abrid ɣer  zdat    simmal irennu di leɣṣeb-is. Mi yewweḍ  yes-neɣ     s anekcum n temdint yettusemman      Ḥusayn Dday, waleɣ di tama-nni tayeffust yettwabna uxxam d ajdid s wagens amezwaru yettilin ɣef wakal, sbedden-as tigejda n wuzzal i wagens wis sin.

Ɣef lewhi n wagens-nni wis sin, yettwaxdem yiwen n rref n umeḥrab. Rref-nni yekcem-d abrid. Mi qrib ad  naweḍ  ɣer ṭṭiq-nni n ubrid, yelḥeq-aneɣ-d    wayeḍ ukamyun yellan yettabaÆ-aneɣ-d.

Akamyun-nni anect n lbabur rnu iḥmeq-d akken ad aɣ-yezwar. Mi waleɣ akken, fehmeɣ anehhar n ukamyun-nni yeqsed-d ad yesseḍru yid-neɣ tawaɣit.

Ma d anehhar n ukamyun-nni deg i nella, yeḥreṣ akamyun   ɣer rrif n ubrid akken ad isaÆef   ɣef twaɣit. Nekni s wid yettwalin di lḥerṣ-nni neqḍeÆ layas ɣef tudert, ad aɣ-d-iḥaz ukamyun neɣ ad aɣ-d-iḥaz rref.

Nekk nniɣ deg wul-iw: ‚Wigi yeddan di tama tazelmaḍt iban leslak-nsen, ma d nekni n tama tayeffust, ur cikkeɣ ara ad yeslek ula d yiwen seg-nneɣ.‛

Di taggara n taluft, neslek di lḥerṣ-nni, ur nedhem ur nettwadhem. Mi  aɣ-iÆedda laÆǧeb-nni i  aɣ-d-itebÆen, nelḥeq  ɣer cceṭ   n lebḥer. Di temdint tamanaɣt yeḥbes ukamyun-nni. Ma d akamyun-nni nniḍen yeḥbes zdat-neɣ di lmarṣa n lbaburat, yuɣal yetti-d d lbabur yeḥbes di tlemmast  n  ubrid mačči di  rrif n lebḥer !  Wwint-iyi
lewhayem, afeɣ-d iman-iw daxel n lbabur-nni yellan berra n waman. Ṭṭfeɣ amkan qqimeɣ ɣer tama n sin n yilmeẓyen n taddart-iw, yiwen isem-is Lḥusin wayeḍ Muḥemmed. I sin yuɣ-iten lḥal d iɣriben di tmurt n Fransa. Mi ufiɣ iman-iw yid-sen, fehmeɣ amzun lliɣ d aɣrib ula d nekk. Waleɣ lmerṣa-nni teččur d lɣaci, a win yersen si lbabur-nni ad iserreḥ s tazzla n lferḥ. Imir fehmeɣ d taswiÆt-nni i ssarameɣ ad tfak lɣerba ɣef tarwa n Lezzayer merra. Lbabur-nni yewwi-d iɣriben ɣer tmurt-nsen.

S wakka ḥulfeɣ s wul-iw yeččur-d d lferḥ. Lferḥ-nni yuɣal d leḥmeq ur i wumineɣ ara tfak lɣerba fell-i alamma yers uḍar-iw deg wakal n tmurt-iw. Ttraǧuɣ nnuba-w n tuffɣa si lbabur-nni, imir ad urareɣ lferḥ d yirfiqen-iw, nniɣ deg wul-iw: ‚Mi ffɣen sin-agi akked qqimeɣ ad ffɣeɣ yid-sen.‘. Maca wid-nni, ttwaliɣ deg-sen ur ḥerklen ara i trusi si lbabur. Uɣaleɣ fehmeɣ-ten d rrwaḥ i qesden ɣer lɣerba mačči d tuɣalin ɣer tmurt-nsen. Imir yeqqim-d kan ad myeǧǧeɣ yid-sen sslam. Nleqmeɣ muddeɣ afus-iw i Lḥusin d Muḥ, nemsalam nniɣ-asen: ‚ǧǧiɣ-awen lehna, ruḥet ad isahel Rebbi fell-awen.‘. Yeḍsa-d ɣer-i Lḥusin, yenna-yi-d: ‚Aql-aneɣ newweḍ-d ɣer Lezzayer, yak dagi ara ners akk.‘. Nniɣ-as: ‚Ḥṣiɣ a Lḥusin maca wicqa ma nemsalam.‘

Yefka-iyi-d afus-is nemsalam. Ufiɣ-d iman-iw greɣ-d weḥd-i daxel n lbabur-nni. Mmuqleɣ si ṭṭaq waleɣ Lḥusin d Muḥ ddan di terbaÆt taneggarut yersen si lbabur-nni. La leḥḥun deffir n terbaÆt la yi-d-ttwehhin s yifassen-nsen,
qqaren-iyi-d : ‚ BqaÆlaxir a Meẓyan.‛ . Nekk qqareɣ-asen :

‚Qqimet di lehna, ǧǧiɣ-ken di lehna.‛; ar dqal nniɣ-d deg wul-iw : ‚ Ula d nekk ilaq ad rseɣ si lbabur-agi uqbel ad iruḥ yes-i ad iyi-iɣerreq di tmura! ‛ Gemneɣ-tt-id i trusi si lbabur-nni. Greɣ asurif, iban-iyi-d lbabur-nni abrid deg-s yewseÆ, ma d imukan, yella kan umkan-nni inu. Mi leḥqeɣ s asqif n lbabur, yella ubrid s tunnḍa gar ssnasel, rnu abrid-nni d imiḍyiq. Leḥḥuɣ gar ssnasel-nni, lweqt fell-i la yettfat ma d ul-iw iḥemmeq ɣer trusi n uḍar-iw s ufella n wakal n tmurt-iw. Lḥiɣ armi d anida i d-nneqḍaÆent ssnasel-nni deg usqif n lbabur, leḥqeɣ uliɣ di tlata trekkabin, dewreɣ ɣef yeffus, waleɣ abrid yettkemmil deg usqif. Abrid-nni simmal d ṭṭiq ɣer zdat. Ansi i d-tenneqḍaÆ tmuɣli-w deg usqif-nni, waleɣ tilemẓit d yilemẓi uzgan-d am tlisa, gar-asen yella uqjun d aseṭṭaf yeftek-iyi-d s wallen-is.

Mi waleɣ akken nniɣ deg wul-iw : « Wissen kan ma ad iyi-anfen ad Æeddiɣ.‛ Mi leḥqeɣ ɣer-sen, ilemẓi-nni yuɣal di rrif. Aqjun-nni ulac-it. Tilemẓit-nni tuɣal-iyi-d d zzerb, la yi-tettaski zdat-i tegguma ad iyi-tanef ad Æeddiɣ. Tban-iyi-d di ṣṣifa-s d tacebḥant, tesÆa lekḥul d iberkanen, yefka-as Rebbi zzin d sser armi ugaren fell-as.

Mi refdeɣ ɣer-s tamuɣli-w s wurfan, ad d-tezmumeg ɣer-i dɣa yurad wul-iw, aɣbel-iw ma furqeɣ tuzyint-agi. Di tazwara tban-iyi-d s ṣṣifa n trumit, simmal rennuɣ deg-s tamuɣli, tettban-iyi-d s ccbaḥa n teqbaylit. Taggara tenṭeq-d ɣer-i s teqbaylit. Imir izad fell-i lferḥ d leḥmala. Nebda nettmeslay s umeslay n ṣṣwab d lmaÆqul xas akken tufrar
tayri gar-aneɣ. S uyagi i d-terna lÆezz ɣer wul-iw. Maḍi mi d-mmekteɣ tamurt-iw ziɣ tettirẓigeḍ a tamment! Yeqqar-d wul-iw :  « Mender  amek   i teḍra d  wid-nni    akked mcarakeɣ lferḥ d lqerḥ? Wissen ma ad leḥqeɣ kra deg-sen neɣ ahat fukken?‛. Mi mmuqleɣ di tuzyint-nni teččur ul-iw.   ḍḥiɣ msebḍaɣ d rray-iw. Uɣaleɣ beddeɣ di ttexmim ɣef umgarad-nni i d-yellan gar wallen-iw d wul-iw. Mi gliɣ ɣef laÆqel-iw, afeɣ-t iwafeq kan laḥmala n tmurt-iw.

Ulamma   bɣiɣ  ad farṣeɣ taswiÆt d tuzyint-nni,  meÆna uggadeɣ ad ifat lḥal ma yuɣal lbabur yes-i, dayen ur yettÆawad ad d-yecreq fell-i yiṭij n tmurt-iw.

Ssedheɣ tamcumt-nni, sɣefleɣ-tt. Rewleɣ fell-as. Lḥiɣ deg usqif-nni, leḥqeɣ ɣer tlata n trekkadin, udreɣ-tent. afeɣ-d iman-iw di dderb n lbabur. Waleɣ tawwurt yessuffuɣen ɣer  berra tella di dderb-nni. Tawwurt-nni ur tban   d tawwurt neɣ d ṭṭaq!  layet ɣef wagens n dderb-nni s lqis n tiddi-w, terna teḍyeq, amdan yuffayen ur yettÆedday ara seg-s.

Ula d tirekkadin ur as-llant ara, llant-as kan tlata tgejda n  usɣar mÆidlent   s lewhi n wemnar   armi   d talemmast n wagens. Fehmeɣ sufella n tgejda-nni i Æeddan wid-nni yersen si lbabur.

Tigejda-nni mqaranent, ttwaxedment d abrid yestugnan. Greɣ aḍar-iw s leḥmeq, tigejda-nni mwexxarent. Ula xas akken yella ṭṭmeÆ ad iyi-yeshel ubrid ad  Æeddiɣ. Greɣ asurif sufella n  tgejdit  tamezwarut, ccḍeɣ-d  seg-s.

Tagejdit tis snat greɣ sin yisurrifen sufella-s, ccḍeɣ-d. Tis tlata-nni, greɣ tlata n yisurrifen neṣfeɣ-tt s tikli, ccḍeɣ seg-s uzgaɣ-d beddeɣ di tlemmast n wagens-nni.
Tigejda-nni ttint-d d isulas mÆidlen si lḥiḍ ɣer lḥiḍ uɣalen-iyi-d d zzerb zdat-i. Ggreɣ-d ttemqellaÆeɣ d yisulas-nni armi i asen-ssurfeɣ. Uzzleɣ ɣer tewwurt-nni, mi leḥqeɣ ad ffɣeɣ deg-s, tennemdal-d fell-i. Wexreɣ ɣer deffir, uɣaleɣ s amkan-nni seg i uzzleɣ. Neṭqeɣ s leḥzen nniɣ-d: ‚LmeÆna n targit-agi d lɣerba-w ara iḍulen!‛. Ṭreḍqeɣ d imeṭṭawen, la ttruɣ ttraǧuɣ melmi ara waliɣ telddi-d tewwurt-nni imedlen fell-i. TaswiÆt akka, waleɣ telldi-d. Mi uzzleɣ ɣer-s teḍra-iyi-d am tikkelt-nni tamezwarut. Mi uɣaleɣ s amkan-iw, ttarǧuɣ ttruɣ, nniɣ-d: ‚Tagi d tinna n bqaÆlaxir.‛

Tikkelt tis tlata mi yi-d telldi tewwurt, daɣen teḍra-yi-d am wakken i yi-d-tḍerru. Beddeɣ zdat tewwurt-nni, meǧdeɣ s yimeṭṭi, nniɣ-d: ‚Yeqqim-iyi-d kan ad uɣaleɣ s amkan-iw.‛. Mi akken qeḍÆeɣ layas, gemneɣ-tt ad uɣaleɣ s amkan-nni deg i lliɣ rekbeɣ-d di lbabur. Lḥiɣ armi d talemmast n wagens n dderb-nni, waleɣ tawwurt telldi-d si tama-nniḍen, uzzleɣ ɣer-s armi qrib ad awḍeɣ, daɣen tennemdal-d. Yuɣal lweqt amzun yettihiy fell-i: ttwaliɣ leḥyuḍ-nni akk d tiwwura. Mi d-telldi tewwurt, ad azzleɣ ɣer-s, mi qrib ad awḍeɣ, ad tuɣal d lḥiḍ ur d-yettban ula d later n tewwurt. Mi akken i yi-d yusa lḥal, kkseɣ-d tamuɣli-w si tewwura-nni n tkelxit, rriɣ tamuɣli-w ɣer tewwurt-nni kan tamezwarut.

Lweqt la yettazzal, nekk la ttraǧuɣ tawwurt imedlen. Rǧiɣ deg-s armi tuɣal telddi-d, mi qrib ad leḥqeɣ ɣer-s tennemdal daɣen. Beddeɣ di tlemmast-nni n wagens, greɣ tamuɣli-w ɣer yal tama di leḥyuḍ-nni, rǧiɣ, uyseɣ ur
waleɣ tawwurt telldi-d neɣ tban-d. Kniɣ i tuyat-iw ad uɣaleɣ s ansi d-kkiɣ. Greɣ asurif, ufiɣ-d iman-iw leḥqeɣ s amkan-nni deg lliɣ daxel n lbabur d yirfiqen-iw. Akken kan sɣimeɣ iman-iw deg umkan-nni, sliɣ i lbabur-nni yuɣwas. Isuɣan-nni amzun d imeǧǧiden n umdan i d-ikecmen deg yimeẓẓuɣen-iw, leḥqen ɣer wul-iw d imegran yerɣan, ssergigin tasa-w, ḥulfeɣ tettquddur am tcumÆat-nni ireqqen ikkat-itt-id ucelyaḍ. Greɣ-d nnehta, ḥulfeɣ yes-s yenhez lbabur-nni. Neṭqeɣ nniɣ-d: ‚Uh ya Rebbi, wid akked i d-ddiɣ uɣalen akk ɣer yimawlan-nsen. Nekk ad yuɣal lbabur yes-i ad iyi-iɣerreq di tmura.‛ Mi yeqleÆ lbabur-nni, mmuqleɣ ɣer deffir, tamuɣli-nni d awadeÆ n tmurt tikkelt taneggarut. Sneɣleɣ-d ayen yeqqimen n yimeṭṭawen deg wallen-iw, neṭqeɣ nniɣ-d: « BqaÆlaxir a tamurt-iw.‛

Ukiɣ-d si targit !

1980

Targit n zzher

Lliɣ di taddart-iw beddeɣ deffir n lǧamaÆ yettusemman s yisem n tgezzant « Lalla Ḥlima ». Iban-iyi-d yiwen n lberj ɣer tama n wadda, fehmeɣ amzun di lberj-
nni i yella uxxam-iw di ṭṭabqa tamezwarut, d aneggaru ɣer yiwet tqernit n lberj-nni. Nnig lberj-nni di tama n ufella llant texxamin ttwabnant d adur deg yiwen umkan yestiwnen. Tixxamin-nni ḍḥant-d myugarent di laÆli. Ta nnig ta am trekkadin. Uɣaleɣ fehmeɣ amzun zedɣeɣ di texxamt yellan ɣer tama ufella Ælayet ɣef tiyaḍ-nni.

Ibedd-d yiwen n yilemẓi zdat-i, d mmi-s n Æemmi, isem-is Meẓyan, yenna-yi-d: ‚Awi-d ad cummeɣ.‛. Ddmeɣ-d taqebsyewwet n cemma, muddeɣ-as icumm. Taggara nniɣ-as: ‚ulac akk uɣur ara tcummeḍ alamma tusiḍ-d ɣer-i?‛, yenna-yi-d: ‚Llah ɣaleb a gma.‛. Rfiɣ fell-as nniɣ-as: ‚Yerna ad d-tiniḍ a gma! Tɣelḍeḍ deg-i, nekk Rebbi-inu d win i yi-d-ixelqen. Kečč Rebbi-inek d ṭṭmaÆ. Ilaq ad d-tiniḍ ṭṭmaÆ ɣaleb.‛

Fakeɣ yid-s awal, ifak mmi-s n Æemmi. Ɣer taggara, telḥeq-d terbaÆt n yirgazen, waleɣ-ten la keccmen ɣer lǧamaÆ-nni, gar-asen yiwen urgaz isem-is ‚AÆli n Ḥmed u Sliman‛ ibedd di tama n tewwurt n lǧamaÆ. Mi immuqel ɣer wid-nni i la ikeččmen, yettmmuqul-d ɣer-i. Di tmuɣli-nni fehmeɣ-t ɣer tifrat n tmeɣra i d-isnejmaÆ irgazen-nni.

La yesmmuqul wid i d-yusan ad ḥeḍren akked wid yeÆreḍ beṭlen ur d-usin ara. Ma d nekk ḥareɣ amek ilaq ad xedmeɣ, ma ḥḍreɣ i tifrat-nni, ur ttwaÆerḍeɣ ara, ma ur ḥḍireɣ ara, yuɣ-iyi lḥal zdat n wallen n urgaz-nni, ssetḥeɣ seg-s. Mi keccmen akk ɣer lǧamaÆ wid-nni i d-yusan ttwaÆerḍen, yenṭeq-d ɣer-i bab n tifrat-nni yenna-yi-d: ‚Yalleh a Meẓyan, ttkel ɣef Rebbi!‛
Kecmeɣ yid-s ɣer lǧamaÆ, ṭṭfeɣ amkan qqimeɣ, netta ibedd la yessenqad di lɣaci-nni armi iwala ula d yiwen seg udrum-is ur d-yusi ara, yenṭeq-d ɣer-i yenna-yi-d: ‚Ttkel ɣef Rebbi a Meẓyan; ayen yellan di lɣaci-agi d lbaraka. Anef-asen i watmaten-iw a wer yid-sen timlilit ula di laxert.‛

Ufiɣ-d la leḥḥuɣ deg yiwen ubrid d aqdim, qesdeɣ abrid- iw ɣer uxxam. Lḥiɣ armi leḥqeɣ ɣer tama n yiwen n wurti d ayla-w yettwasemma ‚Tagnit n umdun‛, waleɣ yiwen n yilemẓi la yettawi yettarra deg wurti-nni taqaakkent ɣef tayet-is. Beddeɣ ad waliɣ d acu yebɣa ad yexdem. Waleɣ-t ikkes-d taqaakkent-nni si tayet-is, yebda afras deg yiwet n tneqlet armi i tt-ifak s ufras, yerra taqaakkent-nni ɣer tayet-is, yuɣal la yettawi yettarra. Nekk la ttferriǧeɣ deg-s armi waleɣ iÆeṭṭel ur yuɣal ara ɣer ccɣel-is, nefleɣ ɣer-s.

Mi leḥqeɣ, qesdeɣ-t s Rebbi, nniɣ-as: ‚D acu-k a lxelq-agi?‛, yenna-yi-d: ‚D lxelq am kečč.‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚D acu i la txeddmeḍ dagi?‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚Mi stufeɣ, ttaseɣ-d ad ak-ferseɣ yiwet n tenqelt.‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Lufan di lbal-ik ad iyi-tÆawneḍ tili tferseḍ s terni.‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚Akka i la k-ttÆawaneɣ bezzaf fell-i.‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Ihi d kečč i d zzher- iw?‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚Ala, nekk ttaseɣ-d ttÆawaneɣ kan s wayen i wumi zemreɣ.‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Kečč d acu-k?‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚TesÆiḍ zzher, maca mačči d nekk i d zzher-ik.‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚i zzher-iw d anwa-t, neɣ anida-t mi mačči d kečč ? ». Yenna-yi-d :« Zzher-ik isem-is ‚Duktur Ğewwazi‛ ; yella zik ixeddem d ṭṭbib, ma tura aṭas aya i la ttnadin fell-as ṭṭebbat akked ixeddem ur t-ufin ara !‛.
Nniɣ-as: ‚i nekk anida ara t-afeɣ?‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚Nadi ɣef zzher-ik anida yebɣu yili ad t-tafeḍ!‛. Lxelq-nni ttwaliɣ-t s ṣṣifa n urgaz, ttwaliɣ-t s ṣṣifa n tmeṭṭut!

Ufiɣ-d iman-iw deg yiwen n wurti-nniḍen yettusemman ‚Agni n ṭṭerḥa‛. Mlileɣ d sin n yilmeẓyen n taddart-iw, yiwen isem-is Meẓyan, wayeḍ SsaÆid. Nnan-iyi-d: ‚Aniɣer akka i la tettedduḍ a Meẓyan?‛. Nniɣ-asen: ‚La ttnadiɣ ɣef zzher-iw, wissen anida ara t-afeɣ?‛. SsaÆid yenna-yi-d: ‚Zzher-ik isem-is Duktur Ğewwazi.‛. Meẓyan yenna-yi-d: ‚Ad t-tafeḍ di lḥedd n Sidi Lḥaǧ, ittɣima deg yiwen n lɣar, kullass isekker. Yalleh ad ak-nawi ɣer-s, ad ak-nemmel lɣar-nni!‛

Ddiɣ yid-sen. Nutni zwaren, nekk ddiɣ deffir-sen. Nelḥa deg wurti-nni. Nelḥeq ad nekcem s abrid, waleɣ sin-nni surfen i yiwen zzerb n yileẓwi, kecmen s abrid yessawaḍen s aniɣer i neqsed. Ma d nekk mi greɣ aḍar-iw ad surfeɣ i zzerb-nni, la d-yettaski zdat-i yiwen n uqjun d awraɣ, la d-itemmeɣ la yi-ttkerric seg yixfawen n yiḍudan-iw. Akerrec-nni fehmeɣ-t d anecreḥ; nniɣ deg wul-iw: ‚Ad as-anfeɣ i ufus-iw deg yimi-s, ad yennecraḥ yid-i, mi yeÆya ad yettixer fell-i.‛. Unfeɣ i ufus-iw deg yimi-s, ḥulfeɣ la yettzad di tkerrac-is; armi i ḥulfeɣ s uqraḥ, ḥewṣeɣ-d afus-iw, wwteɣ-t s rrkel, tḍeggar-it tyita-nni mbaÆid.

Kecmeɣ s abrid, abrid-nni yuɣal-d yestiwen am sellum, yesÆa tirekkadin. Nuli di trekkadin-nni. Sin-nni zwaren, nekk tebÆeɣ; mi nelḥeq d asawen anida i d-nneqḍaÆent trekkadin-nni, nufa d ssaḥelt, yal tama tettban-d mebÆid
tiniḍ yers-d yigenni ɣef tmurt. Ssaḥelt-nni d ṣṣeḥra. Nekk ufiɣ-d iman-iw weḥd-i, nniɣ deg wul-iw: ‚S aniɣer ara rreɣ?‛. Waleɣ aqḍar n yizgaren, tifunasin lḥan-d deg ubid n tmacint. Tamacint tuɣ-d abrid-nni, rnu teɣseb-d am terṣaṣt. Nniɣ deg wul-iw: ‚Atan ur tezgil la yiwen la yiwet.‛. Tamacint tÆedda, actal ulac-iten.

Uɣaleɣ la ttxemmimeɣ amek ara xedmeɣ d yiman-iw? Mi Æyiɣ di ttexmim, nniɣ-d: ‚Lettkal ɣef Rebbi ay anida ddiɣ yella.‛. Lḥiɣ ur ḥṣiɣ s aniɣer armi i d-mlileɣ d yiwen n urgaz, yenna-yi-d: ‚S aniɣer akka i la tettedduḍ a Meẓyan?‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚La ttnadiɣ ɣef zzher-iw anida ara t-afeɣ.‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚isem-is zzher-ik?‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Duktur Ğewwazi.‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚Ssneɣ-t, ssneɣ sbiṭer anida ixeddem, ma tebɣiḍ ad ak-awiɣ ɣer-s, yalleh.

Ddiɣ d urgaz-nni armi d zdat n yiwen uxxam d ameqqran, yenna-yi-d: ‚Ata sbiṭer anida ixeddem zzher-ik, kcem attan tewwurt.‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Kcem-d yid-i.‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚Ala, nekk seg tewwurt-agi ur ttkemmileɣ ara.‛. Yuɣal-d ɣer deffir, nekk kecmeɣ s axxam-nni. Mi kecmeɣ di tewwurt, la leḥḥuɣ deg usqif ttwaliɣ tixxamin sya u sya.

Lḥiɣ armi d snat n texxamin tineggura, siggeɣ ɣer texxamt yellan di tama-w tazelmaḍt, waleɣ ɣer daxel-is tarbaÆt n ṭṭebbat, steqseɣ-ten, nniɣ-asen: ‚D anwa deg-wen i d Duktur Ğewwazi?‛. Ijaweb-iyi-d yiwen deg-sen yenna-yi-d: ‚Isem-agi ur yelli ara dagi ɣer-neɣ, ur sliɣ yes-s anida nniḍen!‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Kunwi d acu-ken?‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚Nekni d zzherrat n yimdanen.‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Ihi Duktur Ğewwazi d yiwen deg-wen, yeffer kan iman-is, axaṭer d
netta i d zzher-iw. Tura init-iyi-d anwa-t deg-wen!‛.

Neṭqen-d s yiwen n wawal, nnan-iyi-d: ‚D lmuḥal ur nessin akk isem am wagi.‛. Nniɣ-asen: ‚Ur ilaq ara ad teffrem fell-i.‛; Nnan-iyi-d: ‚Nenna-yak ulac isem-agi dagi, ad aɣ-tanfeḍ tura, d lawan ad neffeɣ si lxedma.‛.

Nniɣ-asen: ‚Ur awen-ttanfeɣ, ur ken-tthenniɣ, alamma tennam-iyi-d anwa deg-wen i d zzher-iw.‛

Uskeɣ-asen-d ɣef tewwurt, nutni la ddehhamen deg-i akken ad ffɣen. Nekk la ten-ḥebbseɣ, xas akken weḥd-i setɣelbeɣ fell-asen. La ttemÆafareɣ yid-sen armi i d-yelḥeq yiwen n yilemẓi. Mi t-waleɣ, ferḥeɣ nniɣ-d ad iyi-iÆawen deg-sen. Maca iÆawen tarbaÆt-nni. Yeddhem-d yid-sen yiwet n tikkelt, refden-iyi am yifer-nni yeddem waḍu.

Ffɣen-d s asqif-nni ferḥen. Ma d nekk yerɣa wul-iw ladɣa ɣef umÆawen-nni-nsen, neṭqeɣ nniɣ-as: ‚i kečč a lxelq-agi tkecmeḍ-d gar-aneɣ, ur d-tusiḍ d amḥaddi, ur d-tusiḍ d amÆawen. Ma d amḥaddi ilaq ad aɣ-tefruḍ, ma d amÆawen ilaq ad tÆawneḍ bab n lḥeqq. Rnu aten-in la ttheyyin iman-nsen i tikkelt-nniḍen.‛.

Yenna-yi-d: ‚imeslayen-ik metbutit d lḥeqq. Ḥku-iyi-d amek i tella taluft-ik.‛. Mi as-ḥkiɣ, yeḥṣa d nekk i d bab n lḥeqq, yenṭeq ɣer terbaÆt-nni yenna-yasen: ‚Dagi i yella ixeddem d ṭṭbib yid-wen, yesÆa lḥeq Meẓyan.‛

Yedda-d di tama-w yilemẓi-nni, neddhem-iten uɣalen armi d daxel n texxamt-nni. Nuzga-asen-d ɣef tewwurt, nekk gulleɣ deg-sen, nniɣ-asen: ‚Welleh ard d-tinim tidet neɣ ad terwi fell-awen.‛; nnan-iyi-d: ‚Isem-agi iɣef tettnadiḍ, s tidet yella ixeddem dagi d ṭṭbib maca aṭas uya
ur d-iban ara, wissen ma yemmut neɣ yedder!‛. Nekk ur ten-umineɣ ara. Sḥerṣeɣ deg-sen armi i d-yelḥeq yiwen n umsaltu. Amsaltu-nni waleɣ-t yennexrab wudem-is fell-i yenna-yi-d: ‚Isem-agi iɣef tettnadiḍ a Meẓyan ssneɣ-t am wakka ssneɣ iman-iw. Yya-n ad t-nerǧu deg usqif-agi, mi d-yekcem, ad ak-t-mmleɣ.‛

Umneɣ-t, uɣeɣ-as awal. Unfeɣ-asen i wid-nni ideg gulleɣ. Beddeɣ la ttraǧuɣ deg usqif-nni, amsaltu-nni la yettawi yettarra. Ɣer taggara amzun yesseɣfel-iyi, waleɣ-t yeffeɣ di tewwurt. Qqimeɣ-d ul-iw yerɣa, rnu ur zmireɣ ad xedmeɣ kra i umcum-nni ikellxen fell-i. Uɣaleɣ nniɣ-d : « Lettkal ɣef Rebbi, ad nadiɣ weḥd-i!‛, zziɣ ɣer ṭṭebbat-nni. Uqbel ad awḍeɣ ɣer-sen, tezga-d tmuɣli-w daxel n yiwet n texxamt di tama tayeffust. Waleɣ sin n yilmeẓyen, yiwen deg-sen la yessefaḍ udem-is, wayeḍ yerfed ssḍel n waman ad yessired udem-is.

Fehmeɣ-ten llan d ixeddamen di sbiṭer-nni, daɣen fehmeɣ imiren kan i d-ukin seg yiḍes. Neṭqeɣ ɣer-sen, nniɣ-asen : ‚ Duktur Ğewwadi, tessnem-t ? ‛.Nnan-iyi-d : ‚ Nessen-it, di sbiṭer-agi i ixeddem, ma tebɣiḍ ad t-terǧuḍ qqim mi d-yekcem, ad ak-t-nemmel.‛. Nniɣ-asen: ‚ yiɣ deg uraǧu.‛. Wexreɣ-d fell-asen, tban-iyi-d yiwet n tewwurt, ffɣeɣ seg-s.

Leḥqeɣ ɣer yiwet n tgarrawt n ukerruc, mmuqleɣ akkin akka ur waleɣ amdan neɣ ula d lweḥc ad t-steqsiɣ. Uɣaleɣ sliɣ i umeslay s teɣri tarqaqt di teẓgi-nni. Tiɣri-nni d asbecbec. ḍḥiɣ-d wehmeɣ deg-s, awal yella imdanen ulac! Ar dqal fehmeɣ di teẓgi-nni i yella zzher-iw. StebÆeɣ ameslay-nni, lḥiɣ armi leḥqeɣ ɣer tkerruct tamezwarut,
waleɣ yuli fell-as ujgagal. Beddeɣ la ssɣadeɣ. Yuɣal yenneqḍaÆ umeslay-nni. Ssiliɣ tamuɣli-w, waleɣ yiwen n urgaz d amcaybu ikessel iman-is s ufella n ssiwan gar sin n yifurkawen n tkerruct-nni. Nniɣ-d deg wul-iw: ‚Yella ccek d amerbuḥ-nni-inu ayagi i as-yufan ixef-is dagi i ubeḥri tili. Tura ad t-steqsiɣ ma d netta wagi, ad nemsefham.‛ Mi t-luÆeɣ, armi i t-qesdeɣ s Rebbi tlata tikkal d akken i yi-d-yerra awal. Mi as-nniɣ: ‚Anwa-k a lxelq-agi?‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚D nekk i d zzher-ik.‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚D acu i la txeddmeḍ dagi?‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚Lemmer ad twaliḍ d acu xeddmeɣ dagi ad twehmeḍ!‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Aql-i waleɣ txedmeḍ ssiwan teṭseḍ sufella-s. D ayagi i yi-iswehmen, neɣ ma yella ugar uyagi, wissen!‛. Yessusem. Uɣaleɣ nniɣ-as: ‚Imi kečč d zzher-iw, ilaq-ak ad txedmeḍ fell-i.‛. Yeḍsa-d s ukeÆrer yenna-yi-d: ‚D nekk ara ixedmen fell-ak! D lmuḥal.‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Imdanen irkulli xeddmen fell-asen zzherrat-nsen kečč tenniḍ-iyi-d d lmuḥal. Tura meḥtum-ak ad txedmeḍ fell-i.‛
Yenhemm s unazaÆ, yenna-yi-d: ‚A ziɣ d ccix AÆmar ara ixedmen! Ma tebɣiḍ ad d-taliḍ ad nkemmel tiÆeqqayin-agi n waḍil rwaḥ, ma tebɣiḍ ad truḥeḍ ad txedmeḍ ruḥ ad isahel Rebbi fell-ak.‛. Nniɣ-d deg wul-iw: ‚Ad aliɣ ɣer-s imiren ad mtaniɣ yid-s.‛. Greɣ aḍar-iw akken ad aliɣ, ur ḥṣiɣ ansi i d-yekka yiwen uqcic armi i t-id-ufiɣ deffir-iw. Mi ruḥeɣ ad aliɣ ad iyi-d-yerr aḍad. Mi d-wexreɣ ad yettixer. Mi uɣaleɣ, ad d-yuɣal. Nniɣ deg wul-iw: ‚Wagi ad yili d cciṭan, ad t-xzuɣ ad iruḥ fell-i. Xziɣ cciṭan tlata
tikkal yegguma ad iyi-yexḍu. Tikkelt-nniḍen zziɣ fell-as s tyita n rrkel, tḍeggar-it tyita-nni ur iban later-is. Mi gemneɣ ad aliɣ, tban-iyi-d tkerruct-nni terka lǧedra-s; ma rniɣ ɣer lxelq-nni yellan sufell-as ad d-terreẓ. Beddeɣ di ttexmam armi waleɣ aqcic-nni yuɣal-d, la yettaÆraḍ ad yali si tara n ujgagal-nni. Fehmeɣ-t yebɣa ad yi-izuɣer ɣer tÆeqqayin-nni n waḍil. Neṭqeɣ ɣer zzher-iw yeṭsen nniɣ-as: ‚Mmager-iyi-d, eefk-iyi-d afus-ik Æawen-iyi ad n-aliɣ.‛.

Yenna-yi-d: ‚Ali-d neɣ qqim.‛. Yennelqem-d, akken kan i t-id-ḥerreɣ seg yixfawen n yiḍudan-is, jebdeɣ-t-id yemxebbaḍ di tmurt. Uzgeɣ-as ɣef yidmaren-is, afus-iw iḥerr-it si tyersi, nniɣ-as: « Tura ad txedmeḍ fell-i akken ad cbuɣ medden, neɣ ad ak-xenqeɣ. Mi temmuteḍ, meqqar iban-iyi ubrid.‛.

Yenna-yi-d: ‚ccerṭ-ik d lmuḥal ad t-qebleɣ. Ma tebɣiḍ ad iyi-tenɣeḍ nneɣ-iyi wala ma xedmeɣ fell-ak.‛. Meskud i tettḥellileɣ, yeqqar-iyi-d d lmuḥal, rennuɣ ḥemmẓeɣ di tyersi-s, armi waleɣ yeffeɣ-it rruḥ, uyseɣ dayen yemmut. Uɣaleɣ la ttruɣ fell-as qqareɣ: ‚Akka a Rebbi, zik sÆiɣ zzher yeṭṭes amɣer ad yuɣal ad d-yaki, ma tura nɣiɣ-t qeḍÆeɣ layas di ddunit-iw, dayen tura ma ad cbuɣ medden!‛

Ufiɣ-d iman-iw uɣaleɣ ɣer luḍa-nni yecban di ṣṣeḥra, ddukkleɣ d sin n yilmùeẓyen. Yiwen isem-is Lmulud wayeḍ d lxelq ur ssineɣ. Lmulud, mmi-s n xali yedda-yi-d ɣef uyeffus. Nelḥa kra n yisurrifen, tban-iyi-d temdint mebÆid. Fehmeɣ-d: di temdint-nni ideg yella ṣbiṭer-nni seg i d-kkiɣ. Daɣen fehmeɣ-d: kra n wid yellan di temdint-nni, d zzherrat n yimdanen. Nniɣ-d: « Wissen kan ma
ttnuzun zzherrat, ad afeɣ yiwen di temdint-Yenna ad t-id- aɣeɣ. Lxelq-nni ur ssineɣ ara yenna-yi-d: ‚Ttnuzun! yalleh kan ttkel ɣef Rebbi. Mi nelḥeq, ad tafeḍ  yiwen ad t-id- taɣeḍ.‛. Ma d Lmulud yeḍsa fell-i; iruḥ ibeddel abrid. Fehmeɣ-t yeḥseb-iyi d ameslub. Lxelq-nni akked i d-ggreɣ nelḥa kra n yisurrifen, yenna-yi-d: ‚Ula d nekk d zzher.‛.

Nniɣ-as: ‚Ihi ad ak-sÆuɣ  d zzher-iw?‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚Ih, aql-i qebleɣ.‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Yak ad txeddmeḍ fell-i?‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚Merra d kečč, merra d nekk.‛. Nniɣ-as : ‚ Ala, nekk ur xeddmeɣ ara, d kečč kan ara ixedmen. ‛. Imir ufiɣ-d ulac ula  d  amÆawen-nni. Qqimeɣ-d weḥd-i la ttruɣ ttneẓẓifeɣ qqareɣ: ‚Akka a Rebbi, yiwen n zzher nɣiɣ-t wicqa d afenyan. I win i ufiɣ ad yexdem fell-i, ad iyi-d- yettÆawan, nekk ugiɣ! Atan yerwel fell-i, yerna dayen ur yuɣal ad d-yezzi ɣer-i. ‛.

Kemmleɣ abrid weḥd-i armi leḥqeɣ, kecmeɣ ɣer temdint-nni. Ufiɣ s kra yellan di temdint-nni d ixeddamen. Yal wa d acu i d lxedma-s, rnu ur d-tettekkseḍ ula yiwen deg-sen yestehzay di ccɣel-i-s. Fehmeɣ-ten d zzherrat n yimdanen. Ferneɣ yiwet n tḥanut n ssyaɣa, kecmeɣ ɣer-s. Ufiɣ yiwen n yilemẓi ixeddem deg-s d aseyyaɣ, teɣli-d tiṭ-iw fell-as, ula d ṣṣifa-s d ssyaɣa! steqseɣ-t nniɣ-as: ‚Kečč, d zzher?‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚Ih, nekk d zzher.‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Ihi, ad ak-sÆuɣ d zzher-iw ad d-txeddmeḍ fell-i?‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚i zzher-ik kečč? Neɣ  ur tesÆiḍ ara zzher? ». Nniɣ-as : « SÆiɣ zzher, yella ixeddem d ṭṭbib, yuɣal yeṭṭes acḥal netta d akilut yerra-tt ala i yiḍes. Asmi i nudaɣ  fell-as, ufiɣ-t anida yeṭṭes, sukiɣ-t-id akken ad yexdem fell-i, yugi, nɣiɣ-t.
Nudeɣ, ufiɣ wayeḍ. Yenna-yi-d ad ak-ttÆawaneɣ tikwal, ugiɣ dɣa yerwel fell-i, ur fhimeɣ ara ula d leǧwab-is. Yenna-yi-d: ‚Nadi ad tafeḍ, nniɣ-ak s kra ara twaliḍ di temdint-agi, d zzherrat.‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Uggadeɣ ad afeɣ sÆan akk bab-nsen.‛. Yenna-yi-d:‚Wali win urÆad yebdi lxedma. S kra n zzherrat ara yawḍen i lxedma, ɣer temdint-agi i d-yettas ad yesteqsi ɣef win ur nesÆi ara zzher akken ad yexdem fell-as, ad yili d zzher-is‛.. Friɣ-tt d usseyaɣ-nni. Uɣaleɣ ttnadiɣ di temdint-nni, a win waleɣ d axeddam, lxedma-s telha, qqareɣ-as: ‚Ad ak-sÆuɣ d zzher-iw.‛, yeqqar-iyi-d: ‚SÆiɣ bab-iw iɣef xeddmeɣ.‛

Nudeɣ armi Æyiɣ dayen tekkḥes fell-i, ruḥeɣ ad ffɣeɣ si temdint-nni. Lḥiɣ armi d rrif n temdint, waleɣ yiwen n urgaz yeffeɣ-d si lkuca n uɣrum, ttwaliɣ deg-s ur yewwi ara gar yifassen-is aɣrum. Nniɣ deg wul-iw: ‚Wagi ad yili d axeddam di lkuca-agi. Netta akken i yi-d-iwala, yelḥa-d ɣer-i, iqubel-iyi-d s useḍsu amzun yessen-iyi; lliɣ-as d aḥbib, yenna-yi-d: ‚LÆeslama a Meẓyan, aṭas uya ur d-tbaneḍ ara!‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Ur yeksan ḥedd i as-yeḍran, yeṭṭef-aɣ lwaÆd neqqim kan.‛ Yelḥeq-d ɣer-i nemsalam.

YeÆreḍ-iyi-d ad nsew leqhawi. Nruḥ ɣer yiwet n lqahwa i aɣ-d-iqerben, neqqim ɣer ṭṭabla. Yusa-d ɣer-neɣ uqehwaǧi. Nekk ssutreɣ-as lgazuz; lxelq-nni yessuter lqahwa taberkant. Iruḥ uqehwaǧi-nni ad aɣ-d-yawi ad nsew. yennelqem Winna yeqqimen yid-i, neffeɣ-d si lqahwa-nni, nemfaraq zdat tewwurt. Ur iyi-d-yenni, ur as-nniɣ. Netta yerra d asawen nekk rriɣ d akessar.
Lḥiɣ kra n yisurrifen, leḥqeɣ ɣer tḥanut n ssebɣa, beddeɣ zdat tewwurt, ḥulfeɣ yerɣa wul-iw s wurfan. Berneɣ-d la d-leḥḥuɣ snehmuyeɣ qqareɣ: ‚Zzher bu ssyaɣa yugi ad t-sÆuɣ, bu tensutin ulac ay axir-is. Uɣaleɣ mektiɣ-d Winna akked kecmeɣ ɣer lqahwa, nniɣ-d: ‚Winna akked mlileɣ d zzher, nekk ur as-nniɣ ara ad t-sÆuɣ ad yexdem fell-i.‛

Ufiɣ-d leḥqeɣ ɣer taḥanut n ugezzar, siggeɣ ɣer daxel, waleɣ yiwen n urgaz la d-itekkes likutlat n uksum s tqaakkent seg yiɣsan anect n yiqejmar. Nniɣ-d deg wul-iw: ‚Iɣsan-Yenna ad ilin n uɣyul‛.

Mi t-Æeqleɣ d Winna akked i kecmeɣ ɣer lqahwa, nniɣ-d deg wul-iw: ‚Ziɣ wagi yexeddem-itent akk! D akewwac, d agezzar. Mi d-yerfed tamuɣli-s, yeẓra-iyi-d la t-smuquleɣ, yenna-yi-d: ‚D acu akka a Meẓyan?‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Lhi kan d ikaÆruren-ik, anida akka i yi-tessneḍ?‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚Aw! Nekk mačči d aḥbib-ik?‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚D lmuḥal, ad rreɣ cciṭan d aḥbib-iw wala kečč; ula di lÆeqliya nemxallaf, kečč tḍelbeḍ lqahwa taberkant, nekk ḍelbeɣ lgazuz. Xas zzi udem-ik akkin, ur iyi-tessineḍ ur k-ssineɣ, a win i tÆeǧbeḍ muddeɣ-ak- t‛.

Waleɣ-t yenneḥcam, yuɣal yellha d ccɣel-is. Kemmleɣ abrid-iw s unadi di temdint-nni armi ufiɣ yiwen n uxxam yettwabna d ajdid. Waleɣ irgazen uɣalen d adur wa zdat wa s axxam-nni, la keccmen teffɣen. Ttwaliɣ deg-sen s kra n win i d-yeffɣen ad d-yawi tabalizt deg ufus-is.

Nniɣ-d deg wul-iw: ‚Welleh ard kecmeɣ s anida i znuzen tibalizin. Kecmeɣ s axxam-nni, ufiɣ d taḥanut n tbalizin. Di tḥanut-nni llan sin yixeddamen, yiwen d amiɣzif ad yesÆu di laÆmer-is 15 ɣer 16 n yiseggasen, wayeḍ d
amiwzil ad yesÆu 30 n yiseggasen netta d akeÆwan teffeɣ-as-d teÆrurt, yerna yesqejdiḥ. Ma d lxedma-s tÆeǧbeɣ deg-s. Winna-nniḍen yeqqim ɣef tbalizt, lxedma-s siwa s tmuɣli. Seg mi wwḍeɣ, ur t-waleɣ iḥerrek iman-is. Rǧiɣ armi ffɣen akk yimyaɣen-nni, steqseɣ ixeddamen-nni, nniɣ-asen: ‘D zzherrat n yimdanen i tellam?’ AkeÆwan-nni yenna-yi-d: ‘Ih’. Imir ḥareɣ amek, ad as-iniɣ ad ak-sÆuɣ xas ẓriɣ d axeddam, meÆna ssetḥeɣ yes-s gar yimdanen mi d aneÆyabu. Winna-nniḍen d afenyan am Winna nɣiɣ.

Uɣaleɣ ferneɣ ad as-iniɣ i uxeddam-nni xas akken d aÆiban. Nniɣ-as: ‘Ihi, ad ak-sÆuɣ d zzher-iw ad d-txeddmeḍ fell-i?’ Yenna-yi-d: ‘nekk sÆiɣ bab-iw iɣef xeddmeɣ, ini-as i wagi atan tama-k.’ Nniɣ-as: ‘Awwah, wagi am Winna nɣiɣ, d afenyan’. Yenna-yi-d: ‘Ala, mačči d afenyan, urÆad kan i yufa bab-is iɣef ara yexdem.’

Uɣaleɣ ɣer Winna-nniḍen nniɣ-as: ‘Ihi d nekk i d bab-ik, meÆna ad txedmeḍ fell-i’. Yenna-yi-d: ‘Qebleɣ ad xedmeɣ fell-ak nnefṣ n wass’. Nniɣ-as: ‘Acuɣef ur txeddmeḍ ara ass yekmel?’ Yenna-yi-d: ‘Ad xedmeɣ fell-ak nnefṣ n wass. Ad ttnekkareɣ ɣef setta n ṣbeḥ, ad xedmeɣ addal, mi d ṭṭnac ad ffɣeɣ.’ Nniɣ-as: ‘Qebleɣ akka. Ini-iyi-d kan anida ara nemlil ad tebduḍ lxedma fell-i, neɣ kker ad tebduḍ tura.’ Yenna-yi-d: ‘Mačči ass-a; asmi ad nemlil di Wehran, ad bduɣ lxedma fell-ak, rnu ay aniɣer i tebɣiḍ ad truḥeḍ d nekk ara k-issiwḍen, ay ayen i tuyseḍ, d nekk ara k-isleḥqen ɣer-s. Siwel-iyi-d kan s yisem-iw ad iliɣ yid-k.’

Nniɣ-as: ‘Amek i d isem-ik?’ Yenna-yi-d: ‘Isem-iw
Lmulud, nnekwa-w ṭṭes u ṣuni. Ay anida ay tḥareḍ, siwel-iyi-d, ad iliɣ yid-k. Nniɣ-as: ‚S tidet akka ay d isem-ik?‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚Welleh ma skidbeɣ fell-ak, akka ay d isem-iw.‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Ad iyi-tÆahdeḍ s Rebbi ur iyi-txeddÆeḍ ara?‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚uhdeɣ-k s Rebbi ma xedÆeɣ-k.‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Ṭhella ihi!‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚Asmi i nemlil di Wehran, yeffeɣ-ik lḥir, aql-i-in ad xedmeɣ fell-ak, ad ak-ssiwdɣ s aniɣer tebɣiḍ.‛

Ukiɣ-d si targit !

1980

Lefdi n tmurt-iw Lliɣ akked sin n yilmeẓyen n taddart-iw, la nleḥḥu deg yiwet n tmurt tabudrart. Newweḍ ɣer yiwen n umkan, nwala ifuk lexrif di tneqlin-nniḍen akk, yegra-d siwa di yiwet d abujerniḥ. Taneqelt-nni, tefreq ɣef tlata n yifurkawen. Nuzzel nuli ɣer ubujerniḥ-nni, yal wa yeṭṭef afurkiw. UrÆad i nessemeblaÆ tibexsisin timezwura, yelḥeq-d bab n wurti-nni. Irfiqen-nni-inu uggaden-t rewlen. Ma d nekk ur t-uggadeɣ ara, meÆna setḥeɣ seg-s. Beddeɣ sufella n tneqlet-nni. Mi d-yelḥeq ɣer-i, yenna-yi-d: Ur iyi-ttuggad, ur iyi-ttsetḥi, lemmer ad twaliḍ lḥaqiqa,

- 72 -
urtan-agi akk d ayla-nwen. Nniɣ-as: Sefhem-iyi-d amek yella d ayla-nneɣ. Yenna-yi-d: Tamurt-agi tella n jeddi-k, asmi yemmut tegra-d deg ufus n laÆmum-ik, mi ten-yeṭṭef lḥuj, rehnen-tt. Tura ma tebɣiḍ ad d-terreḍ, rrhina ad tt-id-tefduḍ ad tuɣal d ayla-nwen, rnu lefdi-yas d ayen isehlen. Nniɣ-as: Ayen tcerḍeḍ fell-i meqbul, awi-d kan ad d-tuɣal tmurt-nneɣ d ayla-nneɣ.

Yenna-yi-d: Ccerṭ d ayen isehlen, ur tesÆiḍ ara tuggadeḍ. Nniɣ-as: ini-d kan ccerṭ fell-i meqbul, aql-i wejdeɣ. Yenna-yi-d: Ma tebɣiḍ ad d-tuɣal tmurt n jeddi-k d ayla n warraw-ik ad cerḍeɣ fell-ak ad tsemḥeḍ issusem. Nniɣ-as: kemmel awal di ccerṭ-ik fak-it-id, ulayɣer tgezmeḍ awal, nniɣ-ak ayen i tcerḍeḍ deg-i meqbul.

Yenna-yi-d: Ihi ad tsemḥeḍ di rruḥ-ik, ad ak-kkseɣ aqerruy-ik s lfinga dakken ara d-tuɣal tmurt d ayla n wrraw-ik. ḍsiɣ nniɣ-as: D aya-agi kan i tcerḍeḍ? Tenwiḍ d lmuḥal! Teḥṣiḍ i yfkan iqerray nsen, i yebɣan ad ten-efken ɣer lfinga ɣef tmurt-agi. Ahat ur tetÆekkireḍ ara di ccerṭ-ik. Aql-i wejdeɣ. Ma tebɣiḍ tura gzem aksum-iw d ccelxat nekk ad smuquleɣ, awi-d ad tuɣal tmurt-agi n warraw-iw.

Tban-iyi-d zdat-i ṭṭabla n usɣer am tinna iɣef gezzmen aksum yigezzarren. Lxelq-nni yenna-yi-d: Ssers aqerruy-ik ɣef lfinga-agi ad ak t-kkseɣ. Qerrbeɣ ɣer ṭṭabla -nni, sserseɣ anyir-iw sufell-as. Waleɣ lxelq-nni yerfed tacaqurt, yuɣal yesser-itt, sliɣ yenna-yi-d: Yalleh qbel ad ak-id-mleɣ tilisa n tmurt-ik ansi i uɣalent, akken ad tt-tissineḍ!

Lḥiɣ yid-s nekcem ɣer yiwen n wurti deg-s sin leṣnaf n tneqlin, llant tɣunam, llan lerhayeḍ.
rremcacent s lexrif armi rsen yifurkawen-nsent ɣef wakal. Neṭqeɣ ɣer lxelq-nni, nniɣ-as: ‚Uh a lexrif-agi! D lxir u lbaraka.‛.Yenna-yi-d: ‚arraw am waggi ulami wumi-t.‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Aw! Lxir am wa la teqqareḍ ulami wumi-t.‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚Ur twalaḍ ara ifurkawen seg ucebbub aten-in knan-d  ɣef tmurt?‛ lufan ur asen-giɣ   ara tisulal, ahat rrẓen.‛ Nniɣ-as: ‚  La  ttwaliɣ terriḍ-asen tirekkizin  n wuzzal d tiwezlanin s lqis n ufus n umdan, Æǧebent-iyi d lÆali-tent; meÆna mačči i yicaggen-agi i wi wumi laqent kan, laqent ula i yifassen n yimattaren akken ur fecclen ara ma ten-tteẓẓlen seg ṣṣbeḥ ɣer tmeddit. Wissen ma d-ḥellin taxbizt. »

Iban-iyi-d lxelq-nni yuɣal wudem-is d aberkan si zzÆaf. Yuɣal yettwaddem ulac-it. Nekk fehmeɣ     lliɣ di lweqt n yimenɣi gar-aneɣ d yiÆdawen. Waleɣ       lÆesker ẓedmen-d fell-i; rewleɣ-asen, ddiɣ di yiwen n ubrid ur iban d abrid neɣ     d asif yekkawen. Tamesrafegt di tegnawt la iyi-d- tettabaÆ s tyitiwin. Mi qrib ad leḥqeɣ ɣer yiwet n teɣzut, fehmeɣ  am win i yi-d-yennan: ‚Mi tleḥqeḍ     ɣer teɣzut- Yenna, yella din yiwen urgaz ad ak-yeslek‛. Mi leḥqeɣ ɣer teɣzut-nni, Æyiɣ ssawaleɣ:‚Ay argaz-agi yellan di teɣzut- agi, ffeɣ-d sellek-iyi‛. Ulac! Tuɣal truḥ tmesrafegt-nni. Ufiɣ-d iman-iw lliɣ d waṭas n lɣaci i d-yusan ad ferǧen di temsizzelt i yi-d-iḥeḍren akked tlata n yimussnawen n umÆebbar d tqerraḍt. Nutni di tlata nekk weḥd-i. Tella yiwet n teslent Ælayet, lǧedra-s zurret armi d acebbub teÆdel.
Tamsizzelt-nneɣ ad nali ɣer teslent-nni, win i d-yekkan nnig wayeḍ, yerbeḥ-it. Mi nuzzel, zwireɣ-ten s acebbub n teslent-nni. Ulin-d mÆafereɣ yid-sen armi i ten-id-sseɣliɣ si teslent-nni. Lɣaci-nni wwten afus ferḥen. Mi d-rseɣ si teslent-nni, nnan-iyi-d: ‚Tura ad truḥeḍ ad teččeḍ kra n lfakya si lǧennet ». Lḥiɣ di teɣzut-nni, ufiɣ yiwen n lejnan n lxux d lmecmac. Kkseɣ-d yiwet n tÆeqqayt n lxux, tayeḍ n lmecmac.

Ufiɣ-d iman-iw deg umkan-nniḍen ddaw n uÆerqub n uzemmur. Tamesrafegt ad d-tenneḍ fell-i, nekk dduriɣ-as tazemmurt. Tewwet-d tazemmurt-nni, tebḍa d tiqeclalin. Waleɣ iɣzer iqreb-d, rewleɣ. Mi leḥqeɣ ɣer yiɣzer-nni, sduriɣ deg-s iman-iw. Mi truḥ tmesrafegt-nni, ffɣeɣ seg yiɣzer-nni, uliɣ d asawen deg yiwen n uÆerqub. Mi mmuqleɣ deg tegnawt, waleɣ yiwet n tnaÆurt i d-fehmeɣ ceggÆen-tt-id ad d-teɣli fell-i. Mi d-telḥeq s lewhi-w, teḥbes. Ɣliɣ-as ɣer tmurt uɣaleɣ am umeblaḍ. Teɣli-d di tama-w. waleɣ-tt la tettsuḍu dduxxan. Dduxxan-nni la iferreq, ansi yekka ad d-tecÆel tmes. Mi waleɣ terɣa-d tmes seg yal tama, nleqmeɣ, rewleɣ. Times-nni la iyi-d-tesqiṭṭiÆ.

Uɣaleɣ uliɣ ɣer lǧedra n tzemmurt, nniɣ-d : « Lǧedra-agi teqwa aṭas, ur iyi-d-tettalḥaq ara seg-s tmes alamma tfak tmerɣyewwet n uÆerqub-agi ». Mi beddeɣ s ufella n lǧedra-nni, mmuqleɣ ad waliɣ s aniɣer i telḥeq tmes deg uÆerqub-nni. Waleɣ qrib maḍi ad taweḍ ɣer yiwen n yigar n temẓin d yirden. Ɣer tama ufella n yigar-nni d annar anida llant tɣeffiwin n nneÆma, llan daɣen yitemma n
walim. Neṭqeɣ nniɣ-d : « A Rebbi, ifellaḥen nneÆtaben, siweḍ-asen laÆtab s aɣellet ».

Waleɣ tagnawt temɣullaq s usigna, yebda-tt ugeffur la d-iɣelli d aneznaz. Mmuqleɣ ɣer tegnawt, waleɣ asigna yemfaraq, rnu la d-yettban d amellal. Neṭqeɣ nniɣ-d : « a Rebbi, mačči d wagi i d asigna swayes tekkat! ». Waleɣ igenni yesluɣ-it usigna, yebda-tt ugeffur d icercuren.

Times-nni texsi uqbel ad taweḍ ɣer yigar-nni. Ferḥeɣ, ḥemdeɣ Rebbi, nniɣ-d: ‚Yewweḍ laÆtab s aɣellet, lḥemdulleh ».

Ufiɣ-d yiwen n urgaz zdat-i, yenna-yi-d: ‚Sellek iman-ik rwel a bu wanzaren iɣezfanen, aten-in yiÆdawen n lḥeqq ḍefren-k-id, la ttgallan deg-k ad ak-nɣen !‛. Rewleɣ, la leḥḥuɣ seg uÆerqub ɣer wayeḍ armi leḥqeɣ yiwet n terbaÆt i fehmeɣ d imjuhad. La nleḥḥu deg yiwen n uÆerqub nerra d asawen armi nelḥeq ɣer yiwet n tiɣilt.

Mi nesḍil tamuɣli-nneɣ ɣef tiɣilt-nni, nwala yiwet n lekka teqreb-aneɣ-d. Lekka-nni meqqret anect n lkazyerna. TesÆa tiÆessasin s lemdafÆat qublen ɣer yal tama.

Nekk lliɣ d amezwaru zdat terbaÆt-nni. Mi waleɣ lekka-nni, zziɣ-d ɣer yimeddukkal-iw akken ad asen-iniɣ ad heggin iman-nsen ɣer yimenɣi. Mi d-mmuqleɣ ɣer deffir, ufiɣ-d iman-iw lliɣ weḥd-i. Uɣaleɣ-d ɣer deffir, rriɣ d akessar s trewla. LÆesker ẓran-iyi-d si tÆessast.

Sliɣ nnan-iyi-d: ‚ad ak-id-newwet s yiwet n lbumba tesḥyewwiḍ sebÆa n lmitrat‛. Wwten-d lbumba-nni, teɣli-d deffir-iw. Ur iyi-d-telḥiq ara. Sliɣ tikkelt tis snat nnan-iyi-d: ‚ad ak-id-newwet s lbumba tesḥyewwiḍ sebÆa n yikili
wumitren‛. Nekk waleɣ ɣer zdat s lqerb yella wasif yeččur d aman rnu ur yeḥmil ara. Ɣesbeɣ tazzla-w ɣer wasif-nni. Uqbel ad leḥqeɣ telḥeq-d lbumba-nni, meÆna ur iyi-d-tḥuz ara. Tikkelt tis tlata nnan-iyi-d: ‚ad ak-id-newwet s lbumba tesḥyewwiḍ sebÆin n yikili wumitren‛. Nniɣ-d deg wul-iw: ‚tagi, ur iyi-tzeggal ara‛. Cahdeɣ s Rebbi. Ufiɣ-d leḥqeɣ ɣer wasif-nni. Negzeɣ ɣer waman, ɣeḍseɣ iman-iw. Mi sliɣ teṭṭerḍeq lbumba-nni, refdeɣ-d iman-iw ad waliɣ d acu n zzlezla i texdem tyita-nni. Ufiɣ-d siwa d awal kan, ur waleɣ ula d asxibbeḍ n tyaziḍt. Mmuqleɣ asif-nni waleɣ ɣer zdat yenneqḍaÆ-d s ugafa. Agafa-nni, yemɣi-d deg-s usɣersif yemkuddes afurek yekcem deg wayeḍ. Waleɣ tlata n yilmeẓyen i d-fehmeɣ d imjuhad, lḥan-d s tazzla Æeddan deg usɣersif-nni s lḥerṣ, ttwaselḥen s yibeckiḍen n yimenɣi i wwin gar yifassen-nsen. Mi d-leḥqen ɣer-i, nniɣ-asen: ‚d acu yeḍran akka?‛. Nnan-iyi-d: ‚d lÆesker i aɣ-d-itebÆen‛. Neṭqeɣ ɣer umezwaru nniɣ-as: ‚awi-d leslaḥ-nni-inek s afus-iw‛. Yefka-yi-d abeckiḍ-nni, ṭṭfeɣ-t-id, nniɣ-asen: ‚tebÆet-iyi-d ad nuɣal ɣer lÆesker-agi i ken-id-itebÆen, ad newwet neɣ ad nettewwet. Neffeɣ-d ad njahed i wudem n Rebbi, ad njahed ɣef lḥeqq‛. Nuɣal gar-aneɣ wa yeqqar i wayeḍ ɛeddi d amezwaru. Nekk ur uggadeɣ ara. MeÆna ur ttkileɣ ara; armi ḥṣiɣ ma ur zwireɣ ara ulac wayeḍ, nniɣ-asen: ‚d nekk ara iḍillen d amezwaru, maca ma nɣan-iyi, ur ttuɣalet ara ɣer deffir, ilaq ad d-terrem ttar‛. Swejdeɣ iman-iw akken ilaq. Mi ḍilleɣ ɣer deffir ugafa-nni, ufiɣ siwa yiwen uÆsekriw, yeskker armi ur yezmir ad
iḥerrek ula d iles-is. Yeḍleq iman-is di tmurt la yesdemdum am wakli-nni yerfan ɣef ssid-is. Mi d-leḥqen yimeddukkal-iw s aÆsekriw-nni, nnan-iyi-d: ‚Ad t-nenneɣ‛. Nniɣ-asen: ‚Ala, ad as-nekkes leslaḥ, iselsa; ad as-nanef ad iruḥ Æeryan s atmaten-is akken ad ḥṣun s yimjuhad mačči d at tmurḍas am nutni‛. NÆerra aÆsekri-nni, nunef-as. Nkemmel, abrid di tlata yid-neɣ. Wid-nni-nniḍen tiniḍ uɣalen d ulac. Abrid-nni yewsaÆ: ur yefri ma d abrid neɣ d asif akiwan. Nelḥa armi waleɣ deg ubrid-nni ulac taseddarit rnu zdat waleɣ yella uxxam n temsulta.

Neṭqeɣ ɣer yimeddukkal-iw nniɣ-asen: ‚asset iman-nwen ɣef tmesrafgin, dagi iwÆer fell-aɣ ubrid ula d ttejra wuɣur ara neddari ulac, yernu aql-aneɣ qrib ad naweḍ ɣer temsulta, ahat ad tilifunin i tmesrafgin-:nsen. Nekni ilaq d nettkel ɣef Rebbi ad neẓdem fell-asen‛. Nnan-iyi-d: ‚D lwajeb fell-aneɣ aql-aɣ newjed‛.

Neqsed s axxam-nni n temsulta, nniɣ deg wul-iw: ‚Ad d-nḥelli leslaḥ i wiyaḍ-nneɣ neɣ ad nruḥ ulac maḍi‛. La nleḥḥu wa zdat wa. Nekk ḍḥiɣ-d d alemmas. Uqbel axxam-nni, llan sin n yiserdasen Æussen-d abrid: yiwen si tama wayeḍ si tama tayeḍ bedden mqabalen, ṭṭfen timeẓyanin wehhan-tent i tyita.

Ma d amjahed-nni-nneɣ yesÆa tameẓyant di teɣlaft iÆelleq-itt s aggus, la ileḥḥu s laman. Mi qrib ad yaweḍ ɣer gar yiÆessasen-nni, waleɣ-ten rran tixencucin n tmeẓyanin-nni ɣer tmurt akken ad sɣiflen abuneggiw-nni ur ten-nefhim ara d iserdasen n uÆdaw. Mi yelḥeq gar-asen, wehhan ɣer-s timeẓyanin-nni, sliɣ nnan-as: ‚Rfed ifassen-ik‛. Yebda ireffed ifassen-is;
ṭṭṭfeɣ fell-asen s "lmaṭ", nɣiɣ-ten di sin. Nekni nemyelḥaq di tlata la nteddu tayet ɣer tayet. Ula d bu tmeẓyant-nni yuɣal s "lmaṭ" am wakken yella zik. Nelḥa s uxatel. Mi newweḍ s axxam-nni n temsulta, nufa-t yettwaxdem s lmeryat. Mi siggeɣ ɣer daxel, waleɣ yeččur d lɣaci s tlaba taɣerfant. Llan yirgazen, llant tlawin s tlaba n teqbayliyin. Llant tullas d warrac imeẓyanen. Gar lɣaci-nni banen-iyi-d tlata n yirgazen refden tilifun zzin fell-as; fehmeɣ tlata-nni d imsulta iɣerfanen.

Ṭṭfeɣ fell-asen rniɣ-ten ɣer yiÆessasen-nni. Uɣaleɣ fehmeɣ skra yellan daxel-nni d imsulta n uÆdaw d twaculin-nsen. Rriɣ i "lmaṭ"-nni acarjur yeččuren wehhaɣ-tt ɣer tyita s kra yellan din. Uqbel ad jebdeɣ zznad sliɣ i tilawin-nni meǧdent nnant-iyi-d: "Ad ak-yehdu Rebbi a Meẓyan ad tesgujleḍ arrac-agi.". Nniɣ-asent: "Nekni nennum d yigujilen, d Rebbi i ten-id-ixelqen i asen-igen ttawil."

Qerceɣ tuɣmes s wurfan, sserseɣ aḍad-iw di zznad, sliɣ meǧdent, nnant-iyi-d: "Ad ak-yehdu Rebbi a Meẓyan, ad ǧǧlent telmeẓyin!". Nniɣ-asent: "Nekni nennum d tuǧǧal timeẓyanin; argaz d win i d-yeǧǧan isem-is yemmut ɣef wudem n Rebbi."

Tikkelt tis tlata mi sserseɣ aḍad-iw di zznad, sliɣ nnant-iyi-d: "Ad ak-yehdu Rebbi a Meẓyan, ad tenɣeḍ arrac imeẓyanen.". Ḥulfeɣ yefcel udaḍ-nni yersen di zznad; kkseɣ-t-id si zznad, zziɣ ɣer yimeddukkal-iw nniɣ-asen: Yallah, selket iman-nwen, tura ad d-leḥqent tmesrafgin n uÆdaw. Nuɣal-d ɣer deffir, nelḥa-d kra n yisurrifen deg ubrid-nni ansi nekka, waleɣ sin-nni n yimeddukkal-iw
rekkben ɣef sin n yiÆawdiwen d imellalen. Nekk la tentabaÆeɣ s tikli ɣef uḍar; meÆna fehmeɣ-d la nettmestaÆfu di tlata yid-neɣ ɣef sin-nni n yiÆawdiwen. IÆawdiwen-nni ɣeṣben tazzla nekk ddiɣ d uḍar-nsen. Mi neffeɣ i ubrid-nni yestugnan, newweḍ s anida ara nkemmel abrid yestiwnen yerna ur merkud ara, yewÆer ula s tikli ɣef uḍar. Yers-d yiwen si rrakbin-nni, uɣaleɣ deg umkan-is. Mi srekdeɣ iman-iw sufella n uÆawdiw-nni, giɣ-as-d amkan i Winna yersen nniɣ-as: "Ali-d, rkeb-d ula d kečč!". Yuli-d irkeb deffir.

Clegmeɣ aÆawdiw-nni akken ad yazzel sliɣ-as la yettnazaÆ, fehmeɣ-t tzad teÆkkemt fell-as. Nniɣ-as deg wul-iw: "Amek ara xedmeɣ tura? Ma ǧǧiɣ arfiq-iw ad yelḥu ɣef uḍar ad yeÆyu, iɣaḍ-iyi; ma yerkeb-d yid-i ad tt-neddu akka s tikli-agi ad aɣ-d-leḥqen yiÆdawen!". iwdeɣ clegmeɣ aÆawdiw-nni la yettkurrub ad yeɣli. Zziɣ s arfiq-nni nniɣ-as: "Llah ɣaleb a gma, ers tura d nnuba-w ad rekbeɣ." Yers. Clegmeɣ aÆawdiw-nni ḥulfeɣ yuzzel s tazzla n terṣaṣt. Ur ḥṣiɣ ansi yekka neɣ amek i d-ufiɣ iman-iw d sin-nni n yimeddukkal la nleḥḥu ɣef uḍar lmaṭat gar yifassen-nneɣ. Zwireɣ zdat-sen, mi nelḥeq ɣer ddaw n yiwet n tiɣilt, waleɣ tlata n yirgazen Æussen-d abrid di rrif n taddart. Irgazen-nni llan deg yiwet n tmazirt n lebṣel i d-yezgan di tama n wadda n taddart-nni, ṭṭfen ibeckiḍen n ssyada gar yifassen-nsen uɣalen ɣef uÆebbuḍ di tmazirt-nni. Mi nḍil deg-sen, yenṭeq-d yiwen seg-sen yenna-d: "D acu- ken kunwi?". Nniɣ-as: "D
imjuhad. I kunwi d acu- ken?". Yenna-yi-d: "Ziɣ d atmaten-nneɣ, nekni qrib i d-newwet deg-wen."

Nleqmen bedden, rran ibeckiḍen ɣef tuyat-nsen. Mi newweḍ ɣer-sen bedden-d ɣer-neɣ s lemqadra, nemsalam yid-sen. Nniɣ-asen: "Yya-w ad nettkel ɣef Rebbi ad nkemmel ɣer zdat.". Ddan-d yid-neɣ nekcem taddart la nleḥḥu deg yiwen n ubrid d azrug tiniḍ d iɣẓer uḍyiq. Mi newweḍ s axxam i d-yellan d amezwaru, sliɣ i yiwen seg tlata-nni yenna-d: "Ad nekcem s axxam-agi, d bab n uxxam-agi ad aɣ-iniwlen.". Nniɣ-as: "Ala ad nkemmel ɣer zdat mazalḥal.‛ Yenna-iy-d: ‚atan sraḥeɣ la seknafen iÆeẓwan at-uxxam-agi, ad nekcem meqqar ad ten-id-farseɣ deg uÆwin.‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Nniɣ-ak yalleh d acu n ufares-agi, wigi d iẓawaliyen rnu abrid la ɣ-yettraǧu.‛

Nkemmel abrid-nneɣ nelḥa d asawen armi nelḥeq ɣer tqiwect n usawen-nni ufiɣ-d iman-iw weḥd-i leslaḥ ulac, ula d talaba-w tettwabeddel. Ufiɣ-d lsiɣ tabedÆit d tazeggaɣt, aserwal d aberkan, arkasen d izewwaɣen. Fehmeɣ iman-iw lliɣ d imenfi ttnadin fell-i lÆesker n uÆdaw. Beddeɣ di tiɣilt-nni, mmuqleɣ ɣer yal tama, neṭqeɣ nniɣ-d: ‚Sanida ara rreɣ a Rebbi! Kecmeɣ-d tamurt ur ssineɣ.‛

Ata yiwen n urgaz ibedd-d ɣer tama-w yenna-yi-d: ‚Ad taɣeḍ abrid-inna yestiwnen alamma tleḥqeḍ ɣer taddart-inna yellan agemmaḍ. Di taddart-nni yella yiwen n urgaz d ccif n yimjuhad. Mi tleḥqeḍ ɣer-s ad k-yeffer ɣef yiÆdawen.‛

Ṭḥfeɣ abrid ɣer taddart-nni. Asurif amezwaru ufiɣ-d iman-iw daxel n tesraf tella yid-i yemma, llant tlata n
tlawin ur ten-t-ssineɣ ara. Sliɣ i yemma la d-teqqar imeslayen n yihwah aÆdaw ad isetḥi ad ten-id-yini zdat wayeḍ-is. Nekk la as-qqareɣ ad akem-yehdu Rebbi a yemma d lÆib fell-am nekk d mmi-m. Nettat meskud ttḥellileɣ deg-s la tettzad. Mmuqleɣ amek ara selkeɣ iman- iw seg tesraft-nni, ufiɣ ulamek: tasraft lqayet s lqis n tiddi- w, terna tettwaseqqef-d s yiwet n lÆerṣa temzurrab, ameccuc yekcem deg wayeḍ. Awal n yihwah la yettzad nekk weḥleɣ. Taggara iban-iyi-d yiwen n uceqqiq gar yimeccucen, tezga-d tmuɣli-w deg yiwen n ufurk n teslent yemÆiddel-d ɣef tesraft-nni. Nniɣ-d deg wul-iw: ‚Ad Æeddiɣ gar yimeccucen-inna isennanen-nsen Æuḍmen tisegnatin mebla ccek ad d-ǧǧeɣ aksum-iw ɣer deffir; ad qqimeɣ di tesraft-agi lmut axir n tudert, ilaq kan ad ttekleɣ ɣef Rebbi.‛ Negzeɣ uzgaɣ-d ṭṭfeɣ deg yiwen n umeccuc jeÆlulqeɣ. Mmuqleɣ ifassen-iw waleɣ ntan deg-sen yisennanen ffɣen-d yixfawen-nsen seg yidis-nniḍen. Rriɣ tirrugza, la ttÆeddiɣ s lḥers. Isennanen la cerrwen deg uksum-iw. Sebbreɣ iman-iw s Rebbi, nniɣ-d: ‚Lettkal fell- ak a win yessidiren ineqq. Ma yeqqim-d deg-i yiɣes d lbaraka.‛ Leḥqeɣ s afurk-nni, negzeɣ ɣer tmurt, ufiɣ-d iman-iw la leḥḥuɣ deg ubrid-nni i yi-yemla urgaz-nni. Qesdeɣ ɣer taddart-nni yellan agemmaḍ di tqiwect n udrar. Deg ubrid-nni mi leḥqeɣ ɣer zdat, ufiɣ-d abrid n ukerrus yenneḍ ɣef tɣaltin am umeqyas ɣef ufus. La leḥḥuɣ ttwaliɣ di lmut-iw seg dqiqa ɣer tayeḍ. Mi ḍalleɣ di tiɣilt ad d-iniɣ, mi ara awḍeɣ ɣer tayeḍ ad afeɣ lÆesker
Æussen neɣ uɣen-d abrid-agi, ad mlileɣ yid-sen nekk aql-i s ulac gar yifassen-iw i la leḥḥuɣ.

Tamesrafegt iwumi qqaren tamucart la yi-d-tettabaÆ tettainneḍ di tegnawt. Mi leḥqeɣ s anida yella ubrid n uḍar yemlal d ubrid-nni n ukerrus, din suÆfeɣ abrid.

Tamesrafegt-nni tettixer fell-i. Mi kecmeɣ s abrid-nni n uḍar, ufiɣ-d iman-iw tama n yiwen n ufrag deg llant aṭas n texxamin ttwabnant d adur ɣef snat n ṭṭebqat. Tixxamin-nni banent-iyi-d qedmit: llant ttwajeggrent yuɣal lǧir-nni yegra-d deg-sent d lmarat kan.

Waleɣ ixeddamen kra deg-sen la seqcaren lǧir-nni aqdim, wiyaḍ la ttÆawaden lǧir ajdid. Kecmeɣ s afrag-nni akken ad steqsiɣ ɣef winna wuɣur ttwazneɣ.

Mi leḥqeɣ ɣer yixeddamen-nni kukreɣ-ten acku ur ḥṣiɣ ara d acu llan ma d iḥbiben-iw neɣ d iÆdawen-iw. Nutni lhan kan d ccɣel-nsen nekk la ttxemmimeɣ fell-asen.

Yuɣal yelḥa-d ɣer-i yiwen deg-sen cikkeɣ deg-s ad yili d ccif-nsen. Mi d-yewweḍ ɣer-i. yefreḥ yes-i yenna-yi-d: ‚LÆeslama a Meẓyan!‛.

Nemsalam s ccuq d leḥmala yenna-yi-d: ‚Amek i telliḍ a Meẓyan a gma?‛ Nniɣ-as: ‚Aql-i d imenfi la ttnadin fell-i yiÆdawen. ḍefren-iyi-d lÆesker.‛.

Yenna-yi-d: ‚Ur ttuggad, ata ubrid-ik yeḍbeÆ di tewriqt, kemmel ɣer zdat, ass n lǧemÆa uɣal-d ɣer-i tella yiwet n taddart ixuṣṣ-iten urgaz ad ak-ceggÆeɣ ɣer din.‛ Nniɣ-as: ‚yerḥem waldi-k txedmeḍ lemziyya.‛.

Yenna-yi-d: ‚Xedmeɣ lwajeb-iw mačči d lemziyya.‛ Nniɣ-as:‛Yak ɣer zdat d laman ulac lÆesker?‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚Ruḥ kan ur yelli acu ara tuggadeḍ!‛
Kemmleɣ abrid ɣer zdat armi waleɣ qrib ad awḍeɣ ɣer yiwen n umkan ideg llan aṭas n yixeddamen, beddeɣ la ttxemmimeɣ, nniɣ-d: ‚Ad aẓeɣ ɣer zdat, ixeddamen-inna ahat yella ɣer-sen tilifun. Ccif-nsen ur yuɣal ara d ccif armi yella d amucar; ad wexreɣ ɣer deffir aten-in la d-ttwalin deg-i, uggadeɣ ad tilifunin i lÆesker, ilaq kan ad aẓeɣ ɣer zdat mi leḥqeɣ ɣer-sen ad rreɣ iman-iw d lxedma i la ttnadiɣ.‛.

Mi wwḍeɣ ɣer yixeddamen-nni, nniɣ i ccif-nsen: ‚Aql-i la ttnadiɣ lxedma ma teḥwaǧem axeddam?‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚Aql-aɣ ‚kumpli‛, siwa ma tesÆiḍ ‚lisipasi‛.‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Lisipasi ur sÆiɣ ara, meÆna xeddmeɣ ass d yiḍ yerna lxedma n sebÆa n yixeddamen nekk xeddmeɣ-tt weḥd-i.‛

Yenna-yi-d: ‚Ihi ass n lḥed ad tekmasiḍ.‛ Kemmleɣ tikli-w ɣer zdat, waleɣ arrac la leḥḥun tarbaÆt ta zdat ta, zegren i yiwen n yiɣzer. Mi leḥqeɣ ɣer-sen, ufiɣ-ten d arrac n taddart-iw, d wid ukud ɣriɣ di llakul amenzu. arrac-nni mlilen sin sin di tesrafin yeččuren d aman, semlilen izugar-nsen la ttemyerfaden s lleÆb am tqeslin-nni n lmizan. Tisrafin ttwaxedment am tneṭlin.

Aman-nni yellan deg-sent di tegrest ḥman, deg uzɣal semḍit. Ma d amkan iban-iyi-d d amkan ideg tella tmeqbert di taddart-nneɣ. Mi waleɣ akken fehmeɣ-d arrac-nni llan di lferḥ u d arrac n wid yellan ɣer tama n Fransa. Rniɣ fehmeɣ lweqt amzun d zzman mi tella Fransa teḥkem di tmurt n Lezzayer. Arrac-nni llan qqaren.

Mi asen-d-yeḥḍer lweqt n rraḥa, ffɣen ad merren. S wakka ḥulfeɣ yeččur-d wul-iw d lxiq serrḥeɣ d imeṭṭi.
nniɣ-d: ‚A Rebbi, s kra n wid-nni ifeɣ di leqraya tura aten-in la ttkemmilen leqraya-nsen ad ffɣen akk d lfahmin, ad ṭṭfen imukan yelhan. Tura aten-in llan amek i asen-yehwa gar yimawlan-nsen; nekk aql-i ɣerrqeɣ-d si tmurt-iw; rwiɣ lḥif, rriɣ siwa lmut gar wallen-iw!‛. Waleɣ yelḥa-d yiwen n urgaz, Æeqleɣ-t, n taddart-iw isem-is Ḥmed, yella d lamin aqdim di taddart. Fehmeɣ-t d axeddam iqeddcen ɣef warrac-nni. Yewwi-d yid-s taqerÆet n lqahwa tayeḍ n llatay d ssniwa n yifenǧalen. Mi d-yelḥeq ɣer-i yenna-yi-d: ‚A lÆeslama a Meẓyan! D acu i k-id-yewwin akka ɣer tmurt-agi?‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Llah isellem-k, la ttnadin fell-i yiÆdawen aql-i ɣerqeɣ-d si tmurt-iw.‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚Ay anida telliḍ yella Rebbi.‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Fell-as i ttekleɣ. Ihi a Dda ¨¨Ḥmed ma ad tawḍeḍ ɣer yimawlan-iw, tiniḍ-asen ẓriɣ Meẓyan, atan di lḥif d ameqqran; inni-asen atan iɣerreq di tmura.‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚D acu i k-yerran di lḥif a Meẓyan? Ur tenḥafeḍ ara!‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Ixuṣṣ akka a Dda Ḥmed! Tizyiwin-iw aten-an llan amek i asen-yehwa la ttkemmilen leqraya-nsen ad uɣalen s kra n win ifeɣ ad iyi-yif. Nekk aql-i ɣerrqeɣ d imenfi rwiɣ leÆtab, ur iyi-yerwi.‛ Dda Ḥmed yeḍsa yenna-yi-d: ‚D ayagi kan i ak-yecqan? Buh a Meẓyan i yeɣran mebla ccix, yeǧǧa-d isem-is di ttarix, d lamer n Rebbi i iḍerrun a Meẓyan!‛ Ufiɣ-d iman-iw la leḥḥuɣ qrib ad kecmeɣ ɣer yiwet n taddart, taddart-nni tettwazerreb s sselk, nniɣ-d: ‚Mebla ccek mačči di taddart-agi i ten ixuṣṣ urgaz axaṭer dagi ulac lemneÆ. SuÆfeɣ ɣef taddart-nni rriɣ d asawen. Leḥqeɣ ɣer yiwet n tqenṭert yellan temÆiddel ɣef yiwen n yiɣzer
walleɣ tlata n warrac bedden zdat n tqenṭert-nni. Yiwen deg-sen yelsa talaba d tazewwaɣt, ma d wayeḍ iban-iy-d s ṣṣifa n yiwen isem-is Muḥd u eysa d aḍeggal-iw. Ruḥeɣ s tazzla ɣer-s, mi leḥqeɣ, yezzi-d ɣer-i, imuqel-iyi-d, yuɣal yezzi udem-is fell-i; imir ḥṣiɣ-t mačči d netta d acabi kan i t-cubeɣ. Uɣaleɣ lḥiɣ ɣer bu-tlaba-nni tazewwaɣt; mi leḥqeɣ ɣer-s, ifreḥ-d deg wudem-iw yenna-yi-d: ‚LÆeslama a Meẓyan-nneɣ.‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Llah iselm-k a gma, mačči di taddart-agi i ixuṣṣ urgaz?‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚Ala, mačči dagi. Ixuṣṣ di taddart-inna agemmaḍ di tqiwect n udrar, anida i d-ttbanen yixxamen d izewwaɣen.‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Ihi ad d-tedduḍ yid-i ad iyi-temleḍ axxam-agi ideg ixuṣṣ urgaz. Yenna-yi-d: ‚Ala, nekk ur tedduɣ ara yid-k!‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Yya-n kan. Mi newweḍ ad ak-id aɣeɣ lḥelwa.‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚Ihi qebleɣ.‛. Neddukkel armi newweḍ ɣer zdat n tewwurt n uxxam i d-yellan d amezwaru di taddart uɣer i neqsed. Tawwurt n uxxam-nni tqubel-d s abrid. Waleɣ yiwet n tmeṭṭut akked teqcict beddent-d deffir n umnar n tewwurt-nni Æussent-d abrid. Tameṭṭut-nni ur tt-ssineɣ ara, taqcict-nni n taddart-iw isem-is Jeǧǧiga. Mi yi-d-teẓra tefreḥ-d ɣer-i tenna-yi-d: ‚LÆeslama a Meẓyan.‛. Msalameɣ yid-s, luÆeɣ-tt, nniɣ-as: ‚Deg uxxam-agi i ixuṣṣ urgaz?‛. Tuzzel-d ɣer-i s lferḥ, tÆelleq-d ɣer yiri-w tenna-yi-d: ‚Ih, dagi. Rwaḥ ad ak-nejmeÆ ɣur-neɣ ur yelli acu ad ak-ixaṣṣen, ur tesÆiḍ ara tuggadeḍ, ad tiliḍ di laman n Rebbi. Yya-n s axxam!‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Ihi qebleɣ.‛. Teṭṭef-iyi seg ufus, kecmeɣ deg tewwurt-nni. Leḥqeɣ kecmeɣ s asqif. Lḥiɣ deg usqif-nni
armi qrib ad ffɣeɣ s afrag. Ufiɣ amaÆzuz-nni icerḍen lefdi n tmurt-iw s tukksa n uqerruy-iw. Waleɣ-t ibedd deffir n ṭṭabla n usɣar am tinna n yigezzaren, yeṭṭef tacaqurt. Mi yi-d-iwala yenna-yi-d: ‚Tleḥqeḍ-d ɣer dagi a Meẓyan?!‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Nekk leḥqeɣ-d, kečč tezwareḍ-iyi-d.‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚Amek ihi, teṭṭfeḍ deg wawal-ik ɣef ccerṭ-nni i cerḍeɣ fell-ak neɣ ad tuɣaleḍ?‛ Nniɣ-as: ‚Ur ttuɣaleɣ ɣer deffir, ur ttuɣaleɣ deg wawal-iw. Tcerḍeḍ fell-i lefdi n tmurt-iw s tukksa uqerruy-iw. Aql-i qebleɣ.‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚Mačči d nekk, d nnif-ik i t-id-icerḍen. Yerna mačči weḥd-k. muqel ɣer zdat, muqel ɣer deffir.‛

Muqleɣ ɣer zdat waleɣ iqerray n yirgazen ttwakksen si tfekkiwin nsen. Iqerray-nni ttwaliɣ mazal-iten ddren. Allen-nsen la ttmuqulent, udmawen-nsen yufrar-d fell-asen lferḥ. Mi muqleɣ ɣer deffir, waleɣ adur n yirgazen aneggaru deg-sen ur telḥiq ara tmuɣli-w ɣer-s. Irgazen-nni d ucbiḥen, nnḍen-asen yidammen am teɣlacin di tmegraḍ-nsen, tiniḍ mmezlen. Nekk xas akken qebleɣ lfinga-nni, meÆna lliɣ la ttergigiɣ si tuggdi. Sliɣ i yirgazen-nni akken ma llan neṭqen-d nnan-d: ‚Ur ttuggad a Meẓyan, mačči weḥd-k i telliḍ.‛. Imir fehmeɣ-d irgazen-nni d wid yellan deffir-iw rran-d adur wa zdat wa ɣer twikksa n yiqerray-nsen ɣef lefdi n tmurt-nsen. Hulfeɣ s wul-iw yeččur-d d ṣṣber. Tuggdi-nni tuɣal-iyi d tirrugza. Qerrbeɣ ɣer ṭṭabla -nni, serseɣ anyir-iw sufell-as...

Ukiɣ-d si targit !

- 87 -
Yeǧǧa-yi-d Muḥend u isa

Lliɣ deg uxxam-iw aqdim, ufiɣ-d yid-i tlata n yirgazen, neqqim di tlemmast n wagens. Neṭqeɣ nniɣ-asen: ‚Ad iyi-d-tinim kra n yisefra. Mi ukiɣ si targit ad ten-aruɣ.‛ Refden-d snitrat, wwin-d yiwet n lmuziga teÆǧeb-iyi mačči d kra! Nleqmeɣ la ceṭṭḥeɣ. Uɣalen refden-d taɣect n ccna n Ḥsisen ad yettwarḥem ‚Ay ul izegren lebḥer‛. Taɣect-nni daɣen tuzga-iyi-d ɣef wul. La ceṭṭḥeɣ cennuɣ armi i d-ffɣeɣ di tewwurt n uxxam. Ufiɣ-d iman-iw deg yiwen n uzaɣar la tedduɣ akken s ccḍeḥ d ccna di taɣect-nni. Deg uzaɣar-nni yella ubrid n ukerrus, nnig ugafa n ubrid-nni yella ubrid n uḍar d arqiqan. Nekk la tedduɣ s ccḍeḥ deg ubrid-nni arqiqan. Tikkelt ad d-afeɣ iman-iw deg ubrid, tikkelt nnig ubrid neɣ ddaw ubrid. Mi leḥqeɣ sanida i d-nneqḍaÆen sin-nni n yiberdan, ufiɣ d asif. Agemmaḍ n wasif-nni d amadaɣ. Zegreɣ asif-nni s ccḍeḥ d ccna. Cennuɣ ttÆawadeɣ-d i taɣect-nni. Mi leḥqeɣ s amadaɣ-nni, ufiɣ-d ṭṭfeɣ deg ufus-iw nnefṣ n texbizt d tamejṭuḥt. Uliɣ d asawen deg umadaɣ-nni. Mi leḥqeɣ ɣer tama ufella nnig wasif, mmuqleɣ ɣer tama tazelmaḍt-iw, waleɣ tlata n yilmeẓyen bedden agemmaḍ n yiɣzer i d-yellan gar-i yid-sen. Ilmeẓyen-nni d wid n taddart-iw: yiwen d aḍeggal-iw isem-is Muḥ u isa; wayeḍ d Lḥusin, wis tlata ssawalen-as Lḥusin Ḥewwa. Akken i yi-d ẓran, la yi-d-ssawalen ad ruḥeɣ ɣer-sen. Nekk la asen-ttwehhiɣ s nnefṣ-nni n texbizt, la tedduɣ s ccna d ccḍeḥ, rriɣ d
asawen deg umadaɣ-nni. Mi d-siyyben asiwel, nniɣ-d: ‚Ilaq-iyi ad ruḥeɣ ɣer-sen, d arraw n taddart-iw, ulamek i rewleɣ fell-asen!‛

Lḥiɣ armi leḥqeɣ ɣer yiɣzer-nni, ufiɣ-t lqay ulamek i as-zegreɣ. Lḥiɣ d asawen armi d ansi i d-yenneqḍaÆ umadaɣ-nni s ubrid n ukerrus. Ufiɣ tiqenṭert temÆidel ɣef yiɣẓer-nni. Zegreɣ seg-s. leḥqeɣ s anida yenneḍ ubrid. Mi Æeddeɣ di ddura-nni, ḥulfeɣ Æyiɣ, qqimeɣ ad staÆfuɣ. Mi qqimeɣ, ufiɣ-d deg ufus-iw lbunt n dduxxan mejṭuḥet maḍi; ṭṭṭfeɣ-tt gar waccarren-iw. Mi tt-rriɣ ɣer yimi-w, teɣli-as target akked llemc, yegra-d kan lkaɣeḍ-nni. Isuḍ-d waḍu yewwi llemc-nni. Tirget-nni teɣli tuɣal d iɣiɣden. Waleɣ yekker ddexxan ddaw ubrid-nni n ukerrus. Dduxxan-nni yekker-d d abbu la iferreq yettara ɣer yal tama. Rriḥa-s tiniḍ d lbarud-nni iḥerqen. Nniɣ-d deg wul-iw: ‚ad yili d arrac-nni-nneɣ i icaÆlen times.‛

Nleqmeɣ, lḥiɣ ɣer ddexxan-nni, ufiɣ tarbaÆt n yilmeẓyen n taddart-iw bedden zdat n tqenṭert-nni deg waṭas yid-sen. Yella gar-asen Muḥed u isa, yeqqim ɣef rrif n tqenṭert-nni. Waleɣ udem-is yecɣeb, termel-it tamart, talaba-s d taqdimt meÆna zeddiget. Mi yi-d-iwala, yelḥa-d ɣer-i; mi d-yewweḍ zdat-i yuɣal-d s tlaba tajdidt ur yesÆi tamart wala cclaɣem. ḍḥiɣ-d wehmeɣ deg-s! yenṭeq-d ɣer-i, yenna-yi-d: ‚ma ur k-nɣin ad k-sḍeÆfen.‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚ur ḥṣiɣ ara, sefhem-iyi-d!‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚Azekka ad ruḥeɣ ɣer Fransa.‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚La teskiddibeḍ a Muḥ!‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚Azekka ad ruḥeɣ ɣer fransa, ma ur ti wumineḍ ara atan mmi-s n Æemmi yid-s i ddefÆeɣ.‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Tura
cikkeɣ di rwaḥ-ik!‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚Azekka ad ruḥeɣ ɣer Fransa, atan ǧǧiɣ-ak-d kra si tlaba-w; nekk ass n letniyen ad d-uɣaleɣ ɣer-k.‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Ad truḥeḍ azekka, ad d-tuɣaleḍ ɣer-i ass n letniyen! Ihi dagi kan ara tɣabeḍ.‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚Ih, s lqerb-agi kan.‛

Ufiɣ-d iman-iw deg umkan-nni deg i lliɣ qqimeɣ mi ṭṭfeɣ lbunt-nni n dduxxan. Nbedd akken nella d tarbaÆt. Muḥend u isa ibedd zdat-neɣ, yezzi iman-is yefka-aneɣ-d s uÆrur. Iban-iyi-d s tamart, talaba-s d taqdimt tumes d injan. Mi muqleɣ deg-s wehmeɣ, nniɣ-d: ‚Wagi la yettbeddil seg dqiqa ɣer tayeḍ! Waleɣ-t yeṭṭef tawerqet deg ufus-is la yettmuqul deg-s. Mmi-s n Æemmi-s sawalen-as Muḥ u isa. Sliɣ Yenna-yas: ‚Wi t-ilan lkaɣeḍ-nni? N Fransa neɣ n lḥebs?‛. Muḥd u isa yenna-yas s yisuɣan: ‚Tagi d serriyya.‛. Nekk nniɣ-as: ‚Ad yili ɣef uxxam i ast-id-ceyyÆen.‛. Uɣaleɣ refdeɣ-d tizlit-nni ‘Ay ul izegren lebḥer’

Ukiɣ-d si targit !

1981
