- 90 -
# Lwajeb n uzzayri

Lliɣ di tarbaÆt n yirgazen qqimeɣ yid-sen di tama ufella nnig lebḥer. Lebḥer-nni yuska-d di tama n wadda n yiwen n uÆerqub yestiwnen aṭas. Lebḥer-nni yewseÆ aṭas. Ma d rrif-nni i d-yellan ɣer-neɣ d uḍyiq yeffeɣ-d d taqernit am temda tameqqrant.

Waleɣ sin n warrac rran taqernit-nni gar-asen. Yiwen deg-sen ibedd ddaw wanida i nella wayeḍ yeqqim agemmaḍ-nneɣ. Aqcic-nni i d-yellan ɣer-neɣ yerfed-d aleqqaf yewwet yes-s winna yellan agemmaḍ, ilqef-it deg uqerruy. Winna nniḍen yerra-yas-d tiyita ilqef-it-id deg uḍar. Yekker-d yiwen si tarbaÆt-nni-nneɣ d argaz ɣezzifen yeqwa, yezgar s aqcic-nni yellan agemmaḍ.

Mi yewweḍ ɣer-s, yewwet-it s tmeẓyant, yenɣa-t. mi waleɣ akken, fehmeɣ argaz-nni d tuḥsift i yas-yellan gar-as d baba-s n uqcic-nni. Mi d-yuɣal ɣer-neɣ urgaz-nni, yewwi-d tameẓyant-nni deg ufus. Nekni nenna-d: ‚atan yezzi-d ɣer-neɣ ad aɣ-ineɣ akken ur d-yettugray ara win ara yessufɣen lexbar akken ad yettwaṭṭef.‘ Nerra d asawen s trewla, neddukkel tlata tlata.

Mi newweḍ ɣer yiwen n laÆzib yezga-d ddaw n yiwet n taddart d tameqqrant. Di laÆzib-nni, nufa abrid d ixunqan. Nekk ddiɣ d sin n yirgazen. Mi qrib ad naweḍ ɣer uxnaq, nwala tḍill-d ṭṭeyya n tafat deg umḍiq-nni am tafat n trisiti n ufus, ad d-nini: ‚Waqila d amcum-nni i aɣ-d-yesqiṭṭÆen, ixulef-aneɣ-d abrid!‘ Mi nelḥeq s amḍiq-nni, ad naf abrid d lxali.
Nedda-tt akken armi nÆedda i yixunqan-nni. Nekk uɣaleɣ ɣeṣbeɣ tazzla, ǧǧiɣ irfiqen-nni ɣer deffir. Uzzleɣ armi leḥqeɣ ɣer tqiwect n usawen-nni, ufiɣ d agdis. Bdiɣ keccmeɣ taddart-nni tameqqrant. La leḥḥuɣ deg yiwen n ubraḥ gar yixxamen. Mi sliɣ i lḥes n tkerrust, mmuqleɣ ɣer deffir, waleɣ winna yenɣan aqcic-nni yedda-d d uḍar-iw. Nniɣ-d deg wul-iw: ‚ad zziɣ iman-iw fell-as ur t-ttmuquleɣ ara, ad rreɣ iman-iw mačči d nekk‛.

Lḥiɣ ɣer zdat, rriɣ kan abrid gar wallen-iw. Greɣ asurif; argaz-nni yewwet-iyi-d di tayet yenna-yi-d: ‚Amek i tettiliḍ a Meẓyan?‛. Mmuqleɣ-t, ḍsiɣ ɣer-s nniɣ-as: ‚Aql-i rriɣ abrid gar wallen-iw, la tedduɣ ɣer zdat‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚Iḥeqqa a Meẓyan, ansi-k kečč?.‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Nekk d azzayri si tama n Tizi Uzezzu, laṣel-iw d aqbayli. AÆni ur teḥsiḍ ara yes-i‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚Ihi ad tettuÆaqbeḍ s lxedma.‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Lxedma-agi, d akerfi?‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚Ala, mačči d akerfi, d lxedma yellan fell-ak d lwajeb. Yerna ad ak-teÆǧeb.‛.

Nniɣ-as: ‚D acu-tt lxedma-agi?‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚Attan lxedma-k (yessewÆed s uḍaḍ-is ccahed). Mi mmuqleɣ s aniɣer yessewÆed, waleɣ ɣer yiwen n lḥiḍ i ɣ-d-iqublen. Lḥiḍ-nni d aqdim, yettwikkes-as lǧir rnu deg-s ixmujen i d-yettbanen d ccamat n rṣaṣ; argaz-nni yenna-yi-d: ‚Ilaq lḥiḍ-inna ad t-tlebbseḍ alamma rremlen akk yixmujen-inna, ad as-tÆiwdeḍ ajeggar.‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚nekk ɣer uyagi i d-qesdeɣ ad t-xedmeɣ d lwajeb-iw.‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚Ihi azekka ad d-afeɣ lḥiḍ-agi d acebḥan.‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚LmeÆna n yimeslayen-agi, d Lezzayer-nneɣ ara icebḥen.‛. Isuɣ-d fell-i yenna-yi-d:
‚Nniɣ-ak azekka ad d-afeɣ lḥiḍ-agi terriḍ-t d acebḥan!‛.

ḍsiɣ ɣer-s nniɣ-as: ‚Aql-i tebbteɣ iman-iw di targit i lliɣ. Kečč d yiwen seg wid-nni wuɣer i d-ttcareɣ. Fehmeɣ lmeÆna n yimeslayen-ik, d Lezzayer-nneɣ ara tt-irebḥen.‛.

Yeḍsa-d ɣer-i yenna-yi-d: ‚D tidet, d Lezzayer-nneɣ ara tt-irebḥen. Lezzayer ad terbeḥ, nekni d izzayriyen.‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Ihi tura ad iyi-d-tiniḍ melmi ara yi-serreḥ lmektub n Rebbi ad ruḥeɣ ɣer Fransa. Ad iyi-d-tiniḍ ma ad awḍeɣ s ayen i ssarameɣ neɣ ala!‛

Argaz-nni yettwiddem yuɣal amzun d ulac. Waleɣ lḥant-d snat n telmeẓyin lsant talaba n temdint. Mi d-leḥqent ɣer-i, temmuqel-iyi-d yiwet seg-sent neṭqeɣ ɣer-s, nniɣ-as: ‚Kemm d tamcarit?‛. Tenna-yi-d: ‚Ih.‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Ini-yi-d melmi ara ruḥeɣ ɣer Fransa, ini-yi-d ma yella ad rebḥeɣ neɣ ala!‛

Tezzi ɣer terfiqt-is, mlilent la ttemyeḥmaẓent ttemsudanent. Mi waleɣ akken, fehmeɣ iswi-nsent. Rewleɣ fell-asent.

Lḥiɣ kra n yisurrifen ɣer zdat, mmuqleɣ-d ɣer deffir, waleɣ yiwen n uxeddam n lbusṭa iÆelleq aqrab ɣer deffir am wakken ibubb-it. Argaz-nni iban-iyi-d d ari wumi.

Bɣiɣ ad ruḥeɣ ɣer-s ad as-iniɣ car-iyi-d ufiɣ-d yeÆreq-iyi wamek ara s-t-iniɣ s tefransist. Mi t-waleɣ iruḥ ad yekcem s axxam-is, aqrab-is iban-iyi-d d ilem. Fehmeɣ-t ifak lxedma-s. Uzzleɣ ɣer-s, mi leḥqeɣ, luÆeɣ-t s tefransist, nniɣ-as: ‚Melmi ara ruḥeɣ ɣer Fransa?‛, yerra-yi-d s teqbaylit, yenna-yi-d: ‚Ad truḥeḍ di mayyu.‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Ini-yi-d ma ad rebḥeɣ neɣ ala?‛. Yekcem s axxam. Mi d-yemdel tawwurt-nni, iṣṣerbek-itt; nniɣ-d ad tefreq d
tiquclalin. Kemmleɣ   tikli-w ɣer zdat. Leḥqeɣ ɣer zdat n tlawin lsant talaba d  tabudrart. Tilawin-nni    beddent. Yiwet n tlemẓit teqqim gar-asent, teqqen ɣef uqerruy-is tafunart n  tesfift d taberkant. Tilemẓit-nni    teččeḥ-d tamuɣli-s deg-i; nniɣ-d deg wul-iw: Tilemẓit-inna ad tili d tamcarit yerna d tinna ara yi-d-yinin tidet.

Qerrbeɣ ɣer tlemẓit-nni. Mi leḥqeɣ ɣer-s, ufiɣ-tt tegra-d weḥd-s,  tid-nni-nniḍen ulac-itent. Mi as-nniɣ  car-iyi-d waleɣ-tt tuɣal d aÆemmur n yisɣaren. Neṭqeɣ      nniɣ-as: ‚Qesdeɣ-kem s Rebbi, ini-iyi-d d acu-kem?!‛. Sliɣ i teɣri tenna-yi-d: ‚Nekk d yemma-k Faḍma n Summer.‛. Nekk fehmeɣ-tt d  tamcarit, nniɣ-as: ‚Melmi ara ruḥeɣ      ɣer Fransa?‛. Tenna-yi-d: ‚Ad truḥeḍ ‚mayyu‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Ad rebḥeɣ  neɣ ala?‛. Sliɣ   i teɣri-nni la tesremtuy am tin yerfan, ur as-fhimeɣ ula d yiwen n wawal.  iwdeɣ nniɣ-as: ‚Ma yella ad afeɣ   kra n ttawil di Fransa ur sÆiɣ ay uggadeɣ?‛.  Tiɣri-nni tessusem. Waleɣ sin n      yirgazen bedden-d di tama-w lsan ibernas d icebḥanen rran afus deg  ufus la leḥḥun. Mi mmuqleɣ    ɣer zdat, waleɣ     la teddun ɣer yiwen n yifri, win ara yeɣlin deg-s ula d iɣsan-is ad ftutsen.

Irgazen-nni fehmeɣ-ten d lwajeb ad ḍeggren iman-nsen ɣer yifri-nni iwakken ad d-ǧǧen tirrugza i wid ara ten-id-itebÆen deffir-nsen. Irgazen-nni ɣaḍen-iyi, uggadeɣ fell- asen. Nutni la leḥḥun mebla akukru. Nekk la kkateɣ deg yidmaren-iw, qqareɣ: ‚Ay, ay, ay<‛. Mi leḥqen ɣer yifri-nni, negzen ur banen anida ɣlin. Tiɣri-nni tuɣal-d, nniɣ-as: ‚Ini-iyi-d ma ad rebḥeɣ neɣ ala?‛. Tenna-yi-d: ‚Akka ɣer
qabel ad tuɣal tmeṭṭut-ik s lfuḍa n teklatin. Nniɣ-d deg wul-iw lmeÆna n yimeslayen-agi asmi ara ɣabeɣ, tameṭṭut- iw ahat ad tebru i nnif. Nniɣ-as: „Di laÆnaya-m sefhem-iyi- d d acu i d lmeÆna n lfuḍa n teklatin, Ma d lweÆda ad am- fkeɣ ayen i tebɣiḍ?“. Tenna-yi-d: „Akka ar qabel ad iyi-d- tefkeḍ kra n yigujilen ɣef wudem n Rebbi.“. Nniɣ-as: „Sefhem-iyi-d ma d arraw-iw kan ara yeggujlen?“. Tiɣri- nni tessusem. Nekk ssiwleɣ: „A yemma Faḍma!“

Ukiɣ-d si targit !

1981

Abrid n lḥebs

Lliɣ d tmeṭṭut-iw nbedd zdat tewwurt n ufrag- nneɣ; Sliɣ tenna-yi-d: „Urgeɣ-k a Meẓyan, urgeɣ-k !“. Nniɣ-as: „D lxir kan a TasaÆdit.“. La tekkat deg yidmaren- is, tenna-yi-d: „Urgeɣ-k a Meẓyan, aḥlil aḥlil.“. Nniɣ-as: „D lxir kan a TasaÆdit. Ales-iyi-d targit-im!“. Tenna-yi-d: „Urgeɣ fell-ak a Meẓyan, urgeɣ fell-ak!“. yiɣ qqareɣ-as ḥku-yi-d d acu i turgaḍ fell-i, nettat la tekkat deg yidmaren-is tettergigi amzun yeffeɣ-itt laÆqel. Ɣer taggara waleɣ yiwen isem-is ‘SsaÆid n WaÆrab’, yeqqim ɣef teẓrut.

Amkan-nni yezga-d di tlemmast n laÆzib-nneɣ neqqar-as
‚Amraḥ n yimexlaf‛. Neṭqeɣ ɣer SsaÆid nniɣ-as: ‚Uggad Rebbi a Æemmi SsaÆid, mmuqel-d ɣer wudem-iw amek werraɣ, ɣef akken deg-s idammen!‛; ṭṭef-as rrecba rceb-it, i yi-d-yenna. Deg yimeslayen-agi fehmeɣ-d icehha-d deg-i.

Zziɣ-d ɣer tmeṭṭut-iw, mazal-itt tettnezzif fell-i, nniɣ-as: ‚Ḥṣiɣ targit i turgaḍ fell-i a TasaÆdit, meÆna ur ilaq ara ad tugadeḍ. Nekk ma kecmeɣ lḥebs ad t-kecmeɣ d ucbiḥ; ma mmuteɣ ad mmteɣ d ucbiḥ, ur ilaq ara akk ad tugadeḍ akka!‛. Mi tesla i yimeslayen-agi, tuɣal-d s laÆqel-is, tesÆa tirrugza. Sliɣ tenna-yi-d: ‚Urgeɣ-k a Meẓyan!‛

Ufiɣ-d iman-iw kecmeɣ di tewwurt n lḥebs, leḥḥuɣ deg yiwen n usqif armi kecmeɣ ɣer tzeqqa n lḥebs. Ufiɣ xemsa n yilmeẓyen n taddart-iw. Di tallit-nni ttÆicin d iɣriben di tmurt n Fransa. Sellmeɣ ɣef yilemẓiyen-nni, steqseɣ-ten: ‚Ɣef wacu i ken-id-wwin ɣer lḥebs?‛, yerra-yi-d yiwen seg-sen, yenna-yi-d: ‚Nxeddem ‚ṭrafik‘ nettwaṭṭef.‛.

Nniɣ-as: ‚Kunwi aql-aken d tikkelt tamezwarut i ken-id-wwin ɣer lḥebs yerna ma mačči ɣef lḥeqq-nwen i ken-id-wwin, ur tettÆeṭṭilem ara di lḥebs; ma d nekk tikkelt-agi d tis tlata.‛. Fakeɣ-d awal, waleɣ imeḥbas-nni ffɣen di tewwurt n tzeqqa-nni n lḥebs. Nekk fehmeɣ-d ttwaserrḥen seg lḥebs. TebÆeɣ-ten nemyuǧǧa slam. Lḥiɣ yid-sen armi nelḥeq ɣer tewwurt taneggarut n lḥebs-nni.

Tawwurt-nni tban-iyi-d am tewwurt-nni yettilin di lmersa n lbaburat neɣ di tegnit n tmesrafgin. Uqbel ad ffɣen yimeḥbas-nni, leḥqen-d yimeḥbas-nniḍen i ten-id-itebÆen seg lḥebs. Mi ffɣen yimezwura-nni, ḥebsen-ten sin n yiÆessasen n lḥebs yellan zdat n tewwurt taneggarut.
leḥqen ɣer-sen yimeḥbas-nni ineggura, myuǧǧan gar-asen slam. Nekk mi gemneɣ ad qerrbeɣ ɣer-sen, waleɣ iÆessasen-nni medlen tawwurt la d-ttḥarriren imeḥbas-nni ineggura, gguman ad asen-ffɣen seg lḥebs. Waleɣ daɣen kra n yimeḥbas la ttawin ttarran zdat n lḥebs-nni. Wid-nni fehmeɣ-d d imeḥbas iwumi i d-teqreb tuffɣa seg lḥebs, suffɣen-ten ad merrḥen. Mi ffɣen wid-nni yettwaserrḥen, ad uɣalen yimerraḥan-nni ɣer yimukan-nsen di lḥebs.

MeÆna ula d imerraḥen-nni rran iman-nsen d wid yettwaserrḥen. Sɣiflen iÆessasen-nni, ruḥen ur uɣalen ara ɣer lḥebs. Wid-nni i d-yettwaḥerren ɣer lḥebs rran-ten yiÆessasen-nni ɣef sin n yiduren: seg tewwurt-nni n berra armi d tawwurt n daxel. Imeḥbas-nni mlilen sin sin, wa zdat wa. Nekk lliɣ beddeɣ di rrif. Uɣaleɣ uggadeɣ ma ur kcimeɣ ara s adur ad iyi-zzmen yiÆessasen-nni. Mi muqleɣ anida ara kecmeɣ, waleɣ imeḥbas-nni myenṭaḍen.

Mi ttnadiɣ ad kecmeɣ s adur, win iɣer ruḥeɣ ad d-azgiɣ zdat-s, ur iqebbel ara. Nudeɣ armi ufiɣ yiwen n yilemẓi n taddart-iw ssawalen-as Sliman Ḥewwa, winna ḍemÆeɣ ad iyi-d-yeg amkan zdat-is. Mi ruḥeɣ ad d-azgiɣ zdat-is di ṣṣef la yi-d-iḥebbes, yenna-yi-d: ‚Welleh ma tkecmeḍ-d ɣer ṣṣef-agi.‛. Rfiɣ fell-as, skecmeɣ iman-iw ɣer udur-nni mebla lebɣi-s. kecmeɣ s lḥers.

Mi qeÆdeɣ iman-iw, neṭqeɣ ɣer Sliman nniɣ-as: ‚Ɣef wacu i k-id-wwin ɣer lḥebs a Sliman?‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚Ṭṭfen-iyi la xeddmeɣ ṭrafik.‛. Ufiɣ-d iman-iw zdat n tewwurt tadaxlit n lḥebs.

Beddeɣ berra n ṣṣef-nni n yimeḥbas. Waleɣ yiwen n yilemẓi n taddart-iw isem-is Muḥ u Ḥmed, yeqÆed iman-is
di ṣṣef, steqseɣ-t nniɣ-as: ‚Ɣef wacu i k-id-wwin ɣer lḥebs a Muḥ?‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚Wwin-iyi-d ɣef lkif.‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Ṭṭfen-k la teznuzuḍ neɣ ufan-t kan ɣer-k?‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚Wwiɣ-d ciṭ i nekk, ciṭ i yiwen d aḥbib-iw.‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Ma mačči ɣef yiseɣ i k-id-wwin ur tesḍuluyeḍ ara di lḥebs!‛ Ufiɣ-d iman-iw daxel n tzeqqa n lḥebs, yella yid-i yiwen d ameḥbus wayeḍ d aÆessas n lḥebs. Nbedd la nettmmuqul s afrag n lḥebs. Nwala yiwen n yilemẓi d ameḍÆafu, netta d ucbiḥ yesÆa sser. Ilemẓi-nni la yessusuf iÆessasen-nni n lḥebs, la ten-ireggem. AÆessas-nni yellan yid-i sliɣ yenna-yi-d: ‚Ur tessineḍ ara aqcic-inna? Winna d lefḥel.‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Ala, ur tessineɣ ara.‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚Tessneḍ-t am yiman-ik.‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Ihi yeÆreq-iyi. Ad yili d lmeḥna i t-yesḍeÆfen akka am nekk. Ɣef wacu i t-id-wwin ɣer lḥebs mi yugi ad yexdem akerfi?‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚Ḥettmen-as ad yezweǧ akked weltma-s, netta yenna-yasen ad mmteɣ axir wala ad aɣeɣ weltma. Yewwet winna i t-iḥettmen, irẓa-yas axenfuc-is. Atan wwin-t-id ɣer lḥebs.‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Wwin-t-id ɣef yiseɣ, welleh ard lefḥel.‛. Waleɣ ɣer tama-nniḍen sin n yimeḥbas daxel n texxamt yiwen deg-sen yenṭeq-d ɣer-i, yenna-yi-d: ‚Lḥebs n Tizi Uzezzu d ssilulat.‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Ala, d ṣṣalat.‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚D ssilulat.‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚D ṣṣalat, yella kan lebluk d ajdid d ssilulat.‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚Nniɣ-ak d ssilulat d ssilulat!‛. Waleɣ iṭṭinez ɣer-s winna yellan yid-s, sliɣ yenna-yas s tefransist: ‚D la neuf !‛ Ufiɣ-d lliɣ deg yiwet n texxamt akked wid-nni lliɣ di ṣṣala. AÆessas-nni yeqqim ɣef ukersi, ameḥbus-nni yeqqim ɣef wagens, nekk beddeɣ. Aɛessas-nni yenna-yi-d: ‚Aqcic-
nni i ak-nniɣ d lefḥel ula d lqaḍi yewwet-it s rrkel s axenfuc. Yennelqem ad iyi-d-yessenÆet amek yewwet uqcic-nni ameḥbus-nni, yuɣal-as deg umkan-is. Waleɣ aÆessas-nni cerrken wanzaren-is, la ttcerriqen. Yuɣal yezzi s ameḥbus-nni yemmuqel-it, yemmuqel-d ɣer-i. Nekk fehmeɣ-d amzun yenna-yi-d: 'yeḥqer-iyi neɣ fkiɣ-as laman yexdeÆ-iyi.' Ruḥeɣ ad as-d-kkseɣ akersi i umeḥbus-nni ad t-id-rreɣ i bab-is, ufiɣ-d zdat-i yiwen n urgaz anect ilat, yenna-yi-d: 'Rwaḥ ad nemÆafer nekk yid-k a Meẓyan!' Nniɣ-as: 'Fell-ak i la ttnadiɣ.' Nemyuṭṭɣef s umÆebber, sseɣliɣ-t tlata n tikkal s teḥraymit xas akken yugar-iyi tazmert. Yal tikkelt ttarraɣ-as taqerraṭ ur yettfaq ara amek i d-yufa iman-is yeɣli. Mi iwala iman-is ɣelbeɣ-t amÆebber, yeddem-d azal n Æecra n tewriqin n yidrimen n 50 idinaren yerra-tent ɣer lǧib, yenna-yi-d: 'Awi-d rḍel-iyi meyya u xemsin alef a Meẓyan!' Nekk fehmeɣ-t mi t-ɣelbeɣ ddreÆ, yuɣal-iyi ɣer teḥraymit, nniɣ-as: 'Ur sÆiɣ ara. sÆiɣ ala xemsalaf.' Yenna-yi-d: 'Awi-d rḍel-iyi-tent!' Nniɣ-as: 'D kečč ara yi-d-ireḍlen, tesÆiḍ aṭas n yidrimen.' Yenna-yi-d: 'Welleh ma sÆiɣ frank.' Nniɣ-as: 'Ih, ala tiwriqin!' Yeddem-d taxriṭ-is, waleɣ teččur d tiwriqin n xemsalaf, nniɣ-as: 'Tura ad iyi-d-treḍleḍ meyya u xemsin alef.' Yeddem-d tlata n tewriqin, yefka-iyi-tent-id, ṭṭfeɣ-tent-id. Waleɣ ttint-d d tiwriqin n lkaɣeḍ azuran, d tizewwaɣin, ččurent s tira. Nniɣ-as: 'D acu-tent tewriqin-agi i iyi-d-tefkiḍ?' Waleɣ-t yeffeɣ di tewwurt. Taxxamt-nni teččur-d d ikersiyen. Waleɣ yiwen n ukersi Ælay ɣef wid-nni-nniḍen. AÆessas-nni la ijemmeÆ ikersiyen-nni
yettarra-ten wa ɣef wa. Nekk uzzleɣ ɣer ukersi-nni aÆlayan qqimeɣ deg-s, nniɣ-as i uÆessas-nni: ‚Ɣur-k ad tekkseḍ afutay-agi iɣef qqimeɣ, anef-iyi ad staÆfuɣ.‛.

Yenna-yi-d: ‚afutay-nni d ayla-k. alamma teǧǧiḍ-t-id ara t-kkseɣ.‛

Ufiɣ-d iman-iw beddeɣ deg ufrag-nni n lḥebs; afrag-nni izyeb d akessar am yifri. LaÆǧeb-nni ibedd-d zdat-i. yiɣ qqareɣ-as ad iyi-d-yini d acu-tent tewriqin-nni iyi-d-yefka, yugi ad iyi-d-yini. Nuɣal la nettemseččaw. Lɣaci zzin-aɣ-d la ttferriǧen ɣer-neɣ. Uzzlen-d sin d iÆsekriyen, mi ten-nwala, neḥbes amseččew. Mi d-leḥqen ɣer-neɣ, waleɣ yiwen deg-sen yesÆa itri n wureɣ ɣef tayet-is. Itri-nni d imdewwer am tqeffalt, yettwanqer am tẓayert n tṣeffayt.

Yiwen n umeḥbus iruḥ ɣer winna yesÆan itri, icetka-yas ɣef uÆsekri-nni-nniḍen. Sliɣ yenna-yas: ‚AÆsekri-agi iḍleb-iyi-d tajÆalt, mi ur as-tt-fkiɣ ara yuɣal yedda-tt-id fell-i ad yi-ixeddem akerfi.‛. AÆsekri-nni yenna-yas: ‚Imeḥbas akk ḍelbeɣ-asen tijÆal fkan-iyi-tent-id mačči ala kečč.‛.

Ameḥbus-nni yenna-yas: ‚D lmuḥal. Fell-i kan i tt-id-teddiḍ.‛

Waleɣ lÆesker nneɣlen-d ɣef yimeḥbas-nni la ten-id-ttḥerriren d akessar. Mi leḥqen ameḥbus, ad t-deggren ɣer yifri-nni ad yegrireb, mi waleɣ akken, rewleɣ rriɣ d akessar s ugrireb; tebÆen-iyi-d kra n yimeḥbas. Neskerker iman-nneɣ armi newweḍ ddaw yifri, nufa tamdint d tamejṭuḥt. Abrid n lḥebs yella di tlemmast n temdint-nni. Tamdint-nni tennaÆzal d ifragen. Yal afrag llant deg-s texxamin di rrif n ubrid-nni n lḥebs. Nedda-tt s tazzla deg
ubrid-nni armi qrib ad naweḍ ɣer tewwurt yessuffuɣen seg lḥebs. Imeḥbas-nni kemmlen ɣer zdat, nekk ḥebseɣ. Beddeɣ la smmuquleɣ imeḥbas-nni. Waleɣ-ten ffɣen di tewwurt yessufuɣen seg lḥebs, meÆna ttwaliɣ deg-sen la tezzin tennḍen zdat n tewwurt-nni armi uzzlen ɣer-sen yiÆessasen, ḥerren-ten-id s afrag n lḥebs, medlen tawwurt fell-asen. Imeḥbas-nni teddun ad uɣalen ɣer yimukan-nsen di lḥebs. Nekk maḍleɣ armi Æeddan akk yimeḥbas-nni, ruḥeɣ ad uɣaleɣ s amkan-iw. Lḥiɣ armi leḥqeɣ ɣer temdint-nni n lḥebs. Mi leḥḥuɣ gar texxamin-nni, ttwaliɣ tilawin d warrac la d-ttsiggin seg zdaxel n texxamin, selleɣ-asen qqaren: 'D Meẓyan u Muḥ ay akken i d-wwin ɣer lḥebs!'. Nekk rriɣ kan abrid gar wallen-iw, leḥḥuɣ qbala ɣer lḥebs. Mi Æeddeɣ i temdint-nni, leḥqeɣ ɣer sin n yiberdan: yiwen d winna yellan qbala ɣer lḥebs, wayeḍ d abrid arqiqan s lqis n lḥafer isuÆef d asawen. Iberdan-nni ɣer zdat-sen yegzem-iten-id yiɣzer. Abrid-nni n lḥebs tella-yas tqenṭert temÆidel ɣef yiɣzer-nni. Winna-nniḍen ur yesÆi ara tiqenṭert. Beddeɣ, xemmeɣ, nniɣ-d: 'Ad aɣeɣ abrid-agi arqiqan lemmer ad selkeɣ seg lḥebs.' Ddiɣ d ubrid-nni yerran d asawen; leḥqeɣ ɣer yiɣzer-nni, surfeɣ seg wanda yeḍyeq. Mi zegreɣ i yiɣzer-nni, beddeɣ, mmuqleɣ ɣer zdat, waleɣ ulac abrid. Abrid-nni yenneqḍaÆ-d s zzrubat n yileẓwi Ælayit ur ttwalḥaqen ara s tmuɣli ɣer tegnawt. Mi waleɣ akken ulac amneÆ, zziɣ-d ɣer deffir, uɣaleɣ-d armi d lefraq-nni n sin yiberdan, uɣeɣ abrid-nni yettawin ɣer lḥebs. Lḥiɣ armi zegreɣ di tqenṭert-nni, ufiɣ-d yid-i snat n telmeẓyin rrant-iyi gar-asent: yiwet
isem-is Wardiya n Ssɛid, tayeḍ Wardiya n Muḥ. Mi mlileɣ yid-sent, fehmeɣ-d d irgazen-nsent i yellan di lḥebs-nni. Beddeɣ ɣer-sent, neṭqeɣ, nniɣ-d: ‚Üaha ya Rebbi, at Lbir kfan ɣer lḥebs.‛. Werdiya n SsaÆid tenna-yi-d: ‚Yak ur tesÆiḍ i ken-ixuṣṣen a gma Æzizen?‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Aql-aɣ nerɣa la nettemyečča gar-aneɣ.‛. Mmuqleɣ ɣer zdat waleɣ yelḥa-d yiwen n urgaz yeqqen tacacit tazewwaɣt; mi d-yelḥeq ɣer-i, Æeqleɣ-t d yiwen n ccix wuɣur bdiɣ leqraya di temÆemmert. Ccix-nni, ssawalen-as ‘Ccix Sliman’. Nemsalam sslam n tujjma. Ar dqal isuɣ-d fell-i, yenna-yi-d: ‚Anida i teddiḍ akka? Seg ṣbaḥ i la ttnadiɣ fell-ak kečč ur d-teprizantiḍ ara.‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚D tilawin-agi i d-mlileɣ, ṭṭfent-iyi s wawal, ma ur iyi-t umineḍ ara steqsi-tent ad ak-d-inint.‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚Yah! D tilawin-agi i ukked temlileḍ!‛. Yerra afus-is ɣer deffir, yewwet-iyi-d s ubeqqa waleɣ ijujaḥ n tmes myeḥwaṣen gar wallen-iw. Yenna-yi-d: ‚Lufan mačči s nnif n Rebbi ad tettuÆaqbeḍ.‛ Yezzwer tilawin-nni zdat-is, yenher-itent; nekk la t-tabaÆeɣ. Nelḥa armi d anida yella ubrid-nniḍen yerra d asawen. Waleɣ argaz-nni yedda s tilawin-nni deg ubrid-nni, yerra qbala ɣer lḥebs. Mi leḥqeɣ gar sin-nni n yiberdan, beddeɣ stebÆeɣ tamuɣli i tlawin-nni. Waleɣ-tent daxel n lbiru n lḥebs, ccix-nni yeqqim ɣer ṭṭabla la asent-ixeddem lekwaɣeḍ ilaqen akken ad kecment ɣer lḥebs. Mi waleɣ akken, ruḥeɣ ad rnuɣ ɣer-sent ula d nekk. Mi greɣ asurif amezwaru, ufiɣ-d zdat-i aÆsekri-nni yesÆan itri n wureɣ, yeḥbes-iyi-d, yenna-yi-d: ‚S aniɣer kečč?‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Ad kecmeɣ ɣer lḥebs, nekk d ameḥbus.‛. Yenna-yi-d:
‚Ad taɣeḍ abrid-agi yerran d asawen. Kečč telliḍ di lḥebs n yiseɣ.‛. Zziɣ-d s abrid-nni yerran d asawen. Lḥiɣ armi leḥqeɣ s anida waleɣ yiwen n uxxam d aÆlayan. Ddaw uxxam-nni llan yixeddamen la bennun tixxamin am tqubtin. Ttwaliɣ akken kan i bdan, ssilin-d lebni ɣef wakal. Mi leḥqeɣ ɣer yixeddamen-nni, ufiɣ winna i la ibennun ssneɣ-t: d yiwen n umeɣbun d aẓawali ula di lefhama, isem-is ‘AÆli n Ḥmed u umer’. Rriɣ fell-asen sslam, neṭqeɣ s ameɣbun-nni s taÆrabt, nniɣ-as: ‚A Æemmi AÆli, win ṭrig lḥebs yerḥem waldi-k.‛. Waleɣ-t yebra i tmuɣli-s ɣer tmurt, yessusem.

Kemmleɣ abrid ɣer zdat, mi qrib ad awḍeɣ ɣer tewwurt n uxxam-nni aÆlayan, fehmeɣ axxam-nni ad yili d axxam n ccraÆ. Leḥqent-d ɣer-i snat n tlawin: yiwet deg-sent tefka-iyi-d tawriqt tettwaru s tira tizeggaɣin; tira-nni ttwaxerbent, asekkil yekcem deg wayeḍ. Tameṭṭut-nni tenna-yi-d: ‚Wali kan a gma d acu yuran dagi!‛. Ṭṭfeɣ-d tawriqt-nni, nniɣ-as: ‚Nekk a weltma aql-i dagi d ameḥbus; ur ḥṣiɣ ara d acu yuran neɣ d acu ara m-id-iniɣ?‛. Waleɣ tilawin-nni kecment di tewwurt n uxxam-nni. Nekk leḥqeɣ zdat umnar n tewwurt-nni, beddeɣ, mmuqleɣ ɣer deffir. Ṭṭṭfeɣ tawriqt-nni deg ufus-iw, wehheɣ yes-s s ameɣbun-nni, neṭqeɣ nniɣ-as: ‚Win ṭrig lḥebs yerḥem waldi-k‛

Ukiɣ-d si targit !

1981

- 103 -
Deg waṭas yid-neɣ Beddeɣ di tqiwect n yiwen n udrar. Iɣil n udrar-nni iban-iyi-d d abrid yellan qbala ur yettwalḥaq ara ula s tmuɣli n wallen. Ɣer zdat yestiwen armi yuli ɣer tegnawt. Fehmeɣ-d ma ddiɣ deg ubrid-nni s luqran, zemmreɣ ad awḍeɣ s waffug ɣer lesrar n tegnawt. Bdiɣ leqraya di tṣurtin ufiɣ-d iman-iw la ttafgeɣ. Ddiɣ s lewhi n ubrid-nni armi d anida i ufiɣ yiwen n umɣar ibedd di rrif n ubrid-nni. Mi Æeddeɣ tama n umɣar-nni, sliɣ yenna-yi-d: ‚Atan tura a Meẓyan ad tesseɣreḍ!‛. Ufiɣ-d ṭṭfeɣ imru deg ufus-iw. Leḥqeɣ s leqraya n tṣurtin la d-qqareɣ taṣuret ‘Ɣɣer s yisem n Rebbi-inek’. La tedduɣ ɣer zdat s waffug armi i d-ufiɣ iman-iw kecmeɣ leɣmuq n tegnawt. Mmuqleɣ-d d akessar ur d-waleɣ ara tamurt. Imir ḥulfeɣ yeɣli-d fell-i lweḥc. Medleɣ allen-iw, nniɣ-d deg wul-iw: ‚Mi leḥqeɣ s anida i ḥebseɣ, ad lddiɣ allen-iw, ay urǧin waleɣ ad t-waliɣ, ama d lǧennet neɣ d lmalayek; ay ayen yeḍran yid-i Æemdeɣ-t: d lxelÆa neɣ d tislbi !‛ Kemmleɣ s wafug ɣer zdat armi d anida i ḥulfeɣ ḥebseɣ, mi d-lddiɣ allen-iw, ufiɣ-d iman-iw beddeɣ deg umkan-nni ansi ruḥeɣ. Uɣaleɣ bɣiɣ ad afgeɣ tikkelt-nniḍen gar yigenni d tmurt. Ɣriɣ-d yiwet n tṣuret armi tfuk. Neṭqeɣ nniɣ-d: ‚S yes-k a Rebbi.‛. Mi nleqmeɣ s wafug, ur sḍuleɣ ara maḍi ɣliɣ-d ɣer tmurt. erḍeɣ aṭas n tikkal akken ad afgeɣ meÆna tikkelt ad d-ɣliɣ ɣer tmurt; tikkelt mi waleɣ ttejra Ælayet ad ruḥeɣ ad as-ḍilleɣ s wafug, mi leḥqeɣ ɣer-s
ad d-afeɣ weḥleɣ deg udwaxli-s. D afug, d aɣellluy armi i d-ufiɣ iman-iw uɣaleɣ s amkan-nni ideg beddeɣ di tazwara. Mi greɣ tamuɣli-w s amesḍilli n udrar-nni, iban-iyi-d yiwen n uÆerqub n uzemmur. Di tlemmast-is yella ubrid d arqiqan, izyeb d akessar, yessawaḍ ɣer yiwen n yiɣzer. Waleɣ tlata n telmeẓyin la leḥḥunt ta zdat ta deg ubrid-nni arqiqan. Tilmeẓyin-nni yetbeÆ-itent yiwen i ssneɣ d aÆeccaq, isem-is ‘Lḥusin n li’. Nniɣ-d s yes-k a Rebbi, nleqmeɣ s wafug, rseɣ-d zdat n urgaz-nni.

Nniɣ-d deg wul-iw: ‚ilaq ad d-ḥerreɣ tilmeẓyin-inna, ad waliɣ d acu n zzin i iselben uḍfir-agi‛. Nniɣ-d s yes-k a Rebbi, nleqmeɣ s wafug, rseɣ-d zdat n tinna i d-yellan deffir-sent. Mmuqleɣ-tt, waleɣ mellulet, sser ur tesÆi ara, rniɣ ḥerreɣ-d talemmast-nni, waleɣ-tt mellulet terna mesruret; ma d tis tlata-nni mi mmuqleɣ deg-s, wehmeɣ!

D acu i d ccbaḥa, d acu i d sser-nni neɣ lqedd, iḍbeÆ-itt Rebbi mačči d kra ara d-yesban yiles. Ufiɣ-d qqurent wallen-iw deg-s, ma yeffeɣ seg-i laÆqel a wer d-yuɣal. LuÆeɣ-tt ur iyi-d-terri ara ula s tmuɣli, zziɣ iman-iw fell-as. Mmuqleɣ ɣer zdat, waleɣ agemmaḍ n yiɣzer-nni yella ubrid yerra d asawen yessawaḍ ɣer yiɣil n udrar-nni seg i d-udreɣ.

Nniɣ-d s yes-k a Rebbi akken ad zegreɣ i yiɣzer-nni s wafug. Ufiɣ-d ur zmireɣ ara ad afgeɣ. Lḥiɣ armi zegreɣ i yiɣzer-nni. Kemmleɣ tikli deg ubrid-nni yerran d asawen armi leḥqeɣ ɣef yiɣil n udrar-nni. Ufiɣ-d zdat-i tarbaÆt n yirgazen, ddiɣ yid-sen. La nleḥḥu nettnecraḥ, ar dqal iban-iyi-d yiwen gar-asen d win i ssneɣ isem-is ‘AÆli n Ḥmed u Sliman’. argaz-nni yezzi-d ɣer-i yenna-yi-d:
‚Urgeɣ-k a Meẓyan.‛. Fehmeɣ-t ur yebɣi ara ad iyi-d- yeḥku d acu i yurga fell-i. nniɣ-as: ‚Kemmel targit-ik a Dda AÆli.‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚mmuqel ɣer zdat.‛. Mi mmuqleɣ, waleɣ nelḥeq ad nekcem deg usqif n lǧamaÆ. LǧameÆ-nni yettwabna am tgennarit, yiwet n tewwurt tessekcam tayeḍ tessuffuɣ. Nekcem d tarbaÆt di tewwurt n usqif-nni. Zziɣ-d s tmuɣli-w ɣer deffir, waleɣ tarbaÆt n yirgazen la d-leḥḥun deffir-nneɣ; mi d-leḥqen s asqif-nni, xulfen abrid si tama n ufella n lǧamaÆ-nni. Imexlaq-nni fehmeɣ-ten seg wid yellan di ṣṣeḥra n ‘Lkengu’. Maca ur seṭṭafit ara, ttbanen-d d ixemriyen! Neṭqeɣ, nniɣ-d: ‚Attan terbaÆt n yiÆdawen-nneɣ a Dda AÆli, meÆna ur aɣ-d-walan ara, haten rran kan abrid gar wallen-nsen am yilfan neɣ ahat qesden ad aɣ-d-sqiṭṭɛen ɣer zdat yerna aql-aɣ drus yid-neɣ.‛ Dda AÆli yenna-yi-d: ‚Urgeɣ-k a Meẓyan tenniḍ-d s yes-k a Rebbi ad tɣerrbeɣ.‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Maca ḥku-yi-d d acu i turgaḍ fell-i a Æemmi AÆli. ‚Isuɣ-d fell-i yenna-yi-d: ‚Fiḥel ma ḥkiɣ-ak-d.‛. Ufiɣ-d neffeɣ si tewwurt-nni-nniḍen. Zdat tewwurt-nni, d amraḥ. Deg umraḥ-nni nufa tarbaÆt n yirgazen, tayeḍ n tilawin la ttraǧun deg-neɣ. Wid-nni Æeqleɣ-ten d atmaten-nneɣ izzayriyen. Neṭqeɣ ɣer terbaÆt-nni deg i lliɣ, nniɣ-asen: ‚Atan tuggadem kan tarbaÆt-nni n yiÆdawen-nneɣ, ur d-walan ula d yiwen deg-neɣ, yerna atni i d-nufa d atmaten-nneɣ dagi? Ziɣ nella deg waṭas yid-neɣ, kunwi tuggadem.‛. Zziɣ ɣer wid-nni-nniḍen, waleɣ-ten ferḥen yes-neɣ mačči d kra! Nekk daɣen ferḥeɣ yes-sen, tḥenceɣ yes-sen u ttekleɣ fell-asen. Neṭqeɣ ɣer-sen, nniɣ-asen: ‚Amek i tellam ay atmaten-
iw?‛. Neṭqen-d s yiwen n yimi nnan-d: Zik netweḥḥec, tura netḥennec.‛

# Ukiɣ-d si targit !

1981

Lweqt aberkan Lliɣ deg yiwet n tḥanut di taddart yettusemman ‘Taxribt’, neqqim ɣer ṭṭabla di rebÆa yid-neɣ la nleÆÆeb lkarta. Win i la aɣ-d-ijerrayen isem-is ‘AÆli n Ḥmed’, iqubel-d yiwen isem-is ‘AÆli u Muḥ’. Nekk mqabaleɣ d yiwen isem-is ‘AÆli n SaÆid’. Nessuter bab n tḥanut-nni ad aɣ-d-yawi leqhawi. Nekk bɣiɣ ad xellṣeɣ melba ma ttwaɣelbeɣ s lleÆb; rriɣ afus-iw ɣer lǧib ad d-ddmeɣ idrimen, AÆli n Ḥmed yenna-yi-d: ‚Welleh ma txellṣeḍ a Meẓyan.‛. Kkseɣ-d afus-iw si lǧib, waleɣ aqehwaǧi-nni yewwi-aɣ-d snat n teqraÆtin timeqqranin n lgazuz n ččina yerna-d rebÆa n lkisan. Yelḥeq-d yessers ayen akken i d-yewwi ɣer ṭṭabla. AÆli n Ḥmed yeddem-d taqerÆet n lgazuz, yezzi iman-is fell-nneɣ netta d umeddakkel-is. Ameddakkel-iw yeddem-d taqerÆet-nni tis snat akken ad tt-nsew nekk yid-s. Isureg-d ɣer lkas-iw armi i t-id-yezgen, yekkes taqerÆet-nni akken ad yessureg ɣer lkas-is.
Refdeɣ lkas-iw wehhaɣ-as-t, nniɣ-as: ‚Ur ssurug ara ɣer lkas-ik alamma teččureḍ-iyi-d lkas-iw.‛ Yerra-d taqerÆet-nni, yerna isureg-d tajɣimt, yeḥbes. Nniɣ-as: ‚Rnu-d i ak-nniɣ alamma yeččur lkas-iw.‛ Yerra-d taqerÆet-nni, isureg-d armi yeččur lkas-nni-inu.

Ufiɣ-d beddeɣ akked yiwen n urgaz zdat tewwurt n tḥanut-nni la as-ḥekkuɣ targit. Nniɣ-as: ‚Wali kan ɣer targit i urgeɣ! Urgeɣ la leÆbeɣ rrunda akked tlata n lÆibad, ismawen-nsen: AÆli, AÆli, AÆli. Yerna d AÆli-nni i urgeɣ nniɣ-as win ṭrig lḥebs, i ixelṣen ayen i neswa; ma yi-d-yessurug ɣer lkas-iw yugi ad t-id-yeččar. Axaṭer yesla ɣer wid-nni yettamnen s tḥeckulin mi qqaren diri ma teččureḍ lkas i ḥedd; ad as-teččar ad yemmet. Netta la yessurug, nekk la as-qqareɣ ččar-it-id.

AÆli n Muḥ yeffeɣ-d si tḥanut, yuli ɣer tkerrust-is. Nekk qesdeɣ ad ruḥeɣ ɣef uḍar. Yella yiwen yid-i isem-is ‘Remḍan’. Sliɣ yessiwel-iyi-d AÆli n Muḥ, yenna-yi-d: ‚Ma ad ak-awiɣ ɣer Tizi Wezzu a Meẓyan. Maca ad awiɣ sin kan.‛ Nniɣ-as i Remḍan: ‚Yya-n ad ɣ-yawi AÆli u Muḥ.‛

Waleɣ yiwen izwir-aneɣ ɣer tkerrust-nni. Sliɣ i bab n tkerrust-nni yenna-d: ‚Ihi dayen a Meẓyan, mrafaq-d kan akked Remḍan.‛ Nniɣ-as: ‚Ula d nekk fiḥel ma tewwiḍ-iyi, axaṭer d tabrat i gemneɣ ad tt-id-awiɣ si Tizi Wezzu. Attan telḥeq-d.‛ Ufiɣ-d ṭṭfeɣ tabrat gar yifassen-iw, neṭqeɣ ɣer Remḍan, nniɣ-as: ‚yalleh ad nettkel ɣef Rebbi a Remḍan.‛

Ufiɣ-d iman-iw lliɣ di lqahwa n taddart-iw, sliɣ i bab n lqahwa-nni yenna-yi-d: ‚LÆeslama-k a Meẓyan! Aṭas uya
ur d-tbaneḍ  ara!‛   Nniɣ-as: ‚Mačči ur bɣiɣ ara  ad       d-kecmeɣ  ɣer lqahwa-agi  meÆna  kečč  tessewwayeḍ          kan llatay akked lqahwa. Nekk teḥṣiḍ uḍneɣ, lemmer d ayefki i tessewayeḍ  tilli  kullas ad ttiliɣ dagi!.‛.    Yenna-yi-d: ‚Ayefki llah ɣaleb!‛.Yessureg-iyi-d lkas n llatay, ṭṭfeɣ-t-id s leḥya. Waleɣ-t la  yessewway    ayefki. Ḥetmeɣ  kra       n tejɣimin si llatay-nni, serseɣ lkas-nni ɣef ṭṭabla la ttraǧuɣ deg uyefki-nni. Mi d-yewwa uyefki-nni, aqehwaǧi yerfed abeqraǧ-nni n uyefki yessers-it zdat n yiwen yeqqimen weḥd-s ɣer        ṭṭabla yerna-as lkas d ameqqran. Lkas-nni d urqim. Sliɣ yenna-yas: ‚atan swejdeɣ-ak-d ayen i tḍelbeḍ, ssureg i yiman-ik, sew ayen i ak-yehwan yerna durru ur tt-ttawiɣ ara fell-ak.‛.

Mmuqleɣ di lxelq-nni yettwaÆuzzen nnig lÆezz, waleɣ di ṣṣifa-s, ur yessaweḍ   ara d rrbeÆ n urgaz: d ucmit di ṣṣifa, d uÆwij<netta la itess ayefki s ttnefxa. Nekk fehmeɣ-t yebɣa ad yettihi fell-i ukud wid-nni akk i la itessen llatay. Neṭqeɣ ɣer lɣaci-nni s lmeÆna, nniɣ-asen: ‚Lemmer iferrez uyefki, ad yeqbel    ad t-yessew  uberkan?‛       Nnan-iyi-d: ‚Yessesw-as-t lweqt.‛. Mmɣeɣ      ɣer lǧib-iw,        ddmeɣ-d tmenya n durru i yellan d lqima n lkas n llatay, nniɣ-as i uqehwaǧi-nni:  ‚Ax   a laÆǧeb ad  k-id-xelṣeɣ      llatay-agi swiɣ.‛. Yemmuqel idrimen-nni, yenna-yi-d: ‚Ayɣer siwa anect-agi? Teswa tnac n durru.‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Tnac n durru i teswa ay axeddaÆ! La tettfaraseḍ          deg watmaten-ik, ur tettsetḥiḍ seg lÆebd ur tettugadeḍ     Rebbi a lkafer.‛ Yerfa uqehwaǧi-nni, waleɣ-t yembeddal wudem-is, iwexxer ɣer deffir, yerfed-d aÆekkaz d aɣezzfan la yi-d-yekkat yes-s.
nekk refdeɣ-d akersi la t-ssendayeɣ i tyitwin-nni. Mi yi-d-yewwet, ad d-tazgi tyita-s deg ukersi-nni. Ɣer taggara gubreɣ-t, ṭṭfeɣ-as aÆekkaz-nni seg yixef-is, kkseɣ-as-t-id. Yemmeɣ ɣef lkas, yewwet -iyi-d yes-s s anyir. Ḥulfeɣ ifeččex unyir-iw. Refdeɣ ɣer-s aÆekkaz-nni; aqehwaǧi yeffeɣ di tewwurt. ḍefreɣ-t, leḥqeɣ-t ɣer yiwet n teɣmert n lḥiḍ, ɣer zdat d zzerb, refdeɣ aÆekkaz-nni, iban-iyi-d lemri d ameqqran s lqis n tiddi-w. Waleɣ iman-iw di lemri ulac ula d axebbic deg unyir-iw, amzun ur ttuwteɣ ara. Neṭqeɣ s aqehwaǧi-nni, nniɣ-as: ‚Ad ak-anfeɣ ɣef nnif n Rebbi.‛ Wexreɣ-d fell-as, netta mazal-it la yettergigi si tuggdi.

Lḥiɣ kra n yisurrifen, yekcem -iyi ccek, nniɣ-d deg wul-iw: ‚Wagi d aÆdaw n Rebbi, ad iyi-d-yetbeÆ deffir, ad iyi-d-yewwet s lexdaÆ. Neɣ netta ttnaÆaren fell-as watmaten-is, ad iyi-ten-id-yesgini, ad iyi-nɣen. Amek ara xedmeɣ tura?! Ilaq ad ggaǧeɣ ɣer taddart Iẓarruden, din kan ara afeɣ lemneÆ. Lɣaci n taddart-nneɣ ur keccmen ara taddart-nni axaṭer myekrahen akked lɣaci-ines<saḥḥa a zzman aberkan yenneqḍaÆ-iyi ubrid di taddart-iw.‛

Ddiɣ d ubrid s trewla. La leḥḥuɣ s tuggdi, ḥareɣ ma ɣer deffir ara mmuqleɣ, ma yella win i yi-d-iḍefren neɣ ad mmuqleɣ ɣer zdat ad waliɣ ansi ara Æeddiɣ akken ur ɣelliɣ ara neɣ ad Æasseɣ ɣef yiberdiyen-iw ur ttwadaÆeɣ ara.

Yiwet n tikkelt mi mmuqleɣ ɣer zdat, ḥulfeɣ yekka-iyi-d ḥedd si deffir iger-iyi-d timetɣaltin yeṭṭef-iyi. Mi d-zziɣ, mmuqleɣ ɣer deffir, waleɣ d aqehwaǧi-nni. Imir teɣli-d fell-i tuggdi, neṭṭqeɣ nniɣ-as: ‚Yak ur k-id-wwtiɣ ara gar lɣaci!‛. Mi iyi-iserreḥ, heggeɣ iman-iw; tuggdi-nni tuɣal-
iyi d tirrugza. Neṭqeɣ ɣer umcum-nni s wurfan, nniɣ-as: ‘Lufan mačči gar lɣaci!’ Yeḍsa-d ɣer-i, yemmeɣ-d fell-i yeḥmeẓ-iyi ɣer yidmaren s leḥmala; iserreḥ-iyi. Kemmleɣ abrid-iw ɣer zdat s tazzla armi i d-ufiɣ ttwafeččxeɣ deg wudem-iw d uqerruy-iw ur ḥṣiɣ anwa i yi-d-iwwten neɣ amkan deg i ttuwteɣ. Lḥiɣ akken d amejruḥ armi kecmeɣ akal yemcaraken gar Iẓarruden d taddart n Yibehlal.

Waleɣ ɣer zdat tlata n yilmeẓyen qqimen di rrif n ubrid la tessen ccrab. Ilmeẓyen-nni lliɣ mḥababeɣ yid-sen, nuɣal nemsebḍa mebla ssebba. Sin deg-sen n taddart n Yibehlal, wis tlata n taddart n Yiẓarruden. Mi ten-waleɣ, ufiɣ-d ttwakksen-iyi leǧruḥ-nni. Yefreḥ wul-iw twenseɣ s yiḥbiben-iw. Mi leḥqeɣ ɣer-sen, nniɣ-asen: ‘Rebbi ad ken-iÆin.’ Nnan-iyi-d: ‘Amin a Rebbi, lÆeslama a Meẓyan.’

Sliɣ i yiwen deg-sen yenna-yi-d: ‘Ansi akka i d-yeskker Meẓyan, atan rwint wallen-is!’ Nniɣ-as: ‘Aql-i deg yimi n tlafsa, amek ur sekkreɣ ara; sekkreɣ yerna ad rnuɣ tissit n ccrab!’

Sɣimeɣ iman-iw yid-sen, imir uifiɣ-d iman-iw weḥd-i! mmuqleɣ ɣer deffir, waleɣ sin n yirgazen la d-ssetbaÆen lǧarrat-iw. Yiwen deg-sen Æeqleɣ-t n taddart-iw, isem-is ‘Muḥ u Ḥmed’, iÆelleq abeckiḍ n ssyada ɣef tayet-is. Mi ten-waleɣ, nniɣ-d: ‘Anwa ara yi-iḥudden?’ Uqbel ad nleqmeɣ ɣer trewla leḥqen-d am terṣaṣin, Æeddan ur yi-d-walan ara.

Mi faten fell-i s kra n yisurrifen, bedden uɣalen mačči d nutni! Yiwen waleɣ-t yeqqen tamangiṭ ɣef uqerruy-is la ileḥḥu d aneggaru; wayeḍ-nni izwar, iban-iyi-d d ameslub, la yettmeslay d ubrid ula s yifassen-is.
Lḥan ɣer zdat, uɣalen bedden zzin-d iman-nsen la yi-d-smuqulen. Lḥiɣ ɣer-sen, mi leḥqeɣ, mrafaqeɣ yid-sen. Ur iyi-d-steqsan, ur asen-nniɣ. Nelḥa kra n yisurrifen ɣer zdat, newweḍ ɣer yiwet n tmeqbert, nbedd. Ameslub-nni yuɣal iban-iyi-d d aÆeqli ma d bu tkaskiṭ-nni waleɣ-t la yessewÆad s yifassen-is, yesker awal, la yettmeslay di rrayeÆ. Nniɣ-d deg wul-iw: ‚Ziɣ d bu tmangiṭ-agi i d ameslub! Nekk ɣileɣ d wagi yellan s laÆqel-is.‘ Waleɣ ameslub-nni yekref afud gar snat n tneṭlin iwehha iman-is ɣer yiwet n taddart yellan agemmaḍ n taddart n Yiẓarruden. Taddart-nni tettwasemma ‘taddart n at AÆrif’. La yesmmuqul ɣer yiwen n udrum yettusemman ‘Iberkanen’, la yettsuɣu, yeqqar: ‚Iberkanen, iberkanen, iberkanen, iqebqaben.‘

Ukiɣ-d si targit !

1981

Mačči d lawan

Lliɣ di temdint n Lezzayer. Ufiɣ-d iman-iw akked waṭas n lɣaci nerkeb di tkerrust tameqqrant (SNTV) neqsed ad nruḥ ɣer temdint n Wehran. Mi teqleÆ yes-neɣ tkerrust-nni, tedda s leÆqel armi teffeɣ i temdint, tuɣal
teɣseb. Mi teɣseb, temlil-d d yiwen n ukamyun d ameqqran, yeṭṭef-d talemmast n ubrid. Tuɣal tkerrust-nni tedda s leÆqel. Mi qrib ad taweḍ s akamyun, teḥbes dindin. Akamyun-nni isuÆef, takerrust-nni tkemmel abrid s leɣseb. Tḥella-d yiwen n uxnaq, temlil-d d tlata n tkerrusin timejṭaḥ ṭṭfent-d talemmast n ubrid. Takerrust-nni ideg nedda tedda s ttawil tuɣal teḥbes. Tikerrusin-nni suÆfent-as Æeddant. Tkemmel yes-neɣ axunaq-nniḍen s leɣseb. Mi telḥeq ɣer yiwet n ddura, teffeɣ i lgudru, mi tḍil di ddura-nni, aqerru n tkerrust-nni iwehha ɣer yifri. Ddaw n yifri-nni d asif. Teḥbes ur tḍil ara ɣer yifri-nni. Yuɣal unehhar-is la tt-id-yeddewwir akken ad tt-id-yerr s abrid. Yusa-d yiwen n ukamyun, mi d-yelḥeq ɣer tkerrust-nni yeḥbes, iḥres-itt ur tt-yeǧǧi ara akken ad d-tuɣal s abrid. MeÆna anehhar-nni yemqellaÆ armi i tt-id-yeslek si ṭṭiq-nni. Yerra-d takerrust s abrid, ikemmel ɣer zdat yes-neɣ. Iḥella-d axunaq wis tlata ɣer deffir. Waleɣ takerrust-nni tmal ɣer yiwen n yidis qrib ad tetti, neṭqeɣ ɣer lɣaci-nni, nniɣ-asen: ‚ asset iman-nwen! Hattan truḥ ad tenneqlab.‛

Akken waleɣ ad tenneqlab negzeɣ-d, uzgeɣ-d mebÆid beddeɣ. Waleɣ takerrust-nni tetti s rrakbin-nni yellan daxel-is; uɣalent rrwadi d asawen. TÆiwed tuttya, tuɣal ɣef rrwad-is. Mi waleɣ akken, xelÆeɣ, nniɣ-d deg wul-iw: ‚s kra din ttwafaÆjen.‛ Uzzleɣ, ufiɣ yiwen isem-is Sliman d amezdaɣ di taddart-iw, ibedd di tama ufella n ubrid, neṭqeɣ ɣer-s, nniɣ-as: ‚Ahat skra din nnefÆajen!‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚Ala, yiwen n utunsi i -yemmuten. Tnedheḍ s Rebbi
tenneqlab, yiwen di lɣaci-nni mačči yemmut neɣ yettwajreḥ ala atunsi-nni i yemmuten! Qerrbeɣ ɣer tkerrust-nni, siggeɣ ɣer daxel-is si tewwurt, waleɣ ulac win ur nettwaḥuza ara di rrakbin-nni, ɣlin merra; gar-asen wid yettwajerḥen deg uqerruy. Ttwaliɣ yexleḍ walleɣ d yidammen. Bɣiɣ ad ten-id-refdeɣ s yiwen yiwen ad ten-id-ssufɣeɣ s abrid, maca teɣli-d fell-i lxelÆa d tacallawt seg wayen ẓriɣ. Zziɣ ɣer Sliman, nniɣ-as: ‚Ur zmireɣ ara ad ten-id-refdeɣ, aql-i xelÆeɣ seg-sen.‘. Sliman yessusem.

Tezga-d tmuɣli-w deg yiwen n urgaz yellan s lbeÆd-iw ciṭuḥ; argaz-nni ibedd di tiɣilt, yeṭṭef tilifun. Neṭṭqeɣ ɣer-s, nniɣ-as: ‚Sixef ttilifuni, d acu i la tettraǧuḍ!‘. Waleɣ-t iwehha ttilifun akken ad yessiwel. Zziɣ-d mmuqleɣ ɣer wid-nni i tḥuza twaɣit, waleɣ takerrust-nni d tilemt! Ufiɣ-d iman-iw di temdint n Wehran. Waleɣ takerrust-nni i aɣ-yessiwḍen tdewwer akken ad d-tuɣal ɣer temdint n Lezzayer s wid-nni yeddan deg-s.

Teḥbes-d zdat-i, ulin lɣaci armi teččur; nekk qqimeɣ-d weḥd-i la ttxemmimeɣ: ad aliɣ, imukan n yiɣimi ttwaḥerren, abrid iḍul aṭas; ur ttaliɣ ara! Fehmeɣ d tinna i d taneggarut i yessawaḍen ɣer temdint n Lezzayer. Mi qrib ad teqleÆ tkerrust-nni, greɣ tamuɣli-w ɣer yiwet n tama, waleɣ yiwet n tlemẓit la d-tleḥḥu fehmeɣ-tt ɣer-i i d-teqsed, nettat tessen-iyi nekk ur tt-ssineɣ ara.

Mi d-telḥeq, teḍsa-d ɣer-i, nemsalam, aredqal nniɣ-as: « Tessneḍ-iyi u laÆmer i yi-d-turiḍ tabrat! ». Tenna-yi-d: « Akka ɣer zdat ad ak-id-ttaruɣ. ». Nniɣ-as: ‚Yerbeḥ, meÆna nekk d ameɣbun, neɣ teḥsiḍ? ». Tenna-yi-d: « Acuɣer ur tettaṭṭafeḍ ara aṭaksi? ».
as : « Ulac iṭaksiyen. ». Tenna-yi-d: « Yella yiwen yenna-yi-d rnu-d yid-m tlata ad aken-awiɣ. ». Nniɣ-as: ‚Ihi yella ula d aḍeggal-iw ad yeddu. MeÆna ssuma n uṭaksi ɣlayet i lkarya, rnu melmi ara d-yelḥeq uṭaksi-agi?‛. Waleɣ aṭaksi yeḥbes-d ɣer tama-nneɣ. Tilemẓit-nni tenna-yi-d:‚Hatan yelḥeq-d, yettawi xemseṭṭac n alef i yiwen.‛

Nekk ur tt-umineɣ ara deg wayen akk i yi-d-tenna. Uzzleɣ ɣer tkerrust-nni ‘SNTḍ’, uliɣ ɣer-s, beddeɣ di tewwurt n zdat; steqseɣ axeddam n tkerrust-nni, nniɣ-as: ‚Ad yili umkan?‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚Ali-d.‛. Nekk daɣen uggadeɣ ur ttafeɣ ara amkan s yiɣimi, uɣaleɣ ɣer bab n uṭaksi-nni, steqseɣ-t nniɣ-as: ‚Ad iyi-tawiḍ ihi?‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚Ih, ali-d.‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚i ssuma, acḥal?‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚Ttawiɣ rebÆa n lÆibad xemsemyat alef i yiwen. Mi ara nruḥ deg ubrid ixleḍ-d yiwen d tafamilt ad txellsem mitin alef i yiwen.‛.

Nniɣ-as: ‚Ini-d kan mitin alef i yiwen mebla ma tessiɣezfeḍ awal.‛. Tixreɣ fell-as; waleɣ takerrust-nni tameqqrant qrib ad teqleÆ. Uzzleɣ ɣer-s, mi leḥqeɣ, teqleÆ ad truḥ. Negzeɣ, uzgeɣ-d daxel-is beddeɣ di tewwurt n zdat. Waleɣ uzzlen-d sin n yilmeẓyen, negzen-d ɣer tkerrust-nni. Iban-iyi-d yiwen n urgaz qrib d amɣar akken kan i t-id-yebda ccib ibedd tama n unehhar. Argaz-nni imuqel-iyi-d mi asen-uɣaleɣ di rrif i yilmeẓyen-nni; Æeddan zdat-i ur yi-d-ssutren ara ula d ssmaḥ. Neṭqeɣ s argaz-nni s lmeÆna nniɣ-as: ‚Zwaren-aɣ yimessusiyen ara aɣ-yawin imukan.‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚Amkan-ik yella.‛

Iban-iyi-d yiwen n umkan zdat-i, ruḥeɣ ɣer-s. Uqbel ad sɣimeɣ iman-iw waleɣ yiwen n umɣar n taddart-iw,
amɣar-nni d aderɣal yedda s yibeddi ulac win i as-igan amkan. Uẓiɣ ɣer-s, nemsalam; ar dqal nniɣ-as: ‚Yya-n ad teqqimeḍ a Dda Ḥmed .‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚Nekk a mmi ur sɛiɣ ara amkan.‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Kečč d ameɛdur, di lḥaqiqa tesɛiḍ amkan ɣer zdat. Rwaḥ tura ad ak-fkeɣ amkan-iw neɣ ma tebɣiḍ ad ssutreɣ amkan-ik xas ad nnaɣeɣ. ».

Yenna-yi-d: ‚Ala a mmi, ula i k-yettawin! Aql-aɣ gar lberrani, uggadeɣ ad ak-zzin s waṭas, ula xas ma llan wid n taddart-nneɣ ur k-ttḥuddun ara, neɣ ad ak-id-ddun d lberrani! aql-aɣ mačči di lawan.‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Ɣur-k lḥeqq, yya-n ihi s amkan-iw ad teqqimeḍ.‛.

Yenna-yi-d: ‚Ala a mmi, amek ara yi-tmuddeḍ amkan-ik!‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Nniɣ-ak welleh ard teqqimeḍ, kečč d ameɛdur nekk zemreɣ ad beddeɣ yak d nekk i ak-yfkan amkan-iw.‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚Ulamek a mmi, d lmuḥal, ṭṭef kan amkan-ik.‛

Σyiɣ ttḥellileɣ deg-s netta issetḥa; mi t-waleɣ akken teɣleb-it leḥya, ṭṭfeɣ-t seg ufus, zzuɣreɣ-t armi i t-ssiwḍeɣ s amkan-nni, nniɣ-as : « Qqim tura ad testaɛfuḍ. ».

Yeqqim, yenna-yi-d : « Ad k-iǧazi Rebbi s lxir a mmi, a wer tenneḥcameḍ zdat Rebbi. Tgiḍ amkan i umeÆdur, ad ak-ig Rebbi amkan-ik di rreḥma-s.‛. Ǧǧiɣ-as amkan i umeɛdur-nni, nekk nudeɣ anida ara ṭṭfeɣ amkan s yibeddi.

La smuquleɣ, tban-iyi-d tkerrust-nni tesɛa tlata n tewwura: tawwurt-nni n tlemmast tettwaxdem s lmaryat; tama n tewwurt-nni iban-iyi-d yiwen n umkan d ilem ulac bab-is. Uzzleɣ s amkan-nni, nniɣ-d: ‚Welleh ar d amkan-agi ay axir, ad ttwaliɣ ɣer berra.‛. Takerrust-nni tesɛa kan
yiwen n umkan d amejṭuḥ zdat n unehhar; qqimeɣ deg umkan-nni.

Ufiɣ-d iman-iw di temdint n tɣiwant n lɛerc n MÆatqa beddeɣ di rrif n ubrid yessawaḍen ɣer taddart-iw la ttraǧuɣ ttawil n usiweḍ ɣer taddart-iw. Rǧiɣ alami ɛyiɣ, ulac win i d-iger ubrid s tkerrust. Lḥal qrib d lmeɣreb, abrid iḍul, nniɣ-d: ‚Ad ruḥeɣ ɣef uḍar rnu ad xalfeɣ abrid ɣef ubrid-agi n ukerrus xas yestugna. Axaṭer iḍul s tikli.‘.

suɛfeɣ ɣef ubrid n uḍar, greɣ asurif deg ubrid-nni ufiɣ-d iman-iw ḥelleɣ-d yiwet n taddart yettusemman at Zɛim.

Leḥqeɣ zdat taddart-nni anida yemlil ubrid-nni n uḍar d ubrid-nni n ukerrus, waleɣ yiwen s tkerrust R 4, d tamellalt; yeḥbes-d di tlemmast n ubrid; bab n tkerrust-nni isem-is Aɛmar. Yella wayeḍ ibedd ɣer tama n tkerrust-nni isem-is Ssaɛid. Waleɣ-t yeqqen nwaḍer d tiberkanin. Mi qrib ad awḍeɣ ɣer-sen, anehhar-nni yers-d si tkerrust, iruḥ yenfel i ubrid.

Fehmeɣ-t yeḥwaǧ iman-is, ma d takerrust-nni twehha akken ara truḥ ɣer tama n taddart-iw; tuɣal tdewwer, twehha iman-is ɣer tama-nni ansi i d-kkiɣ. Mi d-yuɣal bab n tkerrust-nni nniɣ-as: ‚Ma ɣer-neɣ ara truḥeḍ ad iyi-tawiḍ ad dduɣ yid-k.‘. Yenna-yi-d: ‚Rǧu, mi d-uɣaleɣ ad k-awiɣ.‘.

Lḥiɣ ɣer tkerrust-nni, mi qrib ad awḍeɣ, tuɣal ulac-itt! Nekk ufiɣ-d iman-iw ddaw ttejra yellan di rrif n ubrid-nni yella yid-i Ssaɛid akked mmi-s n ɛemmi-s isem-is Rezqi n Ssaɛid la nettraǧu win ara d-iɛeddin s tkerrust ad neddu yid-s ɣer taddart-nneɣ. Nerǧa armi neɛya deg uraǧu. Bɣiɣ ad asen-iniɣ ad nkemmel abrid ɣef uḍar. Mi waleɣ Ssaɛid yewwi-d yid-s aḍellaɛ d
ameqqran yeččur d lqeḍyan, uɣaleɣ cawreɣ-ten, nniɣ- asen: ‚Amek i tebɣam: ad nerǧut neɣ ad nruḥet ɣef uḍar?.

Ssaɛid yenna-yi-d: ‚Hatan la d-ileḥḥu yiwen n urgaz yewwi-d yid-s taqcict rnu tezyen. ».

Waleɣ argaz d tlemẓit la d-leḥḥun ɣer-neɣ. Tilemẓit-nni yettban-d sser-is si lbeɛd ! nekk fehmeɣ-tt ad tili d yelli-s n urgaz-nni neɣ d tameṭṭut-is.

Ssaɛid yenna-yi-d: ‚Yyaw ad ten-nemmagar ad d-neddut yid-sen!‛

Uqbel ad nḥerrek iman-nneɣ, imexlaq-nni wwḍen-d ɣer-neɣ, ɛeddan zdat-neɣ. lḥal iban-iyi-d ad yili d ttnaṣfa n wass, sliɣ i Rezqi yenna-yi-d: ‚Yyaw ad neddut yid-sen.‛

Nniɣ-as: ‚Haten-an faten-aɣ, ilaq ad nɛeddi seg ubrid-agi n uḍar, ad asen-nxalef abrid, ad ten-nelḥeq ɣer zdat.‛

Nekka seg ubrid-nni n uḍar yella di tama ddaw n ubrid-nni n ukerrus. Abrid-nni simmal nteddu deg-s ɣer zdat ttwaliɣ yettestiwin.

Mi qrib ad naweḍ s anida mcaraken sin-nni n yiberdan, waleɣ mcaraken-d rebɛa n yiberdan n ukerrus. Amkan-nni yewseɛ aṭas.

Di tlemmast n myugar-nni tella teẓrut meqqret, teḍbeɛ d timdewwert am uɣbalu (lbir). Sliɣ i Reẓqi yenna-yi-d: ‚Ɣer lbir-agi i d-tusa teqcict-nni tugem.‛.

Zziɣ ɣer Rezqi waleɣ ulac-it yid-neɣ, mmuqleɣ ɣer zdat, waleɣ tilemẓit-nni nemlil yid-s di myugar-nni n yiberdan.

Ssaɛid yenṭeq ɣer tlemẓit-nni, yenna-yas: ‚A lɛeslama ay aggaw!‛. Mi mmuqleɣ, waleɣ tetti-d d ilemẓi !.

Nniɣ-as i Ssaɛid: A ziɣ d aggaw-ik i ɣ-terriḍ d taqcict ! ». Yenna-yi-d: ‚Ala, d aggaw-iw.‛.

Nniɣ-as: ‚ yalleh ihi ad nkemmel abrid.‛.

Nekcem s abrid-nni n ukerrus ideg nella di tazwara ufiɣ-d
la nleḥḥu zdat n yiwen n laɛzib d aqdim. laɛzib-nni

yettwasemma ‘Tala n Aɛmer u Yeḥya’. Uqbel ad naweḍ s

axxam n Ssaɛid, newweḍ ɣer yixxamen i d-yellan d

imezwura n udrum yettusemman ‘Ibelɛiden’. Fehmeɣ

dinna i-yezdeɣ Ssaɛid. Nbedd ad nemyeǧ sslam. Tezga-d

tmuɣli-iw deg ugafa ufella n ubrid, waleɣ takalitust

acebbub-is yettban-d am lexyal di tegnawt! Imir mmektiɣ-

d takerrust-nni yenneqlaben s yirrekaben. Zziɣ ɣer Ssaɛid

akken ad as-ḥkuɣ ufiɣ-t-id d Sliman-nni iḥeḍren di twaɣit.

Ula d axxam-is din i yella zdat-neɣ. Nniɣ-as: ‘A dda

Sliman, urgeɣ targit tessewhem-iyi.’ Yenna-yi-d: ‘D lxir

kan, ḥku-tt-id!’ Nniɣ-as: ‘A Dda Sliman zemreɣ ad ak-

iniɣ ulac win yettargun tirga yesÆan lmeÆna am tirga-w

rnu ssefruyeɣ-tent akken ilaq. Ur zemriɣ ara ad ak-iniɣ

ulac win izemren ad yessefru targit am nekk, axaṭer nekk

tirga-w ḥseb d leqraya i ttkemmileɣ yes-sent. Maca di

laɛmer Urgeɣ tawaɣit am tikkelt-agi; takerrust-nni tetti-d

am wakken seg ucebbub-inna n tkalitust i d-teɣli ɣer yifri-

agi ddaw n ubrid. Mi tt-waleɣ la tettneqlab, refdeɣ aḍad-

iw ccahed, nedheɣ s Rebbi; mi tetti tikkelt taneggarut,

uzzleɣ, ufiɣ-k tbeddeḍ tama n tkerrust-nni. Sliman yenna-

yi-d: ‘Takerrust-nni tenneqlab maca mi tneddheḍ s Rebbi,

ula d yiwen si lɣaci-nni ur yemmut, ur yejriḥ.’ Sliman

yetti-d ɣer Ssaɛid, waleɣ-t la yesmuqul akkin akka, nekk

fehmeɣ-t ur as-yefki ara azal i targit-nni. Ṭṭfeɣ-t-id si tayet,

zziɣ-t-id ɣer-i, nniɣ-as: ‘Aql-i di lmudda n 12 n yiseggasen

i la qqareɣ s tirga i ttarguɣ, akken ma llan yimdanen ulac

win ara tent-yargun, ulac win ara tent-id-yessefrun. Nekk
yal targit turgaḍ ad ak-tt-id-ssefruɣ, meɛna ma yella d targit yesɛan rruḥ. Sɣed-d amek i ssefruyeɣ tirga: Takerrust-nni tamejṭuḥt (Taxi) d temẓi, tameqqrant-nni d ddunit, tawwurt-nni n tlemmast yettwaxedmen s lmeryat d tamuɣli n walleɣ di targit, tawaɣit-nni d tagrawla n yimenɣi. Ssaɛid yetti-d ɣer Sliman yenna-yi-d: ‚Akka i d targit!‛

Ngar asurif, nezgar i yiwet n terga. Waleɣ Sliman yetti-d d Ssaɛid yezwar zdat-i yewwi aḍellaɛ-nni deg ufus. Nelḥa armi nelḥeq zdat n tewwurt n uxxam-is, ufiɣ-d ṭṭfeɣ deg ufus-iw aḍellaɛ-nni yeččur d aksum. Ssaɛid yenna-yi-d: « Yya-n ad tedduḍ s axxam ad teččeḍ imekli. »

Nniɣ-d: ‚Amek ara dduɣ s axxam-is s uḍellaɛ-agi; ssetḥeɣ ad t-sserseɣ ad uɣaleɣ ad t-id-refdeɣ.‛ Nniɣ-as : ‚Saḥḥa; ur tedduɣ ara.‛ Ssaɛid yenna-yi-d : « Welleh ard tedduḍ s axxam-iw ad tfetreḍ, yerna wwiɣ-d taqerɛet n ccrab ad tt-nsew !». Daɣen nniɣ-d deg ul-iw : «Wagi mačči d lxir ay deg-s, yerna zik ssetḥaɣ ma afeɣ tameṭṭut-is deg uxxam ; xas akken d uqriben-iw i sin. Tura yerna-d tissit n ccrab zdat n tmeṭṭut-is, ikemmel yeggul, ulamek ara t-sḥenteɣ. »

Ddiɣ yid-s s tmara. Yezwar nekk tebɛeɣ-t; mi nekcem di tewwurt n uxxam-nni, afeɣ mačči d axxam n twacult, d axxam n medden irkulli. Bab n uxxam-nni d mmi-s n xali isem-is ‘Lmumud’. Ssaɛid ulac-it! Qqimeɣ ɣer ṭṭabla, waleɣ iqdec-asen i lɣaci-nni yuɣal s amkan-is yeqqim yelha d wayen-nniḍen. Mi waleɣ akken, nleqmeɣ, ruḥeɣ s anida i tella tgella ad d-qedceɣ i yiman-iw. Mi dliɣ ɣef lḥala-nni, afeɣ-tt texreb! Leḥwal zeddigen xelḍen d
wid yumsen, leḥwal ilmawen rsen s ufella n wid yeččuren, lkisan ttuzrewɛen, yal wa anida yennugdam. Bdiɣ la d-reffadeɣ leḥwal-nni ilmawen la ten-ttarreɣ di rrif. Sliɣ i Lmulud yenna-yi-d: « Wid-nni yeččuren haten-an ɣer lqaɛ». Lant snat n tquslin ddaw yilmawen-nni refdeɣ-tent-id. Ufiɣ ula d tigad-nni ulac deg-sent, nniɣ-as i Lmulud: ‚Ulac lmakla‛. Inelqem-d seg umkan-is, yusa-d la yi-d-isenɛat anida i tella lmakla dɣa yedhem s kra din, ur yeǧǧi ula d ikersiyen-nni. Mi waleɣ yerwi lḥala nniɣ-as: ‚Anef-iyi d nekk ara d-iqedcen i yiman-iw‛. Refdeɣ dduzan-nni s yiwen yiwen, friɣ-ten, yal taɣawsa ufiɣ-as-d amkan-is. Mi qeɛdeɣ akk leḥwal, tuɣal lḥala n uxxam-nni testaɛǧab. Nniɣ-d deg wul-iw: ‚Xas akka ur neɛdil ara, meɛna mi ara yi-d-iẓer ẓewreɣ mebla ccek ad iyi-d-isekcem d acrik deg uxxam-agi‛.

Iban-iyi-d yiwen n ṭṭabeɛ di lḥiḍ. Ṭṭabeɛ-nni iwilem ad srusun deg-s lkisan. Tella daɣen tmeḥrabt iwilmen i teqraɛtin. Ufiɣ-d zdat-i snat n teqraɛtin n lgazuz n ččina, tis tlata n llim, rriɣ-tent ɣer tmeḥrabt-nni. Neṭqeɣ ɣer Lmulud nniɣ-as: ‚Wigi ilaq-asen leḥder‛. Wexreɣ-d ɣer deffir, sliɣ i Lmulud yenna-yi-d: ‚Ssaɛa-nni-inek tzad, nekk d lweḥda kečč d zzuǧ‛. Mmuqleɣ s afus-iw, waleɣ qqneɣ ssaɛa ur tesɛi ara ula d lmarat neɣ imzizlen i d-yeskanen taswiɛt. D ssaɛa taderɣalt. Mcikteɣ deg-s d lemri i as-yerrẓen. Mi dliɣ fell-as, afeɣ-tt ur tesɛi ara lemri. Sliɣ iṣuḍ-d uyenni si daxel n ssaɛa-nni. Waleɣ teffeɣ-d yiwet n tugest si ssaɛa-nni la tettiɣzif teddewir armi tuɣal am tugest-nni yettilin di tkaṣiṭ. Nniɣ-as i Lmulud: « Amek
akka i tga ssaɛa-agi?! Yerna d tajdiḍt i tt-id-uɣeɣ ; ma yella kan d win i wumi fkiɣ taqdimt-nni i yi-tt-id-yerran! ».

Ffɣeɣ-d di tewwurt n uxxam-nni, ufiɣ-d leḥqeɣ s tikli ɣer yiwet n tmeqbert yettusemman ‘Timeqbert iqasiten’. Deg umkan-nni llan sin n yiberdan n uḍar d iqdimen : yiwen yettawi d ugdis ɣer snat n temqebrin-nniḍen, wayeḍ yerra d asawen. Beddeɣ gar sin n yiberdan-nni la ttxemmimeɣ : ad kkeɣ seg ubrid-agi yerran d asawen, ibɛed-iyi lḥal, lawan hatan d lmeɣreb, ad d-yeɣli ṭṭlam deg ubrid uqbel ad awḍeɣ s axxam; Ad saɛfeɣ kan seg wagi-nniḍen xas ad ɛeddiɣ ɣef tmeqbert-inna yellan ɣer zdat, syagi iqreb-iyi ubrid rnu d ugdis alamma wwḍeɣ s axxam.

Σeddeɣ seg ubrid-nni i ferneɣ. Ufiɣ-d leḥqeɣ ɣer gar sin n yiberdan yellan ɣer zdat: yiwen d winna yellan srid s axxam-iw, wayeḍ yerra d asawen iɛedda tama n laɛzib yettusemman ‘Iɛisaten’. Ufiɣ-d la leḥḥuɣ deg ubrid-nni yerran d asawen mebla ma ksaneɣ. Leḥqeɣ ddaw n laɛzib-nni, ufiɣ-d la leḥḥuɣ zdat sin n yilmeẓyen, yiwen isem-is Muḥemmed, yezwar; wayeḍ Aɛrab, yettabaɛ-it deffir. Yiwet n tlemẓit isem-is Cabḥa tuder-d deg ubrid-nni, mi d-telḥeq ɣer umezwaru-nni, immuqel-itt. Waleɣ-tt tečča-t-id s tmuɣli. Mi d-telḥeq ɣer wis sin-nni kif-kif. Mi waleɣ akken, nniɣ-d deg wul-iw : « Nekk mi ara tt-mmuqleɣ ad tt-yeffeɣ laɛqel». Mi d-telḥeq ɣer-i, mmuqleɣ-tt tebra s uqerruy-is tezzerweḍ am tileft. Nkemmel abrid d asawen. Mi qrib ad nekcem leɛzib, waleɣ tarbaɛt n tlawin deg yiwet n temraḥt gar yixxamen imezwura. Tilawin-nni yal ta tellha d ccɣel-is. Mi d-walant ilmeẓyen-nni, llhant-d deg-sen s tmuɣli.
Nutni bedden ɣer-sent armi qrib ad ten-leḥqeɣ kemmlen abrid-nsen.

Lḥiɣ armi leḥqeɣ ɣer tilawin-nni. Akken i yi-d-walant uɣalent lhant d ccɣel-nsent. Rniɣ tikli armi leḥqeɣ ɣer yilmeẓyen-nni, nbedd di tlata yid-neɣ. Neṭqeɣ, nniɣ-asen :

« Wehmeɣ deg-wen, ṣṣifa ifeɣ-ken, lefhama ifeɣ-ken, tamusni ifeɣ-ken, kunwi tifem-iyi zzher. Maca ula d zzher ur iyi-tifem ara, d acu kan wagi mačči d abrid-iw ».

Ufiɣ-d iman-iw uɣaleɣ beddeɣ gar sin n yiberdan deg umkan-nni n tmeqbert. Tebɛeɣ abrid-nni yerran d asawen armi leḥqeɣ s anida yella ubrid d ugdis d winna ara iyi-ssiwḍen s axxam. Waleɣ yiwen n yilemẓi la ileḥḥu deg ubrid-nni ittkemmilen d asawen, netta isem-is Laɛmara. Waleɣ-t yelsa igalucen. Issekcem taqerɛet n ccrab deg yiwen n ugaluc. Mi waleɣ akken, tebɛeɣ abrid-nni yerran d asawen.

Lḥiɣ armi leḥqeɣ ilemẓi-nni, mmuqleɣ ɣer ssaɛa-nni yellan deg ufus-iw waleɣ-tt d yiwet n ssaɛa i fkiɣ i uḍeggal-iw. Neṭqeɣ ɣer yilemẓi-nni nniɣ-as: ‚Ad tweḥdeḍ Rebbi; ssaɛa yellan fkiɣ-tt i Ssaɛid-nwen ufiɣ-d qqneɣ-tt deg ufus-iw! Wehmeɣ d anwa i yi-tt-id-yerran deg ufus-iw‛.

Laɛmara yenna-yi-d: «Amer mi d-yeffeɣ di tewwurt !». Nniɣ-as: ‚Amek!? Tura kan i lliɣ di rrisṭura mmuqleɣ ssaɛa ufiɣ-tt d ssaɛa-w tajdidt iruḥ-as lemri; tura mi mmuqleɣ yuɣal-as-d lemri-nni am zik, ufiɣ-tt d ssaɛa-w taqdimt ».

Ufiɣ-d iman-iw di rrisṭura-nni qqimeɣ ɣer ṭṭabla. Waleɣ mm-is-nni n xali yeqdec akk i lɣaci-nni la tetten, yuɣal s amkan-is yeqqim. Nleqmeɣ daɣen ruḥeɣ ad d-swejdeɣ
učči i yiman-iw, sliɣ yenna-yi-d: ‚Mazal ccarba, attan deg ukasrul-nni ɣer lqaɛ». Mi dliɣ ɣef leḥwal-nni, ufiɣ daɣen d agudu, tettwarki lḥala, tennexrab. Mmɣeɣ  qeɛdeɣ akk leḥwal. Qqimen-d lkisan jemɛeɣ-ten-id, rriɣ-ten ɣer ṭṭabaɛ-nni yellan di lḥiḍ. Weṣṣaɣ fell-asen, nniɣ-as i Lmulud : « Aten-i wigi ilaq-asen leḥder, akka ɣer zdat ad d-yas lawan ad asen-xedmeɣ tameḥrabt di ṭṭabaɛ-agi n lḥiḍ‛. Lmulud yenna-yi-d: « Welleh ar d ṣṣeḥ!‛. Ffɣeɣ-d di tewwurt, mmuqleɣ ssaɛa ad waliɣ lawan.

Ukiɣ-d si targit !

1981

Aṣawaḍ uffir

Ufiɣ-d iman-iw beddeɣ deg yiwet n tiɣilt ideg tella lekka n Fransa di tallit n yimenɣi. Yella yiwen n urgaz zdat-i ttwaliɣ deg-s ičča-iyi-d s tmuɣli. Cikkeɣ-t ad yili d axabit! Ula s tmuɣli-s yettemsefham d uɛdaw ɣef watmaten-is. Uqbel ad zziɣ iman-iw fell-as, yelḥeq-d yiwen n uɛsekri s ubeckiḍ gar yifassen-is. Waleɣ aḍad-is yers ɣef zznad. Ɣliɣ-as ɣer tmurt, mi d-iqarres fell-i, tḍill- iyi tyita-nni. La as-rewwleɣ deg ubraḥ n lekka-nni: tikkelt ad as-ɣliɣ ɣer tmurt, tikkelt ad as-uɣaleɣ d tidist.
d-yettqerris fell-i la yi-ttazgal; mi leḥqeɣ ɣer yiwen n ugafa, ttiɣ iman-iw rriɣ d akessar s ugrireb. Amcum-nni la yi-d-yettabaɛ s rrṣaṣ. Leḥqeɣ ɣer yiwen n yiɣzer, ḥulfeɣ ttwaḥuzeɣ s terṣaṣt deg uberdi-w. Ṭṭfeɣ amkan-nni s ufus-iw akken ur sruḥuyeɣ ara aṭas n yidammen.

Ufiɣ-d iman-iw qqimeɣ di tarkkent n uxxam-iw tella rradyu tama-w; sliɣ di rradyu-nni tebda-d tedwilt i d-yettmeslayen ɣef lehlakat. Tadwilt-nni isemma-as bab-is ‘Tabrat i ṭṭbib’. Bab n tedwilt-nni yebda-d ameslay, Yenna-d: ‚Ay atmaten, tikkelt-agi ad awen-d-mmeslayeɣ ɣef leǧruḥ n yimjuhad yettwajerḥen. Amjahed yettwajerḥen deg uberdi, ad tafeḍ sin-nni n yiẓuran yellan deg uberdi-s yemmut-as yiwen yegra-d yiwen n uẓar. Luqran yenna-d: ‚Ad tsebreḍ, ad tsebreḍ, ad tsebreḍ, ad tzeɛfeḍ». Imi i ɣ-yeḥqer akka nekni s yimesdurar, ad ssakiɣ atmaten-iw, ad xedmeɣ lwajeb-iw fell-as alamma nessuffeɣ si tmurt-nneɣ mmi-s n teḥramt.

Ssiwleɣ i tmeṭṭut-iw nniɣ-as: ‚Sixef a Tasaɛdit awi-d tawerqet d yimru ad aruɣ ayen akka i d-yenna umedyaz-agi uqbel ad ttuɣ kra deg-s‛. Tefka-iyi-d tawerqet d yimru nniɣ-as: ‚Ad aruɣ tabrat i bab n tedwilt-agi, ad tt-yeṭṭef tura, ad ruḥeɣ ɣer tedwilt-agi tura, ad as-ḥkuɣ i bab-is targit i urgeɣ ɣef watmaten-iw imjuhad.‛. Serseɣ imru di tewriqt, ufiɣ-d ziɣ d nekk i d-yennan ayen akken i wumi sliɣ di tedwilt-nni! Neṭqeɣ ɣer TasaÆdit, nniɣ-as: ‚ad twehmeḍ di laÆqel i yi-d-yefka Rebbi, ziɣ d nekk i la d-yettmeslayen nekk nwiɣ d rradyu!‛. TasaÆdit tenna-yi-d: ‚ziɣ daymi a Meẓyan I yi-d-qqaren lÆibad: Meẓyan,
ssawalen-as-d at laxert netta yettarra-asen awal i at ddunit. Nniɣ-as: „ula d nekk welleh ar cikkeɣ deg wayagi!“

# Ukiɣ-d si targit !

1981

Ǧǧan-iyi-d d aÆessas Ufiɣ-d la tedduɣ ad kecmeɣ ɣer yiwen n ṣbiṭer; uliɣ ɣer ṭṭabaqa tamezwarut; ufiɣ din argaz n weltma d ṭṭbib! Nniɣ deg wul-iw: « Atan yerna-iyi-d kan Rebbi laÆtab mi d amcum-agi i d-ufiɣ, mebla ccek ur ttÆeddiɣ ara!». Beddeɣ ɣer rrif la ttxemmimeɣ ma ad kemmleɣ ɣer zdat neɣ ad uɣaleɣ ɣer deffir. Mi Æeddan akk wid-nni yellan zdat-i, telḥeq-d nnuba-w; ufiɣ-d iman-iw s tlaba n ṭṭebbat!

Nniɣ-d deg wul-iw: « ziɣ d nekk i d ṭṭbib la ttraǧuɣ aÆdaw-iw ad iyi-d-yefk nnuba ! »

Ufiɣ-d iman-iw d amuḍin d waṭas n yimuḍan, nerra adur deg usqif n sbiṭer-nni akken ad d-nawi imekli zdat n texxamt n usewwi, zdat-s tella tzeqqa n wučči. Imuḍan la ttÆeddin s ndiha; win yeslan s yisem-is ad iÆeddi ad yeṭṭef amkan-is deg ukersi ɣer ṭṭabla n wučči. Ma d nekk mi sliɣ i ndiha s yisem-iw, ur d-tbiteɣ ara mile, nniɣ-d deg wul-
iw : « ad rǧuɣ ma ad d-iÆiwed ndiha; ad seɣdeɣ mile! ».

Waleɣ yiwen n yilemẓi iÆedda s tazzla yeṭṭef akersi ɣer ṭṭabla -nni. Ilemẓi-nni iban-iyi-d mačči d amuḍin. Akken kan yesɣim iman-is, ndiha teḥbes.

Imuḍan-nni yellan deffir-iw Æeddan akk mebla ndiha ṭṭfen imukan ɣer ṭṭabla. Nekk nniɣ-d deg wul-iw : « ilemẓi-inna iÆeddan mebla ndiha mebla ccek iÆedda di nnuba-w, ad yili d axeddam n dagi i t id-yesÆeddan s tsusmi ad yečč baṭel. Maca tura ad d-iban. ».

Qerbeɣ ɣer ṭṭaq n texxamt-nni n usewwi ansi i d-tetteffeɣ teɣri-nni n ndiha, ufiɣ yiwen n uxeddam i isewwan. Uqbel ad t-laÆiɣ sliɣ indeh-d s yisem-iw. Nniɣ-as : « Teǧǧiḍ-iyi armi yettwaṭṭef umkan-iw i d-tnedheḍ fell-i.!». Yenna-yi-d : « Aw ! Nekk seg ṣbeḥ i la d-neddheɣ fell-ak kečč tugiḍ ad d-tesbaneḍ iman-ik! ».

Nniɣ-as : « D tidet; lufan ad ak-iniɣ sliɣ-d i ndiha s yisem-iw maca ur d-tbiteɣ ara. Daymi akka muḍleɣ ciṭ, meÆna i winna yeṭṭfen akersi-inu, d acu i t-id-yewwin ? ». Yenna-yi-d : « amer tÆedlem ismawen! Yalleh ɣer-s tura ad nwali. ».

Nruḥ ɣer yilemẓi-nni. Mi nelḥeq ɣer-s, yesteqsa-t uxeddam-nni : « Isem-ik kečč ? ». Yenna-yas-d : « Isem-iw BenbaÆid. ». Yenna-yas : « nnumru n ukersi : 27.5.1952. Isem-ik BenbaÆid, kečč teṭṭfeḍ amkan n Ɣerram Lḥusin ! ayya, nelqem, ffeɣ. Balak ad k-waliɣ tezzziḍ-d ula s tmuɣli ɣer deffir. ».

Yeffeɣ yilemẓi-nni s tuffɣa n laÆqel. Yezzi-d ɣer-i urgaz-nni, yeḍsa-d, yewwet-iyi-d di tayet, yenna-yi-d : « Atan umkan-ik. ».

Qqimeɣ deg ukersi-nni. Ufiɣ-d lliɣ deg yiwen n lbiru berra n sbiṭer-nni. Ass fehmeɣ-t, d ass n lexmis, lawan d
ttnasfa n wass. Ixeddamen n lbiru-nni ffɣen akk ad staÆfun nekk qqimeɣ d aÆessas, ṭṭfeɣ akersi zdat n tewwurt n berra. Tawwurt-nni tettwamdel, tettwaxdem s lmeryat, tuzga-d di tlemmast n usqif n lbiru-nni. Waleɣ yiwen n urgaz la d-ileḥḥu di berra fehmeɣ-t yeḥwaǧ kra di lbiru-nni. Mi d-yelḥeq, yufa-d lbiru-nni tettwamdel-as tewwurt. Sliɣ -as la yesnehmuy. Fehmeɣ-t deg yixeddamen n lbiru-nni i la ireggem mi d-yufa ulac-iten; nekk lliɣ ffreɣ iman-iw fell-as. Argaz-nni yuɣal-d d ilemẓi. Waleɣ-t yezzi iman-is ad yuɣal. Ibedd ɣer-s yiwen n urgaz, sliɣ yesteqsa ilemẓi-nni, yenna-yas : « Mi d-tusiḍ ɣer lbiru-agi, ansi-k kečč ? ». Ilemẓi-nni yenna-yas : « Nekk d aqbayli. »; argaz-nni iruḥ; ilemẓi-nni yetti-d d argaz. Nekk mi t-ḥṣiɣ akken d aqbayli, sbaneɣ-d iman-iw ɣer-s, siwleɣ-as yusa-d; steqseɣ-t, nniɣ-as : « d acu i teḥwaǧeḍ di lbiru-agi ? ». Yenna-yi-d : « Bɣiɣ ad d-ssuffɣeɣ yiwen n lkaɣeḍ, yerna ḥwaǧeɣ-t ass-a!». Nniɣ-as : « aql-aneɣ deg wass n lexmis tameddit ulac win ara k-t-id-ixedmen, ixeddamen ffɣen akk siwa nekk i d-yegran dagi d aÆessas; alamma d ass n ssebt ṣbeḥ ara d-uɣalen ɣer lxedma. ». Iban-iyi-d la yettxemmim, udem-is yuɣal am yirrig n tmes. Uɣaleɣ nniɣ-as : « ruḥ Æeddi-d ɣer ṭṭaq-inna, eefk-iyi-d nnekwa-k, d nekk s yiman-iw ara k-id-ixedmen lkaɣeḍ-agi i tebɣiḍ. ». Yenna-yi-d : « ad ak-iǧazi Rebbi s lxir a Meẓyan. ». Yekka-d zdat ṭṭaq-nni n usqif n lbiru, nniɣ-as : « awi-d nnekwa-k ad ṭṭfeɣ isem-ik. ». Iwehha-iyi-d nnekwa-s. Uqbel ara-tt-id-ṭṭfeɣ, yenna-yi-d isem-is. Isem-nni d baba-s n tmeṭṭut- iw ad yettwarḥem.
Ufiɣ-d lliɣ d tmeṭṭut-iw deg uxxam-nneɣ lawan n yiḍ.

Taftilt n lgaz tecÆel gar-aneɣ. Bdiɣ la s-ḥekkuɣ targit i tmeṭṭut-iw : « LaÆca-nni, a TasaÆdit, Urgeɣ baba-m yusa-d ɣer-i ɣer lbiru. Yufa-iyi-d d aÆessas, isuter-iyi-d ad as-xedmeɣ lkaɣeḍ xas akken ur ssineɣ ara, yenna-yi-d isem-is Musṭfay AÆli, yerna xas akken di targit (tebteɣ-t d lmeyyet i yella). Tameṭṭut-iw tenna-yi-d : « ula d nekk Urgeɣ-t di tmeɣra. »

Ukiɣ-d si targit !

1981

Ur ttuggad akked ṣellaḥ

Ufiɣ-d lliɣ akked tmeṭṭut-iw d yelli tamenzut, nbedd ɣer yiwet n talast deg yiwen n ubrid n uḍar yellan di tama ufella nnig uxxam n yimawlan n tmeṭṭut-iw.

Talast-nni rekzen-tt irumyen, teskan-d ansi ara yili ubrid n ukerrus. Di tlata yid-neɣ neṭṭef tibedÆiyin n uglim i aɣ-d-yusan si tmurt n Fransa. TabedÆit-nni-inu waleɣ-tt tettucerreg deg wudem n daxel di tama tazelmaḍt.

Acerrig-nni yeffeɣ-d seg wudem n berra s lewhi n umkan n wul. Neṭqeɣ ɣer tmeṭṭut-iw nniɣ-as : « TabedÆit-agi-inu teqqers a TasaÆdit!». Temmuqel-itt-id tenna-yi-d : « Ala!

- 129 -
winna d amkan ideg d-sedduyen lkaɣeḍ n ssuma: acḥal i teswa. Amkan-nni ur d-yettban ara si berra. ». Greɣ afus- iw deg ucerrig-nni, ufiɣ-t d lǧib n daxel. Imir ferḥeɣ aṭas s tbedÆit-nni imi ur tettucerreg ara. Ata yelḥa-d yiwen n yilemẓi isem-is Belqasem d mmi-s n xali-s n tmeṭṭut-iw. Mi d-yelḥeq ɣer-neɣ, waleɣ tabellart gar yifassen-is teččur d ssebɣa. Yenna-d : « Ata wwiɣ-d ssebɣa taberkant ma ad tesseɣmeḍ abernus-ik. ». Nniɣ-as « ala, ur t-sseɣmeɣ ara. ». Tameṭṭut-iw tenna-yi-d : « ad ak-d-tefk abernus amellal teqcict-nni n Fransa, ad ak-t-id-tefk asmi ara s- tefkeḍ ttiÆad. ». Nniɣ-as : « Tinna d yelli-s n Æemti. Ad iyi-d-tefk abernus aberkan. »

Ufiɣ-d iman-iw deg yiwet n tiɣilt yettusemman ‘Azuggar’. Tella yid-i tmeṭṭut-iw. Lḥiɣ armi i d-fateɣ ɣef tmeṭṭut-iw s yiwen n umḍiq, sliɣ-as tessiwel-iyi-d s teɣri n lferḥ, tenna-yi-d : « A Meẓyan, azemmur-nni ur t-ttserrif ara weḥd-k ula d nekk nneÆtabeɣ. » . Teqqar-d tettÆawad- d. Ma d nekk mi d-tessiwel ad zziɣ ɣer deffir ad ḍseɣ ɣer- s, ad kemmleɣ tikli-w ɣer zdat. Mi d-beÆdeɣ fell-as tesssiwel-iyi-d nniɣ-as : « Ur ttuggad, ur ttserrifeɣ ara weḥd-i .». Sliɣ tenna-yi-d : « ihi atan ceyyÆeɣ-ak-d tisura n uxxam i Rabeḥ WeÆli. ». Zziɣ mmuqleɣ ɣer deffir, waleɣ Rabeḥ-nni la d-yettazzal yewwi-iyi-d tisura deg ufus-is la iyi-d-yessewÆad yes-sent.

Beddeɣ deg ubrid n ukerrus deg umkan yettusemman ‘Taqerrabt’, ufiɣ tlata n yimɣaren zdat-i; iban-iyi-d yiwen d ccix-nsen. Sliɣ yenna-yi-d : « A Meẓyan, nekni d lawliyya. ». Yiwen yettwiddem, mazal-d sin. Ccix-nni yenna-yi-d : « Ad truḥeḍ ɣer Fransa a
Meẓyan ? ». Nniɣ-as : « Ad ruḥeɣ ma irad Rebbi. ». Yenna-yi-d : « yella win iɣef tettekleḍ dinna di Fransa ? ». Nniɣ-as : « yella Rebbi. ». Amɣar-nni-nniḍen yenna-yas i ccix-nni : « Meẓyan yella iÆuss di Rǧawna tura yerwel ɣer Fransa. ». Ccix-nni Yenna-yas : « D tidet. » yuɣal-d  ɣer-i, yenna-yi-d : « a Meẓyan ma truḥeḍ ɣer Fransa, xas di drus i tellam ur ttuggad ara. ». Nniɣ-as : «  awed-d kan ad ak-in-sleɣ. ». Yenna-yi-d : « nniɣ-ak ma ad truḥeḍ ɣer Fransa xas teẓriḍ di ciṭ i tellam ur ttuggad ara; bdu-tt-id nekni ad as-nkemmel. Aql-aɣ dagi di Wehran di Æecrin yid-neɣ. U yernu yal amḍiq muddeɣ-as yiwen. ». Amɣar-nni wis sin yenna-yi-d : « nekk d ḍerrab n lmus. ». Ccix-nni yenna-yi-d : « Aql-in ɣer yidisan-ik a Meẓyan, ay anida teddiḍ ur tesÆiḍ ay ad tuggadeḍ. ». Nniɣ-as : « Melmi ara ruḥeɣ ɣer Fransa ? ». Yenna-yi-d : « SsaÆt-agi mazal  azemmur di tseṭṭa. ». Nniɣ-as : « ad iyi-d-tcareḍ ma ad rebḥeɣ di Fransa neɣ ala? »yenna-yi-d : « lmut ur tettmettateḍ ara, rrbeḥ ur trebbḥeḍ ara! »

Waleɣ yuɣal-d winna yellan iɣab fell-neɣ. Sliɣ i ccix-nni yenna-yasen : « tura ad nemfaraqet, nekk ad dduɣ akked Meẓyan. ». Nemyuǧǧa sslam. Sin-nni n yimɣaren rran akkin ; nekk akked ccix-nni nerra-d akka. Nelḥa kra n yisurrifen ɣer zdat, mmɣeɣ ssudneɣ aqerruy n ccix-nni, nniɣ-as : « ad aɣ-yenfeÆ Rebbi s lbaraka-k a ccix. ». Yenna-yi-d : « kečč a Meẓyan tesÆiḍ yiwen n uruḥani d ameqqran yettÆawan-ik. Rnu ḥader ad as-tiniḍ aruḥani d leḥram, d Rebbi i ak-t-id-yefkan ad k-yettÆawan. Ula d nekk, ad k-
id-mmuqleɣ aÆefrit ameqqran ad ak-yettÆawanen. ». Nniɣ-as : « welleh xas mmuqel-iyi-d albaÆḍ. »

Nelḥeq s tikli ɣer yiwet n tmazirt yellan gar sin n yiberdan. Nbedd di tlemmast n tmazirt-nni. Mmuqleɣ ɣer zdat, tban-iyi-d tewwurt di tlemmast n tmazirt-nni. Tawwurt-nni tella ɣef wudem n wakal. Sin n yilmeẓyen bedden zdat n tewwurt mlilen tayet ɣer tayet, lsan talaba tajdiḍt, yiwen deg-sen yeṭṭef tabalizt tettwaxdem am ukerṭab.

Ccix-nni yenna-yi-d : « Winna yeṭṭfen tabalizt d winna i d rrasul llah. ». Banen-iyi-d yilmeẓyen-nni la smuqulen s lbeÆd. StebÆeɣ tamuɣli-w, waleɣ la smuqulen ɣer temdint n Lezzayer i la d-yettbanen s lbeÆd am lewṣifa-s di lkaɣeḍ.

Tban-iyi-d yiwet n telwaḥt nnig n tewwurt-nni tettwaru s taÆrabt s sin leḥruf ‘t’ akked ‘ya’, ɣer zdat tettwaru ‘ad d-tuɣal Lezzayer ɣer yimawlan-is’. Yuɣal yemɣi-d yiwen n ccix zdat-neɣ. Ccix-nni yettban-d am ubudali neɣ ugar.

Nelḥa ɣer-s, nufa-t la yettkerrir di luqran la t-id-yessefham s teqbaylit. Mi nelḥeq ɣer-s, nufa-t yeqqim deg ugudu isenned iman-is ɣer lÆers yewwet ! Deg ufessar-nni mačči d ayen i d-yeqqar s taÆrabt i d-yessefham s teqbaylit.

Sliɣ i ccix-nni yellan yid-i isuɣ fell-as, yenna-yas : « yiwen n lemrennek am kečč ay aqewwad la tessefhameḍ di lkewn n Rebbi; tirga yettargu Meẓyan ur tettizmireḍ ara ad tent-tesfehmeḍ. D acu i la tesbudÆayeḍ ɣef yiman-ik ? ». Nniɣ-as i ccix-nni : « anef ad yesbudÆi ɣef yiman-is, nekk ma umneɣ-t xas ad iyi-yesseɣleḍ. Yya-n ad nettixer fell-as. Yalleh kan mmuqel-iyi-d winna i yi-tenniḍ !». Nuder di tmazirt-nni. Mi ners s abrid, nemlil-d
d yiwen n urgaz  ɣezzif d aqwayan. Nniɣ-as i ccix-nni :

« ini-as i wagi ad yili d aÆefrit ».

Ccix-nni yemmuqel-it, yessusem ur t-iluÆa ara; nekk fehmeɣ-t yuggad-it. Sḥerṣeɣ di ccix armi yuɣal d ulac.

LuÆeɣ leÆǧeb-nni, nniɣ-as : « ad ak-sÆuɣ d aÆefrit-iw ad iyi-tettÆawaneḍ ? ». Yenna-yi-d : « ala. ». Nniɣ-as : « ilaq ad ak-sÆuɣ; ulac din awal! ». Yenna-yi-d : « ini-iyi-d un mǧt de passe ! ». Nniɣ-as : « ayagi d ayen ur ssineɣ ara. Nekk d lxelq am kečč, d Rebbi i aɣ-d-ixelqen, am kečč am nekk. Ilaq ad ak-sÆuɣ ad iyi-tettÆawaneḍ. »

Mi sḥerṣeɣ deg-s, ttwaliɣ-t yettneḍrab armi yuɣal d ulac. Lḥiɣ kra n yisurrifen ɣer zdat, leḥqeɣ zdat tewwurt n ufrag n llikul n taddart-iw, mmuqleɣ ɣer rrif ufella n ubrid, waleɣ taxxamt tesÆa-d afrag-is s abrid. Sliɣ i sin n yirgazen sekkren awal daxel n texxamt-nni. Nniɣ-d deg wul-iw : « wigi d lÆibad mačči d iÆefriten, ilaq ad rǧuɣ wiyaḍ. »

Maḍleɣ taswiÆt armi waleɣ zdat-i lexyal n umdan iban-iyi-d di tmurt am win i la imeccḍen yesmuqul ɣer lemri. Mmuqleɣ ɣer yal tama ur waleɣ ara bab n lexyal-nni ! Ɣer dqal fehmeɣ-d am win ara yi-d-yinin lexyal-nni ur d-yettban ara bab-is alamma tenniḍ-as awal n yiÆefriten. Lexyal-nni la ileḥḥu nekk la t-tabaÆeɣ, armi newweḍ ɣer tlemmast n ufrag n texxamt-nni, yuɣal-d lexyal-nni d amdan, yenna-yi-d : « nekk d aÆefrit. ». Nniɣ-as : « nekk ‘le mǧt de passe’ ur t- ssineɣ ara. »

Iban-iyi-d yella wayeḍ d arfiq-is, waleɣ myesmuqalen, zmumgen s teḍsa ; iÆiwed lxelq-nni yenna-yi-d : « nekk d abẓiẓ. ». Jawbeɣ-t s wurfan nniɣ-as : « nekk d lxelq am
kečč, Rebbi-nneɣ yiwen, le mǧt de passe ur ssineɣ ara.

Usiɣ-d qeṣdeɣ-k-id ilaq ak-sÆuɣ d aÆefrit-iw ad iyi-tettÆawaneḍ.

Ufiɣ lliɣ yid-s daxel n texxamt-nni, yenna-yi-d : « belleɣ tiṭ-ik d asawen. ».

Bellɣeɣ tiṭ-iw armi ḥulfeɣ idis n berra yuɣal ɣer daxel.

Yenna-yi-d : « saḍas » s tefransist. ».

Rriɣ-d tiṭ-iw akken tella.

Yebda-iyi-d ccuruṭ, yenna-yi-d : « ad ak-Æmuɣ allen-ik ur tferrazeḍ ara, ad ak-regleɣ imeẓẓuɣen-ik ur tselleḍ ara, ad ak-kummeɣ imi-k ur tettmeslayeḍ ara. ».

Yeddem-d snat n tzemziyin, yefka-iyi-tent-id; ṭṭfeɣ-tent deg ufus-iw.

Fehmeɣ tizemziyin-nni d ccyara.

Yenna-yi-d : « Ḥmeẓ-itent mliḥ s ufus-ik. ».

Ḥemẓeɣ-tent.

Yenna-yi-d : « lddi imi-k mliḥ. ».

Lddiɣ imi-w, yessers-d imi-s ɣef yimi-w, yebda la yi-d-yettmeslay s agerjum-iw.

Ḥulfeɣ i yidmaren-iw la zluzen, ul-iw la d-yettales i umeslay-nni s teɣri taÆlayant.

Yemmeslay armi ifak ameslay-is, yewwet-iyi-d di tayet yenna-yi-d : « ruḥ tura ur ttuggad akked ṣṣellaḥ. »

Ukiɣ-d si targit !

- 134 -
Ḍsiɣ i zdat

Ufiɣ-d lliɣ akked sin n yimdanen nbedd deg ubrid n ukerrus deg umkan iwumi semman ‘LǧameÆ n Lalla Ḥlima’. Sin-nni, yiwen d mmi-s n Æemmi, wayeḍ yettqarab-iyi ciṭ isem-is ‘Muḥ u Qasi’. Muḥ yenna-yi-d : « d ṣṣeḥ a Meẓyan tregmeḍ-ten di Tizi Uzezzu ? ». Nniɣ-as : « yak ɣef wasmi i d-ssuffɣeɣ le pasport !? Ala ur ten-rgimeɣ ara di Tizi Uzezzu. D tabrat i uriɣ ɣer rradyu regmeɣ-ten deg-s. Yerna ḍelbeɣ-asen ‘ay iṭij ḥader ad teɣliḍ’ tura wwḍen-d warraw-nneɣ. ».

AÆmer yenna-yi-d : « ulamek i ten-tregmeḍ di Tizi Uzezzu. ». Waleɣ AÆmer yejbed iman-is fell-aneɣ. Zziɣ ɣer Muḥ, nniɣ-as : « regmeɣ-ten di Tizi Uzezzu yerna acḥal tikkal! »

Ufiɣ-d lliɣ di myugar n yiberdan deg umkan yettusemman ‘Imidek n Si Teyyeb’. Lliɣ twehheɣ ɣer taddart Iẓarruden. Lḥiɣ kra n yisurrifen, ufiɣ yiwen n urgaz n taddart-nni isem-is Adem isa neɣ isa u Muḥ.

Nemsalam, nuɣal la nettnecraḥ. Di taggara nuɣal ɣer ṣṣeḥ nniɣ-as : « a isa , lÆulama mi d-nnan d Adem akked Ḥewwa i d-yezwaren ɣer ddunit, amek armi i d-ttilin yimdanen s waṭas n leṣnaf di ṣṣifat-nsen ? daɣen lÆulama-agi ur d-nnin ara d acu yessiwḍen imdanen n zik u zik ɣer tmura-agi i d-yennulfan di lqern n 18 neɣ 19! ».

Waleɣ tarbaÆt n lɣaci la d-leḥḥun izwer-d zdat-sen yiwen i fehmeɣ d lÆalem. Uzzleɣ ɣer-s. mi leḥqeɣ, ufiɣ-t d yiwen i yi-ttqaraben, d aÆdaw. Di lefhama xussen-t sin n
wacciwen u nekk fehmeɣ-t d lÆalem. Iban-iyi-d yeṣker ṣṣekran d ajehli ! yelḥa-d ɣer-i s umlelli, ṭṭfen-as-d afus lɣaci-nni. Mi nemlil, nebda ameslay :  ‚D kečč i d lÆalem i d-yennan ddunit yella wasmi i d-tebda ?‛. Yenna-yi-d : « d nekk. ». Nniɣ-as : « ad ak-fkeɣ sin n yisteqsiyen, ma tjawbeḍ-d fell-asen akken ilaq ad amneɣ akk s wayen i d-tenniḍ. ». Yenna-yi-d : « ini-d, ad d-jawbeɣ. ». Nniɣ-as : « ad iyi-d-tiniḍ ma tesÆa lḥedd ansi i d-tenneqḍaÆ tqaÆet-agi n wakal s wadda-s ? ». Yenna-yi-d « tbedd ɣef lxali di lehwa. ». Nniɣ-as : « lemmer ad yebɣu Rebbi ad as-iserreḥ i tqaÆet-agi ad teɣli d akessar, lÆulama ad ddun deg-s rnu ma ur d-teḥbis ara ur ttmettaten ara alamma teḥbes-d; d acu ara d-tiniḍ ad d-teḥbes neɣ ur d-tḥebbes ara ? ». Yenna-yi-d : « I lebda ur d-tḥebbes ara. ». Nniɣ-as : « ihi taqaÆet-agi n ddunit ur tesÆi ara lḥedd s leḥsab n lÆilem n txelqit ; ma s leḥsab n lkewn n Rebbi, d netta kan i d lÆalem-is. Ma d kečč d leḥram fell-ak, d ddnub ameqqran ad d-tḥuddeḍ lkewn yesÆan lḥedd-is ɣer Rebbi. Kečč d lÆalem ur neÆlim ula s yiman-is. »

Sliɣ-as la yesqemqim, iles-is yettwattel, la d-yettm eslay ur d-yesḍill ara ula d yiwen n wawal. Mmuqleɣ-t, ḍsiɣ, ḍsiɣ, nniɣ-as : « meqqer yiles-ik, ur t-yewwi ara uqemmuc-ik, wagi d asteqsi amezwaru. Sɣed-d tÆaseḍ iman-ik ɣef usteqsi aneggaru, ma ur d-tjawbeḍ ara akken ilaq ad terwi fell-ak! ». Imir yeskker isuɣan akken s usqewqew-nni la yi-id-yettmeslay ɣef temsal-nniḍen, nekk sḥerṣeɣ deg-s nniɣ-as : « ma d lÆalem kečč, mi nefra tamsalt n usteqsi aneggaru, ad nuɣal ɣer tiyaḍ. »
Yuɣal lÆalem-nni la yi-id-ireggem. Mi sliɣ i rregmat-nni, nniɣ-as : « hatan wayen i wumi tessnem kunwi. ». Uzzlen-d lɣaci-nni, mi d-leḥqen ɣer-neɣ, sḍelmen deg-i aṭas, nnan-iyi-d : « awwah a Meẓyan, imi ur teÆdilem ara, yerna ass-agi mi t-twalaḍ yeskker, dɣa tesḥerseḍ deg-s. ». Wwin-t yid-sen, ṭṭfen-as afus. La ileḥḥu gar-asen s umlelli itezzi-d ɣer deffir la yi-d-ireggem. Mi waleɣ akken, ḍsiɣ, nniɣ-d : « semmḥet-as yewwi-t yiɣzer. » . Uɣalen-d ɣer deffir kra seg lɣaci-nni. Mi d-leḥqen ɣer-i, zzin-d fell-i d ameqyas la yi-ttḥawaten qqaren-iyi-d : « aha tura dayen a Meẓyan i yelhan d ssmaḥ. Hatan la tettwaliḍ deg-s yesker. ». Nekk nniɣ-asen s wurfan: « ma yesker ad yesker kan ɣef yiman-is. »

Awal-agi yeɣli-d seg yimi-w, ageffur yeɣli-d d lgirra. Lɣaci-nni yal wa d anida yerra ad yesdari iman-is. Qqimeɣ-d nekk qesdeɣ ɣer yiwet n tsirt n uzemmur. Ruḥeɣ s tazzla yetbeÆ-iyi-d yiwen n yilemẓi isem-is ‘Lmulud n Ḥmed’ la yettaÆraḍ amek ara yi-yezwar ɣer tsirt-nni. Leḥqeɣ ɣer yiwet n tsawent, rniɣ di tazzla. Leḥqeɣ ɣer yiwet n tkeddirt yellan ddaw n ubraḥ n tsirt-nni, ufiɣ yekker yixmir d ixerxer. Mi greɣ asurif, ad cḍeɣ ɣer deffir s sin n yisurrifen.. Lmulud yeḍsa deffir-iw, sliɣ yenna-yi-d : « tura ad k-zwareɣ. ». Yuzzel-d, yelḥeq-d ɣer wuccuḍ-nni maca yal mi ara iger asurif ɣer zdat ad yecceḍ, ad yuɣal timendeffirt ini yeɣli. Nuli s tmara di tkeddirt-nni. Mi nÆedda i wuccuḍ-nni, nesla i teɣratin deg uxxam n bab n tsirt-nni. Lmulud yenna-yi-d : « tella tmeɣra deg uxxam-agi. ». Nniɣ-as : « ala, mačči d - 137 -
tameɣra, d tinefkit ara mudden. Hatan leḥqen-d wid ara tt-yawin. »

Mi nwala lɣaci la d-leḥḥun deg- waṭas yid-sen, zwareɣ zdat n Lmulud nga timsizzelt gar yiÆricen n uzemmur deg ubraḥ n tsirt-nni. Mi leḥqeɣ ɣer tewwurt n tsirt, ufiɣ-tt tettwamdel. Waleɣ tella tɣurfet sufella n tsirt-nni n uzemmur. Abrid ɣer tɣurfet-nni d rref i d-yeffɣen di lḥiḍ am tmeḥrabt; aÆeddi seg ubrid-nni alamma s tidist. Mi waleɣ Lmulud yuzzel ad iÆeddi deffir n tsirt-nni, uggadeɣ ad iyi-yezwar.

Nniɣ deg wul-iw : « ad Æeddiɣ s tazzla deg ubrid-agi n lḥiḍ ad zwareɣ Lmulud neɣ ad ɣliɣ. »; Æeddeɣ deg ubrid-nni n lḥiḍ qbala s tiddi-w mačči s tidist. Mi leḥqeɣ zdat n tɣurfet-nni, waleɣ yiwen isem-is Lḥusin u AÆmer yuzzel-d deffir-iw. Kecmeɣ ɣer tɣurfet-nni, ufiɣ yiwen d mmi-s n Æemti d aÆeggun, d aneÆyabu isem-is SsaÆid.

Waleɣ yeskker times s tleẓẓewt tazegzawt, la yesseḥmuy. S lembeÆd n tmes-nni waleɣ yers uqejmur, uzzleɣ ɣer-s akken ad qqimeɣ s ufell-as, tban-iyi-d tkursit tama n SsaÆid. Uzzleɣ ɣer tkursit-nni, yeddem-itt SsaÆid, yefka-tt i Lḥusin mi d-yelḥeq. Mi waleɣ Lḥusin yeqqim ɣef tkursit-nni, ḍsiɣ, nniɣ-as i SsaÆid : « wa yettili-iyi, wa d mmi-s n taddart-iw, seg-wen i d-tekken wuguren-iw.

Leḥqeɣ-d d amezwaru ɣer tkursit-nni, tekkseḍ-iyi-tt, tefkiḍ-tt i Lḥusin i d-ileḥqen d aneggaru. ». Yenna-yi-d : «yehwa-iyi. ». ḍsiɣ, nniɣ-as : « tɣunzaḍ-iyi mi ak-qqareɣ ifeɣ-k di ṣṣifa ? nekk d tidet i ak-qqareɣ. ».SsaÆid iɣaḍ-it lḥal aṭas. Iftek-iyi s wallen-is.. Nniɣ-as : « mmuqel-iyi-d milḥ, ifeɣ-k di ṣṣifa, ifeɣ-k aṭas di lefÆayel. ». Yenna-yi-d :
« anida ara tegreḍ afus ur ggareɣ ara afus!»; meḥsub iɣunfa-iyi. ḍsiɣ ɣer Lḥusin nniɣ-as : « tesliḍ a Lḥusin d acu i yi-d-yenna yiwen n wuÆwij am wagi ! ». Lḥusin yeḍsa yenna-yi-d : « a Meẓyan aql-aneɣ di zzman uÆwij, ula d lḥeqq deg-s d uÆwij. D zzman i la yettmeslayen mačči d ameÆdur-agi. »

Zziɣ ɣer SsaÆid, nniɣ-as : « tesliḍ d acu i ak-id-yenna Lḥusin? D zzman i la yettmeslayen mačči d kečč. Maca asmi ara iṣeggem zzman ad tessetḥiḍ ad d-tesneÆteḍ udem-ik ɣer medden. ». Lḥusin yeḍsa, yenna-yi-d : « deg wayagi mebla ccek. »

# Ukiɣ-d si targit !

1981

# Lǧenn d aclawa

Nella di tlata yid-neɣ daxel n tkerrust i wumi qqaren 404 FL. Takerrust-nni teḥbes deg ubrid n uḍar ddaw yiwen n laÆzib yettusemman IÆisaten di taddart at Lbir. Nekk rekbeɣ ɣer yid-is n unehhar, tameṭṭut-iw tella-d deffir-iw. TeqleÆ yes-neɣ tkerrust-nni, terra d asawen. Abrid ur yestuhna ara ula i tikli ɣef uḍar. Rnu simmal nettqeddim ɣer zdat simmal yettiḍyiq ubrid.
takerrust-nni qrib ad taweḍ yes-neɣ ɣer yiwen n umkan yezyeb aṭas, lemmer ad tÆeddi deg-s tkerrust ad tetti ; di tama ufella n umkan-nni yella ṣṣur n uẓru Ælay s tiddi n lmitra, neṭqeɣ ɣer tmeṭṭut-iw, nniɣ-as : « neggez a TasaÆdit uqbel ad tenneqlab yes-neɣ. ».

Tneggez, tuzga-d di tmurt tbedd; nekk ldiɣ tawwurt Æusseɣ iman-iw. Mi telḥeq tkerrust s amkan-nni uzyib, twehheɣ ɣer tama n ufella, ttwaliɣ di rrwadi-is la temmɣent ɣef ṣṣur-nni am umdan ! mi tuli ciṭ di lḥiḍ-nni ad d-tecceḍ ad d-tuɣal ɣer deffir, armi d yiwet n tikkelt tuli tḍil i ṣṣur-nni, teḥbes zdat-s.

Sliɣ i TasaÆdit tenna-yi-d : « ṣaḥḥa a Meẓyan txedÆeḍ-iyi, tura teǧǧiḍ-iyi. ».

Nniɣ-as : « ur kem-xdiÆeɣ ara a TasaÆdit, aql- i la kem-ttraǧuɣ ur kem-ǧǧiɣ ara! »

Ufiɣ-d iman-iw lliɣ weḥd-i deg umkan-nni deg i teḥbes tkerrust. Telḥa-d yiwet n tlemẓit, mi d-telḥeq ɣer-i, nemsalam, tebda-d yid-i ameslay. Ḥulfeɣ ters-d yiwet n tayri gar-aneɣ muḥal ters-d gar wiyaḍ; ar dqal testaqsa-yi-d : « iruḥ-iyi-d uɣyul, ur t-twalaḍ ara ? ».

Nniɣ-as : « ur t-waleɣ ara a Werdiya. ».

Nelḥa d asawen kra n yisurrifen, waleɣ yiwen qrib d amɣar idda-d d uberdi n tlemẓit-nni.

Argaz-nni ssawalen-as AÆli-cciṭan. Tuɣal tlemẓit-nni la s-tettmeslay i winna nekk la s-ttmeslayeɣ tegguma ad d-tezzi ɣer-i ula s tmuɣli.

Mi waleɣ akken tedda di lǧerra n lǧenn-nni, ḥṣiɣ nekk mačči d ṣṣenÆa-w, jebdeɣ-d iman-iw ɣer deffir.

Ufiɣ-d lliɣ deg yiwen n umkan yettusemman ‘Amalu n LÆiṣer’. Sliɣ yekker wawal di tama n ufella. Mmuqleɣ waleɣ sin n yirgazen mlalen ad mseččawen deg yiwen n
umkan yettusemman ‘Ajerwiḍ’. Irgazen-nni, yiwen isem- is Sliman wayeḍ Muḥemmed. Myuṭṭafen. Tiyitiwin ulac. Lɣaci seg yal tama la d-ttazzalen akken ad ten-frun. Mi gemneɣ ad azzleɣ ɣer-sen, rran-d d akessar s umseččaw- nni-nsen. Leḥqen-d sin n yuɣyal ddan-d s umseččaw di tama n sin-nni n yirgazen. Mi qrib ad d-leḥqen ɣer-i, Sliman yetti-d d yiwen isem-is Lḥusin u Muḥ itbeÆ-it-id Muḥemmed; Lḥusin la s-ireggel. Uzzleɣ mmugreɣ-ten. Mi leḥqeɣ ɣer-sen, ufiɣ Muḥemmed akked yiwen isem-is Ḥmed, bedden la ttemxaṣamen. Uzgeɣ-d gar-asen ad ten- fruɣ s ṣṣwab.

Ufiɣ-d lliɣ zdat n umdun yettusemman ‘Amdun Ibehlal’. Yella ɣer-i ccrab i yi-d-yeǧǧa Muḥ ad t-zzenzeɣ. Llan yid-i sin n yilmeẓyen d arraw n laÆmum. Yiwen isem-is Remḍan wayeḍ Lḥusin ssawalen-as acur. Fehmeɣ-ten usan-d ad awin ccrab; rnu ḥṣiɣ ad iyi-d-inin ad sweɣ yid- sen. Nekk ma swiɣ yid-sen ilaq ad xellṣeɣ amur-iw. Idrimen ur sÆiɣ ara maḍi. Mi la nettnecraḥ, iban-iyi-d umeslay-nsen ɣef ccrab, ilaq ad sen-beddleɣ ameslay.

Yelḥeq-d yiwen akked ur Ædileɣ ara, yefka-iyi-d afus-is ad nemsalam; nemsalam, yemsalam akked sin-nni, Yenna- yasen : « ad d-nawi tlata n teqraÆtin n ccrab ad tent- nsew. ». Nniɣ-as : « ad d-nawi rebÆa n teqraÆtin ay AÆrab n Muḥ; yal yiwen ad ixelleṣ yiwet. ». Imir mi nemwafaq, qqimeɣ-d ḥareɣ acku ur bɣiɣ ara ad awiɣ tudayt, ur bɣiɣ ad awiɣ ṭṭlaba ɣef ccrab. Uɣaleɣ beddleɣ-asen awal. La nleḥḥu nettnecraḥ armi newweḍ ɣer yiwen n umkan yettusemman ’Iɣil n Lḥedd n Ccix’. Nelḥa ɣef yiɣil-nni,
