# Tameɣra n lmut

Ufiɣ lliɣ akked yiwen isem-is Lmulud d mmi-s n xali, nbedd di tlemmast n ufrag. Yemma yuɣ-itt lḥal terzef ɣer temdint n Lezzayer, waleɣ-tt tekcem-d di tewwurt, tenna-yi-d : « wwiɣ-ak-d lehdiyya a Meẓyan, rǧu ad ruḥeɣ ak-tt-id-awiɣ. ». Teffeɣ, tekcem-d, tewwi-d taqerÆet deg ufus-is teččur. Si lqaÆ ɣer tlemmast yettban-d wayen yellan daxel-is d amellal ; si tlemmast ɣer tqemmuct d aberkan.

Ṭṭfeɣ-d taqerÆet-nni, waleɣ azgen n wadda yeččur d ayefki, azgen n ufella d lqahwa. Lqahwa-nni xas ma tennaÆzal maca ṣubben seg-s kra n yiraqqen ttbanen-d deg uyefki-nni am tecbekt-nni n lkermus. Fehmeɣ am win iyi-d-yennan: ‚ḥader a Meẓyan, yemma-k d aÆeqqar n ssem i ak-d-tewwi.‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚amek akk-a? Wigi d iḥeckulen.‛. Tenna-yi-d: ‚ala a mmi, d lqahwa s uyefki.‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚lufan d lehdiyya tilli tefkiḍ-tt i Lmulud i tḥemmleḍ. Neɣ ma skidḍeɣ tasa-m ad aɣ-tt-tebḍuḍ lwaḥid. imi d aÆeqqar tbuddeḍ-iyi-t weḥd-i.‛. Tenna-yi-d: ‚rǧu ad uɣaleɣ ɣer berra, ad ak-id-awiɣ ttbut n lqahwa s uyefki.‛

Teffeɣ, itbeÆ-itt Lmulud, nniɣ-as: ‚ur tesÆiḍ s aniɣer ara teffɣeḍ, rǧu dagi alamma tuɣal-d ad nsew nekk yid-k ayen akka i d-tewwi.‛ Ur iyi-d-yesɣid ara, yeffeɣ di tewwurt, nniɣ-as: ‚trewleḍ ah, acku kečč teḥṣiḍ d aÆeqqar i d-tewwi ulamek teswiḍ.‛. Immuqel-iyi-d, yeḍsa-d ɣer-i, ikemmel tarewla-s. Ffɣeɣ di tewwurt akken ad t-id-ḥebseɣ, mlileɣ-
d akked yemma tefka-iyi-d taqerÆet-nni. Waleɣ-tt teččur d aman. Nniɣ-as: ‚D acu i iyi-d-tÆeqqreḍ deg waman-agi?‛. Tenna-yi-d: ‚ala a mmi, ma ur iyi-tumineḍ ara attan xalti-k Tasa n Muḥ ad tsew seg-s ad twaliḍ.‛ Ufiɣ-d tamɣart-nni temmɣi-d zdat-i, tefka-as taqerÆet-nni. Qerrbeɣ  ɣer-s akken   ad  as-greɣ  tamawt, Waleɣ-tt tessekcem iles-is di tqemmuct n tqerÆet, tesḍill amzun ad tsew, nniɣ-as: ‚kkes iles-im, tesḍilleḍ.‛. Tuɣal tessers imi n tqerÆet-nni ɣef yiles-is. Tikkelt tis tlata tessers-itt ɣef yimi-s, teḥmeẓ icenfiren-is tesḍill. Waleɣ   kra i d-yeffɣen si tqerÆet-nni yenɣel ɣef yidmaren n tɣeddart-nni, tiyersi-s waleɣ-tt ur la tessebleÆ ara. Mi tebteɣ ɣef taluft, nniɣ-as : « yezmer-am Rebbi a sstut. »

Zziɣ ɣer yemma, nniɣ-as: ‚lufan ad iyi-d-tban tafat, akken i iyi-tÆeqqreḍ ara kem-Æeqqreɣ.‛ Yeɣli-d ṭlam d  aseṭṭaf. Ǧǧiɣ timcumin-nni, uɣaleɣ s axxam. Mi kecmeɣ di tewwurt n ufrag, ufiɣ tafat tfeǧǧeǧ, nnur-is yugar win n yiṭij. Beddeɣ di tlemmast n ufrag mmuqleɣ ɣer tegnawt ad waliɣ ansi i d-tekka tafat-nni neɣ d acu i tt-id-yefkan, iban-iyi-d tusa-d d nnur kan! Sliɣ i tebburt teqqerbeb, mmuqleɣ  waleɣ-tt telddi-d iman-is weḥd-s xas akken tella tennemdal s leqfel. Kecmeɣ ɣer tzeqqa, ufiɣ tameṭṭut-iw tbedd di tlemmast n wagens.

Fehmeɣ-tt la tettraǧu deg-i, tenna-yi-d: ‚d acu n tafat-agi a Meẓyan?‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚d lawliya ara d-yasen ɣer-i   iḍ-agi a TasaÆdit. Ad  medleɣ   tawwurt, ad sserseɣ tiṭ-iw      ɣef texmujt-agi n leqfel, ad mmuqleɣ s afrag. Ma waleɣ d nutni ad ffɣeɣ ad ten-mmagreɣ.‛
Xedmeɣ am wakken i as-nniɣ. Mi ters Tiṭ-iw di texmujt-nni, tawwurt tebrireḥ-d. Nniɣ deg wul-iw : « tura ad ffɣeɣ mebla tuggdi, ad ten-mmagreɣ. ». Ffɣeɣ-d s afrag, ufiɣ-d iman-iw nnig laÆzi-nneɣ deg yiwen n wurti d ayla-w yettwasemma tamazirt ufella.

La leḥḥuɣ d asawen ɣer yiɣil ufella. Mlileɣ-d akked yiwen icuba di lewṣayef ɣer yiwen n Æemmi n berra yezdeɣ di temdint yettusemman Murad Rayes di tmanaɣt n Lezzayer. Argaz-nni yenna-yi-d : « aql-i usiɣ-d ɣer-k s axxam, mi d-nemlil dagi d leṣlaḥ, ad nuɣal kan syagi.‛.

Nemsalam, neddukel d asawen. Netta yezwar nekk la t-tabaÆeɣ. Ur t-ḥṣiɣ d anwa-t neɣ d acu i d-yeqṣed ɣer-i wala s aniɣer i la nteddu. Nelḥa armi newweḍ ɣer yiwen n umalu n uzemmur. Di tama ufella-s d axxam n yiḍulan-iw. Nufa sin n yilmeẓyen, neṭqen-d ɣer winna akked ddiɣ, nnan-as : « lÆeslama a Æemmi Muḥ u Qasi. ».

Mi tebbteɣ d netta i d winna iɣer icuba, nniɣ-as : « ziɣ d kečč i d Æemmi Muḥ. Nekk ur k-Æqileɣ ara armi d tura.‛.

Netta yerra kan abrid gar wallen-is: ur yerri ara sslam i sin-nni, ur d-yenṭiq, ur d-yezzi s tmuɣli-s ɣer-i. Mi t-fehmeɣ yeqsed s axxam n yiḍulan-iw, ur bɣiɣ ara ad yerr ɣer din. Maca ssetḥeɣ as-iniɣ ur nkeccem ara. Ddiɣ akken di lewhi-s. Mi yewweḍ ɣer tewwurt n ufrag, yekcem kecmeɣ yid-s.

Deg ufrag-nni waleɣ llant tlata n texxamin d adur ttwabnant s lebni d ajdid. Sliɣ yekker daxel-nsent umeslay s teɣri n tlawin d warrac imeẓyanen. Waleɣ tameṭṭut n uḍeggal-iw teqqim zdat n tewwurt n tzeqqa terra lǧefna
gar yiḍarren-is am tin i la ifettlen. Mi nÆedda tama n texxamin-nni, tilawin-nni nnant-aɣ-d lÆeslama-nwen. Nekk rriɣ-asent, argaz-nni yellan yid-i yessusem. Mmuqleɣ ɣer tlawin-nni, waleɣ-tent cebḥit rnant zeyynent iman-nsent. Tameṭṭut-iw tbedd-d weḥd-s ɣef tewwurt n yiwet n texxamt; waleɣ-tt tecbeḥ aṭas terna tga lekḥul n taẓult taberkant. Sliɣ tenna-yi-d: « lÆeslama a Meẓyan. » Waleɣ Æemmi Muḥ yelḥeq ɣer tmeṭṭut n uḍeggal-iw, tenna-as-d lÆeslama, msalamen.

Lḥiɣ ɣer-s. mi leḥqeɣ, tṣubb aqerruy-is. Mmuqleɣ-tt, waleɣ imezran-is bran, udem-is yumes d injan, lǧefna-nni d tilemt<rǧiɣ ad iyi-d-tini lÆeslama. Imi ulac, muddeɣ-as afus-iw, nemsalam sslam asellaw, wexxreɣ-d fell-as. ḍḥiɣ-d bateɣ di tmeṭṭut-nni; ma d inebgi-nni ur tebɣi ara mi t-wwiɣ ɣer-sen! Hatan waleɣ testerḥeb yes-s; ssebba-nniḍen ur tt-fhimeɣ ara ula d Lḥala-nni deg i tt-ufiɣ kifkif. Nniɣ deg wul-iw: ‚ma d inebgi-agi wicqa, ad neqqim dagi di laÆḍil ad truḥ TasaÆdit s axxam-nneɣ ad seggmeɣ akk lḥala. Imir ad nruḥ nekni.‘.

Waleɣ inebgi-nni la yettawi yettrra deg ufrag. Tezga-d tmuɣli-w di texxamt n usewwi, waleɣ lkanun ulac deg-s ula d iɣiɣden; di tzeqqa daɣen kifkif. Nniɣ-d deg wul-iw: ‚amek a Rebbi? Anida ara ssɣimeɣ inebgi-agi? Kecmeɣ ɣer tzeqqa, lḥiɣ ɣer terkkent, siwleɣ i yinebgi-nni, nniɣ-as ad d-yekcem. Uqbel ad sɣimeɣ iman-iw, waleɣ aḍuggal-iw isem-is Muḥd u isa ibedd di tlemmast n ufrag. Sliɣ yenna-yi-d: ‚ulayɣer i tesɣimeḍ iman-ik a Meẓyan, atan yinebgi-agi iḍaq ad iruḥ.‘
Ffɣeɣ-d s afrag, yenna-yi-d Muḥ: ‚atan la k-yettraǧu tama n tewwurt. Yenna-yi-d usiɣ-d kan ad ẓreɣ Meẓyan ad ruḥeɣ.‛. Lḥiɣ ɣer tewwurt n ufrag, ufiɣ inebgi-nni yerǧa-yi. Neffeɣ si tewwurt-nni, nufa sin n yirgazen di berra la ɣ-ttrǧun. Waleɣ lsan ibernas d icebḥanen am lukfen-nni n lmeyyet, rnan qqnen ticucay tizewwaɣin sÆant tacerrabt n tesfift. Nemsalam nebda tikli, nerra d asawen la nleḥḥu wa zdat wa.

emmi Muḥ yezwer, nekk d aneggaru, sin-nni di tlemmast. Ilemmasen-nni leḥqen ulin deg yiwet n tsawent testiwen am lḥiḍ. Nekk akken leḥqeɣ ad aliɣ, uɣalen-d ɣer deffir, nbedd rran-iyi gar-asen, la nleḥḥu tayet ɣer tayet. Nebda tikli, bdan-iyi-d ameslay. Yenṭeq-d yiwen yenna-yi-d : « tura ula d sseḥra ad as-rren lewzir, ula d sselṭan n leqbayel la ttarun isem-is ula ɣef tqabsiwt n cemma. ».

Wis sin yessewÆed ɣer winna yezwaren, yenna-yi-d : « Winna d Æemmi-k Muḥ. ».

Uzzleɣ. Mi leḥqeɣ ɣer-s, nniɣ-as: ‚ziɣ kečč d Æemmi Muḥ nekk ur k-Æqileɣ ara! Welleh armi sliɣ nnan-ak-id lÆeslama a Æemmi Muḥ i k-Æeqleɣ!‛. Nbedd armi i d-leḥqen sin-nni-nniḍen, Æemmi Muḥ yenna-yi-d: ‚aql-i Æerḍeɣ-k ɣer tmeɣra ‘mai’, ssebt akked lḥed. Balak ur d-tettaseḍ ara.‛.

Nniɣ-as: ‚kečč d Æemmi Muḥ, nekk welleh ma Æeqleɣ-k armi d tura !‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚aql-i Æerḍeɣ-k ɣer tmeɣra ‘mai’, ass n lḥedd. Balak ur d-tettaseḍ ara. Axaṭer d kečč ara yeddun di tkerrust tamezwarut ara d-yawin tislit.‛.

Nniɣ-as: ‚aql-i-in ad n-aseɣ. Maca ard jiǧweɣ zzit, tura ur sÆiɣ ara idrimen.‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚aql-i Æerḍeɣ-k ɣer tmeɣra,
mai’ ass n lḥedd. D kečč ara yeddun di tkerrust tamezwarut ara d-yawin tislit. Nniɣ-as: ‚aql-i-in ad n-aseɣ ma irad Rebbi!‛

Ukiɣ-d si targit !

1981

Tenna-d TasaÆdit

Ufiɣ-d iman-iw lliɣ deg uxxam n mmi-s n Æemmi, tella yid-i tmeṭṭut n gma, yelli-s n Æemmi akked tmeṭṭut n Æemmi. Waleɣ gma Muḥed u isa yeddukkel-d akked mmi-s n Æemmi-s Muḥ n isa. Muḥ n isa yewwi-d ticabcaqin n sserdin deg ufus-is. Ulin-d tlata n trekkadin, leḥqen-d qrib ɣer tewwurt, nnan-yi-d: ‚Kečč a Meẓyan telliḍ la tettawiḍ tettarraḍ deg wagens!‛ Nekk fehmeɣ-d gma mi d-yedda d mmi-s n Æemmi, yusa-d akken ad ken-yessaÆdel deg umgared yellan gar-ak d Muḥ n isa. Maca mi d-kecmen, kečč teffɣeḍ.

Mmi-s-nni n Æemmi yefka-as tacabcaqt n sserdin i tmeṭṭut n gma. Tegguma ad tt-teṭṭef, tenna-as: ‚sserdin n tcabcaqt yessehlak-iyi.‛ Yusa-d ɣer-i gma yenna-yi-d: ‚ax a TasaÆdit ad teččeḍ sserdin n tcabcaqt.‛ Nniɣ-as: ‚ala, ur t-ḥemmleɣ ara. ». Yelli-s-nni n Æemmi tefka-yi-d nnefṣ n
texbizt tamejṭuḥt. Ṭṭfeɣ-tt-id, winna yehwa-yi-d xas ad t-ččeɣ d aḥerfi. Sliɣ tenna-yi-d: ‚yehwa-as kan i Meẓyan yeffeɣ yugi ad yečč sserdin, wamma ur tesÆiḍ lxilaf yellan gar-as d Muḥemmed. Ala ciṭ-nni kan akked Ḥewwa.‛

Ukiɣ-d si targit !

1981

A d-yas lḥeqq Ufiɣ-d iman-iw deg yiwen n wurti yettusemman ‘Aguni n At Cennad’ la leḥḥuɣ deg ubrid n uḍar yellan d aneṣli. Lḥiɣ armi leḥqeɣ ɣer wanda yemlil ubrid-nni s abrid n ukerrus, ufiɣ-d lliɣ deg umkan ansi bdiɣ tikli. Uɣaleɣ la leḥḥuɣ ɣer tama-nniḍen qesdeɣ ɣer taddart-iw.

Mi bdiɣ tikli, zegreɣ i yiwen n yiɣzer, leḥqeɣ ɣer yiwet n tsawent yecban lḥiḍ. Tama n tsawent-nni llan yixeddamen la ttɣizin tagnit i lebni ajdid. Gar-asen Æeqleɣ yiwen d mmi-s n xali isem-is miruc. Mi yi-d-yeẓra, yeččeḥ-d tamuɣli-s deg-i. Iban-iyi-d swehmeɣ-t aṭas. Lwehma-nni fehmeɣ tenna-yi-d: ‚Meẓyan yeɣra aṭas, yeffeɣ-d d amussnaw, yerna di tallit-nni deg yella d anelmad ulac win iÆelmen yes-s amek iga wakk-a!‛

- 200 -
Mi bdiɣ alluy di tsawent-nni, isuma-iyi-d Æeggu, ḥulfeɣ kkawen yifadden-iw. La ttarreɣ tirrugza maca yugar-itt Æeggu-nni. Mi uliɣ s rebÆa n yisurrifen, ad d-ccḍeɣ, ad d-uɣaleɣ ɣer deffir s tmanya. Teḍra yid-i am win i yeɣleb ssekkran; Æerḍeɣ aṭas n tikkal akken ad aliɣ, alluy d lmuḥal. Mi sliɣ i teḍsa, mmuqleɣ ɣer yidis-iw, waleɣ d yiwen n urgaz ur nemÆin i la yettaḍsan deg-i mi i d-iwala tikli-nni n tuccḍa iɣil-iyi sekkreɣ. ḍsiɣ ɣer-s, heggeɣ iman-iw nnig tezmert-iw, ẓedmeɣ s leɣseb uliɣ, mi neṣṣfeɣ tasawent-nni, ccḍeɣ-d armi d amkan-nni seg bdiɣ tazzla. ḥsbeddeɣ-d iman-iw waleɣ yekker uɣebbar. argaz-nni daɣen yeḍsa fell-i. ḍsiɣ ɣer-s nniɣ-as: 'tikkelt-agi yekker uɣebbar.'

Ufiɣ-d iman-iw nnig tsawent-nni, abrid d ugdis. Lḥiɣ kra n yisurrifen ufiɣ ixxamen d ijdiden di tlemmast n ubrid-nni. Ixxamen-nni n winna yeḍsan deg-i, icrek-iten akked waggaw-is. Tawwurt n ufrag tqubel-d s abrid tettwaxdem s yicebbaken n wuzzal. Beddeɣ zdat n tewwurt-nni, waleɣ kra n telmeẓyin deg usqif n uxxam-nni lsant talaba n temdint. Mi iyi-d-walant, uẓant-d ɣer tewwurt la d-ttsiggint ɣer-i. Nniɣ-d: 'tigi mačči n dagi, ad ilint d tinerzufa. Fehmeɣ di teɣri n targit tenna-d: 'axxam-agi alamma tÆeddaḍ seg tewwurt-nni, ad tleḥqeḍ s afrag akken ara tafeḍ abrid ɣer zdat. Yerna at uxxam-agi ttasmen, teggen meḥyaf di lɣaci. Win ara walin yesÆa cci neɣ lǧehd n tayet ad as-gen abrid ad iÆeddi seg ufrag. Ma d win yenḥafen, xas yettwalam-iten atan zerrben-as abrid.'

Ḥulfeɣ s ajajiḥ n tmes deg wul-iw. Waleɣ yiwet n
temɣart tbedd-d tama n tewwurt-nni isem-is Tasa n Muḥ, d lalt n uxxam-nni. Mmuqleɣ ɣer yal tama ansi ara afeɣ amḍiq ad Æeddiɣ, ulac. Uɣaleɣ la sṭebṭubeɣ di tewwurt-nni armi rfiɣ urrif d aqesḥan. Ddehmeɣ tawwurt-nni, telddi-d. teffeɣ-d temɣart-nni, bdiɣ yid-s amqases, nniɣ-as: ‚ur tuggadem ara Rebbi tebnam-d deg ubrid. Tzerrbem abrid i lɣaci; akken ad ruḥeɣ qbala yeqreb-iyi ubrid, ma akka alamma nnḍeɣ-d i ddunit!‛. Tenna-yi-d: ‚ala nekni i yettalasen deg ubrid-agi: win i yi-yehwan ad as-ǧǧeɣ abrid ad iÆeddi seg ufrag ma yella win ur i yi-nehwi ara ur yettÆeddi ara, axaṭer ur yettalas ara abrid.‛.

Nniɣ-as: ‚ur ssimɣur ara aqemmuc-im. Xas akka tugareḍ-iyi di laÆmer, ugareɣ-kem di tmussni. Cfiɣ-d i wayen i wumi ur d-tecfiḍ ara. Abrid-agi d abrid n medden irkelli, d abrid aneṣli. Medden akk ttalasen deg-s, d adaxli neɣ d aberrani.‛

Yeffeɣ-d yiwen n umɣar d aslif n temɣart-nni. Yewwi-d yid-s ssniwa n yifenǧalen ččuren d lqahwa. Yelḥeq-d ɣer-i, yefka-iyi-d afenǧal, yenna-yi-d: ‚ax tura ad tesweḍ lqahwa.‛. Fehmeɣ-t d aḥiwet mi iwala rfiɣ ɣef temɣart-nni. Ṭṭfeɣ-d afenjal-nni, waleɣ-t ur yewwiḍ ara anect n tjuɣlalt n uÆarus.

Ufiɣ-d lliɣ deg yiwet n texxamt deg uxxam-nni. Amɣar-nni d tmeṭṭut-is qqimen sennden ɣer lḥiḍ. Tamɣart-nni teqqim di tlemmast n wagens tqubel-d ɣer-i. Afenǧal-nni yers gar-aneɣ. Nekk llhiɣ la ttqasiɣ ɣef lebni-nni n tlemmast n ubrid. Sḍuleɣ yid-s ameslay ur d-llhiɣ ara d lqahwa-nni. Yennelqem-d umɣar-nni akken ad iyi-d-yefk
afenǧal-nni s afus-iw. Mmɣeɣ ɣef ufenǧal-nni refdeɣ-t-id, sḍilleɣ-t s yiwet n tejɣimt. Tiniḍ lqahwa-nni d aman n yifelfel, neṭqeɣ s amɣar-nni nniɣ-as : « cikkeɣ lqahwa-agi deg-s aÆeqqar. Ini-d kan ma yella kra i as-tgiḍ. Welleh ar deg yiḍ-agi ara ṭṭfeɣ takerrust.‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚ur tesÆiḍ i as-giɣ, akka kan i qerrḥet lqahwa-agi.‛

Waleɣ yiwet n tlemẓit si twacult n uxxam-nni tella deg ufrag teṭṭef tamedwast deg ufus-is amzun la teṭṭummu, nettat tefka-d tameẓẓuɣt ɣer-neɣ. Zziɣ ɣer temɣart-nni, ufiɣ-d beddleɣ amkan uɣaleɣ qqimeɣ ɣer tewwurt n texxamt-nni qubleɣ-d ɣer daxel n texxamt. Tilemẓit-nni teṭṭinez-d ɣef tuyat-iw tessers-d ssniwa n yifenǧalen zdat-i la d-tessurug lqahwa. Ḥulfeɣ tennul-iyi-d s yicimmi-s. Sliɣ i wul-is la iḥebbek la tettarra nnefs s usnexfet am tin yerfan aṭas, neɣ tin irun aṭas.

Mi yi-d-tennul akken, ssetḥeɣ! Xas ma walmen-iyi wat uxxam-nni; ḥṣiɣ ur ttasmen ara fell-i. Sebreɣ s leḥya-nni armi tfuk asureg, teswexxer iman-is, tefka-asen ifenǧalen i wid-nni yeqqimen yid-i. Yegra-d yiwen n ufenǧal i yi-d-iṣaḥen, terfed-it sliɣ tenna-d: ‚rǧu ad sweɣ seg ufenǧal-agi ma ulac Meẓyan ad yeṭṭef takerrust deg yiḍ-agi.‛

Uqbel ad yaweḍ ufenǧal-nni ɣer yimi-s, kkseɣ-as-ti-d, nniɣ-as: ‚welleh ma teswiḍ ma swiɣ-tt.‛. Teḍsa-d ɣer-i mi tefhem sÆiɣ deg-s laman. Sserseɣ afenǧal-nni zdat-i. Ufiɣ-d sin n yilmeẓyen qqimen ɣer yidis-iw. Fehmeɣ-ten la ttraǧun ad swen lqahwa. Mmuqleɣ zdat-i, waleɣ aqedduḥ d aqdim yennugdam, rsen sufella-s sin n lkisan ččuren d llatay, gar-asen yella ufenǧal-nni-inu. Bɣiɣ ad asen-fkeɣ lkisan i
yilmeẓyen-nni ad swen maca llhiɣ d umqases ɣef ubrid-nni, armi waleɣ lkisan-nni malen qrib ad nneɣlen, nniɣ-as i temɣart-nni : ‚ur tettu ara . Ilaq ad teḥṣuḍ ad d-yaweḍ wass n lḥeqq.‛. Yiwen seg sin-nni n yilmeẓyen yenna-yi-d: ‚Ɣurk lkisan-nni ad nneɣlen.‛

Mmɣeɣ ɣef lkisan-nni qaÆdeɣ-ten, waleɣ ttin-d yiwen n seg-sen ! ddmeɣ-d afenǧal-nni n lqahwa, fkiɣ-as-t i yiwen n yilemẓi i-yeqqimen deffir-iw ɣef yiwet n tɣalaṭ. Taɣalaṭ-nni tessiÆli-t armi i d-yufrar nnig-iw. Mi yeṭṭef afenǧal-nni, zziɣ ɣer temɣart-nni nniɣ-as : « welleh lÆaḍim ar d-yas wass n lḥeqq ; d acu kan yebÆed, am wakken ad twaliḍ, ssya ɣer Bumehni, win yelsan talaba tamellalt.‛

Winna i wumi fkiɣ afenǧal-nni yenna-yi-d: ‚am wakken ara twaliḍ ssya ɣer uÆerqub-inna agemmaḍ.‛. Zziɣ ɣer-s nniɣ-as: ‚mačči ɣer uÆerqub-inna, maca welleh lÆaḍim ur nesÆi acrik neɣ amÆiwen ard d-yas wass n lḥeqq am wakken ara twaliḍ bu tlaba mellulen ssya ɣer umadaɣ n Bumehni.‛. Zziɣ ɣer temɣart-nni, kemmleɣ yid-s tazwayt.

Sliɣ i yilemẓi-nni wis sin yenna-d: ‚ur as-tehwi ara lqahwa-nni. Yefka-iyi-d afenǧal-nni, ṭṭfeɣ-t-id.‛. Sliɣ i yilemẓi-nni wis sin yenna-d: ‚yufa deg-s dduru.‛. Ddmeɣ-d lkas-nni n llatay, fkiɣ-as-t i winna i d-yerran afenǧal-nni.

Greɣ aḍad-iw ccached ɣer daxel n ufenǧal-nni akken ad waliɣ ma yekkes dduru-nni i t-id-yesɣulfen neɣ yunef-as daxel. Ufiɣ afenǧal-nni yezgen s ssakker! Nniɣ-d: ‚amer urÆad iḥerrek!‛ Mi Æerḍeɣ lqahwa-nni, ufiɣ ẓidet, ssakker-nni d zzyada.
Zziɣ ɣer yilemẓi-nni, nniɣ-as: ‚azgen d lqahwa, azgen d ssakker, kečč tufiḍ-tt ẓidet! D ssebba-nniḍen. kan axaṭer ur tḥemmleḍ ara tiẓeḍt.‛. Ilemẓi-nni yessusem. Zziɣ s amɣar-nni nniɣ-as ‚twalaḍ lqahwa-agi i yi-d-tefka tlemẓit-agi? Azgen d lqahwa azgen d ssakker.d ẓtidet yerna urÆad tḥerrek.‛. Yeḍsa, yenna-yi-d: ‚axaṭer tebɣa ad k-tḍurr.‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚tiẓeḍt ur tettḍurru ara. D abuddu i yi-tbudd. acku teḥṣa-iyi d argaz aḥeqqi, teẓra d acu i d lqima-w. mačči am kečč ay aÆdaw n lḥeqq, tefkiḍ-iyi-d lqahwa d taqerḥant.‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚tḥemmel-ik axaṭer tecfa ɣef lxir-ik asmi i ten-tettÆawaneḍ<‛. Mi gemneɣ ad t-jawbeɣ, uqbel ad neṭqeɣ s lejwab-nni, sliɣ-as ɣer yiwen n umsafer i d-iÆeddan deg ubrid-nni zdat n uxxam ileḥḥu yeqqar: ‚lellah fi sabili llah<‛. Neṭqeɣ s amɣar-nni nniɣ-as ‚ssɣed kan amek akka i la yeqqar umeɣbun-agi!‛. Waleɣ udem-is yuɣal d awraɣ, tufrar fell-as lḥecma. Imi-s yeldi, awal ifuk-as. Nekk mi t-waleɣ akken, ad sweɣ tajɣimt si lqahwa-nni taẓidant, ad t-mmuqleɣ ad d-iniɣ: ‚welleh a ẓidet lqahwa-agi<‛. Netta teddukkel-as lḥecma d wurfan. Ddiɣ-tt akken fell-as armi i d-igar nnehta ḥulfeɣ tessenhez axxam-nni. Neṭqeɣ nniɣ-as: ‚nniɣ-ak ad d-yas lḥeqq.

Ukiɣ-d si targit !

Lesrar n tegnawt

Sliɣ i teɣri n ttilifun truḥ-d deg umeẓẓuɣ-iw. Ar dqal yenṭeq-d urgaz yenna-d: ‚alu, alu, a Meẓyan, melmi ara truḥeḍ ɣer Fransa?‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚melmi irad Rebbi.‛ Yessusem. Uɣaleɣ ssiwleɣ-as melba ttilifun, nniɣ-as: ‚ansi akka i la d-tettetilifuniḍ?‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚acuɣer? AÆni tebɣiḍ ad d-taseḍ ɣer-i.‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚ih, bɣiɣ ad n-aseɣ.‛.

Ufiɣ-d lliɣ d urgaz-nni deg yiwet n temdint ur ssineɣ. Mi nemsalam, nniɣ-as : « tura ad iyi-d-tcareḍ, ad iyi-d-tiniḍ ma ad awḍeɣ lebɣi-w ad ssiwḍeɣ lÆahed-iw.‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚d acu ara k-iniɣ, yya-n a k-awiɣ ɣer zdat ad tafeḍ win ara k-id-icaren.‛

Lḥiɣ yid-s kra n yisurrifen, neffeɣ seg temdint-nni, newweḍ ɣer yiwet n taddart n tmezduɣin tiqdimin yettwabnan s wakal. Di tlemmast n taddart-nni yella ubrid yewsaÆ tiniḍ d abraḥ. Nelḥa kra n yisurrifen deg ubrid-nni, ufiɣ-d iman-iw nleqmeɣ s wafug. Leḥqeɣ ɣer zdat, ufiɣ-d timezduɣin di tlemmast n ubrid-nni. Ageffur la d-yekkat d lgirra. Rseɣ-d ɣer tmurt, uɣaleɣ ufgeɣ rseɣ sufella n ssqef n yiwen n uxxam. La tedduɣ s tikli d wafug. Tikwal rennuɣ-as agrireb sufella n tmezduɣin-nni.

Mi ffɣeɣ i taddart-nni, leḥqeɣ ɣer yiwen n yifri lqay aṭas. Mmuqleɣ ɣer lqaÆa-is, iban-iyi-d d agudu i yettwaxedmen d ifri. Beddeɣ ɣer yiri ufella, ufiɣ-d ɣer yidis-iw yiwen n urgaz yestmeɣren, isem-is Ḥmed n SsaÆid, ssawalen-as AwdiÆ. Neṭqeɣ nniɣ-as: ‚ay awdiÆ, d wagi i d lebɣi-w, d
wagi i d asiweḍ n lÆahed-iw! S agudu i yi-d-ssiwḍen?‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚yak aql-ik temmuteḍ.‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚d tagi i d laxert.‛. Yetti-d d yiwen n yilemẓi isem-is Lḥusin, ssawalen-as acur. Nbedd zdat n yiwen n umadaɣ ur yettwalḥaq ara ula s tmuɣli: yewsaÆ aṭas, deg-s ala isekla n usennan. Steqseɣ ilemẓi-nni nniɣ-as: ‚anida i tella lǧennet a acur?‛. YessewÆed s uḍad-is ccahed s amadaɣ-nni, yenna-yi-d : « ɣer zdat-inna. ». Nniɣ-as: ‚yalleh ad nruḥ ɣer lǧennet.‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚yebÆed lḥal yerna uggadeɣ.‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚ur ttuggad ara, aql-in ɣer tama-k, yerna ad nruḥ s wafug alamma newweḍ. Yya-n tbeÆ-iyi-d, ttkel ɣef Rebbi.‛

Negzeɣ s amadaɣ-nni ur ḥṣiɣ amek ara teḍru yid-i. Ufiɣ-d la ttafgeɣ, ilemẓi-nni yedda-d di tama-w s waffug. Nebda ameslay nniɣ-as: ‚yak nniɣ-ak ur ttuggad, ttkel ɣef Rebbi ad nafeg.‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚welleh ard ṣṣeḥ.‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚maca yebÆed lḥal. Aṭas uya i d-nufeg ur nelḥiq ara.‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚tura ad nelḥeq. Qrib ad naweḍ. Atan la tettwaliḍ ɣer tmurt ahicur aleqqaq akked yijeǧǧigen. Sya i tebda lǧennet. Yya-n ad ners ɣer tmurt ad nelḥu d imerraḥen.‛

Waleɣ nelḥa-d amadaɣ-nni ɣer deffir, nekcem ɣer yiwet n ssaḥelt anida i d-tenneqḍaÆ deg-s tmuɣli tiniḍ tennul igenni. Ners nelḥa kra n yisurrifen, nelḥeq ɣer yiwen n wasif yewsaÆ aṭas, iruḥ srid. Asif-nni fehmeɣ-t d lebḥer. Aman-is ttwaliɣ d nnur am nnur n yiṭij. Nbedd zdat n wasif-nni, neṭqeɣ ɣer acur, nniɣ-as: ‚qqim ak-id-afeɣ dagi, nekk ad kemmleɣ ɣer zdat ad waliɣ lebḥer-agi ansi i d-yenneqḍaÆ.‛. Nniɣ-d s yes-k a Rebbi, nleqmeɣ s waffug
la tedduɣ nnig wasif-nni. Meskud ttaẓeɣ ɣer zdat ttwaliɣ yettzad nnur-nni, rnu ttÆelliɣ ɣer tegnawt. Asif-nni yettaẓ-d ɣer-i armi ḥulfeɣ kecmeɣ leɣmuq n tegnawt, nniɣ-d: ‚ilaq ad uɣaleɣ ssyagi, d lÆib fell-i ad waliɣ lesrar n Rebbi. Win yettqennÆen yerwa; win yerwan yeɣna-t Rebbi.‛

Uɣaleɣ-d armi d amkan-nni seg i nleqmeɣ s waffug. Mi wwḍeɣ, ufiɣ arfiq-nni ulac-it, nniɣ-d: ‚yuɣal ɣer ddunit.‛ kemmleɣ affug-iw, qesdeɣ tuɣalin ɣer wansi i d-kkiɣ. Leḥqeɣ s anida i d-ufiɣ tawwurt d tameqqrant zdat n yiwen n usqif. Ffɣeɣ di tewwurt-nni, rseɣ ɣer lqaÆa, beddeɣ, zziɣ mmuqleɣ ɣer tewwurt-nni, waleɣ yella yiwen n uÆekkaz n wuzzal zdat-s.

Uqbel tuffɣa seg-s, aÆekkaz-nni yemÆidel am winna yettilin deg ubrid n tmacint deg usqif-nni llan tlata n yiÆessasen d iÆsekriyen. Leslaḥ ulac ɣur-sen. Ttwaliɣ deg-sen d ucmiten i tlata, d iseṭṭafen rnu xerbent lewṣayef-nsen. Wid-nni fehmeɣ-ten d nutni i d-yettarran win iruḥen ad iÆeddi ɣer lǧennet ma ur yesÆi ara lekwaɣeḍ n wanef ad iÆeddi.

Lḥan-d sin n yimdanen akken ad kecmen di tewwurt-nni. Mi leḥqen ɣer yiÆessasen-nni, waleɣ fkan-asen lekwaɣeḍ. Mmuqleɣ-ten, rran-asen-d lekwaɣeḍ-nni, rran-ten-id ɣer deffir gguman ad asen-anfen ad Æeddin. Nekk fehmeɣ-d imdanen-nni mačči d lekwaɣeḍ iṣeḥḥan i wwin yid-sen.

Nniɣ-d deg wul-iw: ‚d acu-ten wigi! Lufan d iÆessasen d tagi i d lxedma-nsen. Amek armi nekk mi d-Æeddeɣ ur ten-id-ufiɣ ara.‛ Waleɣ iÆessasen-nni llhan d umeslay gar-asen, ula d yiwen deg-sen mačči yerfed-d tamuɣli-s ɣer-i. Uɣaleɣ meyyzeɣ, nniɣ-d: ‚amer d wigi i wumi qqaren
Æezrayen.‛ Meyyzeɣ akken-nniḍen, nniɣ-d: ‚Rebbi war acrik. ezrayen n lxelq d lexdayem-is. Wigi ad ilin d yir lexdayem i d-iḥebbsen bab-nsen ur ikeccem ara ɣer lǧennet.‛. Waleɣ zzin-d ɣer-i la yi-d-smuqulen, nekk rfiɣ fell-asen. Ččḥeɣ deg-sen tamuɣli s wurfan, neṭqeɣ nniɣ-asen: ‚nekk ttsetḥiɣ rnu ḥnineɣ, maca lufan d nekk i ken-id-yufan ɣer tewwurt-nni mi d-Æeddeɣ, aken-wteɣ aken-tawi tyita mebÆid, ad Æeddiɣ.‛

Banen-iyi-d wudmawen-nsen tiniḍ s talaxt i ttwameslen. Nniɣ-d deg wul-iw: ‚wigi d yir lefÆayel neɣ d imdanen-nni meslen s talaxt ttÆebbiden-ten. D wigi i wumi qqaren yimaziɣen n zik ‘Musa n talaxt. ». Waleɣ udmawen-nsen ttin-d tiniḍ d ijeqduren n talaxt. Ččḥeɣ tamuɣli-w deg-sen, ttwaliɣ-ten la yettrab lexyal-nsen armi ifak uɣalen d ulac.

Ukiɣ-d si targit !

1981

Tiɣri n yiseɣ

Ufiɣ-d iman-iw beddeɣ ddaw n ufrag-nneɣ nnig tčinat, sliɣ i teɣri n Lewnis At Mengellat la icennu : ay afrux ttkel fell-i am wakken i ttekleḍ ɣef lǧedra n ttejra

Fkiɣ tameẓẓuɣt akken ad ḥṣuɣ ansi i d-tekka teɣri-

- 209 -
nni. Daɣen la smuquleɣ anida ara waliɣ rradyu-nni i deg fehmeɣ la d-icennu. Mmuqleɣ ɣer tama ukessar, tezga-d tmuɣli-w di Lewnis yeqqim ɣef ukersi nnig ttejra n txuxet, la icennu di ccna-nni ay afrux&lt;

Waleɣ yiwen n ufrux d areqman la itenneḍ ɣef yifurkawen n txuxet-nni. Taxuxet-nni mejṭuḥet, lǧedra-s teqwa, lɣella-s tuffay, tiÆeqqayin-is ttbanent-d s ṣṣifa n wureɣ. Lewnis la icennu yettÆawad i ufrux-nni akken ad d-yers ad yečč si lxir-nni. Afrux-nni fehmeɣ-t yuggad, ma yerna taÆkkemt-is ɣef ufurek ad yarreẓ yes-s, dɣa la yettferfir kan itenneḍ. Rniɣ fehmeɣ-t ma yers ɣef leǧdra ikukra si Lewnis. Ma d nekk mi ttwaliɣ akken d ccna kan akked ccḍeḥ, greɣ tamuɣli-w mebÆid ɣer yiwen n umadaɣ yellan ugemmaḍ iqubel-d s afrag-nneɣ, nniɣ-d : « amer ad waliɣ ifrax yecban wagi deg umadaɣ-inna. Ahat ad asen-yessiwel ufrux-agi ad d-asen ɣer-s. Mi ssiwḍen tarbaÆt, ad twensen.‛

Iban-iyi-d Meẓyan ibedd zdat umadaɣ-nni. Yelsa talaba n tserdast, yeṭṭef lmaṭ gar yifassen-is. Ttwaliɣ-t s yitran n wureɣ ɣef tuyat-is. Imir yeččur-d wul-iw d lferḥ mi ttwaliɣ di nnif akked lḥerma&lt; uɣaleɣ nniɣ-d deg wul-iw: ‚acuɣef akka Meẓyan iččeḥ tmuɣli-s s amadaɣ? La ttwaliɣ yebɣa ad yekcem s amadaɣ. Maca iban-iyi-d yetweḥḥec ! Mi wehmeɣ akken, fehmeɣ-d i targit tenna-d: ‚Meẓyan la ttnadin fell-as yiÆdawen-is, semman-as ‚imenfi‛ imi ula d yiwen seg tagmat-is ur yelli ɣer tama-s‛.

Ḥulfeɣ yeɣli-d ṭṭlam n lxiq deg wul-iw. Rnu iɣaḍ-iyi lḥal. Rriɣ-d tamuɣli-w s afrux-nni, waleɣ-t yers ɣef lǧedra n
txuxet-nni iqubel iman-is ɣer Lewnis la t-yesmuqul. Lewnis la icennu, afrux-nni la yesɣad. Rriɣ tamuɣli-w ɣer Meẓyan, waleɣ-t yekcem s amadaɣ-nni, yebda tikli si rrif n wadda la ileḥḥu d asawen. Ttwaliɣ deg-s yenḥaf nnig lḥif. La yettcerrig abrid deg yisennanen. Tikkelt ad yecceḍ, tikkelt ad yeɣli<Ma d nekk la ttneẓẓifeɣ fell-as qqareɣ: ‚yebɣa ad yawi Lezzayer ɣef uqerruy-s.‛. Waleɣ-t yewweḍ s tikli ɣer yiwet n tiɣilt yellan tufrar di tlemmast n umadaɣ-nni. Ibedd, yemmuqel ɣer tegnawt. Sliɣ-as isuɣ s yiwet n teɣri iɣef ur tettili ara tÆuẓẓegt, Yenna-d: ‚ay imawlan n yiseɣ, ilit yid-i.‛

Tiɣri-nni tejmeÆ-d aṭas n yirgazen, tessemɣi-ten-id deg umadaɣ-nni, waleɣ-ten ula d nutni lsan talaba am tinna yelsa Meẓyan, fehmeɣ-ten d imeddukkal-is. Rniɣ waleɣ zzin fell-as d ameqyas rran-t di tlemmast-nsen, la sen-yettmeslay. Ul-iw yeččur-d d lferḥ. Lferḥ-nni yesuki-iyi-d.

Ukiɣ-d si targit !

TasaÆdit 1981

Lḥeqq d idammen Ufiɣ-d iman-iw lliɣ deg yiwen umkan yettusemman ‚Idezza n At CaÆban‛. Llan yid-i tlata n
yilmeẓyen. Nbedd nnig ubrid d aqdim. Gar yilmeẓyen-nni, yella yiwen n taddart-iw, d aderɣal isem-is AÆmer. Lawan d lmeɣreb, yebda la d-iɣelli umḍellas. Sin-nni n yilmeẓyen-nniḍen refden-d aÆlaw, ḍelqen-t. Nekk akked AÆmer nella gar-asen nqaÆed iman-nneɣ akken ad neṭṭes yid-sen. Waleɣ AÆmer iɣiz-d akal, yexzen iman-is, iban-d ala wudem-is, mmuqleɣ-t yenna-yi-d: ‚lufan am nekk fiḥel aɣummu. S wakal ara ɣummeɣ.‘

Neṭqeɣ ɣer yilmeẓyen-nni nniɣ-asen: ‚kkset akkin aÆlaw-nni, d akal ara d-nɣiz ad nɣumm yes-s.‘ ḍeggren aÆlaw-nni. Nekk akked AÆmer nennelqem-d nemlil di rebÆa idis ɣer yidis. Neṭṭef imegguren la nettɣizi akken ad neqÆed tagnit ideg ara neṭṭes, ad d-nejmeÆ akal ad nɣumm yes-s. Mi mmuqleɣ amkan-nni deg i la nettɣizi, waleɣ yestiwen aṭas. Nniɣ deg wul-iw: ‚awwah mačči d kra yetɣizi umeggur.‘ Ufiɣ-d tagelzimt deg ufus-iw, nniɣ-asen: ‚xas wexxret, d nekk ara iqaÆden tagnit.‘

Ufiɣ-d iman-iw deg uxxam n umɣar n weltma. Tella weltma, yemma akked yiwet n tmeṭṭut tettwalam-as i yemma isem-is SaÆdiya n SaÆid. Ur bɣiɣ ara iɣimi yid-sent. Nleqmeɣ ffɣeɣ-d di tewwurt n tzeqqa-nni. Sliɣ i SaÆdiya tebda rregmat deg-i. Beddeɣ zdat tewwurt, nniɣ-asent: ‚anta tagi i la ireggmen deg-i?‘ Tenṭeq-d yemma, tenna-yi-d: ‚d nekk i la icemmaten deg-k.‘ Nniɣ-as: ‚nekk ma sÆiɣ aÆdaw mačči ma ulac-it i reggmeɣ deg-s, sqiṭṭÆeɣ-as deg ubrid, ḥebbseɣ-t uqbel ad yaweḍ s axxam-is. Yerna d awḥid i lliɣ, ur sÆiɣ ḥedd siwa Rebbi. Kemm tesÆiḍ tagmat d waṭas n wiyaḍ i m-ittwalamen. TesÆiḍ daɣen lkarÆin d
imÆiwan-im.  Fren-d ufrin seg  wid-agi i       am-yettarran aÆekkaz deg ufus, ceyyeÆ-it-id ad iyi-d-yezwar s abrid.

Tenna-yi-d: ‚ala, nekk ad  cemmateɣ   kan akka  deg-k berka-iyi.‛

Ufiɣ-d yiwet d weltma-s n yemma, teqqim-d ɣer tama-w. Neṭqeɣ ɣer yemma, nniɣ-as: ‚nekk d mmi-m, ma tewwteḍ deg-i tessusfeḍ igenni.‛ Lliɣ qqimeɣ ɣef yiwet n tɣalaṭ di tzeqqa-nni.

Yekcem  -d yiwen   n uÆsekri isuɣ-d     fell-i, yenna-yi-d : « aya zwir zdat-i. ».

Nniɣ-as : « mi tt-twalaḍ akka teqqim-d ɣer tama-w, mačči d taberranit, d xalti. ».

Yenna-yi-d : « aya, nnelqem, zwir  zdat-i, nxuṣ       argaz tameṭṭut. »

Fehmeɣ-d d yiwet n terbaÆt n lÆesker n waÆdaw i ixuṣṣen argaz akked tmeṭṭut, seg wid yesÆan tirrugza.. Nniɣ deg wul-iw: ‚dɣa akka axir ad asen-rewleɣ s leslaḥ.‛

Neffeɣ-d. zwireɣ zdat-is. La leḥḥuɣ      ttḥawateɣ-t akken ad iyi-yanef ur iyi-ttawi ara yid-s.

Nelḥeq ɣer zdat- tewwurt n ufrag, beddeɣ, zziɣ     ɣer-s, nniɣ-as: ‚ad ak-yehdu Rebbi, nekk d awḥid rnu ass-agi d tameɣra n weltma.‛

Yenna-yi-d: ‚nniɣ-ak yalleh zwir zdat-i.‛

Nelḥa kra n yisurrifen, newweḍ ɣer yiwet n talast yebḍan gar wakal n udrum-iw d wakal  n  yiwen  n  yesÆi n    taddart-nniḍen,    isem-is LaÆmara n WaÆrab.

Beddeɣ ɣer talast-nni, zziɣ s aÆsekri-nni, nniɣ-as: ‚ini-iyi-d d acu i xedmeɣ, ɣef wacu i yi-d-tewwiḍ?‛

Yenna-yi-d: ‚yalleh kan ad nwali lekwaɣeḍ ma d tidet i aɣ-d-nnan ɣef wayen turiḍ.‛

Nniɣ-as: u rtesÆiḍ i uriɣ.‛

Yenna-yi-d: ‚lkaɣeḍ-nni  i turiḍ tesserseḍ    deg-s
‘‘mǧn lieutnant‛. Nniɣ-as ‚ala mačči d nekk.‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚yalleh kan ad k-awiɣ ɣer-s ad nwali amek.‛

Nelḥa armi nelḥeq ɣer yiwet n tewwurt yellan zdat n ufrag n uxxam-iw, nufa-tt temdel. Mi nudeɣ ɣef tsura ulac-itent ɣer-i mmekteɣ-d mi ruḥeɣ s leḥmeq ɣer tmeɣra-nni n weltma, medleɣ leqfel n tewwurt-nni, tisura ttuɣ-tent deg uxxam. Nniɣ deg wul-iw: ‚tura ad d-rnuɣ taluft n tewwurt-agi.‛.

Neṭqeɣ s aÆsekriw-nni, nniɣ-as: ‚tawwurt-agi tettwamdel, tisura daxel n uxxam!‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚aya, erẓ-itt.‛. Yerra aḍar-is ɣer deffir, uqbel ad taweḍ tyita ɣer tewwurt-nni, telddi-d weḥd-s! Nniɣ deg wul-iw: ‚wigi d lawliya.‛

Nekcem s afrag, waleɣ yiwen n uÆsekri ibedd tama n tewwurt n uxxam. Iban-iyi-d d agradi. Leḥqeɣ ɣer tama-s, yenṭeq ɣer-s winna i yi-d-inehren, yenna-yas s taÆrabt: ‚heggi iman-ik.‛. Winna yeswexxer iman-is, nekk kecmeɣ s axxam netta yetbeÆ-iyi-d. Nbedd deg wagens ɣer yiwen n udekkan nemqabal udem ɣer wudem. Iban-iyi-d wudem-is akken kan i tebda la s-d-tettemɣay tamɣert.

Yekcem -d winna-nniḍen ibedd-d ɣer-neɣ. yebda-d ameslay s taÆrabt ugradi-nni. Ur as-fhimeɣ ara ula d yiwen n wawal. Fehmeɣ-d kan d lmaqasa i la yi-d-yettqasa ɣef tira-nni i iyi-d-yenna winna i yi-inehren ɣer-s.

Neṭqeɣ s aÆsekri-nni nniɣ-as: ‚ur ssineɣ ara taÆrabt. Sefhem-as akka i ugradi-agi.‛. yessefhem-as. Yuɣal ugradi-nni yenṭeq-d ɣer-i s teqbaylit yenna-yi-d: ‚tesÆiḍ rrabul n waman daxel n uxxam-ik ur d-txebbreḍ ara fell-as. Amek alarmi ur aɣ-d-txebbreḍ ara akken ad ak-id-nerr
‘la cǧnduite’. Axaṭer tuggadeḍ ad txellṣeḍ daymi ur aɣ d- txebbreḍ ara. Greɣ-d la ttmeslayeɣ d yiman-iw: ‚Akka yal lawan n teÆdawit d atmaten-nneɣ i d-yettilin d ixṣimen. Ttqasan- aneɣ, seḍharen-d lesrar -nneɣ. Tura ma nniɣ-as tidet terwi fell-i acku asmi i xedmeɣ rrabul-agi xedmeɣ-t s tuffra n waÆdaw. Mi t-semlileɣ ɣer rrabulat n ddula weddreɣ-asen la conduite. Ilaq kan ad nekkreɣ.

Nniɣ-as: ‚muḥal sÆiɣ nekk rrabul n waman daxel n uxxam-iw.‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚nniɣ-ak tesÆiḍ rrabul n waman daxel n uxxam-ik. Tugiḍ kan ad d-txebbreḍ fell-as.‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚nekk di Lezzayer i lliɣ seg zik, ur ḥṣiɣ ara ma yella rrabul-agi neɣ ulac-it.‛. Isuɣ-d fell-i, yenna-yi-d: ‚teḥṣiḍ tesÆiḍ rrabul n waman daxel n uxxam-ik.‛. Yeṭṭef tadebbuzt n wuzzal la yi-d- yekkat yes-s s aqerruy. Ḥulfeɣ iḍurr-iyi aṭas. Maca ṭṭfeɣ ṣṣber d truggza, ur d-nniɣ eḥḥ akken ad sneÆteɣ i umesbaṭli d acu i d ṣṣber yesÆa urgaz aḥeqqi.

La yekkat deg uqerruy-iw armi waleɣ idammen ffɣen-d seg-i d aḥemmal. Ahat anect-nni i sÆiɣ di tfekka-w. Amcum-nni i yi-nehren s agezzar, mi iwala ur d-yeqqim wacu ara yernu deg-i s tyita, yerfed afus-is yenna-yas i Æezrayen-nni: ‚Ḥbes.‛

Ukiɣ-d si targit!

Tameṭṭut yeččan tasa-s Ufiɣ-d iman-iw di myuggar n yiberdan deg umkan yettusemman ‘Iẓra n yiɣil’; ẓẓleɣ iman-iw ɣef wudem ṭṭseɣ. Mi d-ukiɣ, ufiɣ-d tayaẓiṭ tezdel gar tuyat-iw. la zluzeɣ akken ad tettixer fell-i, tiniḍ telseq deg-i. Uɣaleɣ mmɣeɣ kkseɣ-tt seg-i. La tleḥḥu, waleɣ turew-d snat n tmellalin ɣef yiwet n (ubrid) tikkelt. Yerna seg tid-nni yesÆan sin n yifuraẓ. Nleqmeɣ, refdeɣ-tent-id, mmuqleɣ tayaziṭ-nni wehmeɣ deg-s amek i d-turew timellalin am tid-nni!. Waleɣ yiwet n tčewčewt tama n tyaziḍt-nni turew-d tamellalt. Ruḥeɣ ddmeɣ-tt-id. Mmuqleɣ-tt, ufiɣ kifkif-nsent akked snat-nni n tyaziḍt. Mmuqleɣ tačewčewt-nni wehmeɣ deg-s, nniɣ-d: ‘tačewčewt am tagi turew-d tamellalt yerna meqqret!’

Ur ḥṣiɣ ansi i d-yekka uqjun armi i t-id-ufiɣ la yi-imecceḥ seg yimi-iw. Swexreɣ-t fell-i, la ttɣulufeɣ seg umcaḥ-nni. Mmuqleɣ (ɣer) zdat-i, waleɣ yiwen d mmi-s n Æemmi isem-is AÆmer, yenna-yi-d: ‘d acu akka a Meẓyan?’. Nniɣ-as: ‘ufiɣ-d tayaẓiḍt tezdel ɣef tuyat-iw, swexreɣ-tt akkin turew-d snat n tmellalin, tačewčewt-inna terna-iyi-d tamellalt tis tlata.’. Waleɣ AÆmer yezmumeg s teḍsa.

Ufiɣ-d iman-iw deg yiwen n uxxam d ajdid yettwabna s tyajurt akked ssiman urÆad yettwalebbes. Waleɣ yemma akked weltma deg wussu, ṭṭsent. Argaz n weltma di tama-nniḍen, yeṭṭes. Nekk la ttawiɣ ttarreɣ la ten-smuquleɣ. Uɣaleɣ sliɣ i yemma la tettmeslay akked yelli-s tenna-as:
abrid-agi Æeṭṭlen-iyi yidrimen-nni ttaɣeɣ ɣef baba-m, swayes ara kem-sferḥeɣ a yelli neɣ ara sferḥeɣ Ḥmed aḍeggal-iw Æzizen. Uẓiɣ ɣer-s nniɣ-as: "ziɣ tettḥebbireḍ i yelli-m akked uḍeggal-im aÆzizen." Tenna-yi-d: "ula d kečč a Meẓyan ttḥebbireɣ fell-ak." Nniɣ-as: "ad akem - iḥecem Rebbi. Tettḥebbireḍ fell-i mi ara iyi-d-tandiḍ tifxet sizegleɣ-tt ur iyi-teṭṭif ara ad ḥebbreɣ amek ara iyi-tandiḍ tayeḍ." Weltma tenna-yi-d: "Ḥemmleɣ-k a Meẓyan, ala kečč i sÆiɣ d gma." Nniɣ-as: "texliḍ-iyi axxam, teǧǧiḍ-iyi-d siwa leḥyuḍ. Rnu ula akken ur tetqenÆeḍ (tesqenÆeḍ) ara. Lufan kemm d tameṭṭut yettḥezziben nekk d gma-m, ma beddeɣ-am-id ɣef tewwurt s wudem-iw axir ma beddeɣ-am-id s tcekkarin n lwiz n lemsaxir-nni ifuḥanen i terriḍ d atmaten-im." Ḥmed yenna-yi-d: "yak nekk ur yella i yi-d-tessikkseḍ ay aḍeggal?" Nniɣ-as: "ad ak - iḥecem Rebbi, d kečč i yi-ssiwḍen armi i yi-tcureÆ yemma terniḍ la tettetteḍ idammen n baba ccahid." Zziɣ ɣer weltma nniɣ-as: "ayen akk akka yeḍran yid-i seg- m i d-yekka a Lǧuher. Maca ur ttayes ara ad d-yas wass ideg ara d-teɣliḍ deg ufus-iw ad txelseḍ ayen akk akka i yi-txedmeḍ." Waleɣ-tt tezmumeg s teḍsa. Taḍsa-nni tettban-iyi-d d taḍsa tuḥcimt. Tenna-yi-d: "ala ass-agi i d-tenniḍ i ur d-tessawḍeḍ ara." Nniɣ-as: "d acu ara am-iniɣ. Ma nniɣ-am ad t-id-ssiwḍeɣ s tussna-w neɣ s ddraÆ-iw xas ur ttamen ara. Maca xas amen ad kem-id-yas wass-agi i am-d-nniɣ. Axaṭer d Rebbi ara t-id-yessiwḍen. Aṭas n tirga ideg i yi-d-yessiweḍ. Ass-agi i am-ttmenniɣ ad kem-id-yaweḍ. D acu kan ma ur as-ḥḍireɣ ara, ad d-ǧǧeɣ
lewṣaya i watmaten-iw ara as-iḥeḍren. Tenna-yi-d: ‚yak siwa nekk i tesÆiḍ di tegmat. Nniɣ-as: ‚d tidet, ala kem i sÆiɣ. meÆna asmi i yi-txedÆeḍ, ttruɣ i Rebbi yefka-iyi-d atmaten-iw s yimelyunen.

Waleɣ lǧuher sseɣrent-tt lewhayem seg wayen tesla seg yimiy-w. Ma d Ḥmed iɣaḍ-it lḥal. Yennelqem-d ɣer-i ad nemseččew. Uqbel ad nemyuṭṭaf, sliɣ i yemma tenna-as i yelli-s: ‚yya-n ad nesiwel i lɣaci mulac amcum-agi ad ineɣ Ḥmed. Ffɣent s tuffɣa n leÆqel.

Ufiɣ nella deg yiwen n uÆerqub d uzyib. Ḥmed yekka-iyi-d si tama ufella. Yal tikkelt mi ara d-yeẓdem fell-i, itegg-iyi-d taqerraṭ. Nekk ttaṭṭafeɣ-t si tuyat sɣimayeɣ-t ɣer tmurt. Mi yeÆya, ibedd, yenna-yi-d: ‚bɣiɣ ad ak-sseɣliɣ s lkarati. Nniɣ-as: ‚tessneḍ lkarati a ccmata? Tebɣiḍ ad iyi-tesseɣliḍ s yemma, d nettat i d taqerraṭ-ik. Nuɣal amzun ur nemcaḥan ara seg umseččaw-nni. Nellha la nettnecraḥ nniɣ-as: ‚yya ak-iniɣ ad neffer iman-nneɣ. Mi ara d-awḍen lɣaci ad inin ɣer lbir-inna i ɣlin. Yenna-yi-d: ‚welleh ar d tidet. Yya-n ad neffer akken ad nwali anwa ara iɣaḍen yemma-k; ma d nekk neɣ d kečč. Nniɣ deg wul-iw: akka i tt-heggeɣ ula d nekk.

Lbir yella s lqerb-nneɣ. Nruḥ neffer. Ḥmed yeddura yiwet n tnijjelt, nekk ddureɣ tazemmurt. AÆerqub-nni ideg nella yettwasemma Ḥlafa. Tezga-d tmuɣli-w mebÆid. Waleɣ yemma akked weltma usant-d weed-sent ulac lɣaci-nniḍen. Amkan-nni deg i nella yetti-d d tamazirt yettusemman Tamazirt n umer. Nniɣ-as i Ḥmed: ‚yya ad ak-iniɣ ad ndewwer si tama-agi n wadda ad nezgar.
agemmaḍ. Mi nwala Æeddan-d lɣaci, ad ten-id-netbeÆ deffir s tuffra, ad nwali amek ara teḍru.‛. Nexdem am wakken i d-nniɣ. Mi nelḥeq agemmaḍ-nni, neqqim la nesmuqul. Waleɣ yiwen n uxxam yemɣi-d deg yiwen n umkan yettusemman Talwaḥt n Wakli. Axxam-nni di tilawt yella di tama-nniḍen.

Teffeɣ-d yiwet n teqcict seg uxxam-nni isem-is Ğeǧǧiga, tuzzel s amkan-nni i deg nella tama n lbir, terna teḍfer-itt Æemmti-s, terna weltma-s n teqcict-nni. Ma d yemma akked weltma nudant ur ǧǧant amkan armi leḥqent s aɣbalu-nni. Waleɣ yemma yeffeɣ-itt laÆqel, nniɣ-as i Ḥmed: ‚yya-n ad nruḥ mulac tamcumt-inna ad tḍeggar iman-is s aɣbalu.‛. Nuzzel. Zwireɣ zdat n Ḥmed. Mi qrib ad naweḍ, sliɣ i yemma tmeǧǧed: ‚a Ḥmed Æzizen.‛ Tḍeggar iman-is ɣer uɣbalu-nni. Nekk mi sliɣ tmeǧǧed, nniɣ-as: ‚ata, dagi Ḥmed.‛ Nettat dayen yeffeɣ-itt laÆqel. Nekk ur tt-lḥiqeɣ ara akken ad tt-id-ṭṭfeɣ. Waleɣ-tt tuflaw-d ɣef waman tefka-d afus-is i Ḥmed akken ad tt-id-yejbed, netta ur d-yellhi ara deg-s. Waleɣ-t la yesmuqul ɣer tama-nniḍen. Nekk uggadeɣ ad tefcel imir ad tezder.

èẓleɣ afus-iw, jebdeɣ-tt-id, tuzga-d di berra tbedd temqabal udem ɣer wudem d tmeṭṭut-nni i d-yuzzlen ɣer-s. Tinna ssneɣ-tt, d sstut-nni yexlan tamdint. Mi mqabalent akken, lɣaci leḥqen-d. waleɣ tameṭṭut-nni yuɣal wudem-is am ujajiḥ n tmes. Ur ḥsiɣ ma seg wurfan neɣ si lḥecma. Neṭqeɣ ɣer lɣaci-nni, nniɣ-asen: ‚mmuqlet a lɣaci, ɣef uḍeggal-is tḍeggar iman-is ɣer lbir.‛. Tenna-yi-d: ‚fell-ak a Meẓyan i ḍeggreɣ iman-iw mačči ɣef uḍeggal-
iw.‛. Nniɣ-asen: ‚meyyzet a lɣaci deg wayen I yi-texdem d wayen i texdem i uḍeggal-is ad d-tafem ma fell-i i tḍeggar iman-is neɣ ɣef uḍeggal-is.‛

Ibedd-d yiwen n urgaz n taddart-iw isem-is Qasi n WaÆrab u Muḥ, yeččeḥ tamuɣli di yemma, yuɣal yeḍsa.

Fehmeɣ-d di teḍsa-nni, lɣaci akk ḥṣan-tt ɣef wanwa i tḍeggar iman-is. Ulin-iyi-d wurfan armi ur frizeɣ ara ula d iman-iw. Kemseɣ tubbekt-iw, ḥemẓeɣ-tt armi teqqur am uẓru, wwteɣ-tt nniɣ-as: ‚d acu ara m-texdem tubbekt-iw mejṭuḥet ad kem-ǧǧeɣ kan i tubbekt n Rebbi.‛

Waleɣ tiyita-nni akken qrib ad tt-telḥeq yefcel ufus-iw yegguma ad ikemmel. Mi tt-tewweḍ tyita ɣer wudem amzun s taduḍt i tt-nnuleɣ. iwdeɣ-as s tayeḍ, ḥuzeɣ-tt di lexwa teɣli la tesselqaf. Tekcem-iyi-d tuggdi, nniɣ deg wul-iw: ‚ma temmut hatan bbuṣaɣ. Ad iyi-tbaṣi di lḥebs. Maca ad asen-ḥkuɣ ɣef wayen akk i yi-texdem ur ḥekkmen ara fell-i d nekk i d uḍlim.‛

Ufiɣ-d yiwen zdat-i isem-is Muḥ u Ḥmed, waleɣ ssaÆa deg ufus-is. Mmuqleɣ ɣer ssaÆa-w waleɣ-tt d lweḥda. Nniɣ-as i urgaz-nni: ‚acḥal ssaÆa a Muḥemmed?‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚d lweḥda swaswa.‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚ssaÆa-agi-inu siwa akked ssaÆa inek i teddunt kifkif.‛

Ukiɣ-d si targit !

# Targit n ttewḥid

Ufiɣ-d  lliɣ d  tmeṭṭut-iw deg  uxxam-nneɣ la nettmeslay ɣef rrwaḥ-iw ɣer tmurt n Fransa. TasaÆdit tenna-yi-d: ‚ur ilaq ara ad truḥeḍ ɣer Fransa a Meẓyan alamma teḥṣiḍ yella win iɣef tettekleḍ dinna ad teččeḍ ad tesweḍ ɣur-s. Ma ulac lɣerba-k ad tḍul. Imir, ssyin ad d-teznuzeḍ tiferkiwin-ik i wid ara tent-yaɣen dagi.‛

Nniɣ-as: ‚ala, ur yella wara tneẓfeḍ fell-i, yella dinna win uɣer ara ččeɣ ad sweɣ. Ur yettḥettim ara fell-i lḥal akken ad ssenzeɣ tiferkiwin-iw.‛

Tenna-yi-d: ‚anwa wagi iɣef ara tettekleḍ?‛ Nniɣ-as: ‚d Rebbi.‛

Ufiɣ-d iman-iw di tmurt n Fransa la leḥḥuɣ ttnadiɣ ma ad afeɣ ḥedd si tmussni neɣ ad yili d aqbayli ad as-ḥkuɣ tameḍrurt-iw amer ad I yi-Æawen. Lḥiɣ di temdint armi leḥqeɣ zdat n lkuca n uɣrum, waleɣ yiwen d axeddam la yettawi yettarra deg ufrag, immuqel-iyi-d, yenna-yi-d: ‚bab n tḥanut-agi d Muḥ n Tizi Wezzu, tura mi ara d- yekcem ad as-iniɣ hatan yusa-d mmi-s n tmurt-ik. Mebla ccek ad ak-yawi, ad yesterḥeb yes-k, ad teččeḍ ad tesweḍ ɣur-s.‛

Nniɣ-as: ‚ihi di laÆnaya-k, aql-i dagi kan ara ddawareɣ. Mi d-yusa, awi-iyi ɣer-s.‛

Yenna-yi-d: ‚ttkel fell-i.‛

Dewreɣ azal n tsaÆet, uɣaleɣ ɣer urgaz-nni, steqseɣ-t, nniɣ-as : « anida ara afeɣ Muḥ n Tizi Wezzu ? ». YessewÆed ɣer lkuca-nni, yenna-yi-d: ‚Attan tḥanut-is, yya-n ak-awiɣ ɣer-s.‛ Ddiɣ yid-s, nekcem di tewwurt n
ufrag, nufa yiwen n uxeddam. Yesteqsa-t winna akked ddiɣ yenna-yas: ‚anida yella Qasi (Muh!) n Tizi Wezzu? Ata wwiɣ-as-d mmi-s n tmurt-is. Mebla ccek ad yesterḥeb yes s lferḥ.‛. Winna yenna-yas-d: ‚atan daxel-agi, yya-w ad ken-awiɣ ɣer-s.‛. Nedda yid-s. Mi nelḥeq zdat tewwurt n tḥanut-nni, waleɣ taḥanut-nni daxel tettwabḍa ɣef snat n texxamin: yiwet d lkuca, tayeḍ ur tban d acu-tt.

Axeddam-nni yenna-d: ‚Ata dagi di texxam-agi. Yezwar yekcem ɣer texxam-nni ur nefri. Nekk beddeɣ di tewwurt, waleɣ yiwen n urgaz akken kan i t-id-yenqer ccib yeṭṭes deg wussu. Yewweḍ ɣer-s umɣid-nni, yeḍsa. Sliɣ yenna-yas: « nnelqem, hata wwiɣ-ak-d mmi-s n tmurt-ik. ».

Yennelqem-d nniɣ-as: ‚ṣbaḥlxir.‛.

Yerra-iyi-d: « ṣbaḥlxir. »

Waleɣ telḥa-d yiwet n tlemẓit d ccbiha n trumit. Fehmeɣ-tt tusa-d ad tawi aɣrum ad tuɣal. Mi d-tekcem ɣer tḥanut-nni, tbedd tama-w la yi-d-tesmuqul. Tuɣal la tettenneḍ kan din. Merra merra ttwaliɣ-tt tečča-iyi-d s tmuɣli. ḍḥiɣ wehmeɣ deg-s d acu-tt! ur iyi-tettixer, ur iyi-d-tenna d acu i tebɣa ɣer-i.

Uɣaleɣ sbenseɣ ul-iw nniɣ-d d aɣrum a la tettraǧu ad d-yewjed. Tezga-d tmuɣli-w ɣer lkuca-nni, waleɣ teččur d aɣrum. Aɣrum-nni d tixbizin timejṭaḥ am tid-nni n lḥebs. Ɣef udekkan n texxam-nni, rsent tlata n texbizin ɣef yiwet n ṭṭabla n usewwi. Tixbizin-nni ttwaxedment d timrebÆin, sÆant rebÆa n tqernay; di temɣer ta tugar ta. Waleɣ tebda-tent-id tiwwin uɣalent d tiwraɣin. Nniɣ-d deg wul-iw: ‚tixbizin-inna qrib ad wwent.‛
Zziɣ ɣer umÆellem-nni, rǧiɣ deg-s ad iyi-d-yini ula yiwen n wawal, ulac. Fehmeɣ-t ur yebɣi ara mi t-qesdeɣ. Ffɣeɣ-d ssyin la leḥḥuɣ di temdint smuquleɣ anida ad iyi-d-iban ula d amkan n lxedma n laÆḍil. Lḥiɣ, lḥiɣ ur i yi-d-iban wara. Neṭqeɣ, nniɣ-d : « a Rebbi anida ara xedmeɣ tura? Ad xedmeɣ di lluzin, ur sÆiɣ ara lekwaɣeḍ ; ad xedmeɣ di berra, ilaq deg unebdu ad xedmeɣ mi d-telḥeq ccetwa ad ruḥeɣ. Akka ur ttalḥaqeɣ ara iman-iw s umeṣruf. Ad iyi-d-yesqam aṭas. Amek ara xedmeɣ a Rebbi?‛

Sliɣ i teɣri tenṭeq-d ur ḥṣiɣ ansi, tenna-d: « a Meẓyan, ulac lmal anect a yekk. ». Ufiɣ-d yiwen n urgaz zdat-i ɣezzif d ahrawan, neṭqeɣ ɣer-s nniɣ-as: ‚Rebbi yella ama deg yigenni neɣ di lqaÆa; yerna ay anida tebɣu tewweḍ tussna n lÆalem ur yezmir ara ad d-yefk rray-is di lecɣal n Rebbi. Rebbi ur yesÆi ara tafekka neɣ ayen akk i yesÆa lxelq-is. Rebbi yella di ddunit merra, ur tettafeḍ ara anida ara yers yixef n tsegnit ur yella ara deg-s Rebbi.‛

Mmuqleɣ argaz-nni, waleɣ-t sseɣrent-t lewhayem, iččeḥ-iyi-d s tmuɣli yebda la yettweḥḥid Rebbi.

Ukiɣ-d si targit !
