- 223 -
Sekṛeɣ s waman

Ufiɣ-d iman-iw deg yiwen n uÆerqub yettusemman ‘Ugni n waydi’, lliɣ akked uqehwaǧi isem-is Muḥdakli n MuḥdaÆrab. Siggeɣ si ṭṭaq ɣer berra waleɣ tusa-d tkerrust n yiǧadarmiyen. Fehmeɣ ad awin deg-s ixeddamen ɣer lxedma. Aṭas n yilmeẓyen n taddart-iw i d-yennejmaÆen ad ddun di tkerrust-nni. Iban-iyi-d yiwen d ccif-nsen isem-is AÆrab. Ttwaliɣ deg-s d aÆdar, d ucmit, d netta i d aÆdar gar yilmeẓyen-nni. Neṭqeɣ d yiman-iw, nniɣ-d: ‘d lewhayem!’

Yiwen n yilemẓi isem-is Ḥmed u Sliman la yi-d-yesmuqul. Wehheɣ-as s ufus-iw s uwehhi n sslam, nniɣ-as: ‘ṣaḥḥa a Ḥmed.’ Yeḍsa-d ɣer-i yusa-d. Izzwer-d yiwen zdat-s d mmi-s n Æemmi isem-is Ḥmed. Leḥqen-d, nemsalam, qqimen-d ɣer ṭṭabla, nniɣ-asen: ‘i tura ad awen-d-xellṣeɣ leqhawi ur sÆiɣ ara ṣṣerf. Llant ɣer-i Æecralaf akked Æecra dduru, lqahwa teswa Æecrin dduru.’

Mmi-s-nni n Æemmi yenna-yi-d: ‘deg uṭableau de prix teswa 75 cm.’ Mmuqleɣ waleɣ uṭṭun 75, nniɣ-as: « d tidet, akka i teswa; nutni snuzen-tt Æecrin dduru. » Mmuqleɣ aqehwaǧi-nni, nniɣ-as: « d tagi i wumi qqaren lÆabudiya. ». Yenna-yi-d: « d acu i d lÆabudiya-agi? ». Nniɣ-as: ‘d lweqt-agi deg i nella. Ad dduklen sin n yirgazen ɣer ssuq; ma yella yiwen yeẓra aɣyul n wayeḍ yeǧhed ɣef uɣyul-is, ad t-iÆebbed s ddemma n uɣyul-nni iǧehden aÆad bu yidrimen. Anef i bu tkaskiṭ, winna mačči
d kra i d-nettmeslay fell-as.‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚welleh ar d tidet i d-tenniḍ (acemmah kan i t-id-yesḍill).‛ ikerrec-iyi-d acenfir, immuqel ɣer win yellan d bab n lqahwa-nni. Fehmeɣ yenna-iyi-d amÆellem-agi ur ibeqqu ara ad isel i yimeslayen am wigi. Bab n lqahwa-nni isem-is Lḥusin d yiwen yellan d aqezzab armi ifak. Mmuqleɣ-t yennelqem iruḥ la yettẓalla. Neṭqeɣ s aqehwaǧi-nni, nniɣ-as: ‚wagi imdanen la ten-yesseɣfal, ula d Rebbi yebɣa ad t-yessayes.‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚bibb-itt neɣ ini-tt-id.‛

Ufiɣ-d iman-iw akked yiwen n yilemẓi isem-is AÆmer la nleḥḥu deg ubrid n ukerrus. Nelḥeq gar sin n yiberdan i tebḍa yiwet n tiɣilt. Amkan-nni yettwasemma taḥeccaṭ m-lexyuḍ. Di zzman aqbur tella din yiwet n tḥeccaṭ ttÆebbiden-tt yimsebriden, win i d-iÆeddan ad d-ikkes lxiḍ si tlaba-s ad t-iÆelleq i tḥeccaṭ-nni.

Waleɣ yiwen n uxxam di tiɣilt-nni bnan-t armi qrib ad icerref. Yiwen n urgaz akked d tmeɣart qqimen sufella n leswar n uxxam-nni mqabalen; argaz-nni isem-is Lḥusin d zzani, tamɣart-nni isem-is TasaÆdit tesÆa axxam s lqerb-nni. Zdat n uxxam n temɣart-nni llant tlata n tlawin d twacult n uxxam-nni, beddent-d zdat n tewwurt. Lḥusin imi-s ɣer temɣart-nni allen-is ɣer tlawin-nni. Tilawin-nni la t-smuqulent s tmuɣli-nni yettmeslayen.

NeǧÆeɣ aderɣal-nni nniɣ-as: « wali kan amexluq-inna la yettmeslay lÆeqliya akked temɣart-inna. ». AÆmer yefhem taluft, yeḍsa yenna-yi-d: ‚Winna d acu i d ccɣel-is?!‛ Nelḥa. Mi nelḥeq tama n uxxam-nni, nufa tilawin-nni qqiment Lḥusin gar-asent la yettnecraḥ yid-sent. Nekk
yers-d fell-i umlelli tiniḍ sekreɣ armi ur zmireɣ ara ad ṭṭfeɣ iman-iw: la leḥḥuɣ s umlelli mebla lebɣi-w. Mi leḥqeɣ ɣer terbaÆt-nni n zzhu, mlelliɣ, serkeɣ akk Lḥusin s yiḍarren-iw. Uɣaleɣ rrant-iyi temlellay-nni s abrid. Sliɣ i Lḥusin yenna-yi-d: ‚waqila terrigliḍ-tt a Meẓyan?‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚aha kan a Dadda Lḥusin, akessar d akessar Rebbi yefka fell-nneɣ afus.‛

Ukiɣ-d si targit !

1981

Tiɣri umadaɣ

Ufiɣ-d lliɣ d tmeṭṭut-iw nekka-d seg lexla la nteddu s axxam. Mi d-nelḥeq qrib s abraḥ yellan zdat uxxam-nneɣ yettwasemma Amraḥ imexlaf, sliɣ i TasaÆdit tenna-d : « azekka ad d-asen wid ara izedɣen dagi. ». Deg ubraḥ-nni iban-iyi-d lebni d amaynut akken kan yettwabda sbedden tigejda n wuzzal akked d ssiman, xedmen igensan yeṭṭilin ɣef wudem n wakal. Daɣen xedmen abrid seg i sÆeddayen tiɣawsiwin n lebni. Abrid-nni ssan-as rrmel akked ssiman, rnan-as sufella ssan-as igeḍman n wuzzal. Neṭqeɣ ɣer TasaÆdit, nniɣ-as: ‚mačči azekka ara d-asen ad zedɣen; alamma d slazekka. Hatan akken kan sbedden tigejda
rnan xedmen abrid. Tenna-iyi-d: ‚i txedmeḍ dagi a Meẓyan deg ucanṭi-agi n les T.I.S.‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚lxedma zdat tewwurt, ilaq-iyi kan ad xedmeɣ. Ulamma ad ruḥeɣ ɣer Fransa, maca ad xedmeɣ ccher di laÆḍil.‛

Ufiɣ-d iman-iw beddeɣ ddaw umadaɣ yettusemman Amalu n Muḥend u umar. Sliɣ i teɣri deg umadaɣ-nni la d-teqqar: ‚amɣar azemni la d-ijebbed isefra ɣef jujya i iḥemmel<‛ tettÆawad-d i yimeslayen-agi. Waleɣ gma-s n tmeṭṭut-iw Muḥed u isa ibedd zdat n taÆwint yettusemman ‘TaÆwint n Muḥed u umar’ tella di tama n wadda n umalu-nni. Neṭqeɣ nniɣ-as: ‚sɣed kan a Muḥed u isa d acu la yeqqar umadaɣ-agi. La d-yeqqar amɣar azemni la d-ijebbed isefra ɣef jujiya iḥemmel aṭas.‛. Nekk fehmeɣ imeslayen-nni fell-i i d-ttwannan. Muḥ yenna-yi-d: ‚yalleh a wlidi ttixer-ik ur sɣad ara i lemnam.‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚ala a Muḥ, nekk sɣadeɣ i lemnam. D lemnam i iyi-d-yelddin allen-iw yemla-iyi iberdan.‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚welleh ar d ṣṣeḥ.‛

Ufiɣ-d iman-iw beddeɣ deg ubrid n ukerrus. Muḥed u isa iruḥ-d s tkerrust ‘R4’, iḥbes-d ɣer-i; fehmeɣ takerrust-nni-inu, si Fransa i tt-id-wwiɣ, fkiɣ-as-tt la ilemmed tanhart yes-s. emdeɣ xas ad tt-yessegrireb wala as-tt-kkseɣ. Yelddi-d tawwurt, yenna-yi-d: ‚ali-d.‛. Nekk kukreɣ tanhart-is. Maca uliɣ ɣer tkerrust s leḥya. Mi yeqleÆ, iban-iyi-d di tenhart tiniḍ d amussnaw aqbur. Iḥella-d yiwen n wuxnaq, yeḥbes takerrust, yenna-yi-d: ‚eddi ad tnehreḍ a Meẓyan, nekk Æyiɣ.‛
Ufiɣ-d rekbeɣ di tkerrust-nniḍen d ‘afurgu’, anehhar-is d yiwen n umɣar yellan si temẓi-s ixuṣ iẓri isem-is LaÆmara n Muḥ. Mi qrib ara naweḍ ɣer yiwet n ddura n ubrid, waleɣ di ddura-nni tella trekkizt n trisiti di rrif n ubrid. Anehhar-nni iruḥ qbala ad yeddhem tarekkizt-nni. Suɣeɣ fell-as, nniɣ-as: ‚ɣur-k bren-d s abrid ma ulac ad teddehmeḍ tarekkizt-nni.‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚ala deg wazal akka ferrzeɣ.‛. Yegzem ddura-nni iruḥ srid ɣer trekkizt-nni. Mmɣeɣ s ameqyas n tenhart, qaÆdeɣ-d takerrust-nni s abrid.

Ikemmel tanhart ɣer zdat. Abrid qbala anehhar-nni iqsed ɣer trekkizt tis snat di rrif n ubrid. Suɣeɣ fell-as, nniɣ-as: ‚err-d takerrust s abrid ma ulac ad tetti yes-neɣ.‛ Yeḍsa-d, icekkeḍ yenna-d: ‚awlidi ur ttuggad, ferzeɣ yerna ssneɣ ad nehreɣ.‛. Mi waleɣ qrib ad nekcem di twaɣit-nni, daɣen qaÆdeɣ-d takerrust-nni s abrid. ḍegreɣ aḍar-iw ɣef ‘lefran’, teḥbes din- din.

Ufiɣ-d iman-iw deg yiwet n temdint di tmurt n Fransa lliɣ akked kra n lɣaci daxel n ttberna. Gar-asen, ssneɣ sin d atmaten. Nekk yid-sen yiwet n taddart-nneɣ. Yiwen deg-sen isem-is Akli, wayeḍ Muḥemmed. Yemmuqel-iyi-d Wakli, yenna-d: ‚anwa ara iqumren?‛ immuqel ɣer Muḥ, Yenna-yas s taÆrabt: ‚men qummer?‛. Yenna-yas Muḥ: ‚makac qummarin.‛. Akli yenna-yas s teqbaylit: ‚Ata yella Meẓyan d aqumer.‛. Nekk bɣiɣ ad qumreɣ yid-sen maca sÆiɣ drus n yidrimen. Mi ruḥeɣ seg Lezzayer ɣer Fransa wwiɣ yid-i tnayen u tltin alef n yidrimen n Fransa, rnu ṣerrfeɣ seg-sen. MeÆna nniɣ-d deg wul-iw: ‚ad ten-
awin, ulac akk neɣ ma yebɣa Rebbi ad rebḥeɣ. Nniɣ-asen: „aql-i da ad qumreɣ. Qerrbeɣ ɣer tesqamut. Uqbel ad qqimeɣ nniɣ-asen: „maca rǧut ad waliɣ acḥal sÆiɣ n yidrimen. Mi rriɣ leḥsab, ufiɣ sÆiɣ 10320 FF. Nniɣ-asen: „ça va. Ad qumreɣ.

Neqqim di tlata yid-neɣ di tesqamut-nni. Akli yenna-yi-d: „maca a Meẓyan ur ččiqlil ara.” Nniɣ-as: „ccerṭ fell-i ur ṭṭalameɣ ara.” Ufiɣ-d iman-iw beddeɣ di berra zdat ttberna-nni. Ibedd-d yiwen n yilemẓi isem-is Lḥusin u SsaÆid, n taddart-iw. Nekk rebḥeɣ di luqmɣer. Uɣeɣ-d takerrust R4 ad tt-id-awiɣ mi ara d-uɣaleɣ ɣer Lezzayer.

Nniɣ-as i Lḥusin: „takerrust-agi ɣlayet aṭas a Lḥusin!” Yenna-yi-d: „ayɣer ɣlayet? Tuɣeḍ-tt-id s sin n yimelyunen, ad txellseḍ amelyun n la douane.” Nniɣ-as: „tlata n yimelyunen tesqam-iyi-d ɣlayet a Lḥusin.” Ur twalaḍ ara mi ara tawḍeḍ ɣer tmurt, ad tt-terreḍ Æecrin n yimelyunen.” Nniɣ-as: „welleh ar d ṣṣeḥ.”

Ufiɣ-d iman-iw di tayeḍ n ttberna beddeɣ zdat n udekkan la ttraǧuɣ melmi ara d-yellhi yid-i uxeddam n ttberna-nni. Axeddam-nni iban-iyi-d d bab n uxxam, netta d aÆrab. La ttwaliɣ deg-s yellha-d akk d wid-nni i ufiɣ daxel akked wid la d-ikeccmen. Yal wa issewjed-as ayen yessuter; ma d nekk tiniḍ ur yettemlaÆi ara yid-i ula s tmuɣli. Isuma-iyi-d yiwen n urgaz.

Neṭqeɣ ɣer-s nniɣ-as: „d wagi i wumi qqaren meḥyaf.” Yenna-yi-d: „hatan yekcem-d umÆellem d aqbayli.” Waleɣ yekcem yiwen n urgaz ɣer deffir n udekkan-nni. Winna i ufiɣ d amÆellem yeffeɣ. Winna i d-ikecmen icuba di lewṣayef ɣer winna yeffɣen. Mi yebda
leqdic-is, tiniḍ msefhamen fell-i! yekkufet-d wul-iw, neṭqeɣ ɣer winna i d-yellan ɣer yidis-iw, nniɣ-as: ‚ma d aqbayli d acu i yi-iruḥen deg-s. ni ad iyi-d-iseddeq?‛ Waleɣ yiwen n yilemẓi yewwi-d yid-s tacekkart iruḥ qbala s anida yella leqjer n yidrimen n ttberna-nni, yessendi tacekkart-nni. Fehmeɣ-t la yettraǧu amÆellem ad as-tt-yeččar d lbira. Nniɣ deg wul-iw: ‚wagi yettwaɣ di rray-is. Lufan si tḥanut, ad tt-id-yaɣ s rrxa; netta yusa-d ɣer ttberna ad tt-yaɣ ɣlayet.‛. Waleɣ-t yessekmumes tacekkart-nni yerra-tt deg umkan n leqjar-nni. Leqjar-nni ulac-it. Amexluq-nni iwexxer-d ɣer deffir, ibedd di tlemmast n wagens. Yekcem-d wayeḍ yewwi-d yid-s tacekkart, ibedd zdat n udekkan-nni n ttberna. Yemmuqel s amÆellem, yeẓra-t mecɣul. Yessekmumes tacekkart-nni, yerna-tt ɣer tmezwarut-nni. Iban-iyi-d yerra-tt s tuffra ɣef umÆellem. Nniɣ deg wul-iw : « a lufan ad yaf ticekkarin-agi umÆellem ! »

Waleɣ ilemẓi-nni i d-ikecmen d aneggaru yuli ɣef udekkan-nni yeqqim s ufella-s s lewhi n umkan-nni deg yella leqjer. Winna ibedden di tlemmast n wagens iruḥ ɣer winna yellan s ufella n udekkan. Yeṭṭineẓ ɣer-s la s-icennu s teɣri n snitra. Yeqqar-as : « ttik ttik ttik, ṭak ṭak ṭak,<». Wis sin-nni la s-d-yettarra s ccna n taÆrabt yeqqar-as: ‚a bbwa ya bbwa, ma Æendic ssaÆd ki iṭiḥ llil<‛. Amezwaru-nni yuɣal s amkan-is ibedd di tlemmast n wagens Yefka-yas-d s uÆrur i winna iɣef i d-iwexxer. Yebda di ccna-nni: ‚ttik ttik ttik, ṭṭak ṭṭak ṭṭak,..‛ i as-yeqqar s lemɣawla.
# Winna yeqqimen sufella n udekkan yettarra-as-d s umeǧǧed: ‚a bbwa ya bbwa, ma Æendic ssaÆd ki iṭḥ llil

# Ukiɣ-d si targit !

# 1981

# CcraÆ n tegnawt

Ufiɣ-d iman-iw kkiɣ-d seg Lexmis MÆatqa la leḥḥuɣ s axxam leḥqeɣ s tikli-w s amkan yettusemman

Amɣit izga-d di taddart At ZaÆim mlileɣ-d d yiwet n tkerrust n tɣiwant, abrid iḍyeq di ṭṭiq-nni, ufiɣ-d yid-i yiwen n mmi d amejṭuḥ isem-is Muḥemmed, yella si tama n ubrid mi waleɣ qrib ad d-taweḍ tkerrust-nni, uggadeɣ ad teddhem-it . jebdeɣ-t-id ɣer-i, rriɣ-t-id ɣer tama-nniḍen.

Mi tÆedda tkerrust-nni, tennul-iyi-d deg yijifer-iw. Zziɣ ɣer deffir, stebÆeɣ-as tamuɣli s reffu. Waleɣ temlil d yiwet n tmacint n uɣizi. Tamacint-nni teqqen-d deffir-s ccɣel n usenduq-nni n lmeyyet. Abrid yella s lqis kan n wakken ara tÆeddi tkerrust.

Nniɣ-d deg wul-iw: ‚hatan ad teḍru twaɣit.‛

Mi qrib ad mlilent, anehhar n tmacint-nni isuÆef. Yerra-tt ɣer yiwen n uxxam yellan di rrif n ubrid. Teddhem axxam-nni, tenneqlab s ufella-s. Nniɣ-d: ‚anehhar ad
yemmet mebla ccek yerna ad d-yeglu s lexṣara i at uxxam.‛. Bɣiɣ ad azzleɣ s axxam-nni ad waliɣ amek i teḍra yid-sen; maca ḥṣiɣ meqqret, uggadeɣ ad xelÆeɣ. Daɣen ma ur ruḥeɣ ara, ssetḥeɣ seg at taddart-nni. Greɣd di sin rrayat: yiwen ad ruḥeɣ, wayeḍ ala. Yelḥa-d yiwen d ilemẓi. Fehmeɣ-t n taddart-nni. StebÆeɣ-as tamuɣli, waleɣ-t iÆedda tama n uxxam-nni. Yemmuqel ɣer din, iÆedda d amsebrid ur yenḥerwa ara di twaɣit-nni. Ula d nekk rriɣ abrid gar wallen-iw Æeddeɣ i uxxam-nni. Waleɣ ɣer zdat yenneḍ ubrid. Uqbel ddura-nni, tella tḥanut. TarbaÆt n lɣaci qqimen zdat n tḥanut-nni, tayeḍ n terbaÆt bedden nnig ubrid la smuqulen s anida i teḍra twaɣit-nni. La ttwaliɣ deg-sen wa itezzi ɣer wa la ttmesteqsayen ɣef wacu yeḍran. Ar dqal yewweḍ lexbar ɣer wid-nni yeqqimen. Waleɣ-ten ula d nutni nleqmen bedden la ttmesteqsayen, smuqulen ɣer twaɣit-nni. Maca rran-tt kan ɣef tmuɣli d umeslay; ula d yiwen deg-sen ur iruḥ ad yedlu ɣef wacu yeḍran.

Mi leḥqeɣ ɣer-sen, rriɣ fell-asen sslam, ḥkiɣ-asen taḥkayt n twaɣit-nni amek i teḍra. Maca banen-iyi-d ḥku neɣ qqim Æuẓgen wul-awen-nsen. Uqbel ad greɣ asurif, tezga-d tmuɣli-w ɣer kra n yilmeẓyen yellan daxel n tḥanut-nni, gar-asen llan kra d tamussni waleɣ-ten mecɣulit akk di lkarṭa akked ddi wuminu. Maca ssetḥeɣ ad Æeddiɣ mebla ma rriɣ sslam fell-asen, uggadeɣ ad iyi-d-gren tamawt. Beddeɣ la ttraǧuɣ ad yestafi ula d yiwen deg-sen ad d-immuqel s abrid. Rǧiɣ armi i d-yemmuqel yiwen, neṭqeɣ s teɣri Ælayen, nniɣ-asen: ‚sbaḥlxir fell-awen.‛.
wehheɣ-asen s ufus-iw akken ma ur d-fhimen ara ad d- walin ad fehmen d acu i asen-nniɣ, acku sekkren isuɣan ɣef  lÆubat-nni-nsen. Ilemẓi-nni iwehha-iyi-d s ufus-is yuɣal ɣer ccɣel-is.

Kemmleɣ ɣer zdat tikli Æeddeɣ i ddura-nni. Ufiɣ inneqḍaÆ- d ubrid-nni s ugafa. Mmuqleɣ ɣer tama ufella, waleɣ amɣar yeqqim nnig ubrid-nni yemqabal akked snat n tfunasin yessemlil-iten s cced am wakken ara tent-yeṭṭef i lbiÆ di ssuq. Rriɣ sslam fell-as. Yerra-iyi-d, rnu yenna-yi-d: ‚lÆeslama a Meẓyan.‛; Nniɣ deg wul-iw : « ziɣ yessen-iyi nekk ur t-ssineɣ ara ! ». Ruḥeɣ ɣer-s ad nemsalam. Mi Æeddeɣ tama n yiwet n tfunast, tessenṭeḍ-d tifejqar-is di taɣma-w; fehmeɣ-tt tebɣa ad iyi-d-tewwet s lǧɣer. D litteÆ kan ur tufi ara. Swexreɣ-d iman-iw fell-as, maca akken bɣuɣ wexreɣ ad waliɣ aḍar-is tiniḍ di taɣma-w i d-yemɣi! nettat tettaÆraḍ amek ad d-tɣef litteÆ akken ad  iyi-d- tewwet s zzur. Armi ulamek, tezzi-d fell-i s tkerrac la iyi- d-tettgabar s aÆebbuḍ neɣ s idmaren. La d-tettemmeɣ ad iyi-tkerrec nekk la ttwexxireɣ fell-as la tt-ḥebbseɣ s yifassen-iw akken ur iyi-d-tettalḥaq ara s ansi ad iyi-tḍurr.

Tikwal tettḥaz-iyi seg yixfawen n yiḍudan-iw, tettkerriÆ- iten nekk ttsuɣuɣ ɣef umɣar-nni qqareɣ-as: ‚yya-d  ḥbes tafunast-ik ay amɣar. Ziɣ twalaḍ-tt tettkerric kečč ur iyi-d- tenniḍ ara.‛

Yuɣal yuzzel-d la tt-iḥebbes fell-i. Maca ur yezmir ara, d lebda tettzad-d deg uḥwaṣ n tkerrac. La ttwexxireɣ fell-as armi leḥqeɣ ɣer yiri n yiwen n yifri lqay s wazal n tlata lmitrat. Mi waleɣ tafunast-nni tugi ad iyi-teg berru, nniɣ-d
ur yelli leslak si temcumt-agi alamma neggzeɣ ɣer lkaf-agi. Mebla ccek ad tuggad yerna ulamek i d-tneggez. Ma isellek-iyi Rebbi ad sellkeɣ; ma mmuteɣ meqqar s lmut tucbiḥt. Ad mmteɣ axir ma ttwaliɣ la yettmečča uksum- iw. Ttcehhideɣ s Rebbi, neggzeɣ ɣer yifri-nni, uzgeɣ-d beddeɣ. Tafunast-nni tedda-d d uḍar-iw, ufiɣ-tt-id zdat-i terna tzad di ccɣel-is. Amɣar-nni yuzga-d gar-aneɣ d amḥaddi xas akken ur yezmir ara. Nniɣ-d mi akka ilaq kan ad suɣeɣ abbuh ay inselmen, ad d-slen si tḥanut-nni neɣ seg wanida teḍra twaɣit-nni, ad d-azzlen ad iyi-ḥudden si temcumt-agi. Suɣeɣ tlata tikkal abbuh ay inselmen. Waleɣ lɣaci-nni la d-smuqulen ɣer-i, slan-d i teɣri-w, ẓran-d d acu i la iḍerrun yid-i. maca ma iḥerrek umeblaḍ ad iḥerrek ula d yiwen seg-sen. Uɣaleɣ qubleɣ tafunast-nni s teḥraymit. Mi d-temmeɣ ad iyi-tkerrec, as-greɣ afus-iw deg yimi-s alamma yelḥeq s agarjum-is. Imir ad d-tettemÆuqqi yerna ulamek tessemlil igumas-is. La ttwaliɣ di tuɣmas-is la ttruẓunt yiwet u snat. Maca xas akken uggadeɣ-tt ad iyi-tesseÆyu. Taggara waleɣ wiyaḍ n lɣaci ugemmaḍ n wanida lliɣ, daɣen suɣeɣ tlata tikkal s wabbuh-nni. Llan wid i d-yemmuqlen uɣalen knan iqerray nsen. Ma d wiyaḍ llan, ulac-iten. Gar-asen iban-iyi-d yiwen s ccbiha n ubudali. YesewÆed ɣer-s umɣar-nni yenna-yi-d: ‚siwel-as i Winna, yezmer ad ak-iḥudd si tfunast-agi, yesen taseḥḥɣert yettamnaÆen wid i tettkerric.‘

argaz-nni iban-iyi-d wezzil maḍi, hraw aṭas. Suɣeɣ abbuh ay inselmen. Waleɣ-t yemmuqel-d. yuɣal yekna aqerruy-is
amzun ur d-isla ur d-iwala. Amɣar-nni yenna-yi-d: ‚ini-as ad ak-xellṣeɣ.‛

Siwleɣ-as, nniɣ-as: ‚yya-d ḥudd-iyi ad ak-xelṣeɣ.‛

Yusa-d la d-ileḥḥu s tikli-nni tazehwanit: rfed aḍar, ssers aḍar.. nekk ssarameɣ ad d-yas s waffug netta ula mi d-yelḥeq ɣer-i ur d-yellhi ara deg-i xas akken lemḥadda s lexlaṣ. Maca ad as-tiniḍ yeḥṣa s lĝibat-iw d ilmawen.

Yenṭeq ɣer-s umɣar-nni, yenna-yas: ‚yya-d sellek-it si tfunast-agi ad ak-xellṣeɣ tajernaṭ-ik.‛

Waleɣ-t yemmuqel tafunast-nni teɣli tenneṣraÆ. Iqerreb ɣer-s yeqqim s uqummec, yesseftutes felgu aquran la s-t-yezzuzur ɣer wallen armi temdel allen-is tenneṣraÆ maḍi.

Nniɣ-as: ‚ziɣ yeshel rray-is nekk ur ḥṣiɣ ara.‛. Kkseɣ-d felgu, sseftutseɣ-t. La s-rennuɣ armi i yi-d-tban tesḍuḍeÆ tiniḍ temmut. Nleqmeɣ s lemɣawla ad rewleɣ uqbel ad d-taki.

Maca greɣ asurif amezwaru, sliɣ i umɣar-nni yenna-d: ‚ɣur-k a Meẓyan attan tekker-d.‛. Zziɣ mmuqleɣ, teẓdem-d fell-i, tban-iyi-d ttejra ddaw ugafa n yifri-nni.

Negzeɣ, uliɣ ɣer-s. Teryel-nni la d-tettÆerric ɣer-i. Nekk ḥṣiɣ anida akken i ḥebseɣ alluy ur d-tettalḥaq ara ay akken i tebɣu tneggez. Ziɣ ɣelḍeɣ di leḥsab-iw. Yiwet n tikkelt telḥeq-d, tekkes tacriḥt seg taɣma-w.

Waleɣ-tt la tt-tetteffeẓ. Greɣ-d nnehta nniɣ-d : « Akka a Rebbi. »

Rniɣ alluy di ttejra-nni armi leḥqeɣ ɣer tcebbut-is, waleɣ-tt teÆdel di laÆli akked ugafa-nni n yifri. Mmuqleɣ tafunast-nni tban-iyi-d tṣaḍ fell-i la d-tetteckentiḍ di ttejra-nni teḍmeÆ ad d-tali ɣer-i. Imi ur tezmir ara tbedd di ttexmim, ar dqal tuzzel, tekka-d si tama-nni ufella ansi i as-yeshel
walluy. Ttejra-nni si tlemmast-is d asawen tebḍa ɣef tlata n yifurkiwen : yiwen yeẓẓel ɣer tama n ufella yennul iri n yifri-nni, wayeḍ srid d asawen. Nekk uliɣ ɣer wis tlata-nni d ameṭṭarfu ɣer tama n wadda. Tafunast-nni telḥeq-d ɣer yiri n yifri-nni, tuli-d ɣef ufurkiw-nni i tt-id-iqerben terna tengez-d ɣer ulemmas-nni tezga-d teckenṭeḍ deg-s. Tezzi iman-is tqubel ɣer tama ufella. Tuɣal tqubel-d ɣer-i. tqeÆÆed iman-is s ufella ufurkiw-nni. Imir tban-iyi-d d tameṭṭut ama di tfekka neɣ di lewṣayef. Maca nekk mazal fehmeɣ-tt d tafunast. Waleɣ-tt la tessewjad iman-is akken ad d-tengez ɣer-i maca uzgeɣ-d baÆdeɣ fell-as. Tban-iyi-d tkukra: ma tneggez-d ahat ad d-tazgi di lxali ur iyi-d- ¨tettalḥaq ara. Ma yiwet n tikkelt; thegga iman-is ad d-tneggez yerna ad d-telḥeq ɣer-i. Beddeɣ di ttexmim; ufiɣ-d amek ara s-menÆeɣ ma imneÆ-iyi Rebbi.

Cehdeɣ s Rebbi; nettat tneggez-d; sdakkleɣ ifassen-iw ddehmeɣ-tt ɣer yidmaren; truḥ di lxali. Waleɣ-tt la tettemhetway ddaw lǧedra n ttejra-nni. Neggzeɣ ɣer tama ufella; uzgeɣ-d beddeɣ nnig yifri-nni. Rewleɣ; ɣeṣbeɣ tazzla deg yiwen n ubrid d arqiqan. Mi beÆdeɣ s umeccaq ɣef temcumt-nni; mmuqleɣ ɣer deffir ma teḍfer-iyi-d; waleɣ aṭas n lɣaci bedden nnig yifri-nni la d-smuqulen ɣer-i. fehmeɣ-ten d wid i d-yuzzlen si tḥanut-nni ɣer wanida i teḍra twaɣit. Sliɣ la s-qqaren i teryel-nni: ‚ha-t anida yewweḍ<‛. Nniɣ-d: ‚ziɣ bɣan-iyi-tt.‛. Ɣeṣbeɣ tazzla-w ɣer zdat; tedduɣ tezziɣ s tmuɣli-w ɣer deffir. Ufiɣ-d iman-iw deg wanida yebda usawen n ubrid aqbur yellan ddaw laÆzib yettusemman iÆisaten. Uliɣ d asawen
armi  leḥqeɣ qrib ɣer  laÆzib-nni; ufiɣ snat n  tfunasin mqaranent di tlemmast n ubrid; yeqqim zdat-sent yiwen n yilemẓi isem-is AÆrab n Muḥ u Ḥmed. Mmuqleɣ ansi ara saÆfeɣ abrid; ur iyi-d-iban umḍiq; luÆeɣ ilemẓi-nni; nniɣ-as: ‚ay AÆrab ; yak tifunasin-agi inek ur kkatent ara s lǧer?‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚ur kkatent ara‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Ḥader ad iyi-txedmeḍ am umɣar-nni. Tafunast-is tekkat netta ur iyi-yessaÆlem ara.‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚ eddi kan ur kkatent ara s lǧer tigi.‛.  eddeɣ tama n yiwet seg-sent; tezzi-d fell-i s tkerrac; nniɣ-d: ‚Akka a Rebbi; menÆeɣ si yiwet weḥleɣ di snat.‛

Tafunast-nni la d-tẓeddem  fell-i nekk la tt-ḥebbseɣ   s yifassen-iw. Mi tent-id-tsugget; suɣeɣ ɣef bab-is nniɣ-as: ‚Ḥbes tafunast-ik ay aÆrab.‛. AÆrab yetti-d d yiwen d mmi-s n Æemmi isem-is Meẓyan. Yuzzel-d la tt-iḥebbes maca  ur  yezmir ara.  Nekk ḥulfeɣ    yebda-iyi-d Æeggu. Uɣaleɣ  waleɣ-tt tettucid seg uḍar.   Imir la tt-ḥebbseɣ ttwexxireɣ-as ɣer deffir armi d anida yenneqḍaÆ umrar-nni ; teḥbes. Rniɣ sbeÆdeɣ iman-iw fell-as. Beddeɣ ḥṣiɣ ur d-tettalḥaq ara ɣer-i. Teẓdem-d fell-i; wexxreɣ ɣer deffir.

Waleɣ-tt  telḥeq-d  s  amkan-nni seg  i  ttixreɣ   tiniḍ yettnejbad umrar-nni!  Beddeɣ; nniɣ-d ɣer dagi ur     d-tettaweḍ ara.

Waleɣ-tt   mi twexxer ɣer deffir ad  d-teẓdem ɣer   zdat akken  ad  d-tesseɣres. Nekk ḥareɣ   deg    yiman-iw: ma rewleɣ, uggadeɣ  mi zziɣ  fell-as ad d-tesseɣres ad iyi-texdeÆ s tkerrac; ma qqimeɣ; la ttraǧuɣ di twaɣit. Uɣaleɣ beddeɣ zdat-is ttwaliɣ deg-s tjebbed deg umrar-nni armi
teÆya; teḥbes. Imir fehmeɣ-tt ayen yellan di tezmart-is tfak-it-id. Zziɣ iman-iw ad kemmleɣ abrid-iw ɣer zdat, ufiɣ lliɣ deg yiwen n udrar anida yella udrum yettusemman At Yeḥya Musa di taddart IÆellalen. Liɣ d waṭas n lɣaci nuder-d seg udrar-nni; neṭṭef-d abrid-nneɣ ɣer tama n MÆatqa. Nekk lḥiɣ-d d alemmas. Wid yellan ɣer deffir mazal-iten deg yiɣil ufella. Imezwura leḥqen ɣer wasif yettusemman asif n Lḥedd. Waleɣ-ten la ttxemmilen rrjulat-nsen akken ad zegren i wasif. Nekk iban-iyi-d ubrid d arqiqan isuÆef rrif n wasif; yessawaḍ ɣer yiwet n tqenṭert. Beddeɣ; neṭqeɣ nniɣ-d: ‚mmuqel kan ɣer wid yebɣan ad zegren asif ur ttalxasen ara! Ad Æeddin meqqar seg tqenṭert-inna.‘

Ufiɣ-d yiwen d ilemẓi isem-is SsaÆid n WaÆrab la d-ileḥḥu yid-i. Sliɣ yenna-yi-d: ‚yalleh a Meẓyan; nekni ad nÆeddi seg ubrid-agi arqiqan yeqreb lḥal.‘. Beddeɣ, stebÆeɣ tamuɣli i ubrid-nni; waleɣ uqbel tiqenṭert-nni, tella tiɣilt n uẓru, abrid-nni yella di tlemmast-is; lqay aṭas ɣef tiɣilt-nni. Lemmer ad yeɣli uleqqaf seg yiri n ugafa, yezmer ad ineɣ amsebrid. Nniɣ-as i yilemẓi-nni: ‚ad nÆeddi seg wansi akka i d-tenniḍ i yeqreb lḥal.‘. Nekcem s abrid-nni; nelḥa armi nÆedda i tiɣilt-nni. Waleɣ ilemẓi-nni yetti-d d yiwen isem-is AÆmiruc. Nbedd; yenna-yi-d: ‚yak nniɣ-ak a Meẓyan; ssyagi i-yeqreb lḥal.‘. Nniɣ-as: ‚welleh ar d ṣṣeḥ.‘

Ufiɣ-d qrib ad awḍeɣ s axxam-iw. Greɣ asurif deg ubrid arqiqan deg yiwen n umkan d ayla-w yettwasemma Tugnatin. Ḥulfeɣ s Æeyyu d akawan. Beddeɣ ad sgunfeɣ
xas akken s yibeddi. Mi beddeɣ; banen-iyi-d yiɣallen-iw s lfaṣmat n lǧerḥ ta ɣer ta. Mmektiɣ-d ayen akken akk yeḍran yid-i. Čččurent-d wallen-iw d imeṭṭawen. Greɣ-d nnehta; nniɣ-d: ‚yella Rebbi.‛. Ufiɣ-d kecmeɣ di tewwurt n uxxam-iw afeɣ tameṭṭut-iw tbedd deg ufrag. Tban-iyi-d am tin yettraǧun deg-i s layas. Mi iyi-d-twala, ḍilleɣ-as di tewwurt tefreḥ. Ma mi d-teẓra lḥala-w yeÆreq leḥsab n ccamat; teččeḥ-d deg-i tamuɣli. Fehmeɣ-tt tebɣa ad iyi-d-testeqsi ɣef wacu yeḍran yid-i. Nekk nniɣ-d deg wul-iw: ‚aÆni ma ḥkiɣ ad ttuɣ. » mmuqleɣ-tt, Æeddeɣ d amsebrid. Kecmeɣ ɣer tzeqqa, snesreɣ isebbaḍen seg yiḍarren-iw. Ṭṭlam yeɣli-d. Fehmeɣ d lawan n tguni. Uliɣ s ameṭreḥ, ẓẓleɣ iman-iw tinnegnit. Fehmeɣ lawan d ttnaṣfa n yiḍ. Nekk lliɣ Æiwzeɣ s ttexmim, iḍes la ireggel ɣef wallen-iw, ẓẓleɣ tinnegnit, ttiɣ iman-iw uɣaleɣ ɣef yidis qubleɣ s afrag, waleɣ tawwurt n tzeqqa telldi-d iman-is, waleɣ zrir lḥal tiniḍ d lawan kan mi yeɣli yiṭij. Ma di tlemmast n ufrag teddukkel tafat deg yiwen n umkan, tnur aṭas tiniḍ d ccumÆa n yiṭij ‚iḍ-agi d ccraÆ n cchada, ad d-yili ibeddi n ccraÆ ɣer lqedra n Rebbi deg umkan-inna n nnur. Tikkelt tamezwarut ad ibedd ṣṣef n lanbiya i d-yellan uqbel Muḥemmed; tikkelt tis snat, ad ibedd Muḥemmed; tis tlata ad ibedd Meẓyan u Muḥ.‛ i d-fehmeɣ di targit. Sliɣ i teɣri tendeh-d si tegnawt tenna-d: ‚ecchadu enna la ilah illa llah u achadu enna marsulin llah.‛ Sliɣ i teɣriwin aṭas, jawbent seg umkan-nni n nnur nnant: « echadu enna la ilah illa llah u achadu enna marsulin llah. » akken armi tlata tikkal. Fehmeɣ telḥeq-d nnuba n
Muḥemmed rasul llah. Tenṭeq teɣri di tegnawt s cchada, tjaweb-as teɣri seg umkan-nni n nnur armi tlata tikkal. Tiɣri-nni tenna-d : « achadu anna la ilah illa llah weḥdahu la carika lah. ». Tiɣri-nni ijawben si lqaÆa twifeq cchada-agi. Nekk lliɣ ɣummeɣ s uÆlaw sbaneɣ-d kan udem-iw. Mi fehmeɣ tewweḍ-d nnuba-w ad beddeɣ ɣer ccraÆ, ḍeggreɣ akkin aÆlaw-nni, ufiɣ-d beddeɣ deg umkan-nni n nnur. Waleɣ amkan n tafat deg tegnawt fehmeɣ ssyin i d-yekka nnur-nni yellan di lqaÆa.

Tendeh-d teɣri-nni n tegnawt s cchada tlata n tikkal. Jawbeɣ am wakken ijaweb Muḥemmed. Yal tikkelt mi ara jawbeɣ, tiɣri-nni tettsuɣu-d fell-i ugar. Fehmeɣ-d am ccix-nni yettjerriben s leɣlaḍ win yesselmad akken ad yetḥeq fell-as ma yessen neɣ yettawi kan lewhi. Maca, nekk tebteɣ ɣef lejwab-iw iṣeḥḥa ur uggadeɣ ur kukreɣ. Xas akken di tikkelt-nni tis tlata tsuɣ-d teɣri-nni ḥulfeɣ tenhez lqaÆa d yigenwan ur sÆiɣ ula d ccek n leɣlaḍ di cchada-w.

Rniɣ fehmeɣ-d amussnaw di ttewḥid ma ixulef tidet xas s leɣlaḍ ad t-iÆaqeb Rebbi s lÆiqab aqesḥan. Mi jawbeɣ tiɣri-nni yesÆan lhiba, suɣeɣ s wakken i tella teɣri-w, nniɣ-d: ‚achadu enna la ilah illa llah, waḥdahu la carika lah.‛ Ifak ccraÆ. ṣSsef amezwaru ɣelḍen di cchada, xeṣren di ccraÆ ɣer lqudra n Rebbi ma dMuḥemmed irbeḥ-it, yewwi lehdiya i as-yefka Rebbi: ‚Kečč a Meẓyan trebḥeḍ di ccraÆ ɣer lqedra, tura ad d-yas wayen ara k-yawin sansi ara d-tawiḍ lehdiya i ak-yefka Rebbi‛ (i d-fehmeɣ di targit).

Waleɣ tawwurt n ufrag telddi-d iman-is; fehmeɣ lamer. Ḥulfeɣ yeččur-d wul-iw d lferḥ. Ffɣeɣ di tewwurt-nni,
ḥusseɣ amzun d amdan i yi-d-yekkan deffir-i iger-iyi-d timetɣaltin, yerfed-iyi ɣer tegnawt. Zziɣ mmuqleɣ akkin wakka ad waliɣ win i yi-irefden ur waleɣ ara. Imir fehmeɣ ttwarefdeɣ s lqudra n Rebbi. Ruḥeɣ s wafug d asawen armi i d-ufiɣ iman-iw deg yiwen n wasif i d-fehmeɣ d lebḥer. Asif-nni iruḥ srid ur yettwalḥaq ara s tmuɣli. Lqay s wazal n lmitra, aman-is bedden ttbanen-d d nnur.

Amkan-nni deg i lliɣ yecba ɣer umkan-nni deg i ttarran tamzizelt iÆewwamen. Fehmeɣ-d lliɣ di lebḥer n ddaw tmurt ur d-ḥebbseɣ ara deg-s alamma leḥqeɣ s anida i d-yenneqḍaÆ ad afeɣ lehdiya i yi-d-yefka Rebbi ad tt-id-awiɣ.

Ufiɣ-d kessleɣ iman-iw ɣef wudem sufella n waman-nni n nnur, la tedduɣ s leɣṣeb-nni n tmesrafegt iɣeṣben di tegnawt, rnu mebla ma ḥerkeɣ aḍar-iw neɣ afus-iw! Meskud tedduɣ ɣer zdat, ttwaliɣ mebÆid nnur am lxiḍ n wureɣ yemÆidel si rrif ɣer rrif deg wasif-nni.

Mi ẓriɣ leḥqeɣ ɣer lxiḍ-nni, ad d-iniɣ waqila d wagi i d lḥedd; ad afeɣ mazal ɣer zdat. Ad Æeddiɣ i lxiḍ-nni n nnur ulac d acu i ttnaleɣ. Ad d-iniɣ ziɣ mačči dagi d nnur kan i d-waleɣ. Yal ameccaq tḍerru-iyi-d akka. Da, mačči da, armi qrib ad awḍeɣ ɣer yiwen n lxiḍ am wid-nni-nniḍen, ufiɣ-d la tedduɣ s laÆqel.

Imir fehmeɣ-d dinna i d lḥedd ansi i d-inneqḍaÆ lebḥer-nni. Nniɣ-d: ‚ma dagi i d lḥedd-is ad nnaleɣ lḥiḍ s yixfawen n yiḍudan-iw.‘

Mi leḥqeɣ ɣer lxiḍ-nni, ẓleɣ ifassen-iw ɣer zdat, nnuleɣ lḥiḍ n lebḥer-nni. Mmɣeɣ ɣef lxiḍ-nni ad waliɣ d acu-t, refdeɣ-t-id, ufiɣ d snesla n wureɣ. Mmuqleɣ ad waliɣ ansi
i d-nneqḍaɛen yixfawen-is, ufiɣ seg snat n twiztin.

Fehmeɣ d lehdiya-nni i yi-d-yettwanefken sɣur Rebbi.

Ḥulfeɣ s lferḥ deg wul-iw xir ma ufiɣ agarruj ur nettfakka.

Rniɣ refdeɣ-d tiwiztin-nni ɣer snesla-nni, sekmumseɣ-tent deg ufus ayeffus, ḥemẓeɣ-tent s yiḍudan-iw akken ur iyi-ɣellint ara deg wasif-nni n nnur i fehmeɣ d lebḥer n ddaw tmurt. Ufiɣ-d iman-iw dewreɣ-d akken ad d-uɣaleɣ.

Teḍra-yi-d deg tuɣalin am wakken mi ruḥeɣ. Mi qrib ad d-awḍeɣ la tedduɣ s laɛqel. Waleɣ amcic d awraɣ rrif n wasif-nni iččeḥ-d tamuɣli s afus-nni yeṭṭfen lamana.

Fehmeɣ-t la yi-d-yettgabar ad d-yemmeɣ fell-as ad tt-yawi, ḥḥemẓeɣ afus-iw, neṭqeɣ s amcic-nni nniɣ-as: ‚tagi d lehdiya i yi-d-yefka Rebbi xas ur ṭṭamaɛ ara ad tt-tawiḍ. Mačči d lɛebd i yi-tt-id-yfkan, welleh ma tewwiḍ-tt.‘

Σeddeɣ i umcic-nni, waleɣ jidda ad tt-yerḥem Rebbi teqqim tsenned ɣer lḥiḍ-nni i d-yellan d lḥedd ansi yebda wasif-nni. Waleɣ-tt tɛuss-iyi-d am umcic-nni. Neṭqeɣ nniɣ-as: ‚xas ur ṭṭamaɛ ara ad tt-tawiḍ a jidda, tagi d lehdiya i yi-d-yefka Rebbi.‘ . Σeddeɣ i jidda ufiɣ-d zdat-i takuzint n useḥmu daxel n wasif-nni n nnur. Takuzint-nni tban-iyi-d-texsi.

Fehmeɣ-tt d asenduq-iw n unejmuɛ. Refdeɣ-as tadimt, skecmeɣ afus-iw ad sserseɣ lamana-nni. Fehmeɣ-d di targit tenna-d: ‚Ḥader ad tebruḍ i lehdiya-nni. Atan yerna-ak-id Rebbi tis snat ad truḥeḍ ad tt-id-tawiḍ a Meẓyan seg umkan-nni ansi i d-tewwiḍ lehdiya tamezwarut.‘. Jebdeɣ-d afus-iw, ḥemẓeɣ-t akken ur iyi-yettruḥu ara ddheb-nni. Dewreɣ iman-iw, uɣaleɣ s amkan-nni. Teḍra-iyi-d am tikkelt-nni tamezwarut. Mi d-
uɣaleɣ leḥqeɣ-d ɣer wansi akken i ruḥeɣ, daɣen ufiɣ-d amcic-nni akked jidda. Rnu tikkelt-agi sḥerṣen-d fell-i ugar n tikkelt-nni tamezwarut. Mi skecmeɣ afus-iw ɣer tkuzint-nni i d-fehmeɣ d asenduq-iw, fehmeɣ-d daɣen mazal lehdiya tis tlata. Uɣaleɣ wwiɣ-d tis tlata-nni rniɣ-tt ɣer tmezwura. Tikkelt-agi ur d-ufiɣ la amcic la jidda. Mi leḥqeɣ ɣer tkuzint-nni, ufiɣ-tt di tlemmast n ubrid yellan d abrid n lkermus deg yiwen n umkan nnig umdun aqbur yettusemman Amdun Ibehlal. Tamdult n usenduq-nni tettwarfed. Beddeɣ rriɣ leḥsab i laɛtab-iw, ufiɣ ur iyi-iruḥ wara; tlata snasel n wureɣ d setta n twiztin. Mi wehheɣ afus-iw ɣer texzant-nni, mmuqleɣ ɣer daxel ad waliɣ anida ara sserseɣ takemmust-iw s lemḥadra, ad waliɣ ma di leḥṣin d tezdeg waleɣ irrig n tmes la yettemlawaj daxel n tkuzint-nni. Imir fehmeɣ-tt d takuzint n tmes, rnu d wid-nni ur nezmir ara ad iyi-sɣiflen akken ad iyi-ḥewṣen lehdiya-nni i yi-xedmen taḥraymit yugaren tayeḍ s tkuzint-nni. Ad teffeɣ nutni ulac, nekk nneɛtabeɣ ɣef ulac.

Nniɣ-d awwah. Swexreɣ-d afus-nni si tmes. Lliɣ qummceɣ uɣaleɣ beddeɣ s tiddi-w. Sserseɣ afus-nni ayeffus ɣef lewhi n wul-iw, rniɣ s ufella-s afus azelmaḍ, ḥemẓeɣ-ten ɣer yidmaren-iw, neṭqeɣ s lferḥ d wurfan, nniɣ-d: « Meẓyan ur yettarra ara ddheb ɣer tmes. »

Ukiɣ-d si targit !

1981

- 243 -
Ṭṭsen yimjuhad

Rezfeɣ s axxam n yimawlan-iw, kecmeɣ ɣer texxamt n jidda. Ufiɣ tasebbalt teččur d baṭaṭa. Fehmeɣ d jidda i tt-ijemɛen d tamekkut-is. Neṭqeɣ nniɣ-as : « ziɣ tesɛiḍ tasebbalt n baṭaṭa.‛. Jidda tessusem. Rniɣ waleɣ taḥbult d tezgnet n temtunt rsent deg ubeḥnuq n uɣrum akked uqedduḥ sufella n lkanun. Fehmeɣ-d ad d-asen yirgazen d inebgawen s axxam-nni. Refdeɣ tamdult i uqedduḥ-nni ad waliɣ ma d tagella ara nessenɛet ur nettsetḥi ara yes-s, ufiɣ d tagella yelhan. Rriɣ tadimt-nni s lferḥ, nniɣ-d: ‚meqqar ur nettneḥcam ara mi ara nqabel irgazen ara d-yawi Meẓyan ad ččen. Tagella-agi d lɛali-tt, yella deg-s ula d aksum.‛

Ufiɣ-d lliɣ di tzeqqa n yimawlan-iw. Waleɣ aṭas n yirgazen ṭṭsen deg wussu, ɣummen iqerray-nsen s waɛlaw. Llant snat n teqcicin d timejṭaḥ: yiwet d yelli, tayeḍ d yelli-s n gma ṭṭsent di rrif s wussu wḥed-sent. Nekk iweḥḥa-iyi-d Rebbi nella di lweqt n lgirra. Irgazen-nni d imjuhad-nneɣ. Lɛesker n waɛdaw usan-d qrib ad d-awḍen. Uggadeɣ ad ten-id-afen ṭṭsen ad ten-ṭṭfen s ufus am iyuzaḍ. Ata yiwen n umjahed yekcem-d di tewwurt. Mi waleɣ lewṣayef n wudem-is d Meẓyan. Mi mmuqleɣ tafekka-s d afɣul! Hraw aṭas, teɣzi yennul asalas alemmas s uqerruy-is. Iruḥ qbala ɣer wid-nni yeṭṭsen yebda-ten s usuki yiwen yiwen. Ttwaliɣ yessenhaz yiwen alamma yuki-d. Mi yuɣal ɣer wayeḍ, win i d-yukin ad yuɣal ɣer
yiḍes. Akken armi i ten-id-yekka akk. Ibedd immuqel deg-sen, iwala mazal-iten akk ɣummen iqerray-nsen. Sliɣ yenna-yasen: ‚mi tugim ad tekkrem; ihi welleh ad ken-rekḍeɣ.‛ Yebda deg-sen si rrif ad ten-irekkeḍ s yiḍarren-is armi i ten-id-yekka akk. Yewweḍ ɣer rrif anida i ṭṭsent tullas-nni, ḥṣiɣ lemmer ad yessers aḍar-is fell-asen ad fexsent. Neṭqeɣ, nniɣ-as: ‚Ɣurk kan ad trekḍeḍ tullas-nni a Meẓyan.‛.Yenna-yi-d: ‚ala, tigi ur tent-rekkḍeɣ ara, ma d wigi yegguman ad kkren, welleh ar ten-rekḍeɣ.‛ Yuɣal ɣer-sen yekcem-iten s yiḍarren-is yerna-asen isuɣan. Neṭqeɣ, nniɣ-as: ‚wid-nni imi ugin ad kkren, hatan ɣer-k rkeḍ-iten.‛

# Ukiɣ-d si targit !

Tasaɛdit 1981

Sliɣ i ndiha

Ufiɣ-d lliɣ gar sin n yiberdan deg umkan yettusemman ‚Iẓra n yiɣil‛ di taddart At Lbir. Yusa-d yiwen s tkerrust, ɛeqleɣ-tt mebɛid( d tin) n Ḥmed n weltma. Mi d-telḥeq ɣer-i, waleɣ anehhar-is d mmi-s n ɛemmi, di lkaɣeḍ isem-is Ḥmed. Yelsa talaba tazeggaɣt,
yeṭṭef ameqyas n tenhart s yiwen n ufus, rnu yeɣṣeb aṭas tanhart-is. Nniɣ-d: ‚attan a Dadda twaɣit.‛

Stibɛeɣ-as tamuɣli, waleɣ ɣer zdat ad yaweḍ ɣer yiwet n ddura anida llant snat n tḥuna ddaw ubrid, gar-asent d ubid yella usqif gar sin n leḥyuḍ n uẓru; lḥiḍ wis tlata yenneqḍaɛ-d yes-s usqif-nni. Anehhar yerra takerrust-nni qbala s asqif-nni. Sliɣ i uqerbeb, fehmeɣ d lḥiḍ n usqif-nni i yeddhem; iɣil d winna i d abrid! Nniɣ-d: ‚mebla ccek anehhar yemmut, takerrust ur d-yettegray wara deg-s.‛.

Uzzleɣ s amkan-nni. Mi wwḍeɣ, ufiɣ teḥbes tkerrust-nniḍen deg ubrid-nni(afurgu). Bab-is d Ḥmed n weltma yeqqim zdat umeqyas n tenhart, ɣer tama-s, yeqqim Ḥmed n ɛemmi akked gma-s Meẓyan. Uɣalen rsen-d la smuqulen takerrust-nni ma ad walin lmara n twaɣit i as-xedmen.

Mmuqleɣ-tt, waleɣ ur tertem ur teqcir! Siggeɣ ɣer daxel, waleɣ ibermilen ččuren d zzit. Fehmeɣ arraw-nni n ɛemmi kran takerrust-nni wwin deg-s zzit-nsen ad tt-ssiǧwen. Gar yibermilen-nni, yella yiwen yugar-iten akk. Waleɣ-t yenqer la yezzazzal zzit. Iruḥ bab n tkerrust-nni yetti-t yerra-as taneqqirt-nni ɣer yidis ufella. Yeḥbes azizzel. Iwexxer-d fell-as. Waleɣ abermil-nni yetti yuɣal am wakken yella, la yezzazzal. Ruḥeɣ seggmeɣ-t. iwala-iyi-d Ḥmed n ɛemmi, yuzzel-d ɣer-i la yettsuɣu fell-i, yenna-yi-d: ‚d acu i k-yewwin ad taɛnuḍ abermil-agi?‛

Rfiɣ si daxel ay ul! Rseɣ-d si tkerrust-nni, tixreɣ fell-asen. La leḥḥuɣ sliɣ i bu tkerrust-nni la itezzem bab n zzit-nni yenna-yas : « Meẓyan yusa-d ad aɣ-iɛiwen, kečč terriḍ-tt d
lexṣara. Nekk ḥemdeɣ Rebbi mi tawaɣit-agi tusa-iyi-d d ttejriba ɣer zdat. » Ufiɣ-d iman-iw di temdint n Tizi Uzezzu. Mlileɣ d yiwen n urgaz ur t-ssineɣ ara. Netta yeqwa ɣezzif. Nelḥa, tayet ɣer tayet, seg ubrid n B.Aɛmiruc armi d le rǧnd-pǧint. Nbedd, yebda la yi-d-iḥekku : « Imaziɣen Imula yenna-yi-d ma d-ttaseɣ ɣer Tizi Uzezzu, lɣaci akk ssawalen-iyi-d ssya-ssya, qqaren-iyi-d ma ak-nawi !? Nekk sɛiɣ sebɛa n watmaten-iw i yi-yettawin yerna zedɣeɣ di Lezzayer ; ttaseɣ-d ad qqimeɣ, mi d leḥdac ad iyi-yawin. Ula d asmi ur seɛɛuɣ ara aṭas n lɣaci, d nekk i ten-izeggiren ɣer zdat.‛

Waleɣ zdat-neɣ tarbaɛt n yilmeẓyen la leḥḥun d akessar deg ubrid n Σebban Remḍan. Argaz-nni yeẓdem ɣer yilmeẓyen-nni la ten-yeswexxir s yifassen-is armi yezwar zdat n terbaɛt-nni. Ufiɣ-d la leḥḥuɣ deg ubrid-nni, zwareɣ zdat-i tarbaɛt n warrac. Mi nelḥeq s anida llan yiǧadarmiyen, waleɣ abrid-nni yenneḍ. Zdat ddura-nni, d yiwet n tgennarit. Uqbel tagennarit-nni, llan sin n yimsulta: yiwen si tama, wayeḍ si tayeḍ. Σussen-d abrid s ddemma n yimesbaniyen-nni.

Arrac-nni sliɣ la ttmeslayen ɣef waddal. Sin seg-sen bɣan ad aɣ-d-sfehmen s umedya ɣef temlilit-nni n waddal deg i wehmen neɣ i asen-iɛeǧben. Mlilen uzzlen amzun yella ččir gar-asen. Mi ten-id-ẓran yimsulta-nni, ɣilen d beddu n tmesbanit. Qẓedmen-d fell-asen, yiwen yeṭṭef aɛekkaz iḥer-iten s tyitwin armi wwḍen ɣer terbaɛt-nni-nsen. Yuɣal umsaltu-nni, s kra n win yelḥeq deg-sen ad as-yesselḥeq tiyita; yesserwel-iten akk. Mi waleɣ rewlen
warrac-nni rewleɣ ula d nekk. Maca greɣ kra n yisurrifen, uɣaleɣ beddeɣ; qebleɣ ad ɣliɣ ur teɣli lqima-w. ḍḥiɣ-d sseḍḥeɣ ma rewleɣ ɣef lḥeq-iw! Mi waleɣ uccen yellha kan d yiɣiden. Lḥiɣ s laɛqel armi sliɣ i tikli deffir-iw, mmuqleɣ, waleɣ amsaltu-nni yerfed aɛekkaz-is, nniɣ-as: ‚lufan ad ak-id-teffeɣ tyita afus ad terwi fell-ak.‛; Čččḥeɣ-t s tmuɣli. Yessers-d aɛekkaz-nni ɣef tayet-iw. Nekk xas akken yerɣa wul-iw mi yi-d-yennul s uɛekkaz, nniɣ-as: ‚arrac-nni mačči d imesbaniyen. D amedya kan i xedmen.‛. Yeḍsa-d ɣer-i. Yuɣal yezzi iman-is yettixer fell-i. Lḥiɣ armi d yiwen n ubraḥ, waleɣ imsulta la ttnadin ɣef wid yettwaɛeqlen di tmesbanit. Win ṭṭfen ad as-ssutren lekwaɣeḍ, ad ṭṭfen isem-is ɣer-sen d ttberga i tikkelt-nniḍen. Ɣeṣbeɣ tikli akken ur iyi-d-ttalḥaqen ara. Ma d arrac-nni waleɣ-ten bedden d tarbaɛt. Fehmeɣ-ten ma rewlen uggaden ad ttwaṭṭfen. Leḥqeɣ s abraḥ wis sin, waleɣ-t ur merkud ara, yestiwen: da d tiɣilt, da d areddix. Greɣ tmuɣli-w ɣer tama ufella, waleɣ tlata n yimɣaren, gar-asen yiwen d lḥaǧ yeqqim di tqiwect n yiwet n tkeddirt. Sin ddaw tkeddirt-nni; Sin-agi, yiwen isem-is Ḥmed wayeḍ Aɛli. Imɣaren-nni ‘d yir leḍyur<’. Sliɣ la ttmestewtawen. Uẓiɣ ɣer-sen ad seɣdeɣ. Sliɣ i yimsulta bdan ndiha ɣef yismawen n wid yettwaṭṭfen di tmesbanit. Nedhen-d ɣef tlata n yismawen. Isem-iw d wis rebɛa. Tfak ndiha.

Ufiɣ-d tama-w yiwen d mmi-s n ɛemmi isem-is Meẓyan, yenna-yi-d: ‚d Rabeḥ –u Aɛli i ixellṣen abwayaj i wid yellan di tmesbanit-agi.‛. Nniɣ-d deg wul-iw: amek? Nekk
ur iyi-ṭṭifen ara, sliɣ nedhen ɣef yisem-iw!‛. Meẓyan yenna-yi-d: ‚d Rabeḥ a la yettaṭṭafen ismawen i wumi ixelleṣ abwayaj!‛. Mmuqleɣ ɣer tama-nni iɣer sliɣ i ndiha, waleɣ yiwen d ilemẓi iɛelleq aqrab ɣer tayet-is, yelsa lbista tettwarqem s yitran n wureɣ akked wid n lfeṭṭa, yeṭṭef tawriqt deg ufus-is. Sliɣ yendeh-d s tlata n yismawen isem-iw d wis rebɛa.

# Ukiɣ-d si targit !

1981

# Awal n yiḍ ‘deffir n uxxam’

Ufiɣ-d iman-iw lliɣ deg yiwen n umkan yettusemman ‘Ugni n At Cennad’ lsiɣ talaba n tserdast. La leḥḥuɣ s uxatel deg yiwen n uzrug n lkermus. Lḥiɣ akken kra n yisurrifen, sliɣ ɣer ugemmaḍ yekker wawal n umceččew. Mi fkiɣ tameẓẓuɣt, ḥeṣneɣ-d awal-nni yekker deg yiwen n uxxam yettusemman ɣef yiwen n umezdaɣ mačči ɣef bab-is amezdaɣ-nni isem-is Sliman u Muḥ, ar dqal sliɣ i teɣri tḍill-d ɣef yiwen n udrar deg i tella taddart Iḥeddaden di lɛerc Mɛatqa. Tiɣri-nni tekka-d si temdint n Tizi Uzezzu. Mi d-teqreb ɣer-i, ad sleɣ la d-tettmeslay seg yal tama. Ameslay-nni ḥeṣneɣ-d d ameslay n tmaziɣt.

- 249 -
Maca yexleḍ am wakken tekcem-d tmeslayt di tayeḍ, ɛyiɣ ssɣadeɣ ur d-fhimeɣ ula d yiwen n yimesli. Lḥiɣ akken s uxatel. La tedduɣ s lekni. Uɣaleɣ beddeɣ s tiddi-w. Ufiɣ-d zdat-i ‘lkaba’ yecban taberduɛt n lɛesker, teččur d ccrab. Fehmeɣ-d am win ara yi-d-yinin: ‚lkaba-nni deg-s tlatin n teqraɛtin n ccrab, attan ad d-tɛeddi tarbaɛt n yikamyunen deg-s setta u tmanyin n yiɛsekriyen.‛

Nniɣ-d deg wul-iw: ‚ad d-ferneɣ settin n yirgazen at nnif seg watmaten-iw, ad asen-fkeɣ azgen azgen n teqraɛt n ccrab akken ad sɛun tirrugza ur ttuggaden ara lmut; ad sqiṭɛeɣ yes-sen i lɛesker, ad nexdem deg-sen axeṣṣar, ad d-nerbeḥ talaba akked leslaḥ.‛

Waleɣ ugemmaḍ-nni s lqerb-iw yettwaxdem ubrid n ukerrus. Ikamyunen ččuren-d d lɛesker la d-teddun. Nekk ɣer-i ulac ula d yiwen n umjahed. Nniɣ-d deg wul-iw: « yewweḍ-d wass-nni i ttraǧuɣ acḥal aya. Maca amek ara qableɣ taluft ?. »

Ufiɣ-d iman-iw ugemmaḍ-nni beddeɣ zdat terbaɛt n yimjuhad, neṭqeɣ nniɣ-asen: « ay atmaten, lmut deg ufus n Rebbi mačči di txencuct n ubeckiḍ. Aṭas i neṣber, aṭas i newwi tudayt<tura tewweḍ-d teswiɛt ideg ad d-nbeggen iman-nneɣ d acu i nella. »

Llheɣ-d yid-sen, qaɛdeɣ-asen imukan. Mi d-iwwḍen lɛesker, neṭṭef fell-asen s rrṣaṣ; ur yeslik ula d yiwen deg-sen.

Ufiɣ-d iman-iw mebɛid deg yiwen n umkan tama n taddart Taxribt. Ttwajerḥeɣ di taɣma la ttazzaleɣ d akessar deg yiwen uɛerqub n uzemmur i d-yezgan nnig wasif. Yiwen n uɛsekri la iyi-d-yeṭṭafar yeqqar-iyi-d: ‚Ḥbes neɣ ad ak-in-wwteɣ...‛
ṭṭef d amuddir. Ddiɣ-tt akken s tmara armi wwḍeɣ ɣer yiwen n umkan iga am tiɣilt. Nniɣ deg wul-iw: ‚ma ɛeddeɣ i tiɣilt-agi dayen selkeɣ.‛ Ttiɣ iman-iw, uzgeɣ-d ddaw tiɣilt-nni. Ḥulfeɣ tuli-iyi-d tfasuxt si lǧerḥ-nni. Ḥṣiɣ ur iyi-tettsellik ara trewla ilaq ad sxedmeɣ taḥraymit.

Èẓleɣ iman-iw tinnegnit amzun mmuteɣ la smuquleɣ s ddaw tiṭ. Mi d-yelḥeq umcum-nni, iṭṭnez-d ɣer-i, iẓẓel-d afus-is ɣer wul-iw ad iẓer ma tfak deg-i tarwiḥt neɣ mazal. Nekk mmɣeɣ ḥewṣeɣ-as-d abeckiḍ-nni, nleqmeɣ ɣer-s, sserseɣ-as abeckiḍ-nni ɣef wul-is, jebdeɣ fell-as s yiwet n terṣaṣt. Yemmermeɣ am uqelwac-nni i tḍurr tugdect.

Yeɣli. Kemmleɣ abrid-iw, zegreɣ ugemmaḍ ɣer yiwen n uɛerqub yettusemman Tala Uɣanim. Rriɣ d asawen deg yiwen n uzrug ur iban ma d abrid neɣ d iɣzer. Ula d tasdarit ur tt-yesɛi ara. Rnu yestewɛa ɣer umkan-nni seg i d-zegreɣ. La leḥḥuɣ yeqqar-d wul-iw: ‚Ahat leḥqen-d lɛesker
Lḥiɣ s usqejdeḥ armi sliɣ i tujjqin n terṣaṣt, beddeɣ waleɣ ɣer zdat tegrurej anect n uleqqaf. Zziɣ s lmaṭ-nni ɣer deffir, mmuqleɣ ɣer ugemmaḍ-nni, ur waleɣ ul d afrux.

Kemmleɣ tikli-w d asawen armi d anida i ufiɣ yenneqḍaɛ-d uzrug-nni s ugafa. Agafa-nni ɛlay s lqis n tiddi-w. Nnig-is, tella yiwet n tiɣilt tga am tirect n wakal neɣ agemmun. Ɣer zdat, tella terga tesɛa tasdarit s ttjur n wulmu.

Nniɣ-d deg wul-iw: ‚Ma ɛeddeɣ i tiɣilt-inna ur iyi-d-ẓran ara lɛesker, ɣur-i ṭṭmeɛ ad sellkeɣ! Tekkaɣ s yifassen-iw ɣef yiri n ugafa-nni, ssiliɣ iman-iw, ttiɣ ɣef tiɣilt-nni, uzgeɣ-d deffir-is d areddix. Zziɣ-d iman-iw, wehheɣ s ubeckiḍ-nni
ɣer tama-nni ugemmaḍ. Mi waleɣ yexla lḥal, lḥiɣ ɣef yifassen d yiḍarren armi kecmeɣ ɣer targa-nni, nniɣ-d: ‚ad ffreɣ iman-iw dagi alamma yeɣli-d ṭṭlam, ad nadiɣ ɣef yimeddukkal-iw.‛

Ufiɣ-d la leḥḥuɣ deg yiwen n uzrug n lkermus deg umkan yettusemman Amalu. Yezga-d ddaw laɛzib-nneɣ. Lḥal qrib d tameddit. ḍilleɣ deg yiwet n tunnḍa n ubrid, mlileɣ-d yiwen n yilemẓi isem-is Rabeḥ. D mmi-s n ccahid aqdim. Ferḥeɣ mi t-id-mlileɣ. Nemsalam, steqseɣ-t ɣef lɛesker ma llan deg wansi akken i d-yekka. Yenna-yi-d: ‚ulac.‛

Nniɣ-as: ‚A Rabeḥ, yya-n yid-i ad tjahdeḍ ɣef tmurt-ik.‛ Yenna-yi-d: ‚Ala a Meẓyan, lǧihad uggadeɣ.‛ Nniɣ-as: ‚lmut deg ufus n Rebbi mačči deg yixef n terṣaṣt. Baba-k yeɣli ɣef nnif. Ilaq ad tedduḍ di later-is. Nniɣ-ak ddu-d yid-i. Mi telsiḍ talaba n yiseɣ, tewwiḍ lḥerma gar yifassen-ik, teddiḍ gar yiḥbiben-ik, tuggdi-nni ad ak-truḥ. Ula d nekk akka i yi-teḍra.‛

Yenna-yi-d: ‚Ala a Meẓyan, uggadeɣ.‛ Nniɣ-as: ‚ur d-yexliq Rebbi aderɣal di ddunit armi i as-yexleq tafat di laxert. D leqrun uya i la ttmettaten yizzayriyen ɣef tmurt-agi. Ula d llufan di dduḥ neɣ di tɛebbuṭ n yemma-s yemmut d ccahid. Amek ara nqabel Rebbi, amek ara nqabel wid ijuhden d wid i mazal ad jahden ɣef tmurt-agi-nneɣ ma nexdaɛ lɛahed<‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚Ala a Meẓyan a gma, uggadeɣ lmut.‛ Nniɣ-as: ‚Ɣur-k lḥeqq a Rabeḥ a gma-tneɣ. Hatan Rebbi ifaq-as i lmut la s-tettaker imdanen-is la ten-tneqq mebla ma tciwer-it. Tura ad yeḥkem fell-as s lmut. Mi tt-yenɣa, kečč d wid i ak-yecban ad tidirem d lebda.‛
Yezmumeg-d ɣer-i s useḍsu-nni n tewreɣ. Nekk rfiɣ fell-as, nniɣ-as: ‚Kečč d Rabeḥ n ddunit neɣ d Rabeḥ n laxert? Welleh ma trebḥeḍ yiwet. Aya afeg fell-i neɣ ad ssifgeɣ laɛmer-ik tura kan.‛. Ssiliɣ abeckiḍ-nni, Rabeḥ ulac-it. Ufiɣ-d iman-iw kecmeɣ ɣer taddart-nneɣ. Ufiɣ-tt ibeddel lḥal-is. Tuɣal d laɛzib n yiɛecciwen yemcaraken s yifragen n uɣanim. Beddeɣ, nniɣ-d: ‚Awwah! Tagi mačči d taddart-nneɣ.‛ ‚Tinna d taddart-ik a Meẓyan. Ixxamen-nni yellan zik, hudden-ten yiɛdawen. Irgazen-nni yellan tekksen lweḥc ɣef taddart, yal wa amek i as-teḍra. Qqimen-d warrac d yimɣaren. Tilawin-nni mi akken tweḥcent, hatent-in cerkent timezduɣin. Ma d axxam-ik yuɣalen d aɛecciw, hatan d alemmas gar yiɛecciwen-nni!‛, i d-fehmeɣ di targit.

Lḥiɣ ɣer zdat. Mi qerrbeɣ ɣer yiɛecciwen-nni, iban-iyi-d ubrid seg ufrag ɣer wayeḍ ulac ansi-nniḍen. La ttwaliɣ tilawin la qeddcent deg yifragen-nni. Beddeɣ nniɣ deg wul-iw: ‚amek ara ɛeddiɣ gar tilawin-agi! D lmuḥal ad ɛeddiɣ nekk di lḥerma n watmaten-iw. Ad uɣaleɣ ɣer deffir, ma yella win i iyi-d-yefka Rebbi, ad yeddu yid-i ad ẓreɣ arraw-iw; ma ulac dayen.‛. Waleɣ lḥan-d tlata n yirgazen, lsan ibernas d iqehwiyen, ccbaḥa n wudmawen-nsen tsiɣ ṭṭeyya. La d-ttezmumugen ɣer-i s teḍssa n sser. ‚Irgazen-nni d arraw n taddart-ik a Meẓyan rnu d imeddukkal-ik.‛ I d-fehmeɣ di targit. Sliɣ nnan-iyi-d: ‚Lɛeslama-k a Meẓyan-nneɣ.‛; ‚Ad aken-iɛuzz Rebbi ay atmaten‛. I asen-rriɣ. Nemlil, nemsalam, nemyesteqsa; ar dqel nniɣ-asen: ‚ulac lɛesker ansi akka i d-tekkam?‛;
ulac, D laman. I iyi-d-nnan., Ihi, ay arraw n taddart-iw ilaq ad tjahdem yid-i. I asen-nniɣ.

Ḍelqen ibernas-nsen, ddmen-d ibeckiḍen, manubrin-ten, bedden-d ɣer-i s lemqadra, nnan-iyi-d: aql-aneɣ yid-k a Meẓyan alamma d ass aneggaru. Ferḥeɣ yes-sen nniɣ-asen: Ddut-d yid-i ad iyi-temlem anida akka zedɣen warraw-iw. Ad ruḥeɣ ad ten-id-ẓreɣ. Ddan-d yid-i.

Nekcem afrag amezwaru, ufiɣ-d iman-iw weḥd-i; kecmeɣ di tewwurt n uɛecciw deg i zedɣen warraw-iw. Ufiɣ tameṭṭut-iw tɛuss-d tawwurt n ufrag amzun taɛlem s tirza-w ɣer-sen. Akken i yi-d-teẓra, thebbec-d ɣer-i s lferḥ yesǧuǧǧgen udem-is am lwerd-nni aleqqaq. A Meẓyan, aql-ak aṭas uya ur d-terziḍ ar twacult-ik. Attan Tasaɛdit teḥseb-ik amzun si laxert i as-d-tuɣaleḍ. I d-fehmeɣ di targit. Nemsalam. Tuɣal tellha-d d leqdic akken ad iyi-d-tgarrez imensi. Acku tɣil ruḥeɣ ɣer-s s lembat. Nekk lliɣ qqimeɣ ɣef tɣalaṭ tama n tewwurt ɛusseɣ iman-iw.

Waleɣ Tasaɛdit teddem-d awren, terna-d aksum amelḥan. Ḥusseɣ s teɣri deg wul-iw tenna-d: seg wasmi i teffɣeḍ ɣer lǧihad a Meẓyan, arraw-ik ctaqen ad rwun lqut, ctaqen aksum ula di lɛid. Ma d Tasaɛdit teḥṣa-k seg wasmi teffɣeḍ ɣer lǧihad, ur teččiḍ talqimt yeḥman. ; I wumi la tqeddceḍ akken a Tasaɛdit? nekk ur sɛiɣ ara lweqt. Ha-ten yimeddukkal-iw di berra la ttraǧun deg-i. Efk-iyi-d kan ciṭ n uɣrum xas d aquran, rnu yi-d sin n yiḥbuben ma llan. Ad awiɣ aɛwin ad ruḥeɣ. I as-nniɣ.

Waleɣ udem-is yerra-t lxiq am yidil yerɣan. Tger-d nnehta ḥulfeɣ tessenhez lqaɛa. Teddem-d tarebɛet n uɣrum;
akken i tgar afus-is s akufi, tuɣal-iyi-d teɣri-nni. Ḥusseɣ tenna-yi-d : « A Meẓyan, aql-ak tettwacegɛeḍ ɣer lɛesker, sellek iman-ik ffeɣ neɣ ad tegluḍ ula s twacult-ik. ».

Neṭṭqeɣ ɣer tmeṭṭut-iw, nniɣ-as: ‚Fiḥel a Tasaɛdit. Dayen ad ruḥeɣ, ḍaqeɣ!‛. Nleqmeɣ wwiɣ lmaṭ-nni gar yifassen- iw ffɣeɣ di tewwurt n ufrag. Lḥiɣ kra n yisurrifen, rṣaṣ yemmeɣ-d fell-i seg yal tama. Mi ḥulfeɣ s tyitiwin-nni, Cahdeɣ s Rebbi. Mi ɣliɣ, uqbel ad iyi-teffeɣ tarwiḥt, ẓriɣ idammen-iw uzzlen ɣef wakal nniɣ-d deg wul-iw: ‚wissen amek ara tkemmel; wissen amek ara tefru; wissen deg yidammen-iw ma ad d-yemmɣi lḥeqq neɣ nneɣlen d iḥramen.‛

Ufiɣ-d iman-iw deg uxxam-nneɣ aqdim, lliɣ akked yemma di lawan n yiḍ. Lliɣ deg wussu Taftilt texsi. Fehmeɣ-d lliɣ urɛad zzewǧeɣ. Sliɣ yekker wawal deffir n uxxam. Awal-nni yexleḍ amzun d awal n warrac mi ara laɛɛben neɣ ttemceččawen. ‚wid-nni a Meẓyan d wid yebɣan ad ak-cewwlen neɣ ak-sbehdlen ɣer yimawlan-ik.‛ I d-fehmeɣ. Ḥulfeɣ yers-d fell-i lweḥc. Rriɣ iman-iw amzun ṭṭseɣ neɣ ur yella wacu i wumi sliɣ. Sliɣ i yemma tessaɛli tiɣri-s, tenna-d: ‚d acu n wawal-agi n yiḍ deffir uxxam-nneɣ?‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Ahat d arrac kan i d-yekkan seg tmeɣra ad ɛeddin d imsebriden.‛; ‚Wigi yal iḍ sekkaren awal deffir n uxxam-nneɣ‛.i yi-d-tenna. Imir fehmeɣ-d ameslay-nni i t-id-yessekkaren d ixṣimen-nneɣ.

Sliɣ i teɣri n urgaz tsuɣ di tlemmast n wagens, tenna-d: ‚ad truḥem neɣ ad d-ffɣeɣ ɣer-wen a ccmayet!‛. Ameslay-nni simmal yettzad, tettzad fell-i teggdi.
uɣaleɣ ssetḥeɣ ma wwiɣ-asen tudayt. Rriɣ tirrugza, suɣeɣ fell-asen, nniɣ-asen : « d acu n wawal-agi n yiḍ deffir uxxam-nneɣ ! ad truḥem neɣ ad n-ffɣeɣ ɣer-wen!‛.

Ameslay yettzad irennu; tuggdi fell-i tettzad trennu. Suɣeɣ akken fell-asen armi tlata tikkal. Nleqmeɣ ffɣeɣ di tewwurt n uxxam. Ufiɣ-d aɛekkaz n wuzzal tama n tewwurt, refdeɣ-t. La leḥḥuɣ . Simmal ttaẓeɣ ɣer zdat awal la yettzad tuggdi la tettzad nekk qqareɣ: ‚Ddnub i yirawen-nwen<‛

Leḥqeɣ ɣer tewwurt n ufrag, tennelday-d weḥd-s. Mi ffɣeɣ ɣer umraḥ, tuggdi-nni tuɣal-iyi d tirrugza. Simmal ttaẓeɣ ɣer zdat tirrugza-nni tettuɣal-iyi-d d lḥerqa, ameslay-nni yettanqas. Mi wwwḍeɣ ɣer deffir n uxxam, ufiɣ lxaṭer! Ferḥeɣ mi ur d-dliɣ ara ɣef twaɣit. Ssiwleɣ-as i yemma nniɣ-as: ‚ulac win yellan dagi deffir n uxxam-nneɣ d awal kan i wumi d-nesla.‛.

‚Mi k-id-ḥulfan teffɣeḍ ɣer-sen i rewlen‛i yi-d-tenna. Mmuqleɣ ɣer tama n wadda, waleɣ sin n wureslen la regglen rran d akessar deg yiwen n uɛerqub iwesɛen aṭas yettwasemma ‘Agni Iḥeddaden’. ‚D ureslen-inna i awen-yessakkaren awal yal iḍ deffir n uxxam-nwen a Meẓyan. Rnu d lewḥuc itetten imdanen.‛ I d-fehmeɣ.

Tzad-iyi lḥerqa, ẓedmeɣ fell-asen. La regglen nekk la tenttabaɛeɣ qqareɣ-asen: ‚Acuɣef i la tregglem ay iḥramen. Rǧut ad nemsefham<‛. Yiwen n wursel ikemmel tarewla-s; ma d wayeḍ yezzi-d fell-i. Netta la d-ileḥḥu nekk la ttaẓeɣ ɣer-s. Mi nemlil refdeɣ aɛekkaz-nni n wuzzal, wwteɣ-t ɣer uqerruy teskurreb-it tyita-nni. Rniɣ-as
tiyitwin. Simmal kkateɣ deg-s yettuɣal d amejṭuḥ armi i d-yuɣal d amcic. Daɣen amcic-nni fehmeɣ-t d lweḥc itetten imdanen. Rniɣ-as tiyitwin yettuɣal-d d amejṭuḥ armi yuɣal d tugdect. Imir fehmeɣ-t yemmut. Zziɣ iman-iw akken ad uɣaleɣ s axxam. Lḥal yella d tiziri amzun d azal. Yuɣal yeɣli-d ṭṭlam d aseṭṭaf. ‚A Meẓyan, amcic-nni yella di ccek ad d-yetḥaya.‛ I d-fehmeɣ. Refdeɣ tamuɣli-iw ɣer tegnawt, nniɣ-d deg wul-iw: ‚Uh a Rebbi yeɣli-d fell-i ṭṭlam ur ferrẓeɣ ara abrid ɣer uxxam. Rnu ma yetḥaya-d umcic-agi, ur t-ferrẓeɣ ara ansi ara i d-yekk alamma yečča-iyi.‛ Tban-iyi-d ṭṭiya di tegnawt amzun d lemri-nni amejṭuḥ deg i d-yewwet yiṭij. Mmuqleɣ zdat-i waleɣ ṭṭya-nni !‛ tafat-nni a Meẓyan, d Rebbi i ak-tt-id-yfkan di ṭṭlam-ik. Aniɣer terriḍ ad teddu zdat-ik.‛ I d-fehmeɣ. La leḥḥuɣ tafat-nni la tetteddu zdat-i. Mi kecmeɣ ɣer ubrid aqdim yellan d abrid uḍar ddaw laɛzib-nneɣ, sliɣ yekker wawal di tama ibeɛden ciṭ ɣef deffir n uxxam-nneɣ. Amkan-nni yettwasemma tugnatin. Uzzleɣ ɣer din. Mi leḥqeɣ, ufiɣ iwtal la ttneggizen ttmeslayen am yimdanen! iwtal-nni d iwraɣen. Ula d yiwtal-nni tetten imdanen. Rnu ccwal-nni ssekkren-t s nneqma-k d nneqma n yimawlan-ik a Meẓyan. I d-fehmeɣ.

Refdeɣ ɣer-sen aɛekkaz-nni n wuzzal, yal wa aniɣer yerra. Yeqqim-d umcic d awraɣ. Fehmeɣ-t ula-d netta seg yiwtal-nni. La iyi-d-yettgaber akken ad d-yemmeɣ fell-i. Gubreɣ-t s uɛekkaz-nni ɣer uqerruy. Teḍra yid-s am umezwaru-nni. Mi yuɣal d tugdect, ḥebseɣ tiyita. Zziɣ iman-iw ad ruḥeɣ ɣer uxxam. Sliɣ yujjaq. Mi zziɣ ɣer-s,
waleɣ-t  yuɣal-d d  azrem. Fehmeɣ-t  ad  d-yuɣal am wakken yella. Uɣaleɣ ɣer-s la t-kkateɣ yettijjiq yettiɣzif. Fehmeɣ-t mi ara yiɣzif, ad d-yuɣal d azrem, ad iyi-yenneḍ ɣef yiri-w. La gezzmeɣ deg-s s yifassen-iw netta irennu teɣzi.

Ufiɣ-d iman-iw beddeɣ di tlemmast n ufrag-nneɣ. Azrem-nni  mazal-it yid-i. Lḥal yuɣal-d d azal. Ssiwleɣ-as i yemma nniɣ-as: ‚sixef-im awi-iyi-d lmus n ttesḍila ad gezmeɣ aẓrem-agi uqbel ad yuɣal d azrem ad iyi-yeqqes neɣ ad iyi-yexneq s yifassen-iw, ata ur lḥiqeɣ ara anegzum deg-s.‘ Yemma la tesmaɛraq. Fehmeɣ-tt ur d-tḥar ara deg-i. Uɣaleɣ am wasmi lliɣ jewǧeɣ. Waleɣ tameṭṭut-iw tbedd di tlemmast n wagens la d-tesmuqul deg-i. Sawleɣ-as, kif kif. Ula d nettat la tesmaɛraq fell-i. Sḥerṣeɣ deg-s akken ad d-tessixef s lmus-nni armi uyseɣ seg-s. Aẓrem-nni yecban d azrem ineggez-d ɣer yiri-w la itenneḍ ɣef temgarṭ-iw. Nekk rfiɣ la gezzmeɣ deg-s s yifassen-iw s taxfafit armi i t-leḥqeɣ s unegzum, kkseɣ-t-id seg yiri-w.

Ufiɣ-d iman-iw kecmeɣ di yiwet n tewwurt ‘uberyir’, ṭṭfeɣ tameṭṭut-iw seg ufus. ‚A Meẓyan, aql-ak tkecmeḍ ɣer laxert, tewwiḍ tameṭṭut-ik ad as-id-tesneɛteḍ leqser n tmeṭṭut n umjahed i as-id-tewwiḍ ad tezdeɣ asmi ara temmet‘. I d-fehmeɣ di targit.

Mi as-ḥkiɣ i Tasaɛdit, waleɣ yessaɣ-d wudem-is s tafat n lferḥ, tenna-yi-d: ‚Anida yella leqser-agi i yi-d-tewwiḍ a Meẓyan?‘;  ‚Ad t-id-naf ɣer zdat-inna‘ i as-nniɣ. La nleḥḥu di tlemmast n yiwen n ubraḥ, nerra d akessar ɣer tama tayeffust-iw ansi i yi-tella Tasaɛdit. La ttwaliɣ d
abraḥ kan. Ma ɣer tama tazelmaḍt, llan yixxamen n ṭṭub d iqdimen ttwahudden. Iɛecciwen d imerka akked yiguduyen. Tasaɛdit mi yi-d-testeqsa ɣef leqser-nni, nniɣ-as : « lḥu kan yid-i ur ttayes ara a Tasaɛdit leqser i am-d-wwiɣ ad t-id-naf ɣer zdat-agi.‛. Ɣer zdat-nni mi nɛedda i liḥala-nni yettwarkin di tama-nni tazelmaḍt, waleɣ yella uhicur aleqqaq akked ttjur-nni yettilin di lejnan. Llan yijeǧǧigen. Ma di tama tazelmaḍt, d abraḥ ilem. Lḥiɣ armi qeḍɛeɣ layes, nniɣ deg wul-iw : « ulac leqser di laxert. Yexdeɛ-iyi Rebbi, yeskiddeb fell-i, tura ad nneḥcameɣ amek ara as-iniɣ i Tasaɛdit. »; ‚mmuqel ɣer tama tayeffust-ik ad twaliḍ a Meẓyan!‛ I d-fehmeɣ. Mi mmuqleɣ ɣer tama-nni, waleɣ yiwet n lbila tella-d s lqerb-iw tettwabna ɣef wagens amezwaru i yeɛlayen ɣef wakal s lqis n tiddi-w. lbila-nni tesɛa ṭṭabeɛ n lebni tiniḍ tettwamsel s lmital! A Meẓyan, d winna i d leqser n tmeṭṭut n umjahed i as-d-tewwiḍ i Tasaɛdit ad tezdeɣ-it dagi di laxert asmi ara d-temmet‛. I d-fehmeɣ. Mi zziɣ ɣer tmeṭṭut-iw akken ad tt-sferḥeɣ, ulac-itt. Nniɣ-d deg wul-iw: ‚aniɣer akka i terra Tasaɛdit? Tura kan i tella yid-i ! anida ara tt-id-afeɣ tura ? »; ‚Tasaɛdit attan daxel n leqser-nni a Meẓyan. Mi tekcem ad twali, taɛǧeb-as lḥala, tewwi-tt zzehwa teṭṭes. Tzemreḍ ad tkecmeḍ ɣer leqser-nni ad tt-id-tessakiḍ. Axaṭer ma teǧǧiḍ-tt-id dagi di laxert ur tt-terriḍ ara yid-k ɣer ddunit, mi ara d-taki si targit ad tafeḍ temmut deg wussu‛. I d-fehmeɣ. Waleɣ lbila-nni i d-fehmeɣ d leqser tesɛa tlata n tewwura. Talmezwarut i d-yellan ɣer berra tettwaxdem s
yicebbaken n wuzzal; tis snat s yicebbaken n wuzzal terna tesɛa lmeryat; tis tlata kifkif terna tesɛa lizer deffir lmeryat-nni; lizer-nni d amellal am lekfen-nni n lmeyytin. Nekk ufiɣ-d ur zmireɣ ara ad ssaliɣ iman-iw ɣer tewwurt-nni tamezwarut; ɛyiɣ tekkayeɣ s yifassen-iw ɣef yiri n wagens-nni armi uyseɣ, wexxreɣ-d ɣer deffir. Nniɣ-d deg wul-iw: ‚Ansi ara yaliɣ a Rebbi? Rnu tiwwura-inna ttwamedlent mebla leqful! seg wasmi i d-ldiɣ allen-iw ɣer ddunit nekk d urfan d lxiq d aneẓẓef<ziɣ lhem n ddunit yeṭṭafar-d ɣer laxert. »; « Mmuqel ɣer tama tayeffust!‛. I d-fehmeɣ. Mi mmuqleɣ, waleɣ aɛekkaz n wuzzal yenta deg wakal. Aɛekkaz-nni yesɛa akruci deg yixef ufella, yennemdal s leqfel d amejṭuḥ. Leqfel-nni iban-iyi-d d leqfel i tesɛa tbalizt n wuzzal tamejṭuḥt ideg i sruseɣ lekwaɣeḍ n tira-w. ‚A Meẓyan, s leqfel-inna i leddint tewwura n leqser-nni‛‛. I d-fehmeɣ.

Ufiɣ-d tisura n tbalizt-nni inu deg ufus-iw. Akken kan wehheɣ taarut ɣer leqfel-nni yelddi. AÆekkaz-nni ulac-it. Sliɣ i useqseq n rrÆud, waleɣ la tezluz lqaÆa-nni. Nniɣ-d: « ay ay ay a tin i xedmeɣ, ikellex-iyi Rebbi. Tura ad ihudd leqser-inna, ad temmet TasaÆdit daxel-is. Mi ara akiɣ seg targit ad tt-afeɣ deg wussu temmut.‛ Waleɣ ddaw wagens-nni tettwaxdem-d snesla am snesla n tmacint-nni i ixeddmen iberdan<tdewwer tlata n tikkal ur zmireɣ ara ad n-kecmeɣ ɣur-m ad akem-ẓreɣ.‛; ‚ eddi-d deffir leqser ad d-tafeḍ tawwurt seg ara tizmireḍ ad d-tkecmeḍ ɣer-i ad iyi-teẓreḍ‛. I iyi-d-tenna. Mi d-kkiɣ deffir-nni, ur waleɣ la tawwurt wala ṭṭaq! daɣen yeɣli-d
fell-i lweḥc. Fehmeɣ-d leqser-nni d tanṭelt. Llheɣ la ssawaleɣ a TasaÆdit armi bbuḥebḥeɣ. Uɣaleɣ la sḥissifeɣ armi i d-nniɣ : « amek ara xedmeɣ a Rebbi ? », ‚A Meẓyan, nadi albaÆḍ seg at laxert, ini-as ad yekcem ɣer tenṭelt ad tt-id-yessaki, axaṭer ulaxert ur yettawḥac ara tanṭelt‛. I d-fehmeɣ.

Waleɣ akamyun yelḥeq-d yeḥbes di tama n wadda. Uzzleɣ ɣer-s. Ufiɣ anehhar zdat umeqyas n ukamyun-nni, sin bedden di tkalict n ukamyun-nni. ‚A Meẓyan, sin-nni n yixeddamen d wid yessizdigen lḥala dagi di laxert.‛ I d-fehmeɣ.

Mi wwḍeɣ ɣer-sen, nniɣ-asen: ‚ad d-tasem ad tkecmem ɣer tenṭelt-inna n TasaÆdit ad tt-id-tessukim akken ad tt-rreɣ yid-i ɣer ddunit. Acku ma ǧǧiɣ-tt-id dagi di laxert; ma ara ukiɣ seg targit ad tt-afeɣ temmut deg wussu. Wwiɣ-tt-id akken ad as-d-sneÆteɣ leqser n tmeṭṭut n umjahed i as-d-ḥelleɣ ad tezdeɣ-it dagi di laxert asmi ara temmet. Attan daxel-is yewwi-itt nadam.‛

Rsen-d sin-nni i d-fehmeɣ d ixeddamen<wwḍen ɣer tɣalaṭ-nni n lbila, ṭṭinzen, refden-as tamdelt am wakken ara ldin tawwurt n deffir n tkerrust. Ddmen-d seg-s akajut n ccrab! Rran-as tamdelt-nni. Neṭqeɣ; nniɣ-asen: ‚yella ccrab dagi di laxert?‛; ‚wagi d ccrab n lehmumat.‛ I iyi-d-nnan. « a Meẓyan, ccrab n laxert ẓid xir n lgazuz n ddunit. » i d-fehmeɣ. Wwin asenduq-nni n ccrab, ssilin-t ɣer ukamyun. Akamyun-nni ur ḥṣiɣ amek yettwaddem yuɣal d ulac ! ; « a Meẓyan, TasaÆdit teṭṭes daxel-inna. Ma teǧǧiḍ-tt-id dagi di laxert, ur tt-terriḍ ara yid-k ɣer ddunit,
mi ara d-takiḍ seg targit ad tafeḍ temmut ṣṣura-s deg wussu; axaṭer teǧǧiḍ-d rruḥ-is dagi di laxert. » i d-fehmeɣ. ‚ay amxix-iw, ay anyir-iw. Amek ara xedmeɣ?...‛ Rriɣ-tt daɣen ɣef yineẓman am wakken i nneẓmeɣ ɣef yir tilufa di tilawt. La ttawiɣ ttarraɣ am Winna i d-teǧǧa tmacint. Ssiwḍeɣ armi i d-nniɣ: ‚lmeḥna n ddunit teḍfer-iyi-d ɣer laxert!‛. Mmuqleɣ ɣer tama n wadda, waleɣ yiwet n temraḥt tettban-d am wannar. Llan deg-s tlata n yirgazen wa zdat wa la tennḍen am yizgaren-nni yessarwaten. Merra merra ad waliɣ yiwen iṭṭinez ɣer lqaÆa amzun d kra i d-yeddem.. ‚a Meẓyan wid-inna d at laxert. I d-fehmeɣ Uzzleɣ ɣer yirgazen-nni, mi leḥqeɣ ɣer-sen, ḥkiɣ-asen tameḍrurt-iw, nniɣ-asen: ‚tura ad tkecmem ɣer-s ad tt-id-tessakim.‛. Ibedd-d ɣer-i uneggaru-nni iwehha-iyi-d s uḍaḍ-is ccahed yenna-yi-d: ‚ala, ala, ala. Nekni memnuÆ fell-aneɣ ad nqerreb akk ɣer lḥurum-inna.‛. Imir banen-d wudmawen-nsen am yiqellalen-nni i teḥres tmes deg wuɣud. ḍḥiɣ-d ttuɣ merra ayen yeḍran yid-i n lḥif d uɣilif<uɣaleɣ-asen ɣer ttiha, nniɣ-as: ‚ayɣer akka i tqeḍÆem tiɣin n wawal? inna i as-d-wwiɣ i TasaÆdit ad tt-id-tessakiḍ la teqqareḍ memnuÆ fell-aneɣ! Yak kunwi d at laxert ur tettawḥacem ara mi ara tkecmem ɣer tenṭelt? Neɣ ula dagi di laxert mazal ad teskiddibem fell-neɣ?‛, ‚Nniɣ-ak ur nezmir ara ad nqerreb ɣer lḥurum-inna ula s tmuɣli‛. I iyi-d-yenna. Mi yerfed tamuɣli-s ɣer din am wakken yemmuqel ɣer ccumÆa n yiṭij<Acuɣef? ‚AÆni tessetḥam s lḥala-agi-nwen? Llah ibarek, aql-aken labas : timira, icebbuben slulben. Mačči d menwala i awen-imecḍen s ucicwar<ikustimen xas qqarsen akk meÆna ḥsiɣ akken i awen-d-ttwaxedmen seg lxareǧ. Tqebbam ma mačči d azzug llah ibarek; ttqacir d iberkanen. Xuṣṣen-ken yisebbaḍen urÆad i awen-d-leḥqen seg tmura n lberrani<anaɣ nekni yessarwaten times n ddunit ur nettsetḥi ara s lḥala i aɣ-d-yefka Rebbi. as, nniɣ-as : « baba ijuhed i yiman-is nekk juhdeɣ i yiman- iw. Mmuqel ɣer leqser-inna n tmeṭṭut n umjahed i as-id- wwiɣ i tmeṭṭut-iw ad tezdeɣ-it dagi di laxert. Mmuqel, mmuqel! Ttixreɣ fell-asen. Lḥiɣ tlata n yisurrifen d asawen deg ubraḥ-nni. Mmektiɣ-d TasaÆdit. Uɣaleɣ armi d aneẓẓef- nni. « a Meẓyan nadi ɣef tilawin n yimjuhad yeffɣen ɣer ttemriḥ amer ad tafeḍ TasaÆdit tella gar-asent. Tilawin n yimjuhad yeffɣen ɣer ttemriḥ ad tent-tafeḍ di tama ufella n ubraḥ-nni.‛ I d-fehmeɣ. Mi leḥqeɣ ɣer tama-nni ufella, ufiɣ yiwet n tlemẓit teqqim ɣef yiwen n ṣṣur tÆelleq-d iḍarren-is ɣef ṣṣur-nni la ten-tesselÆab am tin i sellen i ccna teÆǧeb-as aṭas ; ṣṣur-nni Ælay s lqis n tiddi-w. Tilemẓit-nni d acu d ṭṭabaÆ n lqedd i as-yefka Rebbi! D acu d nnur-nni n ṣṣifa-s! d acu d sser-nni!<uqbel ara awḍeɣ ɣer-s tenna- yi-d: ‚lÆeslama-k a Meẓyan-nneɣ.‛, ‚Ad kem-iÆuzz Rebbi a weltma taÆzizt‛. I as-nniɣ. Ifuk azmumeg-nni, tuɣal-d am wakken i tella d tilemẓit! yes-k‛. I iyi-d-tenna. –Nniɣ-as: ‚Ad akem-iÆuzz Rebbi a weltma. Yewwi-iyi-d Rebbi di targit ad myeẓreɣ yid-wen, ad uɣaleɣ ɣer ddunit‛.

Terna testerḥeb yes-i. Ḥkiɣ-as taluft-iw ɣef TasaÆdit nniɣ-as: ‚ur teẓriḍ ara TasaÆdit ma teffeɣ-d ɣer ttemriḥ akked d tlawin-nni n yimjuhad i d-yeffɣen? » Tenna-yi-d: ‚Ur tt-waleɣ ara. Tilmawin-nni n yimjuhad hatent daxel n texxamt-inna. Ruḥ kcem ɣer-sent amer ad tt-tafeḍ tella gar-asent!‛. Tban-iyi-d texxamt zdat-i. Lḥiɣ, mi leḥqeɣ, siggeɣ ɣer daxel n texxamt-nni. Waleɣ tilawin qqiment.

Banent-iyi-d am tid i la yettraǧun !. ‚Tilawin-nni, d tilawin n yimjuhad i d-yeffɣen ɣer ttemriḥ, hatent-an la ttraǧunt taḥeffaft ad d-tas ad sent-temceḍ icebbuben-nsent. Qerreb ɣer-sent amer ad tafeḍ TasaÆdit teffeɣ-d yid-sent ɣer ttemriḥ.‛ I d-fehmeɣ.

Mi mmuqleɣ ɣer tilawin-nni, d acu i d ccbaḥa-nni-nsent! D acu i d sser-nni n wudmawen-nsent! D acu i ttfaṣil n tlaba-nni-nsent!...ssetḥeɣ seg-sent. Zziɣ-d iman-iw akken ad d-uɣaleɣ. Sliɣ nnant-iyi-d: ‚kcem-d kcem-d a Meẓyan-nneɣ! Mreḥba yes-k ɣer-neɣ.‛. Nniɣ-asent: ‚Ad kent-iÆuzz Rebbi a yisetma.‛. Qerrbeɣ ɣer-sent, steqseɣ-tent ɣef TasaÆdit.

Nnant-iyi-d : « TasaÆdit ulac-itt gar-anteɣ. UrÆad i d-teffiɣ ɣer ttemriḥ. ». Nniɣ-asent: ‚Dayen ihi, qqimemt di rreḥma n Rebbi.‛; « a Meẓyan, TasaÆdit mazal-itt teṭṭes daxel n leqser-nni. » I d-fehmeɣ. Rriɣ deg yidis deg ubraḥ-nni la leḥḥuɣ tneẓmeɣ am wakken i ttneẓmeɣ di tlufa n tilawt.

« a Meẓyan, TasaÆdit teÆǧeb-as lḥala n leqser-nni, tewwi-tt zzehwa teṭṭes. Kečč tura kan ad takiḍ seg targit. Rnu ma
ur terriḍ ara TasaÆdit yid-k ɣer ddunit ad tt-tafeḍ temmut deg wussu, axaṭer teǧǧiḍ-d rruḥ-is dagi di laxert. » I d-fehmeɣ. « Aḥlil a Rebbi aḥlil, ula d lferḥ-iw yettuɣal d lqerḥ; ula d laxert-iw d times. AÆni nekk d uday n Rebbi; aÆni nekk d aÆdaw n Rebbi? Acuɣef akka a Rebbi i ttxelliṣeɣ ayen ur ttwalaseɣ? Acuɣef ur ttɣelliteɣ ayen i iɣef ttneÆtabeɣ! I d-nniɣ.

Waleɣ axxam zdat-i yettwabna d aɣezfan. Yettwaxdem s ssiman ḥesri. YesÆa tawwurt deg yiwet n tqernit. ‚a Meẓyan, axxam-nni d rreḥma n Rebbi. Kcem ɣer daxel-is.‛ I d-fehmeɣ. Kecmeɣ di tewwurt, ufiɣ axxam-nni sqef-is d igenni: ur yesÆi ara ssqef. Rnu yeččur d lɣaci; tilawin d yirgazen. Di lɣaci-nni llan wid i ttwaliɣ d icebḥanen wudmawen-nsen sÆan sser la d-ttezmumugen ɣer-i; llan wiyaḍ d ucmiten di lewṣayef-nsen banen-iyi-d kukran seg-i neɣ uggaden. ‚Aql-ik a Meẓyan tettwakkelfeḍ di rreḥma n Rebbi, tura ndeh ɣef lɣaci-nni: win yellan d uday n lÆibad, ad yeqqim di rreḥma n Rebbi; win yellan d uday n Rebbi, ad yeffeɣ si rreḥma n Rebbi.‛ I d-fehmeɣ.

Ḥulfeɣ s yiwen n lferḥ urǧin ferḥeɣ-t di ddunit-iw. Nedheɣ ɣef lɣaci-nni, nniɣ-asen: ‚a win yellan d uday n lÆibad ad yeqqim di rreḥma n Rebbi; win yellan d uday n Rebbi, ad yeffeɣ si rreḥma n Rebbi.‛. Waleɣ kra d ucmiten, ffɣen di tewwurt. Rniɣ nedheɣ tikkelt tis snat. Waleɣ rnan wiyaḍ d ucmiten, ffɣen di tewwurt. Llan seg-sen yirgazen llant tilawin. Ma d kra-nniḍen d ucmiten ur ffiɣen ara, la d-smuqulen ɣer-i. Banen-iyi-d am wakken ffren iman-nsen la ttraǧun alamma sweÆdeɣ ɣer-sen akken ara ffɣen.
« A Meẓyan, ini-asen i lɣaci-nni ulac tufra zdat Rebbi. » I d-fehmeɣ. ‚A win yellan d uday n lÆibad, ad yeqqim di rreḥma n Rebbi dagi di laxert; win yellan d uday n Rebbi ma yeffer iman-is ad yeḥṣu ulac tuffra zdat Rebbi, ad t-yessufeɣ si rreḥma-s ad as-yernu lÆiqab ugar ɣef wakken i d-yewwi ad yettuÆaqeb ». I asen-nniɣ.

Waleɣ ffɣen-d akk wid-nni i la yettraǧun tuffɣa. Uqbel ad d-nedheɣ tikkelt-nniḍen, waleɣ tarbaÆt n tlawin ffɣent di tewwurt. Tid-nni wehmeɣ ɣef wayɣef i ffɣent seg rreḥma n Rebbi acku ur iyi-d-banent ara d tucmitin! ‚tura a Meẓyan ur d-yeqqim wucmit di rreḥma n Rebbi. Attan TasaÆdit ɣer-k, tzemreḍ ad tt-tesferḥeḍ s leqser-nni n tmeṭṭut n umjahed i as-d-tewwiḍ ad tezdeɣ-it dagi di laxert.‛ I d-fehmeɣ.

Waleɣ TasaÆdit tbedd tama n tewwurt. Tban-iyi-d tecbeḥ tesÆa sser ugar ɣef wakken i tt-ttwaliɣ di tilawt. Uqbel ad neṭqeɣ ɣer-s, tesfinxer-d ɣer-i s yimeṭṭi, xesrent lewṣayef n wudem-is. Sliɣ tenna-yi-d: ‚nekk a Meẓyan d tudayt n Rebbi. Ad ffɣeɣ seg rreḥma n Rebbi.‛

Truḥ akken ad teffeɣ di tewwurt, ḥebseɣ--tt-id acku fehmeɣ-tt d leɣlaḍ i tɣleḍ deg yiman-is. ḍsiɣ ɣer-s; nniɣ-as: ‚ala a TasaÆdit. Kemm d tudayt n lÆibad mačči d tudayt n Rebbi. Dagi ara teqqimeḍ yid-i di rreḥma n Rebbi. TasaÆdit tzad di lḥala-nni tucmit la tẓeddem akken ad teffeɣ di tewwurt, teqqar-iyi-d: ‚nekk a Meẓyan d tudayt n Rebbi ad ffɣeɣ si rreḥma n Rebbi. Ma ulac ad izad fell-i lÆiqab.‛. Nekk ḥebseɣ-tt-id s yifassen-iw acku ur yeqbil ara wul-iw ad teffeɣ seg rreḥma n Rebbi tmeṭṭut-
nni yesrewten yid-i times n ddunit< awdeɣ nniɣ-as: ‚ala a TasaÆdit, ad teqqimeḍ yid-i dagi di rreḥma n Rebbi. Kemm d tudayt n lÆibad mačči d tudayt n Rebbi. Rnu kemm d tameṭṭut n umjahed. Hatan wwiɣ-am-d leqser ad tzedɣeḍ-t dagi di laxert.‛

TasaÆdit terna tzad deg yir lḥala-nni. Nekk yekcem-iyi ccek fell-as. ḥ Ḥulfeɣ s wul-iw yuɣal d uɣud n tmes, yenna-d lemmer ad d-tebteɣ fell-as d tudayt n Rebbi i tella, ad teffeɣ seg rreḥma n Rebbi, ad as-rennuɣ rrkulat deffir. Uqbel ad neṭqeɣ ɣer-s, ibedd ɣer-s yiwen n urgaz d ameqqran d imicbiḥ, d aneccaybu, sliɣ yenna-yas: ‚A TasaÆdit!‛. Tenna-as: ‚AnÆam‛. Yenna-as: ‚Ad kem-iÆem Rebbi s rreḥma-s, tḥemmleḍ leḥnana tkerheḍ lqeḥḍ?‛ Tenna-as: Ḥemmleɣ leḥnana, kerheɣ leqḥeḍ‛

Yenna-as: ‚Tḥemmleḍ lxir, tkerheḍ ccer? I as-yenna. Tenna-as: ‚Ḥemmleɣ lxir kerheɣ ccer.‛.

Yenna-as: ‚Tḥemmleḍ lḥeqq, tkerheḍ lbaṭel?. I as-yenna. Tenna-as: ‚Ḥemmleɣ lḥeqq kerheɣ lbaṭel‛.

Yenna-as: ‚Tḥemmleḍ tidet, tkerheḍ lekdeb?‛ Tenna-as: ‚Ḥemmleɣ tidet, kerheɣ lekdeb‛

Yenna-as: ‚Ihi a TasaÆdit kemm d tudayt n lÆibad mačči d tudayt n Rebbi. Dagi ara teqqimeḍ di rreḥma n Rebbi.‛

Argaz-nni yettwaddem. Nekk neṭqeɣ ɣer TasaÆdit, nniɣ-as: ‚S wayes i d-tufiḍ iman-im kemm d tudayt n Rebbi a TasaÆdit?‛. Tettru tenna-yi-d: ‚nekk a Meẓyan d tudayt n Rebbi. Ur ttẓalleɣ ur ttuẓameɣ, ad ffɣeɣ si rreḥma n Rebbi. » Zmumgeɣ ɣer-s s teḍsa, Æawdeɣ akk i yisteqsiyen i as-yefka urgaz-nni. Tjawb-d fell-asen am wakken i as-
tjaweb. ḍsiɣ ɣer-s, nniɣ-as: ‚ihi kemm a TasaÆdit d tudayt n lÆibad mačči d tudayt n Rebbi. Dagi ara teqqimeḍ di rreḥma n Rebbi. Rnu kemm d tameṭṭut n umjahed. Wwiɣ-am-d leqser n tmeṭṭut n umjahed ad t-tzedɣeḍ dagi di laxert asmi ara d-temmteḍ. Tura ad akem-awiɣ ad t-twaliḍ.‛

Imir iban-d ɣef wudem-is lferḥ. Lferḥ-nni yesbur-d ccbaḥa d sser. Tenṭeq-d ɣer-i tenna-yi-d: ‚lḥemdulileh. Yya-n ihi a Meẓyan ad waliɣ leqser-agi i yi-d-tewwiḍ ad t-zedɣeɣ dagi di laxert.‛. Ṭṭfeɣ-tt seg ufus, neffeɣ-d seg uxxam-nni.

Mi nelḥeq zdat tewwurt, nufa tilawin qqiment d snat n trebbaÆ deg yiwet n temraḥt zdat uxxam-nni. Iɣimi-nni banent-iyi-d am wakken d rreḥba n tmeɣra! ‚a Meẓyan, tilawin-nni d tid i d-yeffɣen seg rreḥma n Rebbi. Ma ɣaḍent-k, ruḥ mmeslay-asent ma seɣdent-ak-d ad uɣalent ad kecment ɣer rreḥma n Rebbi.‛ I d-fehmeɣ.

Di tilawin-nni llant tid i ssneɣ. Banent-iyi-d qqiment zdat n terbaÆt am ccix zdat lexwan. Di terbaÆt i d-yellan zdat uyeffus-iw Æeqleɣ snat d tilawin n yiɣriben. Ma ɣef uẓelmaḍ tella yiwet d tameṭṭut n ccahid teqqim zdat terbaÆt. Tella tayeḍ d tilemẓit isem-is Ḥuriya teqqim zdat n terbaÆt-nni taẓelmaṭ. Waleɣ TasaÆdit truḥ ɣer-sent, teqqim deffir n Ḥuriya. Lḥiɣ ɣer tilawin-nni nutenti sekkrent ameslay d unecreḥ.

Beddeɣ zdat-sent, nniɣ-asent : « ssusmem, ssusment ; seɣdemt-iyi-d ad kent-id-mmeslayeɣ ad tuɣalemt ɣer rreḥma n Rebbi. ».

Rnant taḍsa ɣef umeslay-nni. awdeɣ nniɣ-asent : « ssusmemt ;
Ssusment. », rniɣ  nniɣ-asent : « ad kent-yehdu Rebbi seɣdemt-iyi-d ad tuɣalemt ɣer rreḥma n Rebbi. » Rnant ccna la cennunt. « D zzin-ik i d lÆali, tÆeǧbeḍ-iyi, deg wul-iw yekker uḥaruq ay at Rebbi.‛ ḍḥiɣ-d ḥareɣ deg-sent, rnu lemmer i yi-unfent ad asent-mmeslayeɣ ur ḥṣiɣ d acu ara asent-iniɣ! Nniɣ deg wul-iw: ‚tigi mačči d tilawin n tidet. Ilaq ad tent-ssugdeɣ s lekdeb akken ad d-uɣalent ɣer ṣṣwab.‛ Nniɣ-asent: ‚Ad akent-yehdu Rebbi ssusmemt ad akent-id mmeslayeɣ ad tuɣalemt ɣer rreḥma n Rebbi neɣ ad akent-id-suḍeɣ s nnefs-iw ad tḥerqemt.‛. Rnant tiɣratin ɣef ccna! Nekk ḍḥiɣ la ttneẓmeɣ  « amek ara  xedmeɣ  tura ? tura ad nneḥcameɣ zdat lÆebd, zdat Rebbi. »

A Meẓyan, ḥerrek iles-ik ad tafeḍ tlata n yiÆeqqayen deg yimi-k; suḍ-itent yes-set akken ma llant ad ḥerqent.‛ I d-fehmeɣ. Ḥerrkeɣ iles-iw, ufiɣ-d deg yimi-w tlata n yiÆeqqayen anect n yiÆeqqayen n seksu. Qubleɣ ɣer terbaÆt-nni n tama tayeffust, suḍeɣ. Ffɣen yiÆeqqayen-nni seg yimi-w. Mi leḥqen gar tilawin-nni, ṭṭreḍqen am wakken d iÆeqqayen-nni n lmelḥ yeɣlin ɣer tmes, caÆlen d ifeṭṭiwjen. Waleɣ tarbaÆt-nni merra uɣalen am uqeccuc-nni yerɣan. Nniɣ-asent : « ccah, akka i awent-ilaq a ccmayet. ». Zziɣ ɣer terbaÆt-nni tazelmaṭ iɣer tella Ḥureyya, ufiɣ-d deg yimi-w tlata n yiÆeqqayen-nniḍen, suḍeɣ yes-sen. Teḍra yid-sent am tmezwura-nni. Mi tent-waleɣ ḥerqent, nniɣ-asent : « ccah akka i awent-ilaq a ccmayet ! ». ‚a Meẓyan, tettuḍ Tasaɛdit, tesseddaḍ-tt teḥreq. Yak TasaÆdit teqqim-d deffir Ḥureyya. »
fehmeɣ. « Ay a tin xedmeɣ ! sḥerqeɣ TasaÆdit seddeɣ-tt akked ccmayet-nni ! »

Ssiwleɣ a TasaÆdit. Tenna-yi-d : « anÆam a Meẓyan. ».

Nniɣ-as: ‚Anida i telliḍ akka?‛. Tenna-yi-d: ‚Aql-i dagi‛.

Nniɣ-as: ‚armi d tura i kem-in-ẓriɣ. Nekk ɣileɣ tḥerqeḍ.‛.

Tenna-yi-d s useḍsu.: ‚Ala a Meẓyan, nekk ur ḥriqeɣ ara.‛. Mi yi-d-tenna aql-i dagi imiren i yi-d-tban. Telḥa-d ɣer-i, ṭṭfeɣ-as afus, nniɣ-as: ‚yya-n ihi ad akem-awiɣ tura ad teẓreḍ leqser i am-d-wwiɣ ad t-tzedɣeɣ dagi di laxert!‛.

Tenna-yi-d: ‚Yya-n a Meẓyan, sixef, awi- iyi ad d-ẓreɣ leqser n tmeṭṭut n umjahed i yi-d-tewwiḍ ad t-zedɣeɣ dagi di laxert.‛. Nerra deg yidis deg ubraḥ-nni. Lḥiɣ tlata n yisurrifen. Dliɣ ɣef TasaÆdit, ulac-itt. Nniɣ deg wul-iw : « aw! tura kan i tella yid-i, aniɣer akka i truḥ! Anida ara tt-id-afeɣ? Ad iyi-taÆreq dagi di laxert amek ara xedmeɣ!

Ssiwleɣ-as tlata n tikkal: a TasaÆdit
nniɣ deg wul-iw: ‚ad kecmeɣ ɣer lbiru-inna amer ad afeɣ rruḥ lmumen ad iyi-yeslek si taluft-agi.‛. ‚a Meẓyan TasaÆdit ahat teffeɣ ɣer ttemriḥ. Kečč tura kan ad takiḍ si targit.‛ I d-fehmeɣ. Dayen weḥleɣ, tura ad kecmeɣ ɣer lbiru-agi, ad asen-ḥkuɣ taluft-iw. Xas yella win yebɣan ad iyi-sellek ur yezmir ara. Lemḥayen-iw d imeḥḥinen. I d-nniɣ. Beddeɣ zdat lbiru-nni la ttxemmimeɣ... ‚ a Meẓyan, lbiru-nni d’ladiriksyun’ n laxert. Dinna sÆan tilifun. Ad as-ssiwlen i TasaÆdit. Ay anida tebɣu tili dagi di laxert ad tt-id-afen. Neɣ ma teṭṭes daxel n leqser, ad aznen win ara ikecmen ɣer-s ad tt-id-yessaki. Rnu amḍebber n lbiru-nni ‘chef de serḍice’ d aḥbib-ik.‛ I d-fehmeɣ.

Mi d-fehmeɣ akka, yesterḥem wul-iw. Mi t-setqebleɣ ɣer tewwurt, iqubel-iyi-d yiwen n urgaz d aneccaybu. Iban-iyi-d s ccbiha n yiwen i ssneɣ isem-is AÆrab u Muḥ u SsaÆud. Akken i yi-d-yeẓra, yefreḥ yes-i, yenna-yi-d: ‚LÆeslama ay aḥbib. Mreḥba yes-k, d acu i ak-id-yecqan akka?‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Ad ak-iÆuzz Rebbi; amek i telliḍ; Labas kra!‛. Nemsalam, yenna-yi-d: ‚aql-i di rreḥma n Rebbi. I kečč amek i telliḍ di ddunit ay aḥbib?‛. Nniɣ-as:‚La sserwateɣ times; rrwiɣ ddemmar, rwiɣ lemḥayen, maḥyaf, taḥeqranit< ». Yezmumeg-d ɣer-i, yenna-yi-d : « Ihi ay aḥbib, d acu i k-id-yewwin akka ɣer-neɣ. Mreḥba yes-k‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Ad ak-iÆuzz Rebbi. Yewwi-yi-d Rebbi di targit ad myeẓreɣ yid-wen, ad uɣaleɣ ɣer ddunit.‛.

Fehmeɣ-d: ‚a Meẓyan, amḍebber n lbiru-nni d aḥbib-ik acqiq. Netta yessen-ik, kečč ur t-tessineḍ ara.‛. yenna-yi-d: ‚Kcem a Meẓyan, ayen tebɣiḍ meqbul dagi ɣer-neɣ. Xas
ur ttxemmim ara, d lmuḥal ad tesÆuḍ aɣilif. Nniɣ-as: ‚Ad ak-yekkes Rebbi aɣilif‛. Ḥkiɣ-as taluf-iw. Yeḍsa-d ɣer-i, yenna-yi-d: ‚TasaÆdit tuɣal ɣer ddunit. Newwi-tt-id kan teẓra, nerra-tt‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Yah! Dayen ihi. Maca d kunwi i as-d-isnaÆten times?‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚Ala. Dagi d lmuḥal ad twali times‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Ad ak-iÆuzz Rebbi! Ihi ad d-kecmeɣ ad nqesser, taswiÆt ad uɣaleɣ ɣer ddunit.‛. Netta yezwir nekk ḍefreɣ-t. Yelḥa. Mi yelḥeq ɣer tlemmast n wagens, ibedd. Kecmeɣ, ufiɣ sin n yirgazen d imccuyba qqimen ɣef yikersiyen d iwezzlanen, gar-asen tella lmida d timrebbaÆt, yers suffella-s ttilifun. Irgazen-nni bran s yiqerray-nsen. La lheddra wala d aḥerrek ula s wallen-nsen!

Kemmleɣ tikli-w armi d yiwen n udekkan yellan tama n tewwurt-nni tis snat, tekkaɣ s ufus-iw ɣef udekkan-nni, rriɣ afus ɣef lḥenk. Argaz-nni i fehmeɣ d aḥbib-iw iruḥ ɣer tewwurt-nni imdel-itt. Mi tettwamdel tewwurt-nni, lbiru-nni yuɣal akk d lmeryat. Ur iban ansi tuɣal tewwurt-is! Mi d-yezzi ɣer-i, yezmumeg-d s teḍsa, yenna-yi-d: ‚Akka a Meẓyan i ten-id-nettḥerrir.‛. Fehmeɣ-d: ‚a Meẓyan yexdeÆ-ik uḥbib-ik, iḥerr-ik di laxert. Yerna ma ur yuɣal ara rruḥ-ik ɣer ddunit ad tili ṣṣura-k temmut deg wussu. ».

Ulin-iyi-d yiḥulfan i wumi qqaren s taÆrabt ‚lxucuÆ‛. Nniɣ-d deg wul-iw: ‚meḥsub yexdeÆ-iyi. Meḥsub ikellex-iyi.‛

Suɣeɣ tlata tikkal, nniɣ-d: ‚a Rebbi swayes umneɣ...?‛ Tawwurt-nni telddi-d iman-is, nekk nleqmeɣ s waffug,
ffɣeɣ-d di tewwurt-nni. Mi d-ffɣeɣ di tewwurt-nni, ufiɣ-d nleqmeɣ-d s waffug di tmeqbert-nni n taddart anida i ttwaneṭlen yimawlan-iw. Lawan iban-iyi-d d iḍ yezriren. Qqneɣ allen-iw akken ur ttwaliɣ ara ansi yella ubrid ɣer laxert, nniɣ-d deg wul-iw: ‚wigi d lesrar n Rebbi, ilaq ad ssetḥiɣ seg-s.‛

Ufiɣ-d iman-iw deg uxxam-nneɣ aqdim. TasaÆdit teqqim s lqerb n tkuzint n useḥmu. Takuzint-nni terra-tt tmes am tezrudiyat. Nekk la smuquleɣ TasaÆdit la ttezmumugeɣ ɣer-s  acku  mmektiɣ-d   mi  xeṣrent akken       lewṣayef-is<nettat mi tcikk deg yiman-is, tenna-yi-d : « Ɣef wacu akka i la tettaḍsaḍ fell-i a Meẓyan ? ». # LÆuqqal n tteklix

Lliɣ deg uxxam n rradyu qeddmeɣ-d tadwilt. Tella yid-i yiwet n tlemẓit d tamÆiwent isem-is TasaÆdit. Teṭṭef tabrat gar yifassen-is, sliɣ tenna-d: ‚tabrat-agi a Meẓyan, tura-tt-id yiwet n weltma-tneɣ tenna-ak tamɣart-iw lebda tettcewwil-iyi ur iyi-tettanef ara ad iliɣ di talwit nekk d urgaz-iw. Ilaq tura ad iyi-d-tiniḍ amek ara xedmeɣ. Uqbel ad tt-jawbeɣ, ufiɣ-d lliɣ akked d tlemẓit-nni deg yiwen n ubrid tama n umadaɣ yettusemman ‘Adebbaɣ’. Amkan deg i neqqim yettwasemma ‘TaÆerṣ yewwet Iderɣalen’. Amzun din i yella uxxam-nni n rradyu. Jawbeɣ llal n

- 275 -
tebrat-nni nniɣ-as: ‚a weltma-tneɣ, tadwilt-agi mačči d nnuba n lÆuqqal. Maca ad akem-in-jawbeɣ ad am-d-iniɣ ma yella-am deg wul urgaz-im, tḥemmleḍ-t; ilaq a weltma ad tsebreḍ i wayen akk ara m-texdem yemma-s alamma d asmi ara temmet. Imir ad tuɣaleḍ ad tÆaceḍ d urgaz-im di lehna. Ma yella ur am-yelli ara urgaz-im deg wul, tixer fell-as ad thenniḍ.

Ufiɣ-d iman-iw beddeɣ deg yiwen n ubrid zdat n tmeqbert yettusemman ‘Taḥeccaṭ n lbir’. Lḥiɣ akken ad ruḥeɣ s axxam-iw. Ttwaliɣ di tikli-nni mi greɣ asurif ad t-sɣezfeɣ, ad d-icceḍ uḍar-iw, ad d-yeḥkem usurif-nni s lqis n tɣerdast. Mi greɣ asurif s lqis, ad yiɣzif s uḥelli n tlata n yisurrifen! Ddiɣ-tt akken armi kecmeɣ s abrid-nni anaṣli.

Leḥqeɣ s anida ilaq ad dewreɣ iman-iw ɣer tama tayeffust. Mi zziɣ iman-iw, ufiɣ-d aqjun-iw deg ubrid yettucidd s snesla. Akken ḍilleɣ deg-s, yuzzel-d ɣer-i s lferḥ, yekcem -d gar yiḍarren-iw, iqreḍ-iyi, ṭṭinzeɣ. Netta yellha-d la yi-mecceḥ seg yimi-w. Nekk ɣunfeɣ-t, la t-ḥebbseɣ s yifassen-iw akken ad iyi-yanef ad nleqmeɣ. Maca si leḥmali-nni yugi ad iyi-bru. La t-ḥebbseɣ ttweḳireɣ fell-as armi d anida i tenneqḍaÆ snesla-nni.

Nleqmeɣ, ǧǧiɣ-t. Kemmleɣ abrid-iw s axxam. Lḥiɣ armi qrib ad awḍeɣ ɣer tmeqbert-nniḍen tettwasemma ‘Tineṭlin n Sliman’. Leḥqeɣ ɣer yiwet n terga i d-igezmen abrid-nni. Ddaw n ubrid-nni, targa-nni lqayet, d amarur igan am tenṭelt. Mi zegreɣ i terga-nni, waleɣ tilemẓit d yilemẓi myuṭṭafen afus, mlilen tayet ɣer tayet bedden gar yigufa n terga-nni. Ruḥeɣ ɣer-sen ad ten-steqsiɣ d acu i ten-
yessiwḍen s amkan-nni! Beddeɣ zdat-sen, tezga-d tmuɣli- w di tḥeccaṭ iɣef tettwasemma tmeqbert-nni. Tella gar tneṭlin. Tban-iyi-d tcebbubt-is tettwazlef tiniḍ telḥeq-itt tmes. àčḥeɣ tamuɣli-w ɣer tḥeccaṭ-nni, fehmeɣ amzun yella wasmi bɣan ad myezwaǧen, myfkan lÆahed maca asmi i d-sḥeḍren zzwaǧ ugin-asen yimawlan-nsen dɣa rran afus deg ufus ad ḍeggren iman-nsen ɣer tmes ad mmten lwaḥid wala ma ddren mfaraqen. Haten-an tura di lÆahed-nsen!

Sliɣ i yilemẓi-nni yenna-yi-d: ‚yerna asmi nemlil, nekk la ttwexxireɣ fell-as nettat tegguma ad iyi-tettixer.‛ Waleɣ-t yefka-iyi-d amedya; la yettwexxir fell-as, taqcict-nni tenṭeḍ deg-s. Times tekker deg wafrasen deffir-sen daxel n userfuf-nni n terga. Nutni la leḥḥun timendeffirt rran afus deg ufus armi qrib maḍi ad awḍen ɣer tmes-nni. Taqcict-nni tezzi iman-is tqubel ɣer tmes-nni, tneggez ɣer ujajiḥ.

Ilemẓi-nni yezzi iman-is mi iwala taxḍibt-is tečča-tt tmes, iwexxer yuɣal armi d amkan-nni ansi bdan aqerreb ɣer tmes. La yettuɣal timendeffirt, merra merra la yettmmuqul ɣer tmes-nni ad iÆenqer akken ad yesseɣli iman-is s ajajiḥ, ad yuɣal ad iseggem iman-is, ad iyi-d- yini: ‚Ata a Meẓyan, ulamek ḍergeɣ iman-iw ɣer tmes.‛.

Yerwel ɣef tmes-nni. Nekk yeḥreq wul-iw fell-as, nniɣ-as: ‚yella wamek ara tḍegreḍ iman-ik ɣer tmes, yeshel maḍi, yehwa-ak kan txedÆeḍ tufiḍ-d ssebba.‛

Ukiɣ-d si targit !
