# Weḥd-i di ttewḥid

Lliɣ akked terbaÆt n yilmeẓyen nerkeb di tkerrust tameqqrant. Takerrust-nni tesÆa sin n yimeqyasen n tenhart: yiwen deg umkan-is, wayeḍ tesÆa-t di tlemmast. Anehhar yella ɣer umeqyas yellan s aqerru n tkerrust; nekk qqimeɣ deffir n umeqyas-nni n tlemmast. Waleɣ anehhar-nni yuɣal-d s ameqyas-nni n tlemmast. Mi mmuqleɣ amek i la yettnahar, iban-iyi-d d amussnaw aqbur di tenhart. Maca la ttsuɣuɣ fell-as, la s-qqareɣ: ‚ eddi s ameqyas n zdat uqbel ad tessegrirbeḍ takerrust yes-neɣ.‛ netta yegguma ad iyi-d-yesɣed. ḍḥiɣ-d ḥareɣ ma ad llhiɣ di tmuɣli ɣer zdat deg ubrid-nni neɣ ad llhiɣ d unehhar-nni. Rẓiɣ fell-as aqerruy-iw ‘lqayed d aÆeẓẓug’. Ufiɣ-d yiwen yeqqim ɣer yidis-w isem-is Lmulud, nniɣ-as: ‚i tura a Lmulud, lufan ad d-nemlil d yimsulta, anehhar-agi ad as-rren lexṭiya tameqqrant.‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚Yak ad asen-isenyali ur t-id-ttwalin ara.‛. Mmuqleɣ abrid ɣer zdat, waleɣ qrib ad naweḍ ɣer tunnḍa n ubrid. Mi nelḥeq ɣer tunnḍa-nni, waleɣ rruda tamezwarut teffeɣ i ubrid. Rnu ddaw ubrid-nni d ifri lqayen. Ukessɣar-nni d asif iḥemlen. Suɣeɣ ɣef unehhar-nni, nniɣ-as: ‚err-d takerrust s abrid!‛. Yeḥbes takerrust la tt-id-idewwir s laÆqel armi i tt-id-yerra s abrid. Ikemmel tanhart ɣer zdat. Daɣen tenfel rruda i ubrid. Suɣeɣ ɣef unehhar-nni. Yerra-tt-id s abrid.

- 278 -
Ikemmel tanhart-is. Nekk la s-qqareɣ: ‚ad ak-yehdu Rebbi, Æeddi s ameqyas n zdat<‛ dayen yenteḍ deg umeqyas-nni n tlemmast. Nleqmeɣ, ruḥeɣ s aqerru n tkerrust-nni, qesdeɣ ad tt-ḥebseɣ deg ubrid xir ma nuɣal di twaɣit ur nesÆi lmeÆna. Mi leḥqeɣ s anida i ttilin lefran, waleɣ ulac lefran! Uɣaleɣ ṭṭfeɣ ameqyas s yiwen n ufus la ttnahareɣ; wayeḍ ufus ṭṭfeɣ yes-s la ḍitesse. Akken i sserseɣ afus-iw, ḥulfeɣ, tÆedda la ḍitesse. Takerrust teɣṣeb. Zziɣ s anehhar-nni, nniɣ-as : « rwaḥ ad tnehreḍ ! ». Yenna-yi-d: ‚Truḥeḍ ad tnehreḍ kečč terniḍ-as leɣseb.‛.

Wwaleɣ yiwet n tṣeffiḥt zdat uḍar-iw, fehmeɣ-tt d lefran. Sserseɣ fell-as aḍar-iw, takerrust terna teɣṣeb. Anehhar-nni la yettcekkiḍ irennu. Nekk la sÆeddayeɣ ‘les ḍitesses’ la ttnahareɣ s yiwen n ufus armi waleɣ lemri-nni n tkerrust tiniḍ yettwasbeɣ s lmidad, ur waleɣ ara seg-s abrid ɣer zdat.

Yuɣal unehhar-nni yellan ɣer deffir xas akken mazal la s-irennu acekkeḍ i tkerrust, maca la yi-yemmal abrid. Maca iseggeb-iyi-d tummla. Simmal nteddu ɣer zdat simmal yettseggib di tumla : ‚Err akkin, err akk-a‛. Abrid la d-yettiḍyiq mačči am umeccaq am wayeḍ. Anehhar-nni aqbur mi d-yenṭeq, ddiɣ d wawal-is. Ḥṣiɣ ay akken yebɣu yili ubrid, ay akken tebɣu tili teɣseb, takerrust ur iyi-tetteffeɣ ara i ubrid mi ttuÆawneɣ sɣur anehhar-nni. Maca uggadeɣ lemmer ad d-mlileɣ d ukamyun ameqqran, ahat xas nekni ad nḥader fell-as, anehhar-is ad iÆemmed fell-neɣ. Kemmleɣ abrid s tuggdi. Nelḥeq s anida yestiwen ubrid, ḥulfeɣ i tkerrust-nni tbedd am wakken ara ibedd.
umdan. Sliɣ i unehhar-nni yenna-yi-d: ‚dewwer-itt ɣef uyeffus.‛

Dewreɣ takerrust-nni ɣer tama tayeffust. NÆedda i tsawent-nni. Takerrust teḥbes. Zziɣ s anehhar-nni. Iban-iyi-d newweḍ s aniɣer i neqsed. Anehhar-nni yetti-d d yiwen i ssneɣ isem-is isa nnekwa-s Adem. Neṭqeɣ ɣer-s, nniɣ-as: ‚teẓriḍ ṭṭiq-nni seg i d-nÆedda! Yerna nekk uggadeɣ acku s yiwen n ufus i la ttnahareɣ. Rnu d lmuḥal yemla-iyi-yiwen asmi bdiɣ tanhart. Yak aql-ak la tettwaliḍ ssneɣ ad nehreɣ.‛

Yenna-yi-d isa: ‚Ula d nekk akka asmi bdiɣ, ulac win i yi-yemlan. Weḥd-i kan i bdiɣ tanhart. Nniɣ-as: ‚ula d nekk weḥd-i i bdiɣ tanhart, yerna aql-ak la tettwaliḍ s yiwen n ufus i la ttnaareɣ.‛

# Ukiɣ-d si targit !

1981

* * *

# Seddeɣ lawliyya

Di lawan ttnaṣfa n yiḍ, ffɣeɣ-d seg uxxam. Sliɣ kkren yessuɣan di laÆzib-nneɣ deg ubraḥ yettusemman ‘Amraḥ Imexlaf’. Uzzleɣ mi leḥqeɣ, ufiɣ-d arrac iberraniyen la ttlaÆaben deg ubraḥ-nni timzizzal, sekkren isuɣan. Uɣaleɣ sliɣ yekker umeslay deg yixxamen-nni n at
udrum-iw. Ameslay-nni d uffir neɣ d ameslay n twacult di lawan n yiḍ<nniɣ-d: ‚d arrac-agi ur neǧǧi ara imawlan-iw ad ṭṭsen hani.‛. Llheɣ-d deg-sen la ten-ttḥiziɣ, qqareɣ-asen: ‚ad truḥem neɣ ad terwi fell-awen<‛. Sliɣ i uẓawan la d-tettas tɣri-s seg yiwen n uxxam n Æemmi amenzu di tegmat n jeddi. Unfeɣ-asen i warrac-nni. Ruḥeɣ ɣer tama ufella n ubraḥ-nni. Mi leḥqeɣ ɣer uxxam n Æemmi, kecmeɣ di tewwurt, ufiɣ tarbaÆt n yilmeẓyen qqimen deg wagens n tzeqqa-nni rradyu n tesfaft gar-asen. Yeṭṭef-itt gar yifassen-is yiwen isem-is AÆrab u Lḥusin, wayeḍ AÆrab u Qasi la s-yettakk tisfifin n ccna, wis tlata AÆrab u Muḥ u Ḥmed la yettferriǧ. Nekk leḥqeɣ akken kan tfak tesfift n Lewnis At Mengellat. Yekkes-itt-id WaÆrab u Lḥusin si rradyu. AÆrab u Qasi ihegga-as-d tayeḍ. Akken i as-iwehha tasfift-nni, neṭqeɣ, nniɣ-asen : ‚ d lawan, hatan d ttnaṣfa n yiḍ, ad truḥem.‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚Rǧu ad d-nernu tisfifin-agi tijdidin.‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Ala ay atmaten. Ad truḥem tura kan . Mačči ur bɣiɣ ara ad tsehrem dagi neɣ usmeɣ seg-wen. Nekk twenseɣ yes-wen. Maca arrac-agi i d-tewwim yid-wen, haten ad sekkren isuɣan, la ccictilen. Ula d imawlan-iw bbehban seg yisuɣan-agi ur ten-ǧǧan ara ad ṭṭsen. Yerna mebla ccek ad ilin tweḥcen acku ur Ælimen ara yes-i s aniɣer i rriɣ mi d-ffɣeɣ. Lemmer ḥṣan dagi i lliɣ gar-awen ur ttuggaden ara. Tura ay atmaten ad truḥem. Tikkelt-nniḍen ma tebɣam ad d-tasem ɣer da, ur d-tettawim ara yid-wen arrac-agi. Aset-d kan kunwi weḥd-nwen.‛
Waleɣ sin si terbaÆt-nni ffɣen di tewwurt: yiwen d Akli n Ḥmed, wayeḍ d Akli n ɛmer. Ma d imezwura-nni, ur iyi-d-sɣiden ara. Ibedd-d zdat-i yiwen i rriɣ d aḥbib-iw, isem-is Lḥusin n Warab, yelsa talaba tcuba ɣer tlaba n yimenɣi.

Waleɣ udem-is ibeddel-it reffu. Yenna-yi-d: ‚kečč a Meẓyan anida i ak-yehwa ad tsehreḍ nekni la ɣ-tettḥiziḍ.‛ Nniɣ-as: ‚Ay aḥbib a gma, welleh ma d beqqu ur bɣiɣ ara neɣ d tismin i yusmeɣ seg-wen, welleh ar ferḥeɣ yes-wen mi tellam dagi, twenseɣ. Maca d imcewwlen-agi i d tewwim yid-wen ur bɣiɣ ara. Hatan d ttnaṣfa n yiḍ, imawlan-iw ur ṭṭisen ara. Uggaden d acu i d-ikecmen taddart-agi-nneɣ. Lufan meqqar ḥṣan lliɣ dagi yid-wen, tilli ur ttawḥacen ara, ad twensen yes-i. Tura ad truḥem ad tawim arrac-agi i d-tewwim yid-wen. Tikkelt-nniḍen ma tebɣam ad d-tasem ur d-ttawit ara imcicetlen-agi.‛

Mmuqleɣ s agens, waleɣ ussu, rniɣ waleɣ rran tasfift n ccna! Nniɣ deg wul-iw: ‚imexlaq-agi dagi ara nsen! Haten-i ssan-d di terkkent. Wigi ad asen-anfeɣ, ad ffɣeɣ s arrac-inna ad ten-ḍeggceɣ ssyagi.‛

Ffɣeɣ-d s abraḥ-nni, ufiɣ-d tagnit d laxaṭer! Nniɣ-d ruḥen yimcicetlen-nni. Lawan yetti-d d azal, nekk qesdeɣ tuɣalin ɣer uxxam. Udreɣ; mi neṣṣfeɣ abraḥ-nni s tikli, ufiɣ-d lsiɣ abernus d acebḥan ttwaÆellqeɣ seg uḍad-iw ccahed ɣer yiwen n lxiḍ n yileẓwi yellan nnig-iw. La jebbdeɣ akken ad snesreɣ, aḍad-iw yenteḍ am ufrux-nni iweḥlen seg tqejjirt di lxiḍ n trisiti. Teffeɣ-d tmeṭṭut seg uxxam n jeddi, telḥeq-d s abraḥ-nni, teɣli zdat tewwurt n ufrag. Fehmeɣ-tt d imessigman i tt-yesseɣlin tenneṣraÆ. Yuzzel-d yiwen d
mmi-s n Æemmi isem-is Meẓyan, yerfed tameṭṭut-nni. Sliɣ yenna-d: ‚a ya wwten-tt lawliyya.‛

Ḥulfeɣ yeɣli-d fell-i lweḥc mi fehmeɣ taluft-nni. Nniɣ-d: ‚a ya wigi i la ttḥawazeɣ d lawliyya. Haten-in wwten-iyi-d. La jebbdeɣ iman-iw armi i d-ssnesreɣ seg lxiḍ-nni.

Uzzleɣ s axxam-nni n jeddi. Ruḥeɣ s umlelli. Ufiɣ tameṭṭut-nni teẓẓel di tlemmast n wagens la tesselqaf, nekk ɣliɣ di terkent yeffeɣ-iyi laÆqel armi i Æuggneɣ seg tuggdi.

La ttneẓẓifeɣ qqareɣ: « a ya ḥawzeɣ lawliyya< ! ». Mmuqleɣ ɣer berra amzun allen-iw neqrent leḥyuḍ, waleɣ arrac-nni ččuren abrid la ttruḥun d tirebbaÆ.

TarbaÆt tamezwarut waleɣ-ten ḍillen i udrar anida i tella taddart yettusemman Iḥeddaden. TarbaÆt taneggarut bdan tikli seg ubraḥ-nni yettusemman Abraḥ imexlaf.

Lḥan kra n yisurrifen, leḥqen ɣer yiwet n talast yebḍan gar wakal-nneɣ s imexlaf d wakal n yiwen yettusemman LaÆmara n WaÆrab.

Nxeryaḍen-d tlata n warrac seg tarbaÆt-nni, mmuqlen-d ɣer-i, nniɣ-asen: « sbaḥlxir fell-awen.‛. Nnan-yi-id: ‚Sbaḥ lxir u lehna a Meẓyan‛

Uɣaleɣ nekk la asen-qqareɣ semmḥet-iyi ḥawzeɣ-ken nutni la yi-d-qqaren nsemmeḥ-ak a Meẓyan, armi tlata tikkal.

Uzzleɣ ɣer-sen nutni kemmlen abrid-nsen. Leḥqeɣ ɣer talast-nni, beddeɣ la ssutureɣ ssmaḥ, nutni la yi d-ttsemmiḥen.

Ttwaliɣ deg-sen mačči d kra yettwaqḍaɛen s leḥsab! tikkelt taneggarut mi msamaḥeɣ yid-sen, tarbaɛt-nni iruḥen d ineggura ḍillen i udrar faten di tmuɣli-iw, tḍill-d teɣri-nsen si lbeɛd tentell, sliɣ nnan-d: ‚nsemmeḥ-
ak a Meẓyan armi tlata tikal. Ufiɣ-d iman-iw deg yiwen n udrar yettusemman « iɣil n lḥedd n ccix » lliɣ la ttmeslayeɣ akked yiwen n yilemẓi isem-is : Aɛrab u Muḥ n Ḥmed. Yenna-yi-d : ‚Ttugadeɣ a Meẓyan ma ad rguɣ gliɣ-d si tegnawt ɣer tmurt ! ». Nniɣ-as : ‚Ula d nekk seɛɛuɣ tirga i yi-isuggaden, maca ur ttarguɣ ara gliɣ-d si tegnawt. Tuggadeɣ ma ad rguɣ neggzeɣ ɣer yifri lqayen aṭas. Ula d taguni ḥerrmeɣ-tt i yiman-iw, mi yi-d-yusa yiḍes ssakayeɣ-d iman-iw ; acku ttuggadeɣ ma ṭṭseɣ ad arguɣ neggzeɣ ɣer yifri. Yenna-yi-d: ‚ I kečč a Meẓyan di leɛmer turgaḍ teṭṭef-ik lḥaǧa ?‛. Nniɣ-as : « Ur ttarguɣ ara!‛. Yenna-yi-d : « Nekk urgeɣ ṭṭfent-iyi yessi-s n uwdiɛ si terwiḥt-iw berant-iyi-t, mi d-ukiɣ d awal kan i wumi sliɣ ». Nniɣ-as : « Maca isem n uwdiɛ di targit yesɛa lmeɛna, awdiɛ d lweɛd ma d yessi-s d tilufa ».

Ufiɣ-d beddeɣ zdat tewwurt n texxamt deg ufrag n uxxam-iw, tawwurt-nni mi d-tettwamdel tḥerr kra n yičwečwen si tafriwin-nsen weḥlen ddaw lluḥ. Smerzizɣeɣ lluḥ-nni s tmara akked leḥder armi snesren iman-nsen yičewčwen-nni. Llheɣ la ddhameɣ di tewwurt-nni akken ad telddi. Ttwaliɣ lluḥ-nni di tama ufella la yetnefḍas ad yerreẓ wala ad imwexxar a d-yeldi. Mmuqleɣ dacu i d ssebba-s, ufiɣ ificcet di tlemmast-is. Uɣaleɣ ṭṭfeɣ lluḥ-nni s yiwen n ufus akken ur yetruẓ ara, wayeḍ ufus a ddhameɣ yes-s, rniɣ a ddhameɣ s yiwen uḍrar, wayeḍ uḍrar beddeɣ fell-as. Ufiɣ-d iman-iw la ddehameɣ di tewwurt n tḥanut yellan di taddart yettusemman « Taxribt ». Bab n tḥanut-nni isem-is :
Aɛmer n Ḥmed n Muḥeddakli. Llan yid-i tlata yilmeẓyen d imɛiwan, yiwen d bab n tḥanut-nni. Itekka s yifassen-is ɣef rrzat n lluḥ. Wayeḍ di tama-s isem-is : Muḥ n Waɛrab. Wis tlata isem-is : Renḍan. Nekk la ddehameɣ yid-sen rniɣ a sseḥdareɣ ɣef lluḥ-nni akken ur itruẓ ara; daɣen ad sen-teggeɣ tirrugza i yimɛiwan-nni akken ur fecclen ara. Lluḥ-nni ad ileddi ciṭuḥ ciṭuḥ s tmara. Sliɣ i bab n tḥanut-nni yenna-yi-d : ‚Kečč a Meẓyan s wawal kan i la teddhameḍ, ifassen-ik, d tarusi i rsen kan‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Ifassen-iw ṭṭfeɣ yes-sen lluḥ-agi, wellah la ddehameɣ s yiḍarren-iw ugar-nwen‛

Nerra tazmert i yiman-nneɣ neddhem lluḥ-nni yelddi akken ilaq. Nekni nbedd di tlemmast n wagens nellha d unecreḥ. Uɣaleɣ qqimeɣ ɣef yiwen usenduq. Muḥ n Waɛrab yelḥa-d ɣer-i yefka-yi-d yiwet n tewriqt i d-yetwakksen seg uɣmis, yenna-yi-d : ‚Ax-n kan a Meẓyan ɣɣer-iyi-d tawriqt-agi i yi-d-yefka yiwen yeɛreḍ-iyi ɣer tmeɣra ssebt akked lḥed. Mmuqel kan isem-is wagi!‛.

Ṭṭfeɣ-d tawriqt-nni waleɣ tettwaru s tmaziɣt, maca xerbent tira-nni ur zmireɣ ara a tent-fehmeɣ. Mmuqleɣ ɣer rrif ufella n tewriqt-nni, waleɣ yura deg-s : 4, 5 ssebt akked lḥed, bab-is istenya akka « tmem ». Sliɣ i Muḥ yenna-yi-d : ‚Mmuqel kan ma d tidet akken i k-nniɣ.‛. Nniɣ-as : ‚di tidet iɛreḍ-ik ɣer tmeɣra 4, 5, ssebt uk-d lḥed. Yenna-yi-d Muḥ: ‚ Wali kan isem-is wagi!‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Cikeɣ d astenyi-agi i d isem-is. Ata istenya-d « igmen ». Muḥ yeḍṣa, yenna-yi-d : ‚D wagi i d isem-is!‛. ḍṣiɣ, nniɣ-as : ‚Wagi d isem daɣen!‛. Aɛmer yenna-yi-d : ‚Kečč a
Meẓyan tesɛiḍ taḥraymit. Nniɣ-as : ‚ala a Aɛmer, sɛiɣ taḥraymit deg-wawal kan. Neḍṣa akken ma nella.

Waleɣ Renḍan yuɣ-d tlata tgufriḍin ibḍa-ten, di tlemmast, nefṣ seg-sent yerra-t ɣer yimi-s nnefṣ-nniḍen yefka-yi-it-id rriɣ-t ɣer yimi-w. Mmuqleɣ ɣer bab n tḥanut-nni, di tmuɣli-nni bɣiɣ a s-iniɣ : ‚Akka i d beṭṭu n « Tdukli », yecba ɣer beṭṭu n tgufriḍin agi.

Ukiɣ-d si targit !

1981

Nufa-d tifrat-is Ufiɣ-d lliɣ d waṭas n yirgazen di lejmaɛ, nnejmaɛen akken ad sen-yemmeslay sselṭan, ḥeddren imesǧernanen.

Waleɣ la ttkamirin akken ad d-sɛeddin lejmaɛ-nni di tilifizyu. Nniɣ-d : ad wehhiɣ iman-iw ɣer lkamira, ma d-ɛeddiɣ di tilifizyu ad wehmen lɣaci n taddart-iw, ad inin Meẓyan u Muḥ sɛddan-t-id di tilifizyu. Wehheɣ iman-iw ɣer lkamira, ar dqal waleɣ tilifizyu yers zdat terbaɛt n lɣaci, ttwaliɣ sneɛten-d akk wid iḥeddren di lejmaɛ-nni, ma d nekk amzun ulac-iyi. Nniɣ-d : nekk ur iyi-d-teṭṭif ara lkamira. Ibedd-d lexyal zdat-i, waleɣ lexyal-nni am wakken waleɣ iman-iw di lemri. Lexyal-nni ad d-yekk akk
lɣaci-nni s tmuɣli, ar dqal ad iyi d-yemmuqel ad izmumeg s teḍṣa ! neṭqeɣ nniɣ-d nekk d iman-iw s lekmal i la ttwaliɣ zdat-i.

Uɣaleɣ fehmeɣ lejmaɛ-nni d rreḥba n tmeɣra. Waleɣ yiwet n terbaɛt zdat-i llan deg-s aṭas n yirgazen qqimen akk, ulac win ibedden deg-sen. Di terbaɛt-nni fehmeɣ yella sselṭan gar-asen. Waleɣ inelqem-d yiwen d aberraḥ, yenna-d : ‚Ad ken-yehdu Rebbi a lɣaci ad aɣ-d-tefkem setta. Ttwaliɣ ula d yiwen mačči izzelz iman-is. Yules-d uberraḥ-nni yenna-d : ‚Ay atmaten ad aɣ-d-tefkem setta yimruggzen ad ḍemnen sselṭan-agi a t-ɛassen. Refdeɣ afus-iw nniɣ-as : ‚Aql-i yiwen d nekk d amezwaru.‛

Lḥiɣ ɣer-s, waleɣ yetbeɛ-iyi-d yiwen yilemzi isem-is Lmulud. Mi nelḥeq ɣer terbaɛt-nni fehmeɣ mačči din i yella sselṭan, yella deg uxxam -is, daɣen deg uxxam-is i-yesra wid ad iɛassen fell-as ad t-wansen.

Nruḥ armi nelḥeq zdat tewwurt n uxxam-nni n sselṭan, Fehmeɣ-d axxam-nni d axxam n Lmulud. Nufa yiwen yilemẓi zdat tewwurt, isem-is : Aɛrab d mmi-s n ɛemmi-s n Lmulud. Imir ur ḥṣiɣ ma d sselṭan i-yellan deg uxxam -nni nruḥ ad t-nɛass, neɣ d lmeyyet ad t-neggani.

Aɛrab Yenna-yaɣ-d : ‚Ata sselṭan deg-uxxam-agi, Kecmet-d. Neṭqeɣ s leɛqel nniɣ-asen : ‚Nekk ur qebbleɣ ara ad t-gganiɣ, alamma fkan-aneɣ-d ccrab sɣur-sen. Yenna-d Lmulud: ‚Ahat ad aɣ d-fken‛. Nniɣ-as i waɛrab : ‚Ur qebbleɣ ara a t-ɛasseɣ, alamma tefkam-aneɣ-d ccrab sɣur-wen. Nniɣ-as : ‚d ayen ur qebbleɣ d lmuḥal. Ma yella
ccrab sɣur-wen aql-aneɣ newjed, ma sɣur-neɣ, nekk ur tɛasseɣ ara.

Ufiɣ-d iman-iw deg-wadeg yetwasemman « taɛwint imexlaf », lliɣ deg ubrid arqiqan yellan ddaw ubrid ameqqran. La leḥḥuɣ, tarbaɛt n yirgazen ad d-leḥḥun deffir-iw. Zziɣ ɣer-sen waleɣ yiwen gar-asen n taddart-iw, isem-is : Aɛrab u Musa. Yetti-d, yuffay armi yessewham!

sliɣ i terbaɛt-nni ad as-ssawalen : a ɛemmi Rabeḥ !uẓiɣ ɣer-s nniɣ-as : ‚Saḥḥa a ɛemmi Rabeḥ; nemsalam. Waleɣ wayeḍ isem-is : Sliman u Muḥ. Fehmeɣ-d di terbaɛt-nni usan-d ɣer yiwen uɛeqli ameqqran ad asen-d-yemmeslay.

Yenṭeq-d yiwen deg-sen yebda ameslay s rregmat. Yenṭeq-d ɛemmi Rabeḥ icekker bu rregmat-nni, yenna-d : ‚Ata yiwen di terbaɛt-agi d aɛeqli, ulac win izemren ad yili d ameɣnas am-wagi. Sliman, yenna-yas : ‚Tasertit d leḥdaqa, mačči d rregmat am rregmat uɛeqli-agi i d-tenniḍ.

Ibedd-d ɣer yidis-iw yiwen d ilemẓi isem-is : Rabeḥ u Aɛli. Sliman Yenna-d : ‚Ata Meẓyan akked Rabeḥ u Aɛli ssnen tasertit, rnu ulac win izemren ad yergem rregmat-nsen, maca ur reggmen ara, ɛemmi Rabeḥ yenna-yi-d : ‚A Meẓyan ihi d kečč i xtireɣ ad sen-temmeslayeḍ i lɣaci agi.

Nniɣ-as : ‚ awwah, ur sen-ttmeslayeɣ ara nekk.

Lḥiɣ kra n yisurrifen ɣer zdat yetbeɛ-iyi-d ɛemmi Rabeḥ, beddeɣ mi d-yelḥeq ɣer-i, waleɣ tarbaɛt-nni lḥan armi wwḍen ddaw teɛwint-nni « imexlaf », bedden, neṭqeɣ ɣer ɛemmi Rabeḥ nniɣ-as : ‚Ameslay ur sen-ttmeslayeɣ ara, maca ad k id-fkeɣ kra n yesteqsiyen ma tjawbeḍ-d fell-
asen.!‛. Yuzzel s lferḥ ɣer terbaɛt-nni, sliɣ yenna-yasen :

‚Uɣalet-d atan ad awen-id-yemmeslay Meẓyan u Muḥ‛.

Uɣalen-d, Mi d-wwḍen ɣer-i, Luɛeɣ ɛemmi Rabeḥ nniɣ-as : ‚mačči d ameslay i k-nniɣ ad asen-mmeslayeɣ, nniɣ-ak ad k-id-fkeɣ isteqsiyen acku ass-agi bɣiɣ ad kemmleɣ tussna-w ɣer zdat‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚ini-d d acu d isteqsiyen-agi?‛. Nniɣ-as : « ad iyi-d-tiniḍ ma d cciṭan i d-yexleq Rebbi ɣer ddunit d amezwaru, neɣ ala? ». Yenna-yi-d : « ala, yexleq-d Rebɛa n lmalayek d imezwura. ». Nniɣ-as : ‚isem-nsen lmalayek-agi?‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚Ǧebrail, Ɣezrail, Mikkail, Israffil‛. Nniɣ-as : ‚Amek tlata n lmalayek ɛedlen yismawen-nsen, segrayen-d tlata n yisekkilen kifkif-nsen : ‘ail, ail, ail’, ma d wis rebɛa ixulef-iten : ‘fil’ ! ales-asen-id, ini-ten-id s lɛedlan i rebɛa‛

Yules-d i yismawen-nni, yenna-d : ‚Ǧebrail, Mikkail, Israil ‘ɛezrail’, yeɛreq deg yisem-nni aneggaru ur ifaq ara. Čàčḥeɣ-t s tmuɣli, tɣelleb-iyi-d teḍṣa, waleɣ udem-is yuɣal d awraɣ mi ifaq s lɣelṭa-s, yeḍḥa-d ssekwent-t lewhayem. Nniɣ-as : ‚d acu i k-yeswehmen akka a ɛemmi Rabeḥ ?‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚Swehmen-iyi lɛulama yeskidiben‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Mi teḥsiḍ s wakka llan lɛulama yeskidiben, llan wid yettmeslayen tidet; ihi ula d nekk aql-i qebleɣ ad sen-d-meslayeɣ i lɣaci-agi!‛

Lḥiy armi wwḍeɣ s abrid anaṣli, beddeɣ ddaw taɛwint-nni imexlaf. Tarbaɛt-nni llan zdat-i qublen-d ɣer-i ; neṭqeɣ nniɣ-asen : ‚Ay atmaten, ur awen-id-bedduɣ ara awal s imeslayen-nni imezwura i d-qqaren di lejmaɛat< nekk ad wen-id-bduɣ ameslay s Rebbi akked ccuhada ijuhden
fisabililah. Ay atmaten imeslayen-a ad-naf wilmen ad ten-id-nini xas mačči n tmeslayt-nneɣ, xas mačči d amusnaw-nneɣ i ten-id-yeǧǧan. Ilaq ad ten-id-nini mi wilmen ad aɣ-nefɛen. Ay atmaten win yettun imjuhad ijuhden fisabililah, ula d nekk yettu-iyi. Win inekren leɛtab-nsen, ula d nekk yenker leɛtab-iw. Win ixedɛen lɛahed-nsen, ula d nekk yexdeɛ-iyi. Ay atmaten, imeslayen i bɣiɣ ad awenten-id-iniɣ d imeslayen i d-yenna yiwen uɛeqli d aɛrab, Yenna-d :« Fa la teḥsubna lladina qutilu fisabililahi amwaten, bell aḥyaiun ɛinda Rebbi-him yurzaqun ».

Mmuqleɣ ɣer yigenni, waleɣ qublen-iyi-d yimdanen, ttwaliɣ llan yimɣaren, timɣarin, irgazen, tilawin, tiqcicin d warrac imeẓyanen. Zdat-sen llant snat telmeẓzyin la d-ttqarabent, ad iyi d-ssenɛadent iman-nsent akken ad tent-ẓreɣ dacu i llant. Waleɣ yiwet s tadist, tayeḍ teṭṭef llufan deg yirebbi-s nekk a d-qqareɣ ttɛawadeɣ-d imeslayen-nni n taɛrabt. Imdanen-nni ttbanen-iyi-d s lexyal iwanuɣen, maca ttwaliɣ-ten ddren tḥerriken iman-nsen rremcen s wallen-nsen.

Ma d nekk muḍleɣ deg usmuqel ɣer lexyalat-nni, ur d-llheɣ ara deg wid-nni i la yi-traǧun ad asen-mmeslayeɣ. Llheɣ ɣer lexyalat-nni armi i ttwakksen si gar wallen-iw. Ssidreɣ-d aqerruy-iw, waleɣ serrḥen-d yimeṭṭawen seg wallen-iw uzzlen ɣef wakal, seg yimeslayen-nni i d-qqareɣ s teɣri tukmirt isendafen iẓra. Zziɣ-d ɣer wid-nni i la yettraǧun deg-i, nniɣ-asen : ‚Ay atmaten muḍleɣ-ken ad ssutreɣ deg-wen ssmaḥ, yerna
mačči  stehzeɣ deg-wen,  maca  waleɣ kra  di   tegnawt.

Nnan-iyi-d : Ula d  nekni ncikk deg-k  yella wayen    i tettwaliḍ ɣer tegnawt. Nniɣ-asen : ay atmaten     waleɣ imjuhad yemmuten fisabililah banen-iyi-d am win ten-id- iwesfen  s yimru, maca  ttwaliɣ-ten ddren la  tḥerriken remmcen.

Ay atmaten, gar-asen waleɣ snat n telmeẓyin yiwet teqreb ɣer tadist tayeḍ teṭṭef mmi-s d amecṭuḥ deg yirebbi-s. lmeɛna n snat-agi n telmeẓyin, issenɛet-aneɣ- tent-id Rebbi akken a neḥṣu tilemẓit-nni yeṭṭfen mmi-s amecṭuḥ, tinna d tin nɣan lɛesker n Fransa akked mmi-s amecṭuḥ deg yirebbi-s, seddan ula d llufan-nni!

Dagi ilaq ad neḥṣu imenɣi n useggas 1954 mmuten deg-s ula d arrac imecṭaḥ d ccuhada. Ma d tayeḍ-nni, d tin nɣan akken s tadist ilaq ad neḥṣu  ula d  llufanat deg yiɛebbaḍ    n tyemmatin, mmuten urɛad i ẓran tafat n ddunit.

Ay atmaten, amjahed yulin ɣer udrar ad ijahed fisabililah, d nnif i t-yewwin, mačči d rrbeḥ mačči d zzhu. Yekcem tiẓegwa, iɛedda deg yifriyen yesber i lehwa d usemmiḍ, yelḥa i ṭṭlam, temẓi-s yesɛedda-tt akk di lḥif!

Asmi mi iḥulfa tḥuza-t terṣaṣt, ad yemmet, ur d-yenni ara ay arraw- iw  neɣ a  yimawlan-iw, yendeh  s  Rebbi.

Ay   atmaten, yezmer Rebbi ad as-yefk tudert di laxert xir n tin n ddunit, neɣ ala ?‛.

Nnan-d : ‚yezmer ad as-yefk tudert di laxert, xir n tin n ddunit.‛.

Rniɣ nniɣ-asen : ‚Ay atmaten, llan yirgazen-nneɣ di ddula n Fransa uqbel imenɣi, ɛacen di liser   ṭṭfen adeggiyen deg i ttuqadaren, maca mi walan atmaten-nsen  ɛacen  di  dell, di  tukksa n  sser,   di tmuḥeqranit, di lbaṭel, di lḥif<irgazen-nni sellmen deg
wadeggiyen-nni, maca atmaten-nsen terra-ten Fransa ddaw lḥafer-is, trekki deg-sen. Irgazen-agi yewwi-ten nnif ɣef watmaten-nsen, ulin ɣer udrar seblen tarwiḥt-nsen i leɛtab akked lmut, akken ad d-glun s liser i tegmat-nsen. Irgazen-agi mmuten ɣef nnif. Asmi i d-t tewwi tmurt azarug nnulfan-d kra n yimdanen semman i mmi-s n ccahid : mmi-s n ukerni». A yadra wigi d lḥeqq fell-asen ɣer Rebbi, neɣ ɣer yirgazen at-nnif ?‛. Nnan-iyi-d: ‚ Mačči d lḥeqq fell-asen‛. Nniɣ-asen : ‚D acu i d tifrat n taluft agi?‛. Nnan-iyi-d: ‚Tifrat-is: win i wumi ad nsel yenna i mmi-s n ccahid ‘a mmi-s n m-ukerni’, ad t-nenneɣ ad as-nexdem akerni i tmeṭṭut-is.‛. Nniɣ-asen : ‚ihi taluft-agi nufa-d tifrat-is. Maca mazal tayeḍ i umjahed yewwi nnif ɣef tyesmatin-is ɣef yess-is n watmaten-is, ijuhed yemmut fissabililah, yeǧǧa-yaɣ-d yessi-s d tigujilin, ad ilint di lḥerma-nneɣ d yiseɣ-nneɣ<, maca llan yimḍebren ɣef wadeggiyen n lxedma, ma ad tessuter ɣer-sen lxedma yelli-s n ccahid baba-s yemmut ɣef nnif. Taluft-agi dacu i d tifrat-is ?‛ Nnan-iyi-d: ‚Ad yili yihwah, neɣ a nili nekni; ad yili lbaṭel, neɣ ad nili nekni; ad yili lḥif, neɣ ad nili nekni; ad yili meḥyaf, neɣ ad nili nekni. Ɣer taggara nniɣ-asen : ‚Ay atmaten, tifrat n taluft-agi d lǧihad fisabililah.‛ Ukiɣ-d si targit !

1981

- 292 -
Taḍṣa n lmut Lliɣ deg uxxam-iw qqimeɣ di tlemmast n ufrag, rradyu ters tama-w, sliɣ deg-s i Ben Muḥemmed yebda tadwilt-is s tɣuri n tebratin, di tazwara yenna-d :« tabrat-agi urant-tt-id snat tyessetmatin-nneɣ, nnant-d deg-s » aql-anteɣ nettwaḥqer tḍill fell-anteɣ tɣellabit xas akka nesɛa atmaten, maca ugin ad rren fell-anteɣ ; la qqaren akk nuggad lmut. Tura a Ben Muḥemmed ilaq ad aɣ-d-tjawbeḍ ma sɛan lḥeqq mi uggaden lmut ?».

Ijaweb-itent, yenna : ‚A tiyessetmatin, ilaq ad teḥṣumt ula d nekni d atmaten-nwent. Ma nutni uggaden lmut nekni aql-aneɣ da ad nerr fell-awent ur nettugad ara lmut! ».

Ufiɣ-d tiyessetmatin-nni akked Ben Muḥemmed qqimen-d zdat-i mqabalen la ttmeslayen; ulsen-d akk i wayen akk i sliɣ uqbel ad tent-waliɣ. Neṭqeɣ ɣer telmeẓyin-nni nniɣ-asent : ‚D tidet i went-id-yenna Ben Muḥemmed, ḥeznemt fell-aneɣ ur nettugad ara, nekni d irgazen yettaḍṣan i lmut.‛.

Tezzi-d yiwet tmuqel-iyi-d s teḍṣa, tenna-yi-d : ‚Amek a Meẓyan ad teḍṣeḍ ɣer lmut ?!‛ Nniɣ-s : Mačči imdanen akk ṭṭaḍṣan i lmut, di yal tama n ddunit ulac win yeḍṣan i lmut, bexlaf mmi-s n teqbaylit.‛

Nleqmeɣ beddeɣ nniɣ-as : ‚mmuqel amek ad ḍṣeɣ i lmut ass ma ad iyi-d-teḥder! tmuqel-d, nekk sserseɣ afus-iw ɣef yidmaren-iw, nniɣ-as : ‚ass ma ad iyi-d-ḥazen s terṣaṣt, ad ṭṭfeɣ amkan-nni, ad ḍṣeɣ akka i lmut‛.
ḍṣiɣ s umedya ɣer tlemẓit-nni. Mi ḍṣiɣ ɣer-s, ssetḥeɣ-tt, ḥḥulfeɣ s teḍṣa-nni d taḍṣa n lḥecma. Neṭqeɣ nniɣ-as : ‚A weltma taḍṣa-yagi i n-ḍṣiɣ ɣer-m tegla-yi-d s lḥecma, acku ssetḥeɣ-kem. Maca, ma ad ḍṣeɣ i lmut, taḍṣa-w ad d-teglu s nnur‛.

Ukiɣ-d si targit !

1981

Leɣrur n zzman

Lliɣ deg yiwen n udrar yettusemman « Iɣil Lḥed n ccix» beddeɣ di tama ufella n ttejra yettusemman « Tajujet » llan tlata n yimɣaren n taddart-iw qqimen ɣer ttejra-nni, la ttmeslayen. Yiwen deg-sen isem-is AÆli, sin-nni wiyeḍ kifkif-iten yismawen-nsen Muḥ, Muḥ. AÆli isenned ɣer ljedra n ttejra-nni, iwehha iman-is qbala n temdint n Tizi Uzezzu, sliɣ-as-ifettu i sin-nni yellan am netta, yenna-yasen : ‚La ttwargamen imaziɣen di Tizi Uzezzu, yerna nekni lejdud-nneɣ d imaziɣen. Nekk ḥṣiɣ d acu i llan yimɣaren-nni; yerwi-d lebḥer-iw fell-asen, uẓiɣ beddeɣ nnig n yiqerray-nsen, nniɣ-asen : ‚D imuzzuren mačči d imaziɣen‛. AÆli iban-iyi-d iɣaḍ-it lḥal, la yesnehmu am wakli-nni yerfan ɣef ssid-is.

- 294 -
Waleɣ-ten ttin-d d irgazen ilemmasen di laÆmer. Lweqt yetti-d asmi yebda imenɣi n lgirra 1954. Ufiɣ-d irebbi-w yeččur d leslaḥ ameẓyan n yimenɣi. (LÆeslama a ṣṣaḥ) zwareg si zzaÆim-nni, wehheɣ-as « lmaṭ » nniɣ-as : ‚Ax-n leslaḥ tekreḍ ad tjahdeḍ ɣef nnif-ik, d lǧihad fisabililah. Yenna-yi-d Si AÆli: ‚Ala a gma, nekk ur zmireɣ ara. ».

Nniɣ-as : « Amek, lbaṭel d zzur, tawikksa n sser sɣur uÆdaw tzemreḍ-asen ! Lǧihad fisabililah ɣef lḥerma n tmurt-ik ur as-tezmireḍ ara? Akken i sliɣ ɣef leḥsab n yiles-ik, ɣileɣ-k d kečč ara irefden leslaḥ, wala nekk!‛.

Yenna-yi-d: ‚Ala a gma, ur zmireɣ ara.‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚ Ulac akk win ara sÆuɣ d gma alamma d kečč!‛. Uɣaleɣ ɣer Muḥ Ulḥusin nniɣ-as : ‚I kečč ad tjahdeḍ fisabilillah ? Ata leslaḥ yewjed ? ». Yenna-yi-d : «Ala a gma ur zmireɣ ara‛.

Wis tlata-nni kifkif. Nniɣ-asen :  « Cikkeɣ d lmut i tuggadem ay atmaten-iw ? ». Nnan-n-iyi-d: ‚D lmut i nuggad ad nemmet‛. Nniɣ-asen: ‚Atmaten-nwen xtaren lmut wala tudert ddaw lḥafer n yiÆdawen. Kunwi tuggadem lmut yellan deg ufus n Rebbi, terram-tt di txencuct n tbeckiḍt‛. Nnan-yi-d: ‚ A gma nuggad ad nemmet,.‛.  Nniɣ-asen: ‚Mačči akka i ken-ssneɣ ay-atmaten-iw ! Ssneɣ-ken ɣef ssebba n ulac teqqarem ad nemmet, ad nbaṣi<Tettgallam s wayagi di llem-nwen neɣ deg warraw n taddart-nwen< Nekk ɣileɣ s tidet tesÆam tismin tesÆam leḥrara n yiseɣ<‛

Tleḥeq-d terbaÆt n yimjuhad, ufan-iyi-d a ttemqellaÆeɣ akked imerbaḥ-nni, nnan-iyi-d : ‚Anef-asen a Meẓyan wigi d lkarÆin.‛. Wexxreɣ fell-asen, rriɣ tamuɣli-w ɣer
yimjuhad-nni. Waleɣ-ten s tlaba n tserdast sÆan dduzan n yimenɣi, tissas ufraren ɣef wudmawen-nsen<Dɣa ul-nni yeččuren d lxiq yuɣal yeččur-d d lferḥ. Iqerreb yiwen seg-sen ɣer tlata-nni lkarÆin yenna-yasen : ‚ S yiman-nwen ur tettjahadem ara, maca, teḥrrem yemma-twen ad tjahdem s yidrimen-nwen. Ad tefkem xemsin alef frank 500,00 i yiwen. Nnan-d: ‚Ma d idrimen nezmer ad d-nefk kter n ccerṭ-agi‛. Waleɣ yal wa deg-sen yefka-as tawriqt n xemsin alef yeṭṭef idrimen-nni. Nniɣ-as : ‚Err-asen idrimen-nsen akken ad ḥṣun wagi d ljihad fisabilileh. Tiniḍ-asen ad d-fken kan ayen iɣef teṣfa nniya-nsen, am nutni am wiyaḍ-nneɣ.‛. Ufiɣ-d nella d waṭas n yimdanen, tilawin d yirgazen qqimen, tiniḍ d ṣṣeḥba n tmeɣra, amkan-nni d abraḥ uzyib ur istugen ara. Amjahed-nni yerra-asen ssadiqa-nsen i yirgagayen-nni. Neṭqeɣ ɣer ugraw-nni, nniɣ-asen: ‚Ay atmaten ad aɣ-d-jemÆem idrimen, yal wa deg-wen ad d-yefk ayen iɣef i teṣfa niyya-s d ssadiqa fisabilileh i warraw n yimjuhad ?‛ Ufiɣ-d ɣur-i ssniwa, fkiɣ-as-tt i umjahed-nni la metren, nekk la smuquleɣ. Waleɣ yekka-ten-id akk, yal wa acḥal i d-igar di ssniwa-nni. Mi yelḥeq ɣer tlata-nni n yimjuhad, ḍeggren-as-d kra n ṣṣerf ɣer ssniwa-nni, ur yewwiḍ ara uḥric wis xemsa seg wayen i d-fkan wid-nni-nniḍen ? Ifakk-d ajmaÆ umjahed-nni, nniɣ-asen : ‚Ad awen-d-yexlef Rebbi si leḥlal ay atmaten!‛. Uɣaleɣ bɣiɣ ad asen-sfehmeɣ d acu i d-lmeÆna n tegrawla-nni akken ad Æawnen s wul, yal wa s wacu iwumi yezmer. Daɣen ad asen-sfehmeɣ lmeÆna n lǧihad fisabilileh. ḍemɛeɣ mi asen-
sfehmeɣ, ad ilin kra n yirgazen ara d-inleqmen ad refden leslaḥ ɣer lǧihad. Maca ad as-tiniḍ Æelmen s wacu ara asen-iniɣ, yal tikkelt mi neṭqeɣ ad asen-iniɣ : ‚ay atmaten, ad sekren ameslay d unecraḥ, wa itezzi ɣer wa. Nekk amzun ulac-iyi zdat-sen ! Mi susmeɣ ad ssusmen. Akken armi i tḥeqqeɣ d lmeqṣud-iw i ḥṣan, yewÆer fell-asen uyseɣ seg-sen. Zziɣ-d iman-iw akken ad asen-anfeɣ. Ufiɣ-d sin qqimen di rrif n rreḥba-nni yiwen d ilemẓi, wayeḍ d argaz yestemɣer. Neṭqeɣ ɣer yilemẓi-nni nniɣ-as : ‚Akken i k-sneɣ a mer tesÆiḍ tirrugza, hatan yewweḍ-d lawan ideg ad tt-id-tesbiyneḍ tekmel, Ax-n leslaḥ tekkreḍ-d ad tjahdeḍ d watmaten-ik yeffɣen ɣer lǧihad fisabilileh. Yal yiwen deg-sen yefka lÆahed ad yemmet d ccahid, neɣ ad iÆac d aḥrur di tmurt-is. AÆmer yellan d zzaÆim yezzi udem-is fell-I, yellha d umeslay akked wid-nni yeqqimen ɣer yidisan-is. Uɣaleɣ ɣer zzaÆim-nni amɣar yeqqaren ixuṣ-iyi yiwen unagi wamma nekk d amjahed, nniɣ-as : ‚Ax-n leslaḥ a Æemmi li ad tjahdeḍ fisabilileh<Yenna-yi-d: ‚Ala a gma uggadeɣ‛.

Nekk buddeɣ-t ad yemmet d ccahid, nniɣ-d ad t-awiɣ weḥd-s ad as-sfehmeɣ alamma yefhem tamsalt, nniɣ-as : ‚Iyyan yid-i ḥwaǧeɣ-k‛. Yusa-d, nruḥ ɣer yiwen n uxxam yesÆa taɣurfet tesÆa tirekkadin si berra n ufrag. Nekcem ɣer tɣurfet-nni, nufa ṭṭabla, sin n yikirsiyen, neqqim nemqabal, nniɣ-as : « Nwiɣ a dda li d nekk i d ameẓyan ad ɣefleɣ wala kečč ! aqla-k meqqreḍ s leÆqel-ik, nekni d irgazen i nella d lÆib fell-aneɣ ma newwi ddell, ma nesber i tmuḥeqranit. ». Yenna-yi-d : « A gma ulac win i yi-
ḥeqren yekkes-iyi lbista.‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚A dda  li d lÆib zdat n Rebbi zdat n yimdanen ma nella d irgazen n yiman- nneɣ kan, d lwajeb fell-ak ad tiliḍ d argaz n tmurt-ik, listiÆmar hatan yekkes-ak tamurt-ik mačči d lbista-k i ak- yekkes, ḥseb yekkes-ik ula d kečč si txelqit n ddunit. Ili-k d argaz rfed leslaḥ ad tjahdeḍ‛ . Fkiɣ-as lmaṭ yeḍsa-d ɣur- i yenna-yi-d : ‚Tenwiḍ d lemkellex i lliɣ ? Muqel kan anect n lɣaci di berra-agi ugin ad jahden. Neɣ nutni ad xedmen ɣef warraw-nsen ad zhun, nekk ad fkeɣ iman-iw i lmut akken ad asen-d-ḥelliɣ!‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚A dda  li steɣfer, xas amdan yettkellix, Rebbi ur yettkellix ara lmumnin. Ma nekker ɣer lǧihad akken akk nella d arraw n Lezzayer, winna d lǧihad fisabil n tmurt-nneɣ, mačči fisabililleh. Lǧihad fisabililleh! ma d kečč ad tmuddeḍ iman-ik i lmut, rnu teḥṣiḍ s wid yellan d arraw n tmurt am kečč la zehhun neɣ xeddmen ɣef warraw-nsen. Ur teḥṣiḍ ad temmteḍ, nutni ad tt-ɣelten neɣ mi i tt-id-tḥerreḍ ahat ad ilin xir-ik. Maca kečč tumneḍ s Rebbi ad ak-yefk xir n ddunit. D wa i d lǧihad fisabililleh. lmut deg ufus n Rebbi, lqewwa deg ufus n Rebbi. D lwajeb fell-ak ad t-tjahdeḍ yerna ad tefkeḍ lÆahed am watmaten-ik imjuhad yefkan lÆahed ad mmten d imjuhad, neɣ ad idiren d iḥruren. Nelqem, ili-k d argaz! attan lḥerma n tmurt-ik d leslaḥ-agi i ak-fkiɣ; ili-k d argaz, leÆmer deg ufus n Rebbi.‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚ Yak a gma nekk d aderwic, lufan sÆiɣ leÆqel ad refdeɣ  leslaḥ mebla ma tenniḍ-iyi-d‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Deg wayagi fkiɣ-ak lḥeqq, ula d nekk ur qebbleɣ  ara ad ak-fkeɣ leslaḥ ma ur tesÆiḍ ara leÆqel.‛
Nemyuǧǧa sslam, uɣaleɣ ɣer terbaÆt-iw, mi leḥqeɣ ɣer-sen nniɣ-asen : ‚Yya-w ay atmaten a nettkel ɣef Rebbi ad nebdu lǧihad.‛ Nnan-d akk lettkal ɣef Rebbi. Nebda tikli, nleḥḥu. Nekk zwireɣ, nutni ddan-d d uḍar-iw. Ufiɣ-d nelḥeq ɣer talast yebḍan gar lḥedd n ccix d uÆerqub yettusemman « Ḥlafa ». LÆesker n uÆdaw teǧǧam-ten ɣer deffir, ha-ten deffir n yiɣil-ina ferqen d tirebbaÆ, di tmazirt n « Tgulmamt ». TarbaÆt yellan di tama ufella sÆan lemdafeÆ, tarbaÆt yellan ddaw-as sÆan leslaḥ aẓayan, tarbaÆt yellan di tama n wadda sÆan leslaḥ alemmas. Kečč a Meẓyan ḥebber, twaliḍ amek ilaq ad txedmeḍ, i d-fehmeɣ. Nbedd di ccwear, la nettemyarra tirrugza armi nemwafaq ad nqabel aÆdaw-nneɣ. Yid-neɣ i yebɣun yeḍru. Nuɣal ɣer deffir nleḥḥu s ttawil. Nekk la ttḥebbireɣ amek ara xedmeɣ ? Aqeddem d uṣÆib, awexxɣer d lÆib. Nekni nesÆa leslaḥ alemmas d umeẓyan akked ibeckiḍen n ṣṣyada, ḍḥiɣ-d yebḍa rray-iw!

Ma mmuqleɣ ɣer leslaḥ n uÆdaw, ad as-awiɣ atmaten-iw am yizgaren s aÆric, ad mmten mebla ma nɣan. Ma zziɣ ɣer tirrugza n yimjuhad-nni d laman i sÆan s Rebbi, ɣur-i ṭṭmeÆ ad naweḍ ɣer lebɣi-nneɣ. Xetmeɣ-tt ad neṭṭef tiyita d uÆdaw, Rebbi ad aɣ-yili d amÆiwen. Mi newweḍ ɣer yiɣil-nni yellan gar-aneɣ d yiÆdawen-nneɣ sbeddeɣ tarbaÆt-iw, beddeɣ zdat-nsen, nniɣ-asen : ‚Ay atmaten-iw imjuhad, lmeÆna n lǧihad fisabililleh d lajer ɣer Rebbi i aɣ-d-ixelqen d irgazen. Lmeqsud-nneɣ d lmut ṭṭmeÆ-nneɣ d lǧennet. Ay atmaten-nneɣ, iɛdawen atna deffir n yiɣil-agi, ilaq ad ten-qabel akken i d-yewwi lḥal. Yewweḍ-d lawan
ideg ara d-nbeggen liman-nneɣ s Rebbi, tadukli, tirrugza, tuggdi-nneɣ si Rebbi ma nestehza di lǧihad-nneɣ, ulac awexxer ɣer deffir, ulac win ara iwexxren ɣef uberdi n gma-s yettwaḥuzan yeɣli, alamma yeɣli ɣer tama-s.

Neṭṭqen-d s yiwen n wawal nnan-d : „Tuggdi si Rebbi, lettkal fell-as, ad nemmet d ccuhada neɣ ad nidir d iḥruren.“ Nniɣ-asen : „Ihi ay atmaten nekk ad ken-saÆdeɣ s wayen i wumi ssneɣ d wayen i wumi zemreɣ, Rebbi ad yili yid-neɣ.

Bdiɣ sneÆzaleɣ tarbaÆt-nni ɣef tlata n yiḥricen: wid-nni yesÆan ibeckiḍen n ṣṣyada, heggaɣ-ten ad qablen tarbeÆt-nni n lÆeskar yesÆan leslaḥ alemmas, wid yesÆan leslaḥ ameẓyan, ad qablen leslaḥ aẓayan. Wid deg-nneɣ yesÆa leslaḥ alemmas, ad qablen lemdafeÆ ar dqal nniɣ-asen : „Tura ad sḍilleɣ tamuɣli-w s tufra akken ad waliɣ amek ad teddum mi ara tḍillem ɣer-sen!“ Uɣaleɣ ɣef wudem ddiɣ akken ilaq armi leḥqeɣ ɣer yiri n yiɣil-nni, refdeɣ tamuɣli-w ɣer lÆeskar-nni.

Bdiɣ si terbaÆt-nni yesÆan leslaḥ alemmas mi muqleɣ ɣer-sen, ad zziɣ ɣer wid-nni yesÆan ibeckiḍen n ṣṣyada, ad amreɣ yiwen deg-sen amek ara yeddu, ad rnuɣ ad as-geɣ lmara ɣef yiɣil, ad as-iniɣ ad iwehhi abeckiḍ-is s lewhi n lmara-nni akken ma yeknu zznad ur yettazgal ara. Mi fakkeɣ si tarbaÆt-nni, uɣaleɣ ɣer wid-nni yesÆan leslaḥ ameẓyan qaÆdeɣ-ten ad qablen leslaḥ aẓẓayan. Mi leḥqeɣ ɣer wid-nni-nneɣ yesÆan alemmas, uqbel ad muqleɣ ɣer lÆeskar-nni nniɣ-asen : „Ttheyyit iman-nwen yiwen yiwen acku yeḥmeq-aneɣ lweqt.“ Iqerreb-d yiwen seg-sen, nekk
mmuqleɣ ɣer tarbaÆt-nni yesÆan lemdafeÆ akken ad asen-geɣ lmarat, mi i d-iqerreb yesḍil tamuɣli-s ɣer lÆeskar-nni, mi i d-zziɣ ɣer-s yenna-yi-d : ‚A Meẓyan haten-a lemdafeÆ wa ɣer wa ! ». Suɣeɣ fell-as nniɣ-as : ‚Ulac lemdafeÆ am wid n Rebbi, rnu wid-inna mačči d lemdafaÆ, d ijaÆbuben n ssiman iɣer sduran iman-nsen ɣilen ad ten-sellken ».

Nniɣ-as akka, akken ur feččlen ara yemjuhad-nni. Maca imjuhad-nni neṭqen-d s yiwen n wawal, nnan-d : « Ma d lemdafaÆ, lmut deg ufus n Rebbi, neɣ deg uxencuc n lemdafaÆ ?. Nniɣ-asen : « Lmut deg ufus n Rebbi, mačči deg uxencuc n lemdafaÆ ».

Imir tḥeqqeɣ ɣef yimjuhad-nni uqbel ad nnaɣen d uÆdaw, nɣan tuggdi; Neṭqeɣ nniɣ-asen : « Ihi ay-atmaten wid-inna d lemdafaÆ, maca ad ttekleɣ fell-awen, tura ad mmuqleɣ amek ara awen-d-awiɣ lewhi, yal yiwen deg-wen, ad as-d-geɣ lmara d lɣerḍ ɣer bab n lemdafeÆ‛.

Mi fukkeɣ asgam di terbaÆt-nni n ṭrad, rniɣ snedheɣ kra n yimjuhad seg yal tarbaÆt, nniɣ-asen : « Kunwi ur kkatet ara alamma nwexxer-d ɣer yimukan-nneɣ ad nÆemmer leslaḥ, ad tuɣalem ad teṭṭfem tiyita-nneɣ di laÆḍil ad nessewjed iman-nneɣ". Rniɣ mliɣ-asen amek ara neddu s uxatel alamma nelḥeq, yal yiwen ad iwehhi leslaḥ-is ɣef lmara-s.

Nniɣ-asen :  « Mi nelḥeq  nessers ixencucen ibeckaḍ ɣef lmarat-nneɣ, ad nesselqem iman-nneɣ akken ad nwali ɣer zdat, ad newwet s yiwet n tyita.‛. Mi nelḥeq ɣer lmarat-nni nesnelqem iman-nneɣ, tiyita telḥeq  s aÆdaw. Uqbel ad leqmen tiyita wid-nni i wumi nniɣ ad wwten d ineggura, lÆeskar-nni yellan d ineggura ur ɣlin
ara, waleɣ sersen leslaḥ refden ifassen-nsen la ttsuɣun: ‚Ḥebset tiyita a qleɣ nsellem<‛. Umreɣ imjuhad-nni nniɣ-asen : ‚Ḥebset  tiyita, maca ur ttamnet ara    ixeddaÆen, Æasset ɣef yiman-nwen swejdet i tyita-nniḍen. Ad nqerreb ɣer-sen s leslaḥ gar yifassen, ur ttamnet ara ama d win yeɣlin neɣ d win ibedden; win iḥerken deg-sen ad ten-ḥarrek s rṣaṣ. Mi newweḍ   ɣer-sen umreɣ      imjuhad-nni nniɣ-asen : ‚Ciddet-asen ifassen ad ten-nawi s tyita    d udeggar<‛.    Mmɣen    fell-asen cidden-asen      ifassen timendeffirt.

Ufiɣ-d iman-iw deg umkan-nni lliɣ weḥdi d ameksa ksiɣ sin n yizgaren semqaranen iman-nsen idis ɣer yidis, ksan; beddeɣ zdat-nsen d ameksa akka i d leɣrur n zzman ! Waleɣ     izgaren-nni uzzlen deffir sin n yimdanen yerran afus deg ufus i trewla, ur ḥṣiɣ   d acu i ten-yesrewlen ! Ttwaliɣ deg-sen la regglen rennun, mi d-ḥellan aÆerqub mazal wayeḍ. Nekk uggadeɣ fell-asen ad ruḥen s anida ur ten-ttafeɣ ara, neɣ ad ḍillen deg yifri ad grirben, nutni regglen,  nekk  ad  ten-tabaɛeɣ, qqareɣ-asen :      ‚Ahda wuulah,  ahda   wuulah
Waleɣ-ten sneqqsen di tazzla, ḍemÆeɣ ad ḥebsen, mi ḍillen i tiɣilt-nni, nekk leḥqeɣ, beddeɣ, waleɣ-ten ɣer tama n wadda deg umkan yettusemman « Amalu n lÆinṣer » d ayla n yiwen  isem-is  LeÆmara n WaÆrab. Izgaren-nni      teddun ssrid ɣer yiwen  n yifri lqayen, nekk ttwasemreɣ      deg umkan-nni ideg lliɣ beddeɣ, dayen tfuk fell-i ddunit acku
fehmeɣ izgaren-nni d sin n watmaten-iw yellan d imdanen uqbel ara yawḍen ɣer yifri-nni, waleɣ yiwen d ilemẓi isem-is Meẓyan, ikkes tafunast di tama-nni n wadda, ssawleɣ-as : "Ahya Meẓyan ḥbes-d izgaren-nni. Waleɣ izgaren-nni ḥebsen-d ɣer tfunast-nni. Ma d Meẓyan ur d-yellha ara d yizgaren, iwehha-as s ufus-is i tfunast-nni, terra-d d asawen. Uzzleɣ ɣer yizgaren-nni ad ten-id-ḥerreɣ d asawen Mlileɣ-d tafunast-nni ɣer yiwet n talast yellan gar wayla-w d wayla n LaÆmara n WaÆrab. Nettat teḥbes, nekk beddeɣ ɣer-s nerra talast-nni yellan gar-aneɣ, izgaren-nni ttin-d d iÆejmiyen imeẓyanen ulin d asawen. Smuquleɣ tafunast-nni armi i d-leḥqen ɣer-s fehmeɣ-d d arraw-is. Leḥqen srid ɣer tmaẓẓagt ad ṭṭḍen. Mmuqleɣ ɣer tmaẓẓagt n tfunast-nni waleɣ tenteḍ ɣef uglim, tban-iyi-d tesÆa aṭas n yiffan, maca d ilmawen. IÆejmiyen-nni banen-iyi-d lluẓen aṭas, mi mmɣen ɣer yiff ad t-afen d ilem, ad beddlen wayeḍ; kifkif. Kkan-d akk iffan-nni, sqedlafen armi dayen uysen teqqur tmaẓẓagt n yemma-tsen. Uɣalen ḥebsen asdummer la smuqulen ɣer tmaẓẓagt-nni yekkawen. Nekk ɣaḍen-iyi, neṭqeɣ nniɣ-d : ‚IÆejmiyen-agi messakit rɣan si laẓ ur ufan ara acu ara ṭṭḍen seg yemma-tsen‛. Waleɣ-ten ttin-d d iɣilasen, greɣ tamawt i tmaẓẓagin n tfunast-nni, waleɣ tesÆa sebÆa yiffan d ukmilen, wis tmanya d nnefṣ n yiff, rriɣ tamuɣli-w ɣer warraw n tfunast-nni, sneqdeɣ-ten, ufiɣ-ten d iɣilasen mačči d iÆejmiyen!

- 303 -
Ufiɣ-d  lliɣ di  lqahwa  n  taddart  qqimeɣ   ɣer   ṭṭabla nemqabal d dda AÆli am wasmi nttemqabal ɣer ṭṭabla di tɣurfet-nni. Dda  li yettmeslay s ṣwab d lmeÆqul, lɣaci yellan din-a as-sɣaden am ccix lmefti di lǧameÆ, nekk selleɣ i lÆeqliyya-nni awal ur yeddi d gma-s am win izuzzuren  aclim. Mi  yewwa   wul-iw   neṭqeɣ   nniɣ-as :

„Mačči  akka  i d  lÆeqliya a dda   li‛. Waleɣ     udem-is yennexrab, yenna-yi-d : „Yiwen n uqcic akka am kečč d mmi-s n mmi, tebɣiḍ ad tiliḍ d aÆeqli kter-iw ?“
Lɣaci-nni merra ḍṣan deg-i, akka i d leɣrur n zzman! Nniɣ-as : « Zik sneɣ-k a dda  li ur telliḍ ara di laÆqel-ik ! Neɣ tura aql-aɣ di litteÆ, tuɣaleḍ s laÆqel-ik? ». Yenna-yi-d : « Dadda-k  li ur nelli ara di laÆqel-is ay ameslub ? » Nniɣ-as: „LaÆqel am-wagi i tesÆiḍ awer tesÆuɣ di tussna-w, taslubi axir-is ; laÆqel yettɣaben di ṭṭiq ula wumi-t di litteÆ”. Yenna-yi-d: „Anef-as tura i laÆqel, yya-n tura ad nelÆeb ddi wuminu!“. Nniɣ-as: „Ih ad nelÆeb ddi wuminu“. Nebda nleÆÆeb ddi wuminu, ttwaliɣ mačči d lleÆb n tussna, d lleÆb n jxara.

Tikkelt ttwaliɣ yeqqen adubli gar tḥeǧǧurin, tikkelt ad d-yelÆeb seg leḥfir netta yesÆa lleÆb deg ufus-is<Ṭṭfeɣ ṭṭfeɣ armi  ččureɣ,  suɣeɣ  fell-as, nniɣ-as : „Ddi      wuminu yettwalÆab s tussna, mačči s ddraÆ“. Yerfa-d fell-I, yenna-yi-d : „Nekk s ddraÆ      i laÆbeɣ“. Nniɣ-as: „Maca ddraÆ igellu-d s tendemmit.“ Yenna-yi-d: „Nekk ma yi-d-iɣum allen ur d-ḥareɣ deg yiwen la di lḥebs wala di lmut, i yi-d-yenna.

Yessers tiḥeǧǧurin-nni yellan deg ufus-is, yeččeḥ-iyi-d s tmuɣli, udem-is yuɣal d irrig ireqqen. Nekk teɣli-d deg-i
tugdi, ḥulfeɣ ad-as-tiniḍ d izrem i d-yerfan fell-i, uɣaleɣ deg uḥiwet nniɣ-as : ‚Aha dayen ur reffu ara a dda li, dayen-iyi lleÆb n ddi wuminu yid-k!‛. Wexreɣ seg ṭṭabla - nni, yenna-yi-d : ‚Axaṭer tugadeḍ-iyi‛. Daɣen lɣaci-nni ḍsan deg-i, iɣaḍ-iyi lḥal sḥissfeɣ deg wul-iw, nniɣ-d: « Asmi tella teggdi ur uggadeɣ ara, d nekk i as-yettaran tirrugza ? Tura tfakk tuggdi uggadeɣ-t !» yekkufet-d wul-iw, nniɣ-as : « Asmi tella tuggdi d nekk i ak-yettarran tirrugza, neɣ tettuḍ a dda li ?‛. Yenna-yi-d:  ‚Yiwen n umuggaḍ am kečč terriḍ-iyi-d tirrugza ? Ma d argaz uɣal-d ɣer ddi wuminu mi ur tuggadeḍ ara!‛.

Lɣaci-nni ḍṣan deg-i, nekk ḥulfeɣ kkren-d iḥujaja (ijujaḥ) n tmes deg ul-iw, nniɣ-as : « Mi i k-uggadeɣ, yya-n ad nernu lleÆb ». Nuɣal ɣer ddi wuminu, tazwara d lleÆb n ddraÆ uffir, taggara d uḍhir. Daɣen  tirrugza-nni  sÆiɣ, tufeg; tares-d deg-i tuggdi aceṭṭḥeɣ s targagayt, swexxreɣ iman-iw seg ṭṭabla, nniɣ-as : ‚Dayen a dda li Æyiɣ lleÆb ». Yenna-yi-d : « D tuggdi i tuggadeḍ‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚ A gma uggadeɣ-k‛. Ssiwleɣ i uqehwaǧi nniɣ-as : ‚Ḥaseb-iyi-d, lleÆb-agi, d nekk ara t-ixellṣen‛. Dda li yedda-d d usiwel-nni, yekker-d ɣur-i ireṣṣa-d deg-i allen-is. Nekk tfak fell-i ddunit, tiniḍ d Æeẓrayen i d-ibedden ɣur-i, yenna-yi-d : ‚Meḥsub tesÆiḍ idrimen am nekk akken ad xellseḍ fell-i a yiwen n umuggad‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚ A gma ad xellṣeɣ xas ur sÆiɣ ara, axaṭer uggadeɣ-k‛. Yenna-yi-d : ‚Ass-a teɣliḍ-d deg ufus-iw ur k-teggeɣ ara berru alamma tsuɣeḍ, ad ak-i-d-slen akk yirgazen-agi, ad d-tiniḍ uggadeɣ-k‛. Akka i d-
yecreḍ fell-i «  li zzaÆim ». Suɣeɣ nniɣ-d : ‚Gmat-nneɣ  li uggadeɣ-t ay atmaten ! »

Ufiɣ-d iman-iw beddeɣ deg yiwen n ubrid d arqiqan, ddaw ubrid-nni d asyax. Greɣ asurif, sliɣ deffir yekker umeslay, mi zziɣ mmuqleɣ, waleɣ yiwen n yilemẓi d aḍeggal-iw isem-is Muḥed u isa ad yettwarḥem. Yezwer-d yiwen n yilemẓi zdat-is, d aberrani, ad d-ileḥḥu s umlelli, fehmeɣ-t yesker.

Ma d Muḥ mi it-id-irufeq fehmeɣ swan lwaḥid. Mi it-iwala yesker ur yettkil ara fell-as akken ad as-yanef ad iruḥ weḥd-s ɣer taddart-is<Nekk mi waleɣ tikli n yilemẓi-nni tesseḍs-iyi-d, ur tban d tikli, ur tban d ccḍeḥ.

Lḥan-d armi qrib ad d-awḍen ɣur-i, Muḥ ibedd, la yesmuqul ɣer yiwet n tama s tmuɣli n lbeÆd. Asekran-nni ikemmel-d tikli, mi d-yelḥeq yebda-d argam deg-i, netta ad ireggem, nekk la ttaḍseɣ ɣer-s, acku d yiwen ukurriÆ d akudar d uḍÆif, ma suḍeɣ-t ad yafeg.

Ur bɣiɣ ara ad as-geɣ lÆinad, ssetḥeɣ rnu iɣaḍ-iyi. Lḥan-d sin n yirgazen kkan-d ansi akken i d-yekka, lsan ibernas d imellalen, ticucay tizeggaɣin. Leḥqen-d ɣer-neɣ mmuqlen-d ɣur-i, rran-d fell-i sslam, kemmlen abrid-nsen.

Irgazen-nni fehmeɣ-ten n taddart n usekran-nni, lḥan kra n yisurrifen, iluÆa-ten yilemẓi-nni yenna-yasen : ‚Lufan mačči d kunwi, ass-a ad as-tt-ssiwḍeɣ ɣer lmuḥal‛ ḍsiɣ nniɣ-as : ‚D acu n lmuḥal iɣer ad iyi-tt-tessiwḍeḍ ? Ma aṭas d lefraq ara nemfaraq ».

Zzin-d s tmuɣli yirgazen-nni ḍsan-d ɣer-i, nnan-d : ‚Wellah ma texḍiḍ a Meẓyan d lefraq kan i awen-ilaqen. Zzin kemmlen abrid-nsen. Nekk udreɣ deg usyax-nni leḥḥuɣ sserkadeɣ iman-iw, ufiɣ-d
asekran-nni yedda-d ɣef yidis-iw s umlelli, ugadeɣ ad yeɣli neɣ ad yegrireb, nniɣ-d deg wul-iw : mi d-yedda di lwens-iw, wellah ma ǧǧiɣ-t. Mmɣeɣ ṭṭfeɣ-as afus armi i ners ɣer yiwen n umraḥ yellan d abrid. LuÆeɣ-t nniɣ-as : ‚A gma tessneḍ abrid ɣer taddart-ik?‛. Yenna-yi-d : « Ssneɣ, d wagi i d abrid ad iyi-issiwḍen ɣer taddart-iw‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚ MeÆna muqel iman-ik tura ma tzemreḍ ad truḥeḍ weḥd-k neɣ ad ak-rɣefqeɣ‛. Yenna-yi-d : « Ala, zemreɣ ad ruḥeɣ weḥd-i‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚ Ihi ad isahel Rebbi fell-ak‛.

Iruḥ, waleɣ-t ileḥḥu terked tikli-s, ad as-tiniḍ mačči d asekran-nni ! imir yettkel wul-iw ɣef rrwaḥ-is. SuÆfeɣ akken ad uɣaleɣ s abrid-nni ufella, ufiɣ-d asyax-nni yuɣal d ifri yesÆan tlata n leswar, wa nnig wa am trekkadin Ælayit s lqis n tiddi-w. Mi leḥqeɣ ɣer ssur amezwaru tekkeɣ s yifasen-iw ɣef yiri ufella, neṣṣfeɣ ssur-nni s walluy, ufiɣ-d ilemẓi-nni yeṭṭef-d deg wammas-iw, fehmeɣ-t yebɣa ad at-Æiwneɣ akken ad d-yali ula d netta.

Xas ḥulfeɣ ẓẓay fell-i, maca nniɣ-d mi yid-i i d-yedda ilaq kan ad t-ssiliɣ. Ssiliɣ iman-iw s tmara; nuli. Mi leḥqeɣ ɣer ssur wis sin, daɣen neṣṣfeɣ-t s walluy, aneɣḍim-nni igar-iyi-d timetɣalltin yeṭṭef-d deg wammas-iw. Tikkelt-nni ḥulfeɣ yerna taẓẓayt, rriɣ ccek deg wul-iw nniɣ-d : di lbal-is yebɣa ad iyi-jbed akken ad ɣliɣ, mačči d alluy i d-yeqṣed yid-i. Maca amer d ɛeggu kan i Æyiɣ, tura mi d-yedda yid-i wellah ad at-ssiliɣ, neɣ ad neɣli di sin. Refdeɣ iman-iw s tmara n tmariwin, mi nuli waleɣ mazal-aneɣ yiwen n ssur ad naweḍ s abrid ufella, ḥulfeɣ s Æeyyu
yerra-yi d aceṭṭiḍ. Nniɣ-d deg wul-iw : ilaq tura ad d-jemÆeɣ ayen i d-mazal di tezmert-iw, ad sserseɣ ifassen-iw ɣef yiri n ssur-agi ad  neggzeɣ  ad  ssiliɣ iman-iw s lemɣawla, akken ur d-yettaṭaf ara deg-i uberttitt-agi, mi uliɣ ad as-id-fkeɣ afus ad at-ssiliɣ.

Mi neṣṣfeɣ ssur-nni s walluy wis tlata, ufiɣ-d arfiq-nni deg wammas-iw, rnu tikkelt-agi ḥulfeɣ ad iyi-jebbed d akessar akken ad iyi-sseɣli. Nekk qqareɣ-as : ‚Ad ak-yehdu Rebbi berka-k anejbud deg-i, serreḥ-iyi ad aliɣ ma ulac ad neɣli di sin < Netta meskud ttberriɣ fell-as irennu di nneqma-s, armi waleɣ ssur-nni ad-yettnelqam seg zzur unejbud-nni, nniɣ-as i umcum-nni : ‚Hata-n ssur-agi ad yettnelqam seg ugafa-agi, ad d-yeɣli yes-neɣ ad aɣ-yerdem  di   tmurt, serreḥ-iyi ad aliɣ, neɣ ddnub-ik i yiri-k.‘.

Yessili-d ifassen-is yeṭṭef-iyi seg tuyat, la yessalay iman-is akken ad iyi-d-iḥḥer si tama ufella. Iyɣer akka!?

Tekkeɣ  s yiwen ufus  ɣef yiri n ssur-nni, wayeḍ   ufus ceyyÆeɣ-t ɣer tyersi n uxsim-nni-inu, xennqeɣ deg-s armi yekkes ifassen-is seg-i, ssiliɣ iman-iw. Mi leḥqeɣ nnig n yifri-nni, waleɣ yelḥa-d yiwen n yilemẓi isem-is Lmulud, iruḥ srid ɣer yifri-nni, ijbed-d win-a  i yi-ijebbden d akessar, yessili-t-id  yeẓẓel-it deg ubrid isḍuḍeÆ   la yesselqaf.

Lawan yetti-d d ttnaṣfa n yiḍ, nniɣ-as i Lmulud: ‚Yallah ad nerwel, sixxef iman-ik, ma iḍill-d fell-aneɣ walbaÆḍ ad nbaṣi.

Nruḥ, nelḥa kra n yisurrifen, mmuqleɣ ɣer deffir waleɣ tḍill-d deg-neɣ tafat n trisiti n ufus, nniɣ-as i Lmulud: ‚Ah ya Lmulud nettwaṭṭef, atan anwa i d-iḍillen s trisiti!
telḥeq-aneɣ-d. Nukni nreggel deg yiwet n tmazirt la neddaray tineqlin akken ur nettwaɛqal ara. Trisiti la aɣ-d-tettabaɛ. La nreggel armi nwala tirebbaÆ n lɣaci kkan-d seg wansi-nni iɣer nerra, ad d-leḥḥun d adur wa zdat wa deg ubrid-nni ɣerqiqan.

A Meẓyan lɣaci-nni n taddart n winna i tenɣiḍ, haten-an seg tmeɣra i d-kkan d imetnezhen, i d-fehmeɣ di target. Nekk ugadeɣ imezwura deg-sen ma leḥqen ɣer win-a i neǧǧa yemmut, ad ssiwlen i wid-nni yellan d ineggura ad aɣ-d-ḥarren ad nettwaṭṭef, maca imdanen-nni ttwaliɣ deg-sen rran kan abrid gar wallen.

Mi Æeddan akk faten fell-aneɣ, trisiti-nni, mazal-itt tedda-d d uḍar-nneɣ ay akken nebɣu nuzzel, armi sliɣ i teɣri ɣer deffir tenna-d : ‘Ḥbes a Meẓyan aqla-k tettwaṭṭfeḍ’. Mi mmuqleɣ ɣer deffir, waleɣ d yiwen n uqcic i aɣ-d-yettabaÆen, yuzga-d zdat n Lmulud, ibbed. Fehmeɣ-t yeḥseb iman-is, dayen yettwaṭṭef, nniɣ-d deg wul-iw : mi yettwaṭṭef Lmulud ula d nekk ḥseb ttwaṭṭfeɣ.

Rniɣ tarewla, tarewla di tmazirt-nni; aqcic-nni i iyi-d-yettabaÆen s trisiti yeqqar-iyi-d: ‘Ḥbes aql-i leḥqeɣ-k-id<’. Nekk mazal ḍemÆeɣ leslak, mi kecmeɣ s abrid ufiɣ-t-id zdat-i, yenna-yi-d: ‘Ḥbes aql-ak tettwaṭṭfeḍ.

Aqcic-nni, xas akken di leÆmer neɣ di tfekka meẓẓi, maca di lhiba-s ɣer-i yugar izem iṣaḍen ! Mi t-mmuqleɣ waleɣ-t d amirqiq d ameḍÆafu, yelsa tacluḥt teqdem, tumes. Nekk ufiɣ-d lsiɣ abernus d acebḥan zeddig, ṭṭfeɣ deg ufus tisura n tbalizt ideg jemÆeɣ lekwaɣeḍ n tira-w. Rriɣ tisura-nni ddaw n ucḍaḍ, wehheɣ-tent ɣer-s akken ad iɣil d
tameẓyant i  ṭṭfeɣ nniɣ-as : « Ddnub-ik i yiri-k ad ak-rnuɣ ɣer dadda-k, attan tmeẓyant deg ufus-iw, tixer fell-i neɣ ad  ak-nɣeɣ ! ». Nekk  ‚la ttberriɣ fell-as, netta la d-yettqeddim   ɣer-i armi i d-yewweḍ  zdat-i, yenna-d : ‚D tisura n tbalizt i teṭṭfeḍ deg ufus-ik mačči d tameẓyant. ».

Nniɣ-as : « Mačči d tisura, d tameẓyant ttixer ddnub-ik i yiri-k‛.

Yuẓa-d ɣer-i yemmeɣ-d ad iyi-ṭṭef, rriɣ afus-iw ɣer deffir wwteɣ-t   s  axenfuc, tewwi-t tyita-nni  yeɣli.  Waleɣ-t yesḍuḍeÆ   am  umezwaru-nni.   Unfeɣ-as, lḥiɣ kra      n yisurrifen deg ubrid-nni arqiqan, kecmeɣ s abrid anaṣli d azrug  gar tÆersiwin, waleɣ zdat-i rebÆa n     yilmeẓyen leḥḥun wa zdat wa, nniɣ-d : ilaq ad azzleɣ      akken ur gemnen ara fell-i mi ara sen-Æeddiɣ, ma ulac ad iyi-ṭṭfen!

Uzzleɣ armi qrib ad aten-leḥqeɣ, waleɣ  ṭṭfen tiÆekkazin leḥḥun sÆukkuzen. Yal yiwen deg-sen mi igar asurif, ad yesÆakkez tlata n tikkal, ad d-yeg tlata n lmarat ta zdat ta deg wakal, ad d-yini : « Laylah-illah, Muḥemmed raṣul- lleh ». Mi leḥqeɣ, beddeɣ ɣer-sen ad ten-smuquleɣ d acu- ten wigi !

A Meẓyan wid-nni d ṭṭelba, d igezzanen Æelmen s wayen akk yeḍran d wayen ara d-yeḍrun » i d-fehmeɣ. Neṭqeɣ ɣer-sen, nniɣ-asen : ‚Win-a d nekk  i t-ixenqen,    maca yeḍlem-iyi, mi ruḥeɣ akken ad aliɣ, netta ad iyi-d-yesseɣli; berreɣ fell-as aṭas n tikal, netta la yettzad, xenqeɣ-t. Ula mi yemmut yenna-aneɣ-d lufan ur iyi-xniq ara, ad gluɣ yes- sen i sin am Meẓyan am Lmulud, i yi-d-yenna yiwen seg ṭṭelba-nni. Nniɣ-asen:‛Twalam ay-atmaten ! Yak yeḍlem-
iyi ?‛. Yenna-yi-d ṭṭaleb-nni: ‚yeḍlem-ik, maca a Meẓyan wellah ad tbaṣiḍ‛. Nniɣ-d deg wul-iw : tura atan ṭṭfen Lmulud ad yesÆeddi lḥebs di leÆḍil, nekk asmi ara iyi-ṭṭfen ad baṣiɣ. Neṭqeɣ nniɣ-asen: ‚Maca ay-atmaten, yeḍlem-iyi!‛

Nniɣ-asen akka, akken ahat ad beddlen fell-i ccyara-nsen<Ṭṭaleb-nni yenna-yi-d : ‚A Meẓyan a gma wellah ad tbaṣiḍ.‛. Imir teḥqeɣ ulac fell-i leslak, neṭqeɣ s wurfan nniɣ-asen : ‚Bbuṣeɣ i wakken ad baṣiɣ, asmi ad iyi-ṭṭfen ad baṣiɣ.‛

Ukiɣ-d si targit !

# Iɣaḍ-iyi lḥal

Ufiɣ-d iman-iw deg uÆerqub yettusemman « Ugni Iḥeddaden ». AÆerqub-nni yezga-d ddaw leÆzib « imexlaf », d ayla n yiwen isem-is LeÆmara n WaÆrab. Waleɣ zdat-i sin n yilmeẓyen yiwen isem-is Belqasem, wayeḍ Ḥmed adiɣec. Ṭṭfen iÆekkazen d izuranen ad myewwaten yes-sen ? Ttwaliɣ deg-sen yal wa itekkes-d i wayeḍ si tsawent, la ttemgabaren maca banen-iyi-d mačči seg wid yettnaɣen. Ar dqal Belqasem ineggez yuli ɣer
teslent, Ḥmed yetbeÆ-it yekka-as-d sufella yessers-it-id. MyetbaÆen di tmurt rran d asawen. Waleɣ Ḥmed yetti-d d yiwen isem-is AÆmer u Belqasem. Belqasem yekkes-as aÆekkaz-nni i AÆmer, yewwi-t rran d asawen. Lḥan kra n yisurrifen, Belqasem yewwet AÆmer s uÆekkaz-nni i as-yekkes. AÆekkaz-nni mi t-yewwet tizerṭeṭṭit yerra-d srid ɣer-i, kniɣ tḍill-iyi tyita-nni, nleqmeɣ, yerna-d tiyita s uÆekkaz-is, aÆekkaz-nni ad d-itetti di tmurt armi i d-yelḥeq ɣer-i, wexxreɣ ɣer deffir, yelḥeq-d s amkan-nni seg i d-ttixreɣ, yeḥbes.

Ufiɣ-d iman-iw deg yiwen n udrar llant deg-s tizemrin meqqrit aṭas, yal tazemmurt tsenned ɣer-s tezrut tameqqrant. Llan yid-i tlata n yilmeẓyen, nelsa talaba n tserdast. Fehmeɣ nella di lawan n beddu n imenɣi d yiÆdawen-nneɣ, neṭṭef leslaḥ gar yifassen nhegga iman-nneɣ ɣer yimenɣi. Sliɣ i yilmeẓyen-nni la ttemcawaren, lemcawra-nni d aneẓẓef i uggaden mi iÆdawen-nneɣ deg waṭas, nukni drus yid-neɣ. Rǧiɣ deg yilmeẓyen-nni armi i d-ḥeṣṣneɣ, uɣalen di tandemmit ɣef wayen i wumi nḥerkel ad t-nexdem, neṭqeɣ nniɣ-asen : ‚Xas ulayɣer i tneẓfem ay-atmaten, d nekk ara iqablen lgirra-agi weḥd-I‛. Ḥulfeɣ ḥersen-iyi-d waman n tasa, zziɣ iman-iw lḥiɣ kra n yisurrifen dduriɣ taẓrut, ggareɣ aman n tasa ɣer teẓrut-nni. Iḍill-d deg-i yiwen n uÆsekri iwehha-d ɣur-i s ifassen-is d ilmawen, yestarḍeq s yimi-s amzun yeqqars-d fell-i s uzrar n rṣaṣ. Sliɣ yenna-id : ‚Dayen nenɣa-k a Meẓyan‛.

- 312 -
Nekk fehmeɣ-d asterḍeq-nni s yimi ineqq amzun d rṣaṣ, maca tebteɣ-d iman-iw mazal ur mmuteɣ ara; xas akken d aÆsekri i d-istreḍqen fell-i d amezwaru, dduriɣ taẓrut, lÆesker ad ttḍillin yiwen yiwen, win i d-iḍillen deg-i ad wehhiɣ ɣer-s s yifassen-iw am wakken s leslaḥ, ad setreḍqeɣ s yimi-w armi i d-myelḥaqen di sebÆa ɣlin d lmeyytin.

Nekk ufiɣ-d ttwajerḥeɣ, rriɣ d akessar s trewla, itbeÆ-iyi-d s lmus yiwen d mmi-s n xali isem-is Lmulud. Ttazzaleɣ s tmara, armi zegreɣ i yiwen n yiɣzer, mi greɣ asurif ɣezzifen zegreɣ i yiɣzer-nni, tuli-yi-d tfasuxt seg ljerḥ-nni.

Kurrbeɣ ɣer tmurt, Lmulud yelḥeq-d deffir-i, zziɣ-d ɣer-s zwireɣ-as-d s yifassen-iw, akken ma yewwet-iyi-d s lmus-nni ur d-issawaḍ ara tiyita s aniɣer yebɣa. Maca mi yi-d-yufa akken d amejruḥ, yenna-id: ‚Atta-n Dehbiya n Ḥmed ad ak-tawi ad ak-teṭṭef afus a Meẓyan, ufiɣ-d tameṭṭut-nni ɣer tama-w tesnelqem-iyi-d beddeɣ s yiwen n uḍar sserseɣ iɣil-iw ɣef tayet-is, teṭṭef-iyi-d afus.

Leḥḥuɣ s usqejdeḥ. Mi nelḥeq s abrid ameqqran yestiwen aṭas, ufiɣ-d zdat-i Lmulud yesqiṭṭeÆ-iyi-d s lmus; tameṭṭut-nni ulac-itt! Lmus-nni d amecṭuḥ anect n yiccer n umdan. Lmulud la yi-d-yettgabar yes-s akken ad iyi-nneɣ.

Nekk Æusseɣ iman-iw, gubreɣ-t armi i as-d-kkseɣ lmus-nni, yuɣal ɣer deffir, nekk kemmleɣ abrid-iw ɣer zdat d asawen. Lḥiɣ kra n yisurrifen, daɣen ufiɣ Lmulud yesqiṭṭeÆ-iyi. Llheɣ la ttberriɣ fell-as armi i t-sɣefleɣ kkseɣ-as lmus-nni wis sin, kemmleɣ tikli-iw s lewhayem nniɣ-d wehmeɣ ansi akka i as-d-tekken lemwas-agi, mi as-d-kseɣ yiwen ad d-yawi wayeḍ!

Cikkeɣ ad yili win i as-id-

- 313 -
yettaken lemwas-agi, maca deg ubrid-agi ur yella umdan wala axxam, tigi d lewhayem!

Kemmleɣ abrid ɣer zdat, ufiɣ Lmulud yesqiṭṭeÆ-iyi- akked gma-s s ujenwi. Sliɣ i teɣri tenṭeq-d tenna-yi-d: ‚Lmus-nni d lmus bu tcekkalt, d Ḥsen ibehlal i as-t-id-yefkan i Lmulud‘. Mmuqleɣ di lmus-nni la ceṭḥeɣ s tergagit.

Waleɣ yiwen n uÆecciw di tama n wadda, yesÆa afrag yezzi s uɣanim; tawwurt n ufrag-nni tqubel s abrid. Walaɣ yiwen n urgaz ibedd-d deg ufrag-nni, takɣerc yewwet-is teffeɣ-d d lÆella qrib ad as-taweḍ ɣer tmurt!

MqellaÆeɣ d Lmulud armi i as-d-kkseɣ lmus-nni, neṭqeɣ nniɣ-d: ‚Tebra yemma-s i Ḥsen ibehlal i as-d-yefkan lmus!‘. Yeffeɣ-d urgaz-nni, yenna-yi-id: ‚Ula d kečč tebra n yemma-k‘. Yelḥa-d mi i d-yewweḍ zdat-i, yeṭṭef lmus-nni deg ufus-is yenna yi-d: ‚Mmuqel hata, d lmus bu tcekkalt‘.

Yerra ixef-nni n lmus d asawen, waleɣ aḍad-is ccahed yers di tcekkalt-nni n lmus amzun di zznad n ubeckiḍ. Kemmleɣ abrid-iw d asawen, leḥḥuɣ ttmektiɣ-d ayen akk yeḍran yid-i, ttḥulfuɣ yettsax-d fell-i udrar n lxiq.

Rriɣ ɣer wul-iw mi ur sÆiɣ ara tagmat ad d-ineÆren fell-i. La ttruɣ ttneẓifeɣ armi sliɣ i teɣri tenna-d: ‚D acu-t akken a Meẓyan?‘. Mmuqleɣ ɣer deffir, waleɣ d yiwen i rriɣ d aḥbib di tallit-nni, i d-yelḥan.

Beddeɣ rǧiɣ-t armi i d-yewweḍ, twenseɣ yes-s amzun kra ur yeḍri yid-i, ttekleɣ fell-as ad inÆer fell-i. Yenna-yi-d: ‚D acu-t akka a Meẓyan?‘. Nniɣ-as: ‚A Lḥusin a gma d Lmulud i la iyi d-yettabaÆen s lemwas, tiniḍ d nekk i as-yenɣan baba-s.
netta aṭas i la t-id-yettÆawanen, ma d nekk d awḥid ur sÆiɣ ara ula yiwen d amḥaddi siwa Rebbi. Lmulud, yal mi ad d-yawi lmus ad as-t-id-kkseɣ, armi i as-ten-id-kseɣ irkulli‛. Nelḥa kra n yisurrifen ɣer zdat, nbedd, yenna-id Lḥusin: ‚Maca a Meẓyan uqbel ad d-awḍeɣ ɣer-k sliɣ-ak-d tettruḍ, tuggadeḍ!‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚ A Lḥusin wellah ma d tuggdi i yuggadeɣ, bexlaf iɣaḍ-iyi lḥal ttruɣ‛.

Lḥusin yenxaryaḍ ɣer deffir yuɣal d ulac. Mmuqleɣ ɣer zdat, waleɣ abrid-nni yettkemmil d asawen, srid am ubrid n terṣaṣt, yerna iḍul aṭas aṭas. Rriɣ rrna d ssber i wul-iw, nniɣ-d :‛ ttkal ɣef Rebbi‛. Greɣ asurif ɣer zdat, Lḥusin yella-d yid-i amzun ur iwexxer ara fell-i, sliɣ yenna-yi-id : ‚Di lejdid-nni waleɣ-d imeṭṭawen deg wallen-ik a Meẓyan, yerna yehwa-ak kan tettruḍ lliɣ ak-id-tabaÆeɣ‛.

Nniɣ-as: ‚ Welleh ma d tuggdi a Lḥusin, bexlaf iɣaḍ-iyi lḥal ɣef wid i yi-kerhen, ad as-d-ttaken lemwas i Lmulud ad iyi-d-yettabaÆ yes-sen, iɣaḍ-iyi lḥal ttruɣ‛.

Ufiɣ-d iman-iw di tmaneɣt n Lezzayer di temdint yettwaseman Lmuradiya, lliɣ di lejmaÆ qqimeɣ di rrif. Yiwen urgaz d amcaybu ibedd ɣer usawaḍ yebda ameslay : ‚Di tallit n lgirra-nni iÆeddan, llan tlata n yimezdaɣ di tmanaɣt n Lezzayer, yiwen isem-is Racid Messayasi, nleqqmeɣ beddeɣ s asawaḍ, neṭqeɣ nniɣ-as : ‚Teslam ay-atmaten acu i awen-d-yenna gma-tnneɣ AÆmer UyaÆqub, yenna-awen-d : llan sebɛa n yirgazen di tmanaɣt n Lezzayer. Ma tura hatta-n teččur d imezdaɣ, yerna deg-sen siwa wid-nni ur neÆtib ara di lweqt n yimenɣi. Asmi i tefra lgirra d nutni i d imezwura ṭṭfen
timezduɣin akked lmaḥellat. Ma d ibudraren msakit ur d llhan ara d uyagi seg lferḥ mi ifak fell-asen leÆtab u lÆiqab n Fransa! llhan d « taḥya lezzayer » ferḥen s wid yemmuten d ccuhada, mi yewweḍ lÆahed-nsen; farḥen daɣen s warraw-nsen i d-mazal yesseḥder-iten Rebbi i tuffɣa n ufransis seg wakal azzayri yettwasqan s yidammen n ccuhada. Yerna ur gminen ara ad d-yili akka uɣellet s leqfaza, nutni ɣilen dakken Æetben ara ɣelten maca teffeɣ-asen targit mxalef. Haten-a ariḍa mazal-iten di leÆtab

Argaz-nni ileqqem-d ameslay yenna-d : ‚D tidet i awen-d-yenna Meẓyan ay atmaten, yir lweqt yezha wid swayes tettendelli tmurt. Ma d wid s wayes tettzuxxu, haten-an di leḥzen seg teɣriwin i sen-d-tessawaḍ ɣer wulawen d wallaɣen-nsen. Yerna Æuhden-tt ad ḥeznen alamma tzux yes-sen.

Di tmanaɣt ufiɣ-d iman iw deg ubrid « Xlifa buxalfa » lweqt fehmeɣ-t d asmi i tefra lgirra: 1962. Ttwaliɣ tamdint texla, tiḥuna ttwamedlent, tikerwas ḥebsent, kra din ur yesÆa bab ! Beddeɣ smuquleɣ akkin akka armi waleɣ yiwet n tḥanut telddi tewwurt-is, taḥanut-nni tufrar akk ɣef tiyaḍ-nni, teÆǧeb-iyi mačči d kra ! Nniɣ-d : ‚Taḥanut-agi ad tt-sÆuɣ d ayla-w, maca ur tt-keččmeɣ ara acku uggadeɣ ad d-tnadi fell-as ddula, imi ur sÆiɣ ara lekwaɣeḍ-is; ad ttuÆaqbeɣ. Ad beddeɣ kan dagi zdat n tewwurt ad rǧuɣ ma waleɣ tnuda-d ddula ɣef tḥanut-agi, ad wexxreɣ, ur qqareɣ ara d ayla-w, ma rǧiɣ ulac win i d-inudan, ad as-d-xedmeɣ lekwaɣeḍ s tejÆal ad tuɣal inu.

Takerrust-agi daɣen tufrar akk ɣef tiyaḍ-agi, ad tt-sÆuɣ d
ayla-w.‛ Mi  rǧiɣ ulac ddula, taḥanut-nni tban-iyi-d   d lqahwa   kecmeɣ  d   bab-is, ɣur-i yiwen uxeddam       d aqehwaǧi. Ata yekcem -d yiwen n urgaz yewwi-d yid-s sin n  warraw-is  d  arrac, argaz-nni isem-is SsaÆid   d ameɣras aqbur, yeqqim   ɣer ṭṭabla    d warraw-is. Netta yessuter  lqehwa, arrac-nni d  llatay,    yessewjed-asen uqehwaǧi. Nekk   ḥulfeɣ yeffeɣ-iyi leÆqel si lferḥ. Ma d amjahed-nni yufar ɣef wudem-is lekmir (leḥzen). Uzgeɣ-d ɣef tewwurt smuquleɣ ɣer barra armi ẓriɣ yiwen n urgaz iqseḍ-d srid ɣer lqahwa-nni. Fehmeɣ-t ad yili d amceyyeÆ n ddula seg wid yettnadin    ɣef cci i d-teǧǧa Fransa mi teffeɣ tamurt n Lezzayer. Imir ur zmireɣ ara ad    ṭṭfeɣ iman-iw seg targigit nniɣ-d : ‚Ma yestqsa-yi-d ɣef bab n lqahwa-agi, ad as-iniɣ     ur tesÆi ara bab. Mi d-yewweḍ urgaz-nni, iruḥ srid ɣer umjahed-nni ileḥḥu ɣer-s s uxatel armi yewweḍ    deffir-is; yettsiggi akken ad iẓer d  acu yessuter i yiman-is d wacu yessuter i warraw-is, yuɣal yezzi-d ɣur-i yenna-id : ‚I wagi ixelleṣ ayen akka yeḍleb netta d warraw-is ?‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Ssusem ma ulac ad ak-id-isel, winna  d amjahed‛.. Yenna-d  s  isuɣan: ‚Ma      d amjahed! d acu iyi-ruḥen deg-s‛.

Mmuqleɣ-t ɣer wudem, waleɣ-t iberquqec akk wudem-is ad as-tiniḍ yuḍen tazarzayt. Nniɣ-d deg ul-iw : waqila ula d wagi d amjahed, atan yeččur wudem-is d ccamat ! Ufiɣ-d ddukleɣ yid-s nleḥḥu deg yiwen ubrid d rrif n tebḥirt taɣerfant; nelḥeq ɣer tqernit taneggarut n tebḥirt-nni nbedd nniɣ-as : ‚Maca mi i d-tenniḍ wagi ma ixelleṣ neɣ ala, winna d amjahed, ur tuggadeḍ  ara ad ak-id-isel ?‛.
Yenna-yi-d: ‚Ayɣer i ma yesla-id! i nekk ur juhdeɣ ara yid-s, tenwiḍ nekk d zzuǧ ṣurdi? D akken ijuhed i juhdeɣ‛. Mmuqleɣ ɣer wudem-is waleɣ-t yezmumeg-d s teḍṣa, maca taḍṣa-nni tufrar fell-as lḥecma. Rrekkzeɣ allen-iw di tmuɣli-s, neṭqeɣ s rrfu nniɣ-as: ‚D amjahed kečč?‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚D amjahed yerna ih!‛.

Ufiɣ-d lliɣ d snat n telmeẓyin d tiyessetmatin: yiwet isem-is TasaÆdit, tayeḍ isem-is Cabḥa, ṭṭfent tirni leqqḍent azemmur deg yiwen n uÆerqub yettusemman « Agni iḥeddaden » tilmeẓyin-nni, mi i d-ufiɣ lliɣ yid-sent fehmeɣ ad asent-iliɣ d aÆessas neɣ d amwanes. Ṭṭfeɣ tirni gar-asent ad tent-ttÆawaneɣ armi nessili tirni, uɣalent ɣer tzemmurt-nniḍen. Llhant d ccɣel-nsent nekk beddeɣ nnig n terni llhiɣ deg-sent s tmuɣli d umeslay n ugaber <Nutenti la seÆraqent ameslay, llhant kan d uzemmur-nsent.

Mi waleɣ ččurent tacwarit, iban-iyi-d lḥal d lawan n jjuǧ; tisaÆtin-nni i sÆeddeɣ yid-sent amzun d ddqiqat. Maca uɣaleɣ di llum: amek ara iniɣ i babat-sent seg tṣebḥit ar tmeddit d acu i tent-imuḍlen di lexla?. Neṭqeɣ nniɣ-asent: ‚Yyamt ad nruḥ sixfemt‛. Tameẓyant tarfed tacwaritt-nni; lḥiɣ ɣer-s amzun ad tt-id-Æawneɣ, nekk sduriɣ iman-iw ɣef weltma-s, ččḥeɣ tinna s tmuɣli n tayri la as-ttmeslayeɣ. Mi d-tmuqel ad as-remceɣ s tiṭ, nettat tban-iyi-d tessetḥa seg-i, Mi sḥerseɣ deg-s tmuqel-d, tarmec-d tiṭ, waleɣ tiṭ-is ad as-tiniḍ d tiṭ-nni n tyaẓiḍt mi ara tt-termec. Tewwet-d gar-aneɣ tafat n trisiti ufus, waleɣ trisiti-nni telḥa-d deg yiwen ubrid n uḍar d anaṣli, ṭṭlam
yeɣli-d mazal-d tafat siwa di ṭṭeyya-nni n trisiti. Nniɣ-as i tlemẓit-nni : ‚Anwa wagi i d-iḍillen deg-nneɣ s trisiti, yya-n ad nruḥ ma ulac ad aɣ-d-iwali‛.

Nelḥa armi qrib ad nekcem s abrid-nni, nbedd. Tilemẓit-nni tenṭeḍ-d s abardi-w, nekk ḥulfeɣ ters-d fell-i leḥya.

Lḥal yetti-d d azal, tamexluqt-nni teččeḥ-d deg-i s tayri. Nekk ma refdeɣ tiṭ-iw ad d-isax udrar n nnif, taggara sliɣ tenna-d : ‚Ayɣer akka a Meẓyan tseɣliḍ-d leḥzen fell-ak !

Teǧǧiḍ tamert, icebbuben ula d amcaḍ ur temcciḍeḍ ara, ayɣer akka i testehzayeḍ deg iman-ik ? Kečč a Meẓyan ur tettxemmimeḍ ara. Mmuqleɣ-tt, waleɣ tufrar-d tayri ɣef wudem-is, sṭebṭbeɣ s ufus-iw lewhi n walleɣ-iw, nniɣ-as : ‚D nekk ur nettxemmim ara ? Lufan ad twaliḍ d acu yellan deg ugarruj-agi n walleɣ-iw, ad wehment lewhayem-im‛.

Tenna-yi-d : ‚ Ihi ayɣer i tḥezneḍ ?‛. Nniɣ-as :

Ad am-id-iniɣ asefru : «

I d-yewwin izli s yisem-iw

Mi ṣubbeɣ i wallen-iw

Ad iclex deg yiles-ines »

Nniɣ-d ixef usefru, ayen mazal deg-s yeÆreq-iyi. Nelḥa negzem deg ubrid-nni, nerra d asawen deg ubrid yessawaḍen ɣer leÆzib-nneɣ, taqcict-nni tedda-d d uberdi-w, weltma-s-nni tezwar zdat-neɣ. Nekk leḥḥuɣ smektayeɣ-d deg usefru-nni, nelḥeq ɣer yiwet n tɛettabt deg ubrid-nni, mmektiɣ-d kra deg usefru-nni, nniɣ-d: ‚A wi t-yerran d iman-iw Ad t-izdeɣ wul-iw
Iẓer acu d lebayen-ines

Nella deg yiwet n tmazirt yettusemman « Amalu » tezga-d ddaw n uxxam-iw, tamazirt-nni tban-iyi-id tenneÆzal d sin n yiqwiren. Tarfiqt-nni tenna-yi-id : « D acu i d lmeÆna n yimeslayen-agi a Meẓyan ?. Nniɣ-as : ‚Lemmer ḥed ad t-yezdeɣ wul-iw, ad iẓer d acu i d leɣbayen-is‛. Waleɣ deg yiqwiren-nni temɣi-d cclaḍa d taleqqaqt, sin n yuɣyal ksan-as, yiwen di tlemmast n uqwir n tama ufella, wayeḍ deg uqwir n tama n wadda, nekk mmektiɣ-d taggara n usefru-nni nniɣ-d :

« Leḥzen yers-d d amur-iw

Yura-d ɣef yisem-iw

Ur yeksan ḥed tunt-ines »

Tezga-d tmuɣli-w di tmeṭṭut-iw, waleɣ-tt tbedd-d tama n ttejra n tčinat, la yi-d-tesmuqul. Nekk mi tt-waleɣ ssetḥeɣ seg-s mi d-tettwali akken ddukleɣ d tlemẓit-nni xas ma ttwalament-iyi. Dɣa ufiɣ-d ssebba s ccɣel i d-ddukleɣ yid-sent, neṭqeɣ ɣer tlemẓit-nni yellan d aberdi-w, nniɣ-as : ‚Ad d-ḥwiɣ aɣyul-inna, ma ulac ad yerki kra din. Tenna-yi-d: ‚Ala, ur k-id-yecqi ara, anef-as‛. Lliɣ snefleɣ aḍar-iw s aqwir-nni, uɣaleɣ swexxreɣ-t-id. Uɣaleɣ ɣer tis snat-nni ciwreɣ-tt ɣef uɣyul-nni wis sin, tenna-d: ‚Anef-as ur k-yecqi ara‛. Unfeɣ-asent i telmeẓyin-nni, qesdeɣ abrid s axxam-iw.

Ukiɣ-d si targit !

- 320 -
D aɣyul d amdan !

Lliɣ d tmeṭṭut-iw deg uxxam-nneɣ, lawan n lmeɣreb akken kan yebda ad d-yettrusu umḍellas. Sexsiɣ taftilt, taftilt-nni seg tid n zzman aqbur. Nettmeslay ɣef tlufa n lweqt-nni deg i nella, uɣaleɣ mmektiɣ-d aɣyul-iw ǧǧiɣ-t di berra, neṭqeɣ ɣer TasaÆdit nniɣ-as : ‚Ǧǧiɣ aɣyul-nni-nneɣ di lexla, uggadeɣ ad t-ččen wuccanen, ad ruḥeɣ ad t-id-jemÆeɣ s axxam‛.

Nleqmeɣ-d beddeɣ di tarkkent n tzeqqa, waleɣ tagust tenta di tlemmast n wagens, yettwaccid ɣer-s umrar yeffeɣ seg lḥiḍ n tarkkent ɣer berra ! nniɣ-d: ‚Ziɣ yettuccid, ad ruḥeɣ kan ad t-id-awiɣ s axxam‛.

Fɣeɣ mi leḥqeɣ deffir n uxxam, ufiɣ aɣyul-nni, mi i leḥqeɣ ɣer-s, lawan yetti-d d aneɣelluy n yiṭij. Waleɣ aɣyul-nni ur yettuccid ara, nehreɣ-t-id ad t-id-awiɣ s axxam.

Llheɣ yid-s akken ad t-id-skecmeɣ s abrid, maca ansi i bɣuɣ kkiɣ-as-d ad yerr anda-nniḍen; yegguma ad yekcem s abrid yuɣal ad as-tiniḍ d asif iḥemlen. Sḥerseɣ deg-s anekcum s abrid d awezɣi.

Nehreɣ-t-id s tmara nleḥḥu nnig ubrid, ddaw ubrid, armi newweḍ nnig n uxxam. D tamazirt i yellan nnig ubrid. Waleɣ ulac ẓẓerb di tamazirt-nni seg yal tama, yella-d kan gar-as d ubrid ɣer zdat.

èẓerb-nni yesÆa tiseɣlit teḍyeq aṭas i unekcum seg-s ɣer ubrid. Din-a daɣen rwiɣ amhetway d uɣyul-nni, bɣiɣ ad t-id-sÆeddiɣ seg umḍiq-nni ad yekcem s abrid, maca d netta yettara akin d wakka.

Nekk ad as-qqareɣ : ‚Ad ak-yehdu Rebbi kcem s abrid
akken ad ak-awiɣ s axxam‛. Ḥyewweteɣ s lehdiya n Rebbi armi tlata n tikal, yenṭeq-d amzun d amdan, yenna-d :

‚Yerna acḥal n tikal i yi-d-temliḍ iberdan ufiɣ-ten lhan‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Ad ak-yehdu Rebbi imi iberdan akk i k-mleɣ tufiḍ lhan, ad tafeḍ ula d wagi d abrid yelhan, Æeddi seg umḍiq-inna ad d-tkecmeḍ s abrid‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚D lmuḥal ad aɣeɣ abrid-a i yi d-temliḍ kečč‛.

Ufiɣ-d lliɣ deg umkan ideg ufiɣ aɣyul-nni, waleɣ azgar yettuccid seg wacciwen-is ɣer tama-w. Azgar-nni fehmeɣ-t d areggal. Nniɣ-d deg wul-iw : lamer ad yerwel ad yeglu yes-i ad iyi-skerker. Waleɣ yiwen n urgaz yeṭṭef azgar-nniḍen seg yimeẓẓuɣen ad t-yezzuɣur ɣer dduzan n tyerza yersen gar sin n yizgaren-nni.

Argaz-nni fehmeɣ-t d afellaḥ i d-yewwin azgar afellaḥ ad t-yeqqen d uruggal-nni, akken aruggal-nni ad t-id-yerr d azgar afellaḥ. Azgar-nni afellaḥ mi yeẓra d areggal ara ikerzen, yegguma ad d-yefk  aqeddem ɣer lmaÆun d uzaglu. Afellaḥ-nni yeskerker-d azgar-nni afellaḥ ad t-id-yettqeddim s tmara.

Nekk tekkeɣ di tmurt s yiḍarren d yifassen akken ad sÆuɣ tazmert ur iyi-iɣelleb ara uruggal-nni i d-yettwacidden ɣer tama-w. Afellaḥ yisemlil sin-nni n yizgaren, yerfed azaglu, akken yers ɣef tmegraḍt-nsen bdan ttembarrazen armi i d-leḥqen ɣer-i srewten-iyi. Ttembarrazen rekkin deg-i armi mmuteɣ.

Ukiɣ-d si targit !

1981

- 322 -
Inebgawen n ddunit

Beddeɣ di tlemmast n wagens deg uxxam-iw, hulfeɣ yusa-d usallay deg wul-iw yenna-d: Hatna-n usan-d sin n yeḥbiben-ik d inebgawen qqimen deg uÆecciw-nni yellan zdat n uxxam. Mi dliɣ s aɛecciw-nni, ufiɣ-ten yiwen d aḍeggal-iw Muḥed u isa, wayeḍ d aḥbib-iw di tallit-nni isem-is Rabeḥ u Reẓqi. Qqimen tayet ɣer tayet, rran gar- asen tagejdit yellan di tlemmast n wagens n uÆecciw-nni.

Weltma teqqim tsenned s aɣrab n uÆecciw tqubel s wudem ɣer yinebgawen-nni. Kecmeɣ ɣer-sen sterḥbeɣ yes-sen, ufiɣ ameslay deg yimi n weltma d taḥkayt n urgaz-is asmi yesker yennuɣ « taḍeggalt d yemma-s » yenna-yas: ‚Mačči mmi-m texliḍ-as axxam, tebɣiḍ ad iyi-tgeḍ am netta. Yuɣal yeddem-d rruba n unejmuÆ ad as-yefk times, suɣeɣ fell-as kkseɣ-as-tt-id, maca iserɣ-itt, i d-tenna Lǧuher di teḥkayt-is.

Neṭqeɣ nniɣ-as: ‚YesÆa lḥeqq mi yesker, axaṭer d kemm akked yemma-m i t-id-yekksen i baba-s i t-yesÆan d amaẓuẓ n tasa-s, ixummes fell-as, ula ɣer Tizi n tewser-is. Lǧuher tezmumeg s teḍṣa, nekk nniɣ-as: ‚A Lǧuher a weltma, ur ttamen ara s rrbeḥ mi yella leflas. Ur ttamen ara s tezmert mi yella waṭṭan. Ur tettdummu ara tudert, mi tella lmut. Lemmer ad taɣeḍ awal-iw axir-am ad tamneḍ s Rebbi i kem-id-ixelqen, ad as-terreḍ mmi-s i baba-s, ad as-terreḍ yemma-s i mmi-s, uqbel ad akem-ifat lḥal ma tnedmeḍ!‘

Weltma tqerreb iman-is ɣer inebgawen-nni, sekkren taḍṣa d unecreḥ.

- 323 -
Ufiɣ-d lliɣ deg umkan yettusemman Izezza n at CaÆban deg ubrid aqbur. Ddukleɣ d sin n yeḥbiben-iw i d-yerzan ɣer-i. Muḥed u isa ulac-it yid-i, yuɣal-d deg umkan-is yiwen n uḥbib-iw isem-is Remḍan. Nelḥa kra n yisurrifen ẓriɣ yiwen d mmi-s n Æemmi isem-is AÆmer, ineqqec tineqqlin di tmazirt yellan ddaw ubrid-nni. Rriɣ tamuɣli-w ɣer-s, afeɣ-d qqimeɣ weḥd-i. Nniɣ-d : Anida-ten yirfiqen-nni ?‛. Nekk wwiɣ-ten-id ɣer tegnit n umdun ad xerrfen, nutni ur ḥṣiɣ ara ma Æeddan ɣer zdat, neɣ uɣalen ɣer deffir. Ad ruḥeɣ ɣer teÆwint-inna amer ad afeɣ albaÆḍ seg tid-nni yettnecraḥen s tayri ad tt-gabreɣ.

Uliɣ-d d asawen qesdeɣ ɣer taÆwint-nni yellan deg umkan yettusemman Lḥedd n Muḥ u AÆli. Mi uliɣ d asawen s sin n yisurrifen, ad d-teccḍeɣ d akessar s tlata n yisurrifen. Uliɣ s tmara armi qrib ad Æeddiɣ i ugafa-nni. Leḥqeɣ ɣer tnijjelt ṭṭfeɣ deg ugeṭṭum-is Æemmdeɣ ad id-ntun isennanen wala ad grirbeɣ. Mi selkeɣ seg tuccḍiwin-nni mmuqleɣ ifassen-iw ulac ula d lmara n usennan deg-sen.

Mmuqleɣ ɣer teÆwint-nni ulac tin i d-yusan ad tagem, beddeɣ di ttexmim armi sliɣ i umeslay yekka-d seg tama ugemmaḍ yuder-d ɣer teÆwint-nni. Ameslay-nni tebteɣ d tiɣri n yiwen yellan d igellil si temẓi ar tewser-is, netta di laÆmer yemmuɣben. Yezga d axeddam s telqimt amzun d amÆiwen, maca lxir-is tettɣummu-t tgullelt-is.

Ssawalen-as Muḥ n baṭel; ččḥeɣ tamuɣli-w ur waleɣ ara argaz-nni, selleɣ kan i teɣri-s. Zziɣ mmuqleɣ ɣer deffir waleɣ taqcict teksan sin n yizgaren deg umkan yettusemman « Amalu imexlaf ». Taqcict-nni isem-is Ǧeǧǧiga,

- 324 -
Tbedd zdat n yizgaren-nni tqubel ɣer-sen. Di tama n wadda tella Æemmti-s, tezga tmuɣli-s ɣer Ǧeǧǧiga; Ǧeǧǧiga teṭṭef aÆekkaz, izgaren-nni qqarnen iman-nsen tayet ɣer tayet, ṣṣifa-nsen deg wudem d icebḥanen, di tfekka d iberkanen, i yewwet fell-asen yinezḍ d amellal. Ǧeǧǧiga telsa taqendurt tamellalt. Mi i d-tezzi teẓra-iyi-d la yi-d-tesmuqul ɣer yizgaren-nni. Nekk ttwaliɣ deg yizgaren-nni amzun ksan, nutni bedden am yiblaḍen ur ḥarken ula s wallen-nsen! ḍḥiɣ wehmeɣ deg-sen. Ar dqal, taqcict-nni, s tmuɣli n tayri, tuɣal tetti-d d ṣṣifa n tmeṭṭut-iw, nniɣ-d: ‚D TasaÆdit i la yi-d-yesmuqulen ahat ur tbeqqu ara ma tẓer anida akka ttagment telmeẓyin. ḍḥiɣ-d nneḥcameɣ seg-s. Tetti-d d Ǧeǧǧiga, uɣaleɣ daɣen ɣer tmuɣli-nni n tayri. Tamexluqt-nni tettbeddil, ma yi-d-tmuqel d TasaÆdit, mi tuɣal d Ǧeǧǧiga ad tmuqel ɣer sin n yizgaren yuɣalen am yimeblaḍen, knan i tmegraḍ-nsen ad as-tiniḍ ddaw n uzaglu i llan!

Lḥiɣ qesdeɣ abrid s axxam-iw, mi leḥqeɣ ɣer tmeksawt-nni ufiɣ-d lliɣ weḥd-i, kemmleɣ abrid-iw. Mi wwḍeɣ s axxam ḥulfeɣ s Æeyyu, ẓẓleɣ iman-iw deg wussu i-yellan di tlemmast n wagens. Iḥbiben-nni i d-yennebgan ɣer-i waleɣ-ten deg umeṭreḥ yellan di terkent. Rabeḥ yeṭṭes, ma d Remḍan yesgunfa kan, ttwaliɣ-t ldint wallen-is, neṭqeɣ ɣer-s nniɣ-as: ‚A Remḍan amek armi ur teddim ara yid-i? Kemmleɣ abrid weed-I‛. Yenna-yi-d Remḍan: ‚D Rabeḥ u Reẓqi i d-yuɣalen s axxam‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Nudeɣ fell-awen ad aken-awiɣ ad txarfem, ziɣ kunwi deg uxxam i tellam‛. Waleɣ-t yesselḥay igumas-is fehmeɣ-t d
tabexsist ara iteffeẓ. Mi yismeblaÆ ; yenna-d : ‚Targit am tagi a Meẓyan, Rabeḥ u Reẓqi d Muḥed u isa. Ma d Remḍan d kečč, tuẓameḍ-as ». Nniɣ-as : « Targit am tagi ɣileɣ d nekk i d Rabeḥ u Reẓqi. Maca tura fehmeɣ-tt am akka i d-tenniḍ‛. Yetti-d lḥal d lawan n yiḍ, aftilt tecÆel deg uxxam-iw, nekk lliɣ deg wussu weḥd-i, ẓẓleɣ iman-iw la ttmettateɣ, ttneẓẓifeɣ ula d lewṣaya-w ulac, win iwumi ara tt-id-ǧǧeɣ, ḥulfeɣ s wul-iw la yettferfir. Sserseɣ afus-iw s lewhi-s. Ufiɣ la iɣeṣṣeb aṭas, zziɣ s tmuɣli-w ɣer tama n zelmeḍ, ufiɣ-d yemma teqqim-d ɣer-i, neṭqeɣ nniɣ-as : ‚A yemma la iɣeṣṣeb wul-iw ad mmteɣ!‛. Tenna-yi-d: ‚Ala a mmi ur tettmettateḍ ara.‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Nniɣ-am a yemma la iɣeṣṣeb wul-iw ad mmteɣ‛. Tenna-yi-d: ‚Attan ula d taqcict-nni la iɣeṣṣeb wul-is, ur temmut ara!‛. Mmuqleɣ ɣer tama n uyeffus, waleɣ snat n telmeẓyin ẓẓlent deg wussu-nni. Fehmeɣ d tinna i d-yellan ɣer-i i d-tenna yemma tuḍen ul-is ula d nettat. Maca waleɣ udem n tlemẓit-nni mačči d udem n tin yuḍnen, d udem n tin yennecraḥen. Ufiɣ-d neẓẓel di tlemmast n ubrid uḍar, neṭqeɣ ɣer yemma nniɣ-as : ‚Tagi xas tuḍen tettara-d tisegnatin ad teḥlu. Ma d nekk la iɣeṣṣeb wul-iw ad mmteɣ!‛. Ufiɣ-d yiwen tama-w fehmeɣ-t d ṭṭbib, argaz-nni yestemɣer d amecyabu, yessers-d afus-is ɣef lewhi n wul-iw, yesṭebṭeb, yeḍsa-d ɣer-i, yenna-yi-d : ur ttuggad a Meẓyan ur tettmettateḍ ara. Ul-ik ur yehlik ara, ul-ik yeččur d ‘dd heb’.

Ukiɣ-d si targit !

1981

- 326 -
Mazal amennuɣ

Ufiɣ-d iman-iw lliɣ deg umkan yettusemman Timeqbart n yiÆmaraten, beddeɣ zdat n tneṭlin, lsiɣ tabluzt tettemcabi ɣer tlaba n tserdast, llheɣ di tebluzt-nni la tt-ttqissiɣ ma fell-i i d-tettwaxdem. Qublen-iyi-d sin n yilmeẓyen d atmaten, ččḥen-d tamuɣli; ameqqran deg-sen isem-is Muḥ n Ḥmed, wis sin Akli n Ḥmed Akli iluÆa gma-s, yenna-yas: « Yyan kan a Muḥemmed ad twaliḍ talaba-agi yelsa Meẓyan! Uzzlen-d ɣer-i rran-iyi gar-asen, nleḥḥu la yi-d-smuqulen ɣer tlaba-nni la ttmestewtawen fell-i. Di serriya-nni-nsen fehmeɣ-d kan wehmen amek i ssawḍeɣ ɣer tlaba-nni n tserdast, ansi i d-tekka! Mi newweḍ s amkan-nni ideg yella Muḥ yuɣal d ulac, Akli yuɣal d akuder ugar ɣef wakken yella, di lewṣayef-is ibeddel ad as-tiniḍ mačči d netta! Zdat-neɣ tella yiwet n terga srid d akessar armi d anida i d-tenneqḍaÆ s tÆersyewwet. Targa-nni fehmeɣ-tt d abrid ideg ara nerr timzizelt akked Akli, win ara yesḍallen aḍar-is i tÆersyewwet-nni, yerbaḥ di temzizelt.

Yuzzel ukuder-nni ttwaliɣ deg-s xas akken yedda s lewhi di terga-nni tuḍyiqt, maca mi yewweḍ ɣer tÆersyewwet-nni yesnelqem aḍar-is, yecceḍ uḍar-nni iɣef ibedd yeɣli. Mi leḥqeɣ nekk rriɣ aḍar-iw ɣer deffir, wwteɣ yes-s ɣer zdat, iḍill i tÆersyewwet-nni Ælayen s lqis n tiddi-w. Mi d-rriɣ aḍar-iw akken ad beddeɣ fell-as, waleɣ asennan yenta deg uḍad-iw ccahed. Imir rriɣ ɣer wul-iw, nniɣ-d: ad
ferḥeɣ mi i rebḥeɣ tamzizelt-agi lemmer ur iyi-yenti ara usennan. Lḥiɣ kra n yisurrifen s wurfan d uɣilif, uɣaleɣ beddeɣ akken ad d-kkseɣ asennan-nni. Refdeɣ aḍad-iw mmuqleɣ-t ur waleɣ ara deg-s ula d lmara n usennan.

Zziɣ s tmuɣli-w ɣer deffir, ẓriɣ tarbaÆt n yilmeẓyen lsan talaba n tserdast, nutni d ucbiḥen n wudem, ttbanen-d s ṣṣifa n yimaziɣen, mmuqleɣ ɣer zdat iban-iyi-d ubrid n ukarus yettwaxdem d amaynut yebda-d seg yiwen n leÆzib aqbur yettwasemma « LaÆzib n yimusaten » di laÆzib-nni llan aṭas n ikamyunen n tserdast, ččuren d lÆesker n waÆdaw, ara sewjaden ad ruḥen deg ubrid-nni.

Nekk fehmeɣ lliɣ d amḍebbar ɣef terbaÆt n yimeɣrasen, nniɣ deg wul-iw: yettɣaḍ-iyi lḥal, yettḥettim-iyi. La ttwaliɣ aql-aɣ drus yid-neɣ, nxuṣ ula d leslaḥ. AÆdaw s yal ttawil n yimenɣi, maca ad as-neqwu s tduki-nneɣ, ilaq ad ten-nqabel akken i ten-qublen imezwura-nneɣ, rnu d nekk ara yezwiren.

D acu kan ur asen-nettruḥu ara udem allen, ilaq-as usqiṭeÆ mi akka yegget fell-aneɣ, neṭqeɣ ɣer tarbaÆt, nniɣ-asen: ‘Yyaw ay atmaten ad nettkel ɣef Rebbi ad nruḥ ad nsqiṭeÆ i waÆdaw-nneɣ’. Nessewjed iman-nneɣ, uzzleɣ d amezwaru zdat n tarbaÆt.

Mi leḥqeɣ zdat n LaÆzib-nni ufiɣ aṭas n yibardan n ukerrus ttwaxedmen d ijdiden, gar-asen iban-iyi-d yiwen n ubrid ddaw n LeÆzib-nni, yewseÆ aṭas ḥebsen deg-s ikamyunen, sufella-nsen ttwarekkzen lemdafeÆ. Ttwaliɣ lemdafeÆ-nni wehhan-d akk ɣer-i, ma d lÆesker ur ẓriɣ ula d yiwen!

Nniɣ-d deg ul-iw: awwah, win yennan tiẓgi texla, d netta i-yexlan.
Tedduɣ s uxatel, ufiɣ-d iman-iw weḥd-i, maca nniɣ-d ulac tuɣalin ɣer deffir. Leḥḥuɣ deg yiwen n ubrid gar yixxamen armi qrib ad awḍeɣ ɣer lemdafeÆ-nni, ẓriɣ zdat-i aÆemmur n rrmel dduriɣ ɣer-s, heggaɣ iman-iw s leslaḥ.

Ar dqal nniɣ-d : aÆemmur-agi n rrmel ur yettara ara fell-i tiyita n lemdafeÆ. Wexreɣ kra n yisurrifen ɣer deffir. Kerfeɣ tagecrart, wwteɣ s usarjur n rṣaṣ armi ifuk. Mmuqleɣ ɣer deffir, waleɣ yiwen d amjahed d yiwen n yilemẓi n taddart-iw isem-is AÆrab, yella-iyi-d d aḥbib di targit !

LuÆeɣ-t nniɣ-as : ‚Yya-n ṭṭef-d amkan-iw di laÆḍil ad swejdeɣ iman-iw, atan ceÆleɣ times deg ikamyunen-inna n waÆdaw‛. Imuqel ɣer zdat iwala tekker tmes s tyita-nni i wwteɣ, yuzzel-d yuzga-d deg umkan-iw, wexreɣ ɣer deffir swejdeɣ-d rṣaṣ, ttraǧuɣ AÆrab ad yewwet, waleɣ-t yeqqur am umeblaḍ nniɣ-as : ‚Wwet ur ttuggad, laÆmer deg ufus n Rebbi ay AÆrab‛.

Yessufeɣ yiwet n terṣaṣt, yeḥbes tiyita, yezzi-d ɣer-i yenna-yi-d : ‚Dayen fakeɣ-ten‛.

Iwexxer-d ɣer deffir, nekk uzzleɣ s amkan-nni rniɣ tiyita armi ifak usɣerjur-nni. Waleɣ ikamyunen-nni tekker deg-sen tmes, heggaɣ i tyita-nniḍen. Nniɣ deg wul-iw : wigi ur d-nerri ara tiyita ad ilin sduran iman-nsen ɣef lmut, neɣ bɣan ad iyi-d-ḥerren si tama-nniḍen, ad id-wwten s lexdaÆ.

Wexxreɣ-d ɣer deffir, leḥḥuɣ smuquleɣ ɣer yal tama armi qrib ad d-ffɣeɣ seg LaÆzib-nni, waleɣ tarbaÆt n yilmeẓyen la ttawin ttarran cebbḥen iman-nsen s tlaba n zzhu, ḍḥiɣ wehmeɣ deg-sen ! Nniɣ deg wul-iw : ad twehmeḍ deg yilemẓyen-inna amek i ten-ihennan.
wulawen-nsen, la ttwalin di lbaṭel iḍerrun, atmaten-nsen la ɣellin, nutni ur ḥaren ara, mačči ad kkren ɣer lǧihad. luÆeɣ yiwen deg-sen, nniɣ-as : ‚Ulac lÆeskar di tama-inna ansi i d-tekkam ?‛. Yenna-yi-d: ‚Ulac, ur d-usin ara akken ad k-id-ḥrren‛. Nniɣ-asen: ‚Kunwi amek i ken-mazal d ičičiten ? Atmaten-nwen la tettwalim deg-sen ffɣen ɣer lǧihad, mačči ad ten-tecbum, imezwura-nwen yessufɣen aÆdaw si tmurt‛. Nnan-iyi-d: ‚Mi aɛdaw yeffeɣ amek i tebɣiḍ ad d-nexleq aÆdaw-nniḍen ?‛. Nniɣ-asen: ‚Yeffeɣ waÆdaw mazal wayeḍ, ur yettwaɣumu ara yiṭij s uɣerbal, tettafem-d ssebba am win i iwumi i tekkes tuggdi n ṭṭlam yeqqar-as uggadeɣ leḥram. Teḥṣam kan yihwah yettwaxdem s zzhu. Ur teḥṣim ara deg-s tufḍiḥt, fell-as tandemmit. Ma d iseɣ xas fell-as leÆtab, deg-s tucbiḥt d rreḥma, ulamma twenseɣ si lǧiha n Rebbi, tweḥceɣ si lǧiha-nwen, iɣaḍ-iyi lḥal mi di yal lḥers d waÆdaw. AÆdaw yeddukul fell-aneɣ, nekni tuget deg-nneɣ teddun ɣer tama-s, nniɣ-awen ilit d irgazen yettawi nnif, ad nemmet d imjuhad, neɣ ad nidir d iḥruren.

Ufiɣ-d lliɣ weḥd-i d ameksa mebla actal, deg umkan yettusemman Lḥedd n Muḥ u Qasi. Ul-iw la yettḥebbir ɣef yinnig i yi-yehman di tallit-nni, xas akken innig-nni iban-iyi-d d d aɣerreb maḍi, maca mačči d aÆraq, rnu d llwajeb. Dayen yellan d lwajeb fell-i ad ǧǧeɣ arraw-iw am yifrax-nni imecṭaḥ yeǧǧa babat-sen di lÆecc<Lliɣ ttḥebbireɣ armi sliɣ i umeslay di rradyu i d-yersen zdat-i, fkiɣ tameẓẓuɣt, fehmeɣ d tadwilt i d-tsewjad yiwet isem-is TasaÆdit, tsemma-as « Ayen i d-nesmekti ». Mi d-tefka udem n
tedwilt, ar dqal tqeddem-d s asawaḍ yiwen n yilemẓi i d- yusan d inebgi n tedwilt. Ilemẓi-nni d acennay. Di tazwara yebda-d s uẓawan yesÆan rruḥ n ccna n tmaziɣt, mi i d- yessetbeÆ imeslayen-is, yenna-d di ccna-s : ‚Ḥṣiɣ nekk nnaÆtabeɣ, kečč atan tezhiḍ aṭas, tendemmeḍ ɣef wussan-nni, tewwiḍ tamegḥelt ɣef wammas, tura ad as-iniɣ i gma, ad ak-id-nesseḥder yiwen wass‛. Mi yesneqḍaÆ, tenṭeq-d llal n tedwilt tsuÆef ccna-nni s rruḥ n tsertit. Mi tessusem, yenṭeq-d ucennay-nni s useḍsu, yenna-d : « Yeḥreq ddin n lemqamat-nsen‛.

Ufiɣ-d lliɣ ugemmaḍ deg wayla n yiwen isem-is LeÆmara n WaÆrab. AÆerqub-nni yettwasemma « Urti n Ḥsen ». Ufiɣ yiwen d ilemẓi yeksa tifunasin, isem-is ebdelqader yettwasemma d amrabeḍ. Ilemẓi-nni di tilawt d amdan n yiman-is kan, iḥemmel ad imeslay yid-i acku tedduɣ-as di lewhi-s‛. LuÆeɣ-t nniɣ-as : ‚A ebdelqader, tesliḍ i yilemẓi-nni i d-yecnan di tedwilt-nni iwumi tsemma TasaÆdit ‘Ayen i d-nesmekti’, yecna-d. Ar dqal yenna-d « Iḥreq ddin n lemqamat-nwen » yak yesÆa tirrugza ɣef tidet ?‛. Waleɣ udem-is yexṣer, yenna-yi-d : ‚Aywah ! Mi tura akka i aɣ-d-qqaren, yegra-d kan ad d-nehreɣ actal- iw!‛.

YertaÆ tifunasin-nni s uÆekkaz, uɣaleɣ banen-iyi-d llan ula d izgaren. Tiyita deg uzgar tayeḍ di tfunast. YetbaÆ actal-nni armi ur frizen ara s aniɣer ara rren, mi waleɣ akken yeffeɣ-it laÆqel, uzzleɣ ɣer-s nniɣ-as : ‚S laÆqel kan a ebdelqader, ula d nekk ihi d amrabeḍ, laṣel-iw seg udrar n at Mexluf, at Mexluf d imrabḍen, d uqriben n at Uḥwari.
Imir yesteḥla amzun kemzeɣ-as anda yebɣa, nuɣal nemlil tayet ɣer tayet nleḥḥu nettmeslay, sliɣ yenna-yi-d : ‚Ccix-nni n at Uḥwari qrib ad yaweḍ ɣer yigenni‛. Nniɣ-as : ‚ d tidet i d-tenniḍ a ebdelqader, ula di lgirra-nni iÆeddan, sliɣ ɣef ccix-nni yewweḍ ɣer yigenni s lberhan-is‛.

Ufiɣ-d iman-iw deg yiwet n taddart deg udrar di tmurt ur ssineɣ. Lḥiɣ d asawen deg ubrid awesÆan armi kecmeɣ ɣer taddart-nni. Leḥqeɣ ɣer yiwen n umraḥ ideg ufiɣ rreḥba n tmeɣra tebḍa ɣef snat n trebbaÆ, yiwet d irgazen, tayeḍ d tilawin.

Zdat n terbaÆt-nni n yirgazen, yella yiwen d accenay yeqqim ɣef ukersi iqubel ɣer tlawin-nni, yeṭṭef snitra gar yifassen-is icennu. Mi wwḍeɣ kecmeɣ talemmast n rreḥba s ccḍeḥ-nni i d-wwiɣ d amaynut.

Selleɣ i yirgazen i d-qqaren : akken a Meẓyan akken, tilawin gummant ad sneqḍaÆent taɣratin. Nekk tḥenceɣ aṭas, simmal rennuɣ di ccḍeḥ simma rennuɣ di tussna-s, ɣer taggara, acennay-nni Æerqent-as ad as-tiniḍ d abujad n ccna.

Mi teḍra akken, nniɣ-as : ‚Awi-d snitra-nni gar yifassen-iw, ad twaliḍ wid yekkaten‛.

Qqimeɣ ɣer tama-s, yefka-iyi-d lewṭer-nni imir mmekteɣ-d nekk yellan ur ssineɣ ara, rriɣ iman-iw ssneɣ ! nniɣ-d : Ad ttekleɣ ɣef Rebbi amer ad tt-id-awiɣ di ṣṣwab.

Ttnadiɣ di ccna s snitra-nni tizlit i rriɣ ad tishil fell-i ad tt-id-awiɣ s snitra, ad afeɣ ur ssineɣ ara ula s ccna n yimi.

Imnezzhen ttraǧun deg umusnaw, amusnaw d nekk. ḍḥiɣ-d tfakk fell-i ddunit, nniɣ deg wul-iw : waqila ɣurreɣ kan iman-iw!. Sliɣ yekker wawal di snitra-nni s teɣri n llal n tedwilt-nni i wumi sliɣ di rradyu ! Imir yuɣal-iyi-d rruḥ
mi fehmeɣ « Ameslay-nni n truḥanit i yi-ttÆawanen, tella-d seg lawliya  ṣṣaliḥin ». Fkiɣ tameẓẓuɣt sliɣ tenna-d :

‚Awi-d tizlit-nni n Ḥnifa « Ruḥ di laman ay aḥmam...

Xas, akka mazal ur yettkil ara wul-iw, armi sliɣ i lexyuḍ n snitra Ælayet teɣri-nsen. Imir refdeɣ tizlit-nni tuzga-d di ṣṣwab n tussna. Mi tebÆeɣ s yisefra-is, ad d-tcennu yid-i snitra s yisefra n tezlit-nni, selleɣ deg-s teɣriwin n yirgazen d tid n tlawin.

Cniɣ yid-sen: Ruḥ di laman ay aḥmam, nekk ul-iw wellah ur imal, ruḥ ay aḥmam, ul-iw yettaɣ-ak awal. Mi refdeɣ ixef n tezlit s yisefra, cniɣ: Ruḥ ay aḥmam di laman, seg wul-ik kkes aḥebbir; daɣen Æiwnent-iyi-d teɣriwin.

Mi ssiwleɣ s anegzum n tezlit, nniɣ-d: akken bɣunt ṣeÆbent lemḥan labud aɣrum ad yezwir<Dagi cniɣ kan weḥd-i, ttwakksent teɣriwin-nni.

Dɣa rriɣ ɣer wul-iw nniɣ-d : ma ttwakksent-iyi teɣriwin i yi-d-yettÆawanen, yettwakkes-iyi lberhan. iwdeɣ-d i wayen i d-cniɣ armi tlata n tikal, tḍerru-yi-d am tikkelt-nni tamezwarut.

Tikkelt taneggarut mi ssiwḍeɣ nniɣ-d : labud aɣrum ad d yezwir ; ufiɣ-d iman-iw cniɣ weḥd-i.

Ukiɣ-d si targit !
