- 333 -
# Tamurt-nneɣ

Lliɣ akked yiwen n yilemẓi deg udrar yettusemman « Iɣil lḥedd n ccix »; amkan-nni tella deg-s talast yebḍan gar sin n laÆrac di zzman iwumi qqaren (MÆatqa, Tirmitin). Ilemẓi-nni fehmeɣ-t d aḥbib-iw n taddart n Iẓerruden; ulamma d lxelq ur ssineɣ. Tezga-d tmuɣli-w ɣer yiwen n wurti i d-yellan s lqerb-nneɣ; urti yettusemman « Ugni n AÆli » waleɣ sin n watmaten akked Æemmi-tsen la ttḥerkilen ad qqnen tayuga n yizgaren.

Atmaten-nni amenzu deg-sen isem-is Muḥ u Ḥmed, amaẓuẓ Akli n Ḥmed. Gar-i d uḥbib-nni ukked lliɣ tella snitra. Refdeɣ-tt-id gar yifassen-iw wehheɣ-tt amzun d abeckiḍ, neṭqeɣ s aḥbib-nni, nniɣ-as: ‘Yallah ad nruḥ’. Bɣiɣ ad t-rafqeɣ alamma d taddart-is, nleḥḥu, zziɣ ɣer yifellaḥen-nni s tmuɣli-w, waleɣ unfen i ccɣel-nsen rran-d lwelha-nsen ɣer-neɣ.

Ufiɣ-d snitra-nni ṭṭfeɣ-tt s yiwen n ufus, iḍudan-iw rsen ɣef lexyuḍ-is, ad tettawi tizlatin, nekk ssetḥeɣ seg yifellaḥen-nni yemcaraken tagmat maca ur ksaneɣ ara i tukksa n iḍudan-iw seg lexyuḍ-nni n snitra; ma snelqmeɣ-ten-id neṭḍen, ma ḥemẓeɣ-ten tettzad-d teɣri n uṭenṭen di lexyuḍ.

Ufiɣ-d nuɣal s amkan-nni seg i d-nebda tikli, tezga-d tmuɣli-w deg yiwen uÆerqub n uzemmur yettusemman « Ḥlafa ». Waleɣ yiwen n ufellaḥ d amrabeḍ ssawalen-as Si Reẓqi, ilemẓi-nni ukud qqimeɣ yetti-d d yiwen n uḥbib-iw, zeÆma ula d netta d amrabeḍ isem-is Reẓqi, neqqim
deg yiwen n ubrid d arqiqan, d abrid n tala. Sliɣ i ufellaḥ-nni isuɣ-d fell-aneɣ yenna-d : ‚D acu la txeddmem kunwi deg umkan-nni ideg teqqimem ?‛ . Nekk fehmeɣ yusem seg-neɣ xas akken abrid-nni d abrid n yinugamen, mačči n tnugamin,  ddiɣ-as di  tecnant, nniɣ-as : ‚la nettraǧu aggur‛. Afellaḥ-nni yetti-d d yiwen ssawalen-as Si SsaÆid. Aḥbib-nni yetti-d d lxelq ur ssineɣ, nniɣ-as : ‚Yalleh ad nruḥ ɣer Iẓarruden!‛.

Iẓerruden d yiwet n taddart i d-yellan ɣer zdat n wanida akken i nella. Nelḥa kra n yisurrifen, ilemẓi-nni yetti-d d yiwen n yilemẓi n taddart-iw, isem-is AÆrab, d aḥbib-iw zeÆma. Waleɣ AÆrab tufrar tuggdi fell-as seg yimezdaɣen n taddart-nni n Iẓerruden, yenna-yi-d : ‚A Meẓyan, nekk uggadeɣ!‛.  Nniɣ-as :  ‚Nekk ur uggadeɣ ara acku at taddart n Iẓerruden merra d iḥbiben-iw, yella kan yiwen deg-sen mxallafeɣ yid-s, maca zemreɣ ad d-iniɣ ma yufa-yi-d deg ufrag-is ur ireffu ara fell-I‛. Aḥbib-nni n taddart-iw yetti-d d yiwen n uḥbib n taddart Iẓerruden, sliɣ yenna-yi-d : ‚Yerna win-a ukkud temxallafeḍ, tura yegguǧ si taddart n Iẓerruden‛.

Ufiɣ-d leḥḥuɣ akked yilemẓi-nni, newweḍ qrib ad neffeɣ i yiwen n umadaɣ, imir ḥṣiɣ ssiwḍeɣ winna i rufqeɣ s anida iwilem ad t-ssiwḍeɣ. Myuǧǧeɣ yid-s s sslam. Netta ikemmel abrid ɣer taddart-is, nekk uɣaleɣ-d s ansi i kkiɣ. Ufiɣ-d leḥḥuɣ akked WaÆrab-nni n taddart-iw, mi nelḥq ɣer tlemmast umadaɣ-nni, nbedd. Amadaɣ-nni d lxelwa n yimrabḍen yettusemman « Ibehlal » nukni neḍḥa-d nuggad seg at lxelwa-nni, zziɣ ɣer WaÆrab akken ad t-
sruggzeɣ, waleɣ-t iÆelleq abeckiḍ n ṣṣyada, luÆeɣ-t nniɣ- as : ‚Awi-d abeckiḍ-nni ay AÆrab ad ttwaliḍ amek i kkateɣ rṣaṣ. Win ara d-iḍillen ɣer-neɣ ad t-sÆeddiɣ, maca Æemmer abeckiḍ-ik s rṣaṣ‛. Yemmeɣ ɣer tɣuggaḍt n ukrṭuc, yeddem-d yiwen yerra-t i ubeckiḍ-nni yellan d ilem, yefka-iyi-t-id. Mi d-kkseɣ akerṭuc-nni mmuqleɣ-t waleɣ daxel is d aḥlalas! Mmuqleɣ AÆrab, yenna-yi-d : ‚D rṣaṣ ! »

Wifqeɣ lekdeb, rriɣ akerṭuc-nni s abeckiḍ. Ṭṭfeɣ abeckiḍ-nni s yiwen ufus serseɣ aḍad-iw di zznad. Waleɣ tarbaÆt, n yirgazen seg At lxelwa-nni, kecmen-d s amadaɣ-nni ttraǧuɣ deg-sen ma d nukni i d-qesden. Win ad irefden tamuɣli-s ɣer-neɣ ad ṣubbeɣ fell-as zznad. AÆrab-nni yellan d amwanes-iw waleɣ-t tfak deg-s tarwiḥt seg tuggdi; ma d nekk twenseɣ s ubeckiḍ.

Mi waleɣ imdanen-nni ulac win yeṭṭfen ula d aÆekkaz, rnu seg umezwaru-nsen ɣer uneggaru ula d yiwen deg-sen ur d-yerra ddehn-is ɣer-neɣ, Æeddan d imsebriden deg umadaɣ-nni. Yelḥa-d yiwen n yilemẓi si tama n MÆatqa, Æeqleɣ-t n taddart-iw isem-is Lḥusin, yemlil-d d tarbaÆt-nni, uqbel ad yaweḍ ɣer-sen ibedd; immuqel-iten, immuqel-d ɣer-i.

Waleɣ-t yejbed di lbunt n ugirru yekkes-itt-id seg yimi-s, iḍeggar-itt. TarbaÆt-nni leḥqen-d ɣer-i Æeddan d ubrid-nsen. Iban-iyi-d yiwen urgaz yenneÆzal di tarbaÆt-nni, iÆelleq abeckiḍ n ṣṣyada ɣef tayet-is la ileḥḥu weḥd-s, tama n tarbaÆt. Ula d Winna yerra kan abrid gar wallen-is.

Mi faten fell-aneɣ, afeɣ-d nezzi-d s tikli ɣer tama n taddart-neɣ, nleḥḥu di tlata; nekk ṭṭfeɣ abeckiḍ ttnadiɣ ad sḍadeɣ. Mi nekcem akal n lÆerc-nneɣ sliɣ i Lḥusin yenna-
yi-d : ‚Atan ujeḥmum‛.  Waleɣ  ajeḥmum   la iceṭṭeḥ    s waffug, yuɣal yers sufella n teslent i d-yellan zdat-neɣ...

Mi wehheɣ   ɣer-s s ubeckiḍ, yennelqem  la iceṭṭaḥ   ɣef teslent-nni, nekk ttabaÆeɣ deg-s armi i t-id-wwiɣ     di nnican. Yetti-d d izinzer-nni ixellun tiɣrasin n tzizwa, yers ɣef lǧedra n teslent-nni ; zziɣ mmuqleɣ ɣer deffir, waleɣ ajeḥmum-nni la iceṭṭeḥ nnig iqerray-nneɣ, ṭṭfeɣ fell-as. Mi yeffeɣ waÆber, yeffeɣ  d aÆbar n nnefs ! fehmeɣ  isebṭel ubeckiḍ nni. Nniɣ-as i WaÆrab : ‚ D acu yuɣen abeckiḍ-agi ay AÆrab ? ». Yenna-yi-d : « Amer  ur  s-tekkiseḍ    ara tacekkalt!‛

Ufiɣ-d tacekkalt-nni n ubeckiḍ tedda-d deg ufus iw. Rriɣ-tt s amkan-is, ṭṭfeɣ tikkelt tis snat ɣef ujeḥmum-nni yeɣli, mi   dliɣ   fell-as    ufiɣ-t  d  yiwen    n       ufrux yettusemman « Melqeḍ   izan ». Refdeɣ-t-id, lḥiɣ     ɣer yirfiqen-iw, ufiɣ wayeḍ n ufrux am winna, nniɣ-d : ‚Ziɣ mačči yiwen i sseɣliɣ!‛. Nniɣ ufiɣafrux wis tlata, winna yettcabi s aÆarus, nniɣ-d : ‚Ziɣ mačči yiwen neɣ   sin i sseɣliɣ s waÆber-nni!‛.  Mi  leḥqeɣ  ɣer    yirfiqen-iw, mmuqleɣ  s ifassen-iw ufiɣ siwa afrux-nni i d-sseɣliɣ si tegnawt, mmuqleɣ-t nniɣ-d : ‚ziɣ mačči d winna ssneɣ, wagi d afrux yessewhamen, ur tessineɣ ara gar yifrax n tmurt iw ! Yenna-yi-d: ‚Wagi qqaren-as ‘Abiffi’‛.  Nniɣ-as : ‚D melqeḍ izan i wumi qqaren Abiffi ?‛. Yenna-yi-d Lḥusin: ‚Ih‛.

Afeɣ-d iman-iw leḥḥuɣ deg yiwen n ssuq, d win ur ssineɣ; ttnadiɣ win  ixeddmen   isebbaḍen   ad     iyi-d-isemmer isebbaḍen-iw. Leḥḥuɣ   armi i ufiɣ taxxamt i fehmeɣ    d
taxxamt n usemmar n yirkasen. Beddeɣ zdat n tewwurt, waleɣ ɣer daxel tella ṭṭabla tesÆa rebÆa n tqernay, qqimen ɣer-s tlata n yirgazen d imcuyba. Yal wa deg-sen, yeṭṭef amkan ɣer tqernit n ṭṭabla. Sin ur ten-ssineɣ ara ula di lewṣifat-nsen, ma d wis tlata d zzaÆim AÆmiruc. Afeɣ-d beddeɣ ɣer ṭṭabla-nni gar snat n tqernay i d-yellan ɣer tewwurt n texxamt-nni. Mqabaleɣ d AÆmiruc ad yettwarḥem ttwaliɣ deg-s yelsa talaba n tserdast, maca tacacit-is tettwaxdem am tcacit-nni tazewwaɣt, n yiqbayliyen. Taqernit-nni tama n AÆmiruc, d tilemt, ma d sin-nni i d-yellan ɣer-i, yiwen la iberren lxiḍ d takurin. Mi yebren takurt ad tt-isÆeddi ɣer tqernit-nni tilemt ur nesÆi ara bab-is. Ma d wis sin-nni yeṭṭef izḍi, ibedd sufella n tqernit n ṭṭabla-nni ittenneḍ lxiḍ deg yizḍi-nni. Lxiḍ-nni d lqez amellal yella deg-s uzuwwaɣ; di yal lqis n tɣerdast di lxiḍ-nni, azuwwaɣ-nni yettwasbaɣ s lqis n uḍad cached. Uɣaleɣ waleɣ ula d lmarḥum AÆmiruc la iberren lxiḍ ɣef yizḍi. Ttwaliɣ abran n lxiḍ-nni mačči d ayen isehlen, yessewham aṭas! Mi nnḍen takurt s yizḍi, ad tt-isÆeddi wis tlata-nni ɣer tqernit-nni tilemt yellan tama n « lmerḥum ». Nekk, fehmeɣ-ten d iṣemmaren n yisebbaḍen, ttraǧuɣ deg-sen ad iyi-d-rren imesmaren i yisebbaḍen-iw.

TaswiÆt akka waleɣ xedmen-d lkettan s lqis n ṭṭabla-nni; lkettan-nni d amellal yesÆa arqem d azewwaɣ am yidammen. Rrqem-nni yettban-d di lkettan-nni yecban lukfen, am yiẓuran di tfekka n umdan! Waleɣ lmerḥum AÆmiruc yestaÆfa mi ifakk lxedma-s si tama yellan ɣer-s.

- 338 -
Lkettan-nni yuɣ-it-id akk rrqem-nni azewwaɣ. Lmerḥum isemxallaf ifassen-is ɣef ṭṭabla, yerfed-d tamuɣli-s ɣer-i. Tamuɣli-nni tettmeslay, yella wayen i d-fehmeɣ deg-s. Mmuqleɣ ɣer lkettan-nni urÆad ifakk s rrqem di tama-nni i d-yellan ɣer-neɣ; mazal lkettan-nni d amellal am lekfen. Maca mazal irgazen-nni ttkemmilen lxedma-nsen. Afeɣ-d iman-iw uɣaleɣ ɣer ssuq-nni, ddukleɣ d tarbaÆt n yilmeẓyen, leḥḥuɣ ttalseɣ-d deg wul-iw i target-nni iwumi ḥusseɣ d leḥzen. Rnu fehmeɣ ilmeẓyen-nni llan yid-i anida akken i lliɣ zdat n yirgazen-nni i la ireqqmen lkettan; neṭqeɣ nniɣ-asen : ‘Lmaɛna n target-nni mi nella di txxamt-nni, wid-nni d takbab n yimaziɣen i la xeddmen’.

# Ukiɣ-d si targit !

Berka waleɣ di lemnam Lliɣ di lawan n yiḍ, yuɣ-iyi lḥal deg wussu di terkent n uxxam-nneɣ; bɣiɣ ad ṭṭseɣ ur iyi-d-yusi ara yiḍes, uɣaleɣ llheɣ d uxemmem. Waleɣ yekcem-d lexyal n ṭṭlam; lexyal-nni iban-iyi-d d tafekka n urgaz, yelḥa-d armi d tarkent-nni, yeɣli-d fell-i. Nekk nleqmeɣ ttergigiɣ si lweḥc, ssiwleɣ i tmeṭṭut-iw nniɣ-as : « Efk-iyi-d
tazalamiḍt ad ceÆleɣ taftilt, ur ḥṣiɣ ara d acu-t akka i d-yeɣlin fell-i ! ».

La iyi-d-tettak tixellal, mi yi-d-tefka taxellalt ad Æerḍeɣ ad att-ceÆleɣ ; mi ur tecÆil ara ad tt-ḍeggreɣ. Tixellal-nni n zalamiṭ ad as-tiniḍ llexsent tkebrit-nsent. Nekk yettzad fell-i lweḥc, uɣaleɣ kkseɣ-as-d tazalamiṭ-nni i tmeṭṭut-iw, ṭṭfeɣ-tt deg ufus-iw la tt-ttcaÆileɣ. erḍeɣ setta n txellal ur cÆilent ara, ma d tis sebÆa akken wwteɣ, tecÆel tezwar-d s dduxxan am uÆbar ma yeffeɣ seg ubeckiḍ.

Waleɣ Taftilt-nni tecÆel uqbel ad tt-ceÆleɣ, ffɣeɣ di tewwurt n uxxam ; beddeɣ di tlemmast n ufrag ceṭṭḥeɣ si tergigit. Ttwaliɣ zrir lḥal, ulac ṭṭlam aṭas di berra, fehmeɣ-d ad yili lawan qrib ad yali wass. Dɣa yella-yi-d di lbal ad beddeɣ din deg ufrag alamma yuli wass akken ara kecmeɣ s axxam.

Imir ur yettili ara wayen akken i d-yeɣlin fell-i; dɣa ad ṭṭseɣ di laman. Tuɣal tmeṭṭut-iw teffeɣ-d, tbedd deffir-iw, sliɣ tenna-yi-d : ‚D acut akka a Meẓyan?‛. Nniɣ-as: ‚Nekk ur ksaneɣ ara s leǧwab. D gma n baba u yemma i d-yeɣlin fell-i di terkent‛.

Tezzi tekcem s axxam, nekk tebÆeɣ-tt. Lḥiɣ armi d tarkent, ufiɣ-d iman-iw lsiɣ tabedÆit n uglim d taziwwaɣt. TabedÆit-nni tuska-yi-d ad as-tiniḍ s lqis-iw i tettwaxdem.

LuÆeɣ tameṭṭut-iw nniɣ-as : ‚LmeÆna n tbedÆit-agi i lsiɣ, d lgirra ara yilin; ad sizzleɣ deg-s idammen-iw‛. TessewÆed s ufus-is ɣer yiwen n ukebci yellan di lḥiḍ n terkent, tenna-yi-d : ‚TabedÆit-nni mačči n inek, n mmi-k; kečč meẓẓiyet fell-ak‛. Waleɣ tabedÆit-nni i lsiɣ tettwaÆelleq s akebci-nni; ttwaliɣ deg-s ad tazgi i uqcic ameẓyan.
nekk d tmeṭṭut-iw neqqim s uqummec di tlemmast n ufrag, nemqabal udem ɣer wudem, nettmeslay. Ḥulfeɣ yefcel ufus-iw ayeffus, refdeɣ-t d asawen. Sliɣ i tmeṭṭut-iw tenna-yi-d : Ɣur-k a Meẓyan ad tseɣliḍ taftilt-nni ɣer tbasant-nni n waman yeḥman!‛. Mmuqleɣ waleɣ taftilt-nni ters-d tama-w; tama n teftilt-nni ters-d tbasant teččur d aman. Neṭqeɣ ɣer tmeṭṭut-iw nniɣ-as : ‚Ur seɣllayeɣ ara taftilt-agi, xas ur ttuggad ara!‛.

Ufiɣ-d beddeɣ di terkent, tameṭṭut-iw tbedd-d deffir-i. Waleɣ iman-iw lsiɣ aserwal d aberkan, deg rrjel-nni ayeffus, llan tlata n yiṣriden n rrqem : amellal, azegzaw, azewwaɣ. Nniɣ-d deg wul iw : iṣerdan-agi d lgirra ara yilin, ad sizzleɣ deg-s idammen-iw. Yetti-d userwal-nni d azegzaw, iṣriden-nni yesÆa di rrjel akessar uɣalen leḥqen lewhi n taɣma-w. Tameṭṭut-iw tbedd-d ɣer yidis-iw nemlil tayet ɣer tayet.

Ufiɣ-d qqimeɣ deg yiwen n yiɣil deg umkan yettusemman « Azeggar ». Di lawan n yiḍ, sliɣ i wawal ddaw n yiɣil-nni. Ameslay-nni d yiwen n yilemẓi la iḥekkun target-is i yirfiqen-is, sliɣ yenna-yasen : ‚Urgeɣ lliɣ dagi; atan usiɣ-d ɣer dagi!‛. Neṭqeɣ ɣer-s nniɣ-as : ‚Tura kan i lliɣ ttarguɣ lliɣ deg yiɣil-agi, aql-i lliɣ dagi ».

Iban-iyi-d yiwen n ubrid d awesÆan di tama n wadda. Waleɣ yiwen n yilemẓi yettawi yettarra di rrif n ubrid-nni. Ilemẓi-nni n taddart-iw isem-is : LaÆmara n WaÆrab. ḍḥiɣ-d wehmeɣ deg-s d acu n ccɣel i yesÆa deg ubrid-nni. Ufiɣ-d yiwen nuḥbib-iw yeqqim-d ɣer tama-w, ilemẓi-nni isem-is Remḍan. Neṭqeɣ, nniɣ-as : ‚D acu la ixeddem tura
LeÆmara n WaÆrab deg ubrid-inna ? ». Remḍan yenna-yi-d : ‚D AÆli n Ḥmed u Sliman i as-t-yefkan‛. Nniɣ-as : ‚wehmeɣ deg-s amek i t-iwekkel ɣef ubrid am winna, ur as-yelli d ajenyur, ur as-yelli d axeddam!‛. Remḍan yenna-yi-d : ‚Dinna i wehmeɣ ula d nekk!‛. Ufiɣ lliɣ deg yiwen n umkan d asuki, yettwasemma « Ugni n Qasi n Muḥ u AÆmer. Lawan qrib ad yali wass. Llan zdat-i sin n yilmeẓyen yiwen n taddart-iw isem-is Qasi u SsaÆid, wayeḍ-nni ur t-ssineɣ ara, fehmeɣ-ten llan d inelmaden di tseddawit. Qasi ibedd di rrif n ubrid; ilemẓi-nni-nniḍen yella ddaw wanda ibedd Qasi. Yeqqim s uqummec yekref tigecrar, rebÆa tezmamin rsent zdat-is. Tella gar-asent yiwet meqqret. Sliɣ i Qasi yenna-yas-d i urfiq-nni-ines : ‚Yalleh d lawan‛. Nekk fehmeɣ yelḥeq-asen-d lawan ideg ara ruḥen ɣer wulmud-nsen di tseddawit. Ilemẓi-nni yerfed tizmamin-nni yerra-tent ɣer yirebbi-s. Ibedd, yeddem-d tazmamt-nni tameqqrant, yeṭṭef-itt gar yifassen-is, yeččeḥ s tmuɣli deg-s; nekk fehmeɣ-d : tazmamt-nni tameqqrant d yiwen umedyaz i tt-yuran s tirga yettargu. Sliɣ i Qasi iÆiwed yessawel i urfiq-is, yenna-yas : ‚Yalleh a wlidi berka; waleɣ di lemnam!‛. Ilemẓi-nni iḍebbeq tazmamt-nni yellan gar yifassen-is yelḥa s arfiq-is; yewweḍ ɣer-s mlilen tayet ɣer tayet.

Ukiɣ-d si targit !

yid Meziane U Lesrar n Ilul Muh di taddart n at Lliv deg yiwen n umkan yettusemman Meatqa . di 27 magu "Amalu n lhedd n ccix 1952. Yebda beddev di rrif yivzer; tamedyazt di 1977 n i8 Imir-nni t-id-yelfa edda-d yiwen n urgaz s tker- leqraya gawaz n wudan vef rustyetteddu yis-s di Ikafat. ddunit; yezzem allav-is armi Takerrust-nni tecbeh atas, i d-vlin yidrisen i yura di &lt;Lesrar anehhar-is daven tecbeh yid,. Di 1982 i yemlal d Dda Lmulud i tlaba-s: Yewwed-d ver-i wumi eegben yidrisen-is atas, am yehbes, yeldi-d tawwurt wakken as-teegeb tmacahut tamezwa- n rut i d-ieeddan deg umattaf wis sindeg tkerrust, yessawel-iyi-d S useggas 1986. Imir-nni t-yuzen ver yisem-iw, yenna-yi-d Tiddukla Tadelsant "Idles" dva dinna Rwah, hwagev-k ! tufa tqabact afus-is Ferhev nniv-d deg Meziane U Muh yura atas n yidlisen, wul-iw timucuha; isefra akked : yidrisen Lemmer ad yili d wagi i d tvamsa. amkellef sleqraya taelayant; ad dduy yid-s ad iyi-yawi $ anda ara kemmlev leqraya:
